# 3.7 Carrier Aggregation Control

## 3.7.0-2 Carrier Aggregation Control Document Owner Jingbo Huang (ID: 11120240)

## 3.7.1 SCell Configuration and Release

### 3.7.1.0-2 SCell Configuration and Release Document Owner Deputy Jing 1. Wu; Jingbo Huang (ID: 11120249)

### 3.7.1.1 Feature Flag

### 3.7.1.2 SCell Configuration

#### 3.7.1.2.0-1 SCell Configuration C-RNTI collision check in SCell (ID: 11120260)

**3.7.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11120265`)

SCell Configuration [Before CB008140-I-UPD008]

In case FR1 CA, during CA UE ext-SCell addition procedure, ext-L2-PS shall check whether the C-RNTI is in use or not. If there is one existing UE using the allocated C-RNTI from prime-Cell, the ext-SCell addition shall be rejected with reason C-RNTI collision.

[CB008140-I-UPD008]

In case FR1 CA, during CA UE SCell addition procedure, L2-PS in SCell shall check whether the C-RNTI is in use or not. If there is an existing UE connection is already using that C-RNTI from PCell, the SCell addition in SCell shall be rejected with reason C-RNTI collision.

[End CB008140-I-UPD008]

---

#### 3.7.1.2.0-2 SCell Configuration P(S)Cell UE Context Update for FR1 CA during Scell Addition (ID: 11120269)

**3.7.1.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12882317`)

SCell Configuration During FR1 CA UE SCell addition procedure, UE context over P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall be modified according to CA UE SCell configuration change. Following parameters shall be included for CA UE SCell context update.

  * numOfCellToModify and cellConfigurationForModification [numOfCellToModify], including configurations of numOfPerCsiReportConfig and perCsiReportConfig[] for SCell channel state report and beam report* and pucchConfig for HARQ-ACK and pCSI report.



Specifically, when gNB-DU receives from C-Plane the request for SCell addition, if the following settings in UE context are different from those included in the SCell addition request, gNB-DU shall update the UE context in P(S)Cell according to the SCell addition request:

  * PDSCH configuration: max number of DL layers (note1);



[CB014871-A]

  * ~~simultaneousPUCCH-PUSCH-SamePriority-r17~~ parallelTxPUCCH-PUSCH-SamePriority-r17: if this field is present in the UE modification request from C-Plane, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall save it in UE context.



[End CB014871-A]

P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall initiate the PUCCH receiving of CSI report and beam report* after SCell activation successfully. Following parameters of SCell configuration in perCsiReportConfig shall determine the number of UCIs bits to decode on PUCCH resource (used to select the appropriate channel decoding method, see 38.211 §6.3.2.1) or the number of CSI bits (part 1) in UCI report to decode on PUSCH resource. 

  * reportQuantity for SCell CSI report for according to 5G_UP_ALG_3626_replaced([11160044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktN0EfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when dlMimoMode don’t equal to “ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4”; Note for FDD + FDD CA UE, dlMimoMode cannot be “ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4".
  * CA UE while FR1 TDD Scell with BF activated: nrOfReportedRS according to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2684_replaced([11303281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tqj_0PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SCell beam report according to 5G_UP_ALG_28236_replaced([11160420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktN0F_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3631_replaced([11160432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktN0GfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) based on SCell actBeamforming feature flag of SCell and dlMimoMode according to 5G_UP_ALG_2680_replaced([11120547](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR02fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * Beam report is not used in FDD and FDD CA.




dlMimoMode: NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode

actBeamforming: NRBTS.NRCELL.actBeamforming

reportQuantity: Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2574_replaced([11300116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqVWZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Notes:

1\. If maxNumDlLayers is downgraded from 4 or 2 to a smaller value during RRC reconfiguration, and the rank of PDSCH before the reconfiguration is larger than the new value of maxNumDlLayers after reconfiguration, then PDSCH scheduling before the 1st CQI report after reconfiguration shall refer to 5G_UP_ALG_12151_replaced([11139277](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3490_replaced([11159137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktHtc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). maxNumDlLayers = 8 is not supported currently, PDSCH scheduling after maxNumDlLayers downgrade from 8 to lower value needs to be explicitly specified when maxNumDlLayers = 8 is supported.

---

#### 3.7.1.2.0-3 SCell Configuration UE context update for SA mode FR2 CA during SCell addition (ID: 11120281)

**3.7.1.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13471623`)

SCell Configuration When 5G-L2-PS instance receives user setup request from C-plane without SCell configuration, then the instance shall:

  * accept the request and handle it without adding any SCell(s),
  * await user modify request with SCell configuration(s) to be added.



When 5G-L2-PS instance receives user modify request following the user setup request in the aforementioned paragraph, then the instance shall update the UE context with the following CA configuration information:

  * Number of SCell(s) to be added.
  * periodic CSI report configuration for channel acquisition for each SCell (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_8301_replaced([11313276](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrplA_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * PUCCH configuration for HARQ-ACK feedback (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_8297_replaced([11313664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrsoQPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * DRBs that can be scheduled in each SCell to be added (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * Periodic CSI-RS allocated to UE in each SCell to be added (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_8485_replaced([11302151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqegQPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * SCell operational mode (“DL only” or “DL and UL”) of each SCell to be added (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2440_replaced([11288415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp6fm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



Note: periodic CSI report for beam management is not configured for SCell in FR2 CA.

[CB013712-B] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-B]

---

#### 3.7.1.2.0-4 SCell Configuration SCell UE Context Update for FR1 CA during SCell Addition (ID: 11120289)

**3.7.1.2.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `12882319`)

SCell Configuration In UE context setup over SCell 5G-L2-PS, DRB configurations, UE capability and P(S)Cell and SCell configurations as follows shall be included in the UE context.

  * numDrbs and drbAddReqPs[numDrbs], for DRB which can be scheduled over SCell.
  * numOfCellConfiguration and cellConfiguration [numOfCellConfiguration], for the SCells to be added while including perCsiRsResConfig (CSI-RS resource) and perCsiReportConfig (periodic PUCCH resource) for SCell beam management* and channel state feedback, For P(S)Cell while including perCsiReportConfig (periodic PUCCH resource) for P(S)Cell channel state feedback;
  * ueCapability, including maxDataRateDl, maxDataRateUl if current SCell is configured with UL CA.
  * Max number of DL layers supported in SCell;



If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PUCCH resources are allocated based on Distributed PUCCH Algorithm (5G_UP_ALG_2884_replaced([11123433](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqi6nfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In UE context setup over SCell 5G-L2-LO, DRB configurations, UE capability and P(S)Cell and SCell configurations as follows shall be included in the UE context.

  * numDrbs and drbAddReqPs[numDrbs], for DRB which can be scheduled over SCell.



5G-L2-LO shall not start to send flow control status information to 5G-L2-HI according to 5G_L2_1932_replaced([11216925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_BiEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* Beam management is not used in FDD and FDD CA.

Note:

  * Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2404_replaced([11285954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp1ABvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for maxDataRateDl and maxDataRateUl.
  * Refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_3816_replaced([11348112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wXgBN_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for simultaneousHarqAckCsi.
  * Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2220_replaced([11282038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpclgvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for perCsiRsResConfig.

---

#### 3.7.1.2.0-5 SCell Configuration Transient Period of SCell Addition for FR1 CA (ID: 11120306)

**3.7.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11120310`)

SCell Configuration Overview

---

**3.7.1.2.0-5.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `12647016`)

SCell Configuration 5G-L2-PS shall consider transient state of SCell addition [CB010741-C] / upgrade [End CB010741-C] during the SCell addition [CB010741-C] / upgrade [End CB010741-C] period.

\- 5G-L2-PS will refer to ([11120331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_pPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as start of transient state;

\- 5G-L2-PS will refer to ([11120344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_p_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as stop of transient state;

  * 5G-L2-PS shall handle the transient period according to ([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11195069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv5UqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));



\- 5G-L2-PS shall suspend the Speculative DTX algorithm according to ([11184154](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

\- For FR1 CA where PCell is a TDD cell, 5G-L2-PS shall not trigger aperiodic SRS during the transient state if nrofSrsPorts is changed in SCell addition [CB010741-C] / upgrade [End CB010741-C];

a) In case of one-shot SCell Addition (see Remark):

\- For FR1 CA where PCell is a TDD cell, 5G-L2-PS shall conduct DL scheduling using only CSS (DCI 1_0);

\- For FR1 CA where PCell is a FDD cell, DL assignment shall be sent in CSS only, that is PCell 5G-L2-PS shall schedule UE with DCI 1_0 scrambled with C-RNTI.

In case of DSS, if SCell Addition is executed after DSS transient phase ([11143994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_233KLvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) was completed and LTE CRS rate matching configuration is known by UE, DL assignment shall be scheduled in PCell with DCI 1_0 scrambled with C-RNTI and PDSCH with configured LTE CRS rate matching pattern ([11098260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km9bEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be applied.

b) In case of step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] accompanied with L1 configuration changes in the PCell, the gNB-DU’s handling of the transient state shall depend on several factors, as described below.

 Not all L1 configuration changes in the PCell require PCell's gNB-DU to enter the transient state. For details on UE’s scheduling during a certain L1 reconfiguration, refer to the relevant requirements describing modifications of the given L1 configuration.   
Among these L1 reconfigurations, which require the transient state:

 for reconfigurations described in ([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall schedule the UE in CSS with DCI format 1_0 (DL) or DCI format 0_0 (UL), as in one-shot SCell Addition case described above in point 1a);

 in cases listed in ([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11195069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv5UqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall exclude the UE from DL/UL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set.

**Notes:**

  * According to TS38.133 section 8.2.1.2, UE is allowed an interruption on any active serving cells (including P(S)Cell) due to SCell addition [CB010741-C] / upgrade [End CB010741-C] or release. **Scheduling shall be interrupted from the time RRC message for SCell addition [CB010741-C] / upgrade [End CB010741-C] is sent and till RRC processing delay timer expiry (see ([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

  * Refer to ([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for nrofSrsPorts.




**Remark:  
To improve the readability of this document, the following terms are applied in this section, although they are usually referring to C-Plane procedures:**

1) ‘one-shot SCell Addition’, which refers to the case, when maximum configurable number of SCells for this UE in this PCell is added on the UE, which is not configured with any SCell yet (i.e. it is reconfiguration: nonCA -> maxCCs); all of the added SCells are configured in a single RRC Reconfiguration procedure.

2) ‘step-wise SCell Addition’, which refers to the case, when a single SCell is added on UE, which is already configured with SCell(s), and no SCells are released during the procedure. [CB010741-C]

3) ‘step-wise SCell Upgrade’, which refers to the case, when already configured DL-only SCell is reconfigured to DL&UL SCell. [End CB010741-C]

---

**3.7.1.2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11120331`)

SCell Configuration Start Point of Transient State

---

**3.7.1.2.0-5.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12647017`)

SCell Configuration When non-CA UE received a Scell configuration request for the first time, this UE will start transient period of Scell addition.

In case of CA UE, which is already configured with SCell(s) (with number of configured CCs lower than maximum for this UE in this PCell [CB010741-C] or is only configured with DL-only SCells [End CB010741-C]), when gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell receives from gNB-DU C-Plane notification that step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] procedure requiring change of L1 configuration in the PCell (see Note) has been started, after N DPA scheduling cycle (see ([11123985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) PCell 5G-L2-PS shall enter the transient state (see ([11123985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11195069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv5UqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note:

Not all L1 configuration changes in the PCell accompanying the step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] require PCell’s gNB-DU to enter the transient state. For details refer to ([11120310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqPYnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.7.1.2.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11120344`)

SCell Configuration Stop Point of Transient State

---

**3.7.1.2.0-5.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12647018`)

SCell Configuration When non-CA UE in transient state received successful Scell addition, this UE will stop transient period of Scell addition, and start to work as CA UE.

In case of CA UE, which was already configured with SCell(s) (with number of configured CCs lower than maximum for this UE in this PCell [CB010741-C] or was only configured with DL-only SCells [End CB010741-C]), when gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell receives from gNB-DU C-Plane notification that step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] procedure requiring change of L1 configuration of the PCell (see Note) has been successfully completed, PCell 5G-L2-PS shall leave the transient state.

Note:

Not all L1 configuration changes in the PCell accompanying the step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] require PCell’s gNB-DU to enter the transient state. For details refer to ([11120310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqPYnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.7.1.2.0-6 SCell Configuration Transient period of SCell addition for SA mode FR2 CA (ID: 11120356)

**3.7.1.2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13471633`)

SCell Configuration For aspects related to UE transient phase on SCell addition, please refer to 5G_UP_7826_replaced([11357617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucdbbfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB013712-B] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-B]

#### 3.7.1.2.0-7 SCell Configuration SCell Configuration for DL and UL (ID: 11120363)

**3.7.1.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11120367`)

SCell Configuration 5G-L2-PS receives for each SCell CaConfigDu parameter(refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2440_replaced([11288415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp6fm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) . If this parameter is set to 1 (DL_ONLY), sCellConfigDedicated.uplinkConfig should not be configured, then the L2 PS UL should ensure that for DL ONLY SCell scheduling in UL is not activated.

Note: For FR1 CA UE, DL_ONLY shall be configured for TDD SCell or FDD SCell so 5G-L2-PS will schedule the TDD SCell or FDD SCell with DL only carrier. With FR1 UL CA support, CaConfigDu = 0 can be supported for SCell configured with both DL and UL.

  * Refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_5114_replaced([11361076](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZV0R_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for sCellConfigDedicated.uplinkConfig.

---

#### 3.7.1.2.0-8 SCell Configuration Buffer based SCell Configuration in FR1 CA (ID: 11120371)

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11120375`)

SCell Configuration Overview of buffer based SCell Configuration in FR1 CA

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `12639227`)

SCell Configuration When gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell requests gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE's PCell to start or stop monitoring of buffer status of all DL [CB010741-A] or UL [End CB010741-A] non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note 1) for given UE, gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE's P(S)Cell shall perform checks and decide when such buffer status monitoring shall be started or stopped – for more details refer to ([11120403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqQmtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB010741-A] for DL or ([12639250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CuK5QEC-EfCal_QUJn4xrg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) for UL [End CB010741-A] .

Upon P(S)Cell’s gNB-DU U-Plane decides to perform DL buffer monitoring, if the DL buffer overflow criterion for SCell Addition is met ([11120516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR00fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and PCell link quality check is met ([11120536](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR01vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell shall notify it to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell.

[CB010741-A]

Upon P(S)Cell’s gNB-DU U-Plane decides to perform UL buffer monitoring, if the UL buffer overflow criterion for SCell Addition is met ([12639251](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Qc0akEC-EfCal_QUJn4xrg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell shall notify it to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell.

If both DL and UL buffer overflow criterion for SCell Addition are met in the same slot, Two notifications shall be sent from gNB-DU to gNB-DU C-Plane, First message shall be for UL, then for DL.

[End CB010741-A]

In addition, if the UE's PCell is TDD FR1 cell, the required power per PRB (It means the non power limited TX power per PRB) which is calculated from the latest PHR report based on a real transmission (V = 0) on PCell (see ([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall also be notified to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell.

[PR878414]  
In addition, for TDD FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE, if UE is not a single Tx UE and aperiodic SRS is configured on PCell and rank1 is used on PCell (see 5G_UP_ALG ([11139957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq79_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))), information about rank1 usage shall be notified to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell.

Rationale: This information shall be used by gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell to exclude TDD SCell candidate from SCell selection for SCell Addition because otherwise such TDD SCell if added will not be activated (see 5G_UP_ALG ([11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))). [End PR878414]

Note 1:

QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in ([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call) and ([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for NSA call).

Note 2: The Buffer Based SCell Addition mechanism is:

 generic, i.e. applicable for one-shot and step-wise SCell Addition;   
in case of one-shot SCell Addition all calculations are executed for P(S)Cell only

\- supported for DL [CB010741-A] or UL [End CB010741-A] non-GBR CA eligible DRBs only.

Note 3:

To reduce CPU cycle cost per slot, buffer status check for SCell addition shall be distributed evenly in a time window. If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE, the interval between 2 checks for a specific UE may vary depending on the number of UEs awaiting buffer status check (not all UEs with check opportunity in a specific slot can be checked in one occurrence of that slot); moreover, the buffer status check can be suspended due to scheduler overload, see ([11120403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqQmtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)[CB010741-A] (DL) [12639250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CuK5QEC-EfCal_QUJn4xrg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) (UL) [End CB010741-A] ) for more information. **Else all the UEs with check opportunity in a specific slot shall be checked in one occurrence of that slot.**

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11120403`)

SCell Configuration Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Configuration in DL Branch – Trigger Conditions

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11120407`)

SCell Configuration Starting of DL Buffer Status monitoring of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-2.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `12879956`)

SCell Configuration P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall **start UE’s all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note1) buffer monitoring for purpose of SCell Addition when:**

\- dlL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Allowed (5G_UP_ALG_29511_replaced([11120477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqRNyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), AND

\- UE does not have any inactive SCell(s) which can be activated (see Note 2), AND

\- PCell’s 5G-L2-PS performed UE overheating handling (5G_UP_ALG_2821_replaced([11121920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and as a result determined MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL > configured number DL_SCell(s) and MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL > configured number DL+UL_SCell(s) (5G_UP_ALG_2824_replaced([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), AND

\- UE is not configured with power saving BWP (5G_UP_ALG_1870_replaced([11111163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), AND

\-  _Inter-gNB_CA_InSync_ _check is passed, (see below point 1.1) , AND_ **

\-  _VoNr_Sag_ON_ _check is passed (see below point 1.2). ._ **

This check shall be triggered when any of the abovementioned condition changed.

If the request to start DL buffer status monitoring for SCell Addition from gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell **is received when the respective monitoring is already running, the request shall be ignored and P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall continue the monitoring without restarting the internal counters related to the monitoring algorithm.**

**(1.1)_Inter-gNB_CA_InSync **check:_** **

If

\- UE is configured with inter-gNB DL CA, and

\- synchronous state for all UE’s {PCell, ext-SCell} pair is ‘InSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22304_replaced([11174858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_22306_replaced([11174867](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

OR

\- UE is not configured with inter-gNB DL CA

then

check is passed

else

check is failed

**(1.2)_VoNr_Sag_ON **check:_** **

If

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = Deact_Scells_VoNr_Sag, and

\- UE is not in the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state (see 5G_UP_ALG_19252_replaced([11205370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwo7h_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19415_replaced([11204797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4MfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

OR

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = None

then

check is passed

else

check is failed

Note 1:

QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call) and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for NSA call).

Note 2, the SCells, which can not be activated:

1\. SCells permanently deactivated due to bad RLQ (5G_UP_ALG_2774_replaced([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) cannot be activated again.

2\. In case of inter-gNB CA, eligibility of ext-SCell to SCell Activation is determined as follows (5G_UP_ALG_15801_replaced([11121970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 If ext-SCell is deactivated due to Xp-U link change to ‘unavailable’ (5G_UP_ALG_12814_replaced([11121981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the ext-SCell shall not be available for activation till Xp-U link recovers to ‘available’ (5G_UP_ALG_14018_replaced([11122068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[CB014088-F]**

3\. Scell not available for activation due to scheduler processing overload, see 5G_UP_ALG_31927_replaced([11122191](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the DL branch specific actions.

**[End CB014088-F]**

4\. In case NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = Deact_Scells_VoNr_Sag and UE is already configured with SCell(s):

 If UE enters the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state the SCells are deactivated; the SCell shall not be available for activation till UE exits the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state (see 5G_UP_ALG_19252_replaced([11205370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwo7h_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19415_replaced([11204797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4MfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11120432`)

SCell Configuration Stopping of DL Buffer Status monitoring of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-2.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `12879998`)

SCell Configuration P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall **stop UE’s all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer monitoring for purpose of SCell Addition when:**

\- dlL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Forbidden (5G_UP_ALG_29511_replaced([11120477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqRNyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), OR

\- UE is configured with inactive SCell(s) which can be activated (see Note 2), OR

\- PCell’s 5G-L2-PS performed UE overheating handling (5G_UP_ALG_2821_replaced([11121920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and as a result determined MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL <= configured number DL_SCell(s) or MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL <= configured number DL+UL_SCell(s) (5G_UP_ALG_2824_replaced([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), OR

\- UE is configured with power saving BWP (5G_UP_ALG_1870_replaced([11111163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), OR

\- If UE is configured with inter-gNB CA and synchronous state for at least one UE’s {PCell, ext-SCell} pair is ‘OutOfSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22304_replaced([11174858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_22306_replaced([11174867](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , OR

\- If NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = Deact_Scells_VoNr_Sag and UE is in the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state (see 5G_UP_ALG_19252_replaced([11205370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwo7h_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19415_replaced([11204797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4MfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

This check shall be triggered when any of the abovementioned condition changed.

If the request to stop DL buffer status monitoring for SCell Addition from gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell is received when the respective monitoring is not running, the request shall be ignored.

Note 1:

QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call) and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for NSA call).

Note 2, the SCells, which can not be activated:

1\. SCells permanently deactivated due to bad RLQ (5G_UP_ALG_2774_replaced([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) cannot be activated again.

2\. In case of inter-gNB CA, eligibility of ext-SCell to SCell Activation is determined as follows (5G_UP_ALG_15801_replaced([11121970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 If ext-SCell is deactivated due to Xp-U link change to ‘unavailable’ (5G_UP_ALG_12814_replaced([11121981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the ext-SCell shall not be available for activation till Xp-U link recovers to ‘available’ (5G_UP_ALG_14018_replaced([11122068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[CB014088-F]**

3\. Scell not available for activation due to scheduler processing overload, see 5G_UP_ALG_31927_replaced([11122191](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the DL branch specific actions.

**[End CB014088-F]**

4\. In case NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = Deact_Scells_VoNr_Sag and UE is already configured with SCell(s):

 If UE enters the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state the SCells are deactivated; the SCell shall not be available for activation till UE exits the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state (see 5G_UP_ALG_19252_replaced([11205370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwo7h_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19415_replaced([11204797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4MfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11120477`)

SCell Configuration Handling of gNB-DU C-plane request to start/stop DL buffer monitoring and the internal SFS variable dlL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11120486`)

SCell Configuration P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall set internal SFS variable dlL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd for each CA eligible UE as follows:

Initial value of dlL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Forbidden

(1) If:

o gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell is requested by gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell to start monitoring of buffer status of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note1) for given UE (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_9291_replaced([11316174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr6qufvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Then:

o dlL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Allowed

(2) If:

o gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell is requested by gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell to stop monitoring of buffer status of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note1), OR

o P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS determines that DL buffer criterion for SCell Addition is met (5G_UP_ALG_15838_replaced([11120516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR00fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **AND PCell link quality check is met (see 5G_UP_ALG_22735_replaced([11120536](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR01vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), OR**

o gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell is informed by gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell that the last SCell is being released and UE shall be reconfigured to non-CA mode

Then:

o dlL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Forbidden

**[CB014088-F] When NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) is set to 0, due to overload detected by the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler**, gNB-DU U-Plane for a cell acting as a PCell for the UEs, shall notify the gNB-DU C-Plane to suspend CA relationships as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31922_replaced([11120584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Further gNB-DU U-Plane shall not expect gNB-DU C-Plane hosting this cell to send buffer monitoring start indication for all the UEs for which this cell is acting as PCell. gNB-DU U-Plane hosting this cell, then shall set the above internal SFS variable dlL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd to Forbidden.****

When gNB-DU U-Plane for this cell acting as a PCell for the UEs notifies the gNB-DU C-Plane to resume CA relationships as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31922_replaced([11120584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then this cell shall expect gNB-DU C-Plane to resume buffer monitoring activity when requested.

**[End CB014088-F]**

Note 1:

QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call) and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for NSA call).

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `11120491`)

SCell Configuration Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Configuration in DL Branch – Measurements

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11120499`)

SCell Configuration When gNB-DU hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell is triggered to initiate monitoring of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note 1) buffer status for purpose of SCell Addition for the given UE (5G_UP_ALG_15831_replaced([11120403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqQmtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS of the DL branch shall measure:

\- RLC SDU buffer level in 5G-L2-HI(s) (DU) + the sum of RLC PDU buffer level in 5G-L2-LO instances of P(S)Cell and configured and active SCell(s) i.e.

sum[RLC SDU buffer level in 5G-L2-HI(s), sum(RLC PDU buffer level in P(S)Cell 5G-L2-LO, RLC PDU buffer level in all active SCells 5G-L2-LO)]

\- RLC SDU buffer level in 5G-L2-HI(s) (DU)

of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs for given UE to determine if DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer overflow criterion is met, i.e. whether data buffer of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs cannot be drained by P(S)Cell and already configured and active SCells (5G_UP_ALG_15838_replaced([11120516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR00fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

Note 1:

QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call) and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for NSA call).

Note 2:

P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS is aware of amount of data buffer levels listed above due to legacy internal communication between System Components:

1\. Each time when data is split from 5G-L2-HI (DU) to serving cell’s (P(S)Cell or SCell) 5G-L2-LO, 5G-L2-HI (DU) updates 5G-L2-LO instance of the serving cell(s) to which the data is split with RLC SDU buffer level (in 5G-L2-HI (DU)) for all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs.

2\. 5G-L2-LO of the serving cell forwards this information to serving cell’s 5G-L2-PS along with amount of RLC PDU buffer level (in 5G-L2-LO) for all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs.

3\. Each and every SCell 5G-L2-PS forwards this information to P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS. Since P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS may receive the RLC SDU buffer level (in 5G-L2-HI (DU)) from own PCell 5G-L2-LO and also from each of SCell 5G-L2-PS, PCell 5G-L2-PS shall select only one, the newest RLC SDU buffer level (in 5G-L2-HI (DU)).

Detailed signalling between System Components is out of SFS scope, therefore shall not be provided here.

[CB006139-AA]

Note 3:

Monitoring of buffer status of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs for purpose of SCell Addition is a generic algorithm, i.e. it is specified for any number of already configured SCells.

[End CB006139-AA]

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-4**  (ID: `11120504`)

SCell Configuration Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Configuration in DL Branch – 5G-L2-PS Threshold

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11120513`)

SCell Configuration P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall calculate rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K):

\- as threshold for addition one or more SCells, where ‘K’ is the number of already configured and active SCell(s)

\- for a given UE by taking into account CA UE’s estimated throughput from P(S)Cell and all already configured SCells; the estimated throughput shall be calculated by sum of estimatedFullBufferTbs(j) of [Before PR816804] all [End PR816804] DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note 1) across all active carriers according to 5G_UP_ALG_4676_replaced([11192682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

\- which cannot be lower than rdScellAdditionMinDataThreshold (see 5G_UP_ALG_15995_replaced([11124273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) parameter:

rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) = max(rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K), (K+1)* rdScellAdditionMinDataThreshold)

where:

  * rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) is the estimated throughput of P(S)Cell and all current active SCells for [Before PR816804] all [End PR816804] DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs;

  * K the number of active Scells;

  * rdScellAdditionMinDataThreshold (see 5G_UP_ALG_15995_replaced([11124273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to definition in 5G_UP_ALG_15995_replaced([11124273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));




The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

Note 1:

QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call) and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for NSA call).

[CB006139-AA]

Note 2:

Monitoring of buffer status of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs for purpose of SCell Addition is a generic algorithm, i.e. it is specified for any number of already configured and SCells.

[End CB006139-AA]

[PR816804]

Note 3:

estimatedFullBufferTbs(j) is delivered to P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS only for the DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs, for which some data is still buffered in P(S)Cell or active SCells 5G-L2-LO after the UE's latest scheduling in the respective serving cell. This is independent on setting of NRBTS/NRCELL-actOptimizedFlowControl. For more details see 5G_UP_ALG_4676_replaced([11192682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In the case of NRBTS/NRCELL-actOptimizedFlowControl = optimizedAllUe, this functionality can be enabled or disabled by the R&D flag rdActNoEstimatedFullBufferTbsForDrbWithNoDlData (5G_UP_ALG_33121_replaced([11124437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqq2YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In case of NRBTS/NRCELL-actOptimizedFlowControl = nonOptimized this functionality is always enabled.

[End PR816804]

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-5**  (ID: `11120516`)

SCell Configuration Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Configuration in DL Branch – Execution

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11120531`)

SCell Configuration P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall determine whether the DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note 1) buffer overflow criterion is met. For this purpose P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall periodically (see Note 2) execute two checks:

1) If the total amount of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs data in 5G-L2-HI(s) (DU) and in 5G-L2-LO instances of P(S)Cell and all active SCells waiting for initial transmission divided by an operator configurable number of TTIs (NRBTS.NRCELL.dlSCellConfigLevel) exceeds the threshold rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) (5G_UP_ALG_15835_replaced([11120504](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqRNzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in NRBTS.NRCELL.dlSCellConfigLevelNum consecutive checks i.e.

if {sum[RLC SDU buffer level in 5G-L2-HI(s), sum(RLC PDU buffer level in P(S)Cell 5G-L2-LO, RLC PDU buffer level in all active SCells 5G-L2-LO) ] / dlSCellConfigLevel } > rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) in dlSCellConfigLevelNum consecutive checks

2) If the amount of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs data buffered in 5G-L2-HI exceeds the threshold rdDlCaMinNonGbrDataInL2HiThresholdScellAdd (5G_UP_ALG_15981_replaced([11124260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpBPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in NRBTS.NRCELL.dlSCellConfigLevelNum consecutive checks

If results of both checks (1) and (2) are positive, it means that DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer is overflown, i.e. data buffer of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs cannot be drained by P(S)Cell and already configured and active SCells. P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS determines that DL buffer criterion for SCell Addition is met and:

\- P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS stops all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer monitoring for SCell Addition and

\- gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell sends DL buffer overflow notification to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell

If P(S)Cell is selected for dummy load generation toward UE/All UEs as per 5G_UP_ALG_25972_replaced([11184088](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvP0ZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and rdEnableDummyLoadDl (5G_L2_12664_replaced([11189570](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 'true',in Check (1) and check (2) above, 5G_L2_PS of P(S)Cell shall put current DL RLC SDU (5G_L2_HI) buffer size equal to the value of rdDummyLoadDlBsr (5G_L2_12668_replaced([11189594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) multiplied by the number of Component Carrier defined for this UE context.

If results of both checks (1) and (2) are positive, it means that DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer is overflown and P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS determines that DL buffer criterion for SCell Addition is met and :

\- P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS stops all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer monitoring for SCell Addition and

\- gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell sends DL buffer overflow notification to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell

Rationale:

Total DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs data waiting for the initial transmission is buffered in 5G-L2-HI(s) (DU) and 5G-L2-LO(s) of P(S)Cell and all active SCell(s). This total amount of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs data is subject of check (1).

Addition of new SCell make sense only in the case if the amount of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs data buffered in 5G-L2-HI is large enough to utilize the capacity of new SCell. This is the reason why check (2) is required.

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

Note 1:

QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call) and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for NSA call).

Note 2:

Periodicity of the checks depends on R&D parameter rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 (5G_UP_ALG_9771_replaced([11120866](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which ensures that measured UEs are equally distributed amongst the available checking resources and that only a certain number of UEs can be processed per checking occasion. Details are left to CP3 phase.

[CB006139-AA]

Note 3:

Monitoring of buffer status of all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs for purpose of SCell Addition is a generic algorithm, i.e. it is specified for any number of already configured SCells.

Note 4:

Dummy load functionality is enabled for purpose of internal/ benchmark/field tests of configuration providing peak/maximum throughput. When dummy load is enabled together with Carrier Aggregation, the throughput is supposed to be tested for UEs configured with maximum number of CCs for this UE in this PCell. Dummy load is not supposed to be tested with step-wise buffer based SCell Configuration.

[End CB006139-AA]

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-6**  (ID: `11120536`)

SCell Configuration PCell link quality check before sending DL buffer overflow indication for purpose of SCell Addition

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11120540`)

SCell Configuration In addition to buffer monitoring, gNB-DU U-Plane shall check if the following conditions are met before indicating DL buffer overflow for purpose of SCell Addition to gNB-DU C-Plane:

If UE has a 5QI1 bearer established:

 corrected average SINR (see 5G_UP_ALG_3073_replaced([11130124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_dvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is greater or equal to ulCaMinPcellSinr5qi1 for ulCaSinrWindow consecutive ms) or ulCaMinPcellSinr5qi1 is equal to 0 (special value)

 UE’s wideband CQI (MIMO compensated and OLLA corrected, including delta CQI, see 5G_UP_ALG_7557_replaced([11125689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is greater or equal to dlCaMinPcellCqi5qi1 for dlCaCqiWindow consecutive ms) or dlCaMinPcellCqi5qi1 is equal to 0 (special value)

Else (UE has not any 5QI1 bearer established):

 corrected average SINR (see 5G_UP_ALG_3073_replaced([11130124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_dvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is greater or equal to ulCaMinPcellSinr for ulCaSinrWindow consecutive ms) or ulCaMinPcellSinr is equal to 0 (special value)

 UE’s wideband CQI (MIMO compensated and OLLA corrected, including delta CQI, see 5G_UP_ALG_7557_replaced([11125689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is greater or equal to dlCaMinPcellCqi for dlCaCqiWindow consecutive ms) or dlCaMinPcellCqi is equal to 0 (special value)

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-7**  (ID: `11120462`)

SCell Configuration **Suspend/Resume DL and UL Buffer Status monitoring**

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `13418972`)

SCell Configuration Suspending Buffer Status Monitoring for Scell Addition Due to Overload

If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE:

[CB014088-F] If NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) is set to 0,

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of rdCaSuspendRelFddPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32492_replaced([11216909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxbltfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD cell or rdCaSuspendRelTddPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32494_replaced([11216949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 TDD cell, then:

[PR873300-26R3] If rdModifiedCaOvlActionEnabled ([13399508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_txS0IAsHEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) = False, then, [End PR873300-26R3]

  * When gNB-DU detects overload for atleast one of the schedulers in a CPU core based on the above condition, then:



gNB-DU shall suspend the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition, if it is running, for all the PCell schedulers deployed on the CPU core.

[PR873300-26R3] Else If rdModifiedCaOvlActionEnabled ([13399508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_txS0IAsHEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) = True, then, 

  * If there is one DL or one UL scheduler or at the max one DL and one UL are scheduler deployed on the same core then the following rules are applied,
  * If gNB-DU detects overload based on the above condition for the DL scheduler of a cell, then gNB-DU shall suspend the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition for the DL direction if it is running for the PCell DL scheduler (if running on the core). If buffer status monitoring is running in the UL, it must also be stopped for the respective cell, no matter on which core the UL scheduler is deployed.
  * [Before PR876905] If gNB-DU detects overload based on the above condition for the UL scheduler of a cell, then gNB-DU shall suspend the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition for the UL direction if it is running for the PCell UL scheduler (if running on the core).[End PR876905]
  * [PR876905]If gNB-DU detects overload based on the above condition for the UL scheduler of a cell, then 
    * if the UL scheduler belong to PCell (if running on the core) then gNB-DU shall suspend the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition for the UL and DL direction for the respective cell, no matter on which core the DL scheduler is deployed.[End PR876905]
  * If multiple schedulers are hosted in the same core (i.e more than one DL schedulers or UL schedulers running), then
  * If gNB-DU detects overload for at least one of the DL schedulers in a CPU core based on the above condition then gNB-DU shall suspend the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition (for both DL and UL directions), if it is running, for all the PCell schedulers deployed on the CPU core (for DL) and another core (for PCell UL).
  * [Before PR876905]If gNB-DU detects overload for at least one of the UL schedulers in a CPU core based on the above condition then gNB-DU shall suspend the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition (for UL directions), if it is running, for all the PCell UL schedulers (if running on the core) deployed on the CPU. core.[End PR876905]
  * [PR876905]If gNB-DU detects overload for at least one of the UL schedulers in a CPU core based on the above condition, then gNB-DU shall, suspend the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition (for DL and UL directions) for the respective cell, no matter on which core the UL/DL scheduler is deployed. [End PR876905][End PR873300-26R3]



Else [End CB014088-F]

When gNB-DU detects scheduler overload (see 5G_L2_19965_replaced([11213408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj3vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the CPU core to which PCell is deployed, then buffer status monitoring for SCell addition shall be suspended if it is running.

Resuming Buffer Status Monitoring for Scell Addition After Exiting Overload

If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE:

[CB014088-F] If NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) is set to 0,

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is below the value set for deactivation threshold of rdCaSuspendRelFddPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32492_replaced([11216909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxbltfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD cell or rdCaSuspendRelTddPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32494_replaced([11216949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 TDD cell then:

[PR873300-26R3] If rdModifiedCaOvlActionEnabled = False ([13399508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_txS0IAsHEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), then, [End PR873300-26R3]

  * When gNB-DU detects that all the schedulers in a CPU core recovered from overload based on the above condition.



gNB-DU shall resume the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition, if it is running before the suspension and no request to stop the monitoring has been received from C-Plane, for all the PCell schedulers deployed on the core. 

[PR873300-26R3] Else If rdModifiedCaOvlActionEnabled = True ([13399508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_txS0IAsHEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), then, 

  * If there is one DL or one UL scheduler or at the max one DL and one UL are scheduler deployed on the same core then the following rules are applied,
  * If gNB-DU detects that the DL scheduler recovered from overload based on the above condition then gNB-Du shall resume the buffer status monitoring for Scell addition in the DL direction, if it is running before the suspension and no request to stop the monitoring has been received from C-Plane for the cell. If the UL buffer status monitoring was suspended due to DL overload, then resume the same for the UL direction if it was running before the suspension and no request to stop the monitoring has been received from C-Plane, for the PCell UL scheduler.
  * If gNB-DU detects that the UL scheduler recovered from overload based on the above condition then gNB-DU shall resume the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition (for the UL direction for the respective cell), if it is running before the suspension and no request to stop the monitoring has been received from C-Plane, for the PCell UL scheduler (if running on the core). Note that to resume the above, the DL direction of the respective cell must not be forbidden from buffer status monitoring. [PR876905] Note that the DL direction could have been suspended due to the UL overload and it must be ensured that the DL is not currently overloaded to the resume the above for the respective cell. [End PR876905]
  * If multiple schedulers are hosted in the same core (i.e more than one DL schedulers or UL schedulers running), then
  * If gNB-DU detects that all the DL schedulers recovered from overload based on the above condition then gNB-DU shall resume the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition (for DL direction of the respective cells), if it is running before the suspension and no request to stop the monitoring has been received from C-Plane, for all the PCell DL schedulers deployed on the core. If the UL buffer status monitoring was suspended due to DL overload, then resume the same for the UL direction if it was running before the suspension and no request to stop the monitoring has been received from C-Plane, for the PCell UL scheduler for the respective cells.
  * If gNB-DU detects that all the UL schedulers recovered from overload based on the above condition then gNB-DU shall resume the buffer status monitoring for SCell addition (for UL directions of the respective cells), if it is running before the suspension and no request to stop the monitoring has been received from C-Plane, for all the PCell UL schedulers deployed on the core. Note that to resume the above, the DL direction of the respective cell must not be forbidden from buffer status monitoring. [PR876905] Note that the DL direction could have been suspended due to the UL overload and it must be ensured that the DL is not currently overloaded to the resume the above for the respective cell. [End PR876905][End PR873300-26R3]



Else [End CB014088-F]

When gNB-DU detects all schedulers recover from overload (see 5G_L2_19965_replaced([11213408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj3vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the CPU core to which PCell is deployed, then buffer status monitoring for SCell addition shall be resumed if it is running before the suspension and no request to stop the monitoring has been received from C-Plane.

Note: The same handling is applicable to DL and UL buffer monitoring.

SCell Configuration Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Configuration in UL Branch – Trigger Conditions

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `12639254`)

SCell Configuration Starting of UL Buffer Status monitoring of all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-8.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12639257`)

SCell Configuration PCell 5G-L2-PS shall **start UE’s all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note1) buffer monitoring for purpose of SCell Addition when:**

  * ulL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Allowed ([12639256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4lUEDDEfCal_QUJn4xrg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), AND



\- UE does not have any inactive DL+UL SCell which can be activated (see Note 2), AND

\- PCell’s 5G-L2-PS performed UE overheating handling ([11121920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and as a result determined MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL >= configured number DL_SCell(s) and MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL >= configured number DL+UL_SCell(s) ([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), AND

\- UE is not configured with power saving BWP ([11111163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), AND

\-  _VoNr_Sag_ON_ _check is passed (see below point 1.1). [PR868408] AND_ **

\- VoNr_allowedServingCells check is passed (see below point 1.2). [End PR868408][PR878414] AND

\- MAC_layer_monitoring check is passed (see below point 1.3). [End PR878414]

This check shall be triggered when any of the abovementioned condition changed.

If the request to start UL buffer status monitoring for SCell Addition from gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell **is received when the respective monitoring is already running, the request shall be ignored and PCell 5G-L2-PS shall continue the monitoring without restarting the internal counters related to the monitoring algorithm.**

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = Deact_Scells_VoNr_Sag, and

\- UE is not in the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state ([11205370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwo7h_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11204797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4MfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

OR

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = None

then

check is passed

else

check is failed

[PR868408]

(1.2) VoNr_allowedServingCells check:

If

  * logicalChannelConfig.allowedServingCells (see 5G_UP ([11358775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucjiCPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fmd_tghk4pveee-aqvopbp1qhq&artifactinmodule=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_ucjicpvkee-aqvopbp1qhq&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_kh7y4o3wee-rl47x_rccmw%2fcomponents%2f_kjbyao3wee-rl47x_rccmw")) and 5G_CP_OTH ([11598124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y2_VvfwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fmd_48vvspweee-aqvopbp1qhq&artifactinmodule=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_y2_vvfwoee-aqvopbp1qhq&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_euvego3ree-rl47x_rccmw%2fcomponents%2f_evmaio3ree-rl47x_rccmw"))) is not configured (see [11123414](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqi6mfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kqi6mfvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")), and

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `12639255`)

SCell Configuration Stopping of UL Buffer Status monitoring of all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12639261`)

SCell Configuration PCell 5G-L2-PS shall **stop UE’s all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer monitoring for purpose of SCell Addition when:**

  * ulL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Forbidden ([12639256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4lUEDDEfCal_QUJn4xrg)), OR



\- UE is configured with inactive DL+UL SCell which can be activated (see Note 2), OR

\- PCell’s 5G-L2-PS performed UE overheating handling ([11121920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and as a result determined MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL < configured number DL_SCell(s) or MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL < configured number DL+UL_SCell(s) ([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), OR

\- UE is configured with power saving BWP ([11111163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), OR

\- If NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = Deact_Scells_VoNr_Sag and UE is in the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state ([11205370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwo7h_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11204797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4MfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[PR868408] OR

\- logicalChannelConfig.allowedServingCells (see 5G_UP ([11358775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucjiCPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fmd_tghk4pveee-aqvopbp1qhq&artifactinmodule=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_ucjicpvkee-aqvopbp1qhq&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_kh7y4o3wee-rl47x_rccmw%2fcomponents%2f_kjbyao3wee-rl47x_rccmw")) and 5G_CP_OTH ([11598124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y2_VvfwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fmd_48vvspweee-aqvopbp1qhq&artifactinmodule=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_y2_vvfwoee-aqvopbp1qhq&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_euvego3ree-rl47x_rccmw%2fcomponents%2f_evmaio3ree-rl47x_rccmw"))) is not configured (see [11123414](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqi6mfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kqi6mfvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")), and UE has configured at least one non CA eligible DRB (e.g. has active VoNR call) [End PR868408] [PR878414] OR

\- NRBTS.actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom is set to enable, and MAC layer monitoring is triggered for UE (which causes UL/DL transmission suspension) (see 5G_UP_ALG ([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))) [End PR878414]

This check shall be triggered when any of the abovementioned condition changed.

If the request to stop UL buffer status monitoring for SCell Addition from gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell is received when the respective monitoring is not running, the request shall be ignored.

Note 1:

QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in ([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call).

Note 2, the SCells, which can not be activated:

1\. SCells permanently deactivated due to bad RLQ ([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) cannot be activated again.

2\. SCell not available for activation due to scheduler processing overload, see ([11122191](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UL branch specific actions.

3\. In case NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactInPoorRf = Deact_Scells_VoNr_Sag and UE is already configured with SCell(s):

 If UE enters the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state the SCells are deactivated; the SCell shall not be available for activation till UE exits the ‘TP Enabled::SAG ON’ state ([11205370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwo7h_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11204797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4MfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `12639256`)

SCell Configuration Handling of gNB-DU C-plane request to start/stop UL buffer monitoring and the internal SFS variable ulL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-8.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13423042`)

SCell Configuration PCell 5G-L2-PS shall set internal SFS variable ulL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd for each CA eligible UE as follows:

Initial value of ulL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Forbidden

(1) If:

o gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell is requested by gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell to start monitoring of buffer status of all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note1) for given UE ([11316174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr6qufvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Then:

o ulL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Allowed

(2) If:

o ~~gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell is requested by gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell to stop monitoring of buffer status of all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note1), OR~~ (see Note 2)

o PCell 5G-L2-PS determines that UL buffer criterion for SCell Addition is met ([12639251](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Qc0akEC-EfCal_QUJn4xrg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), OR

o gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell is informed by gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell that the last SCell is being released and UE shall be reconfigured to non-CA mode

Then:

o ulL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd = Forbidden

[CB014088-F]When NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) is set to 0, due to overload detected by the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See ([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler**, gNB-DU U-Plane for a cell acting as a PCell for the UEs, shall notify the gNB-DU C-Plane to suspend CA relationships as defined in ([11120584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Further gNB-DU U-Plane shall not expect gNB-DU C-Plane hosting this cell to send buffer monitoring start indication for all the UEs for which this cell is acting as PCell. gNB-DU U-Plane hosting this cell, then shall set the above internal SFS variable ulL2BufferMonitoringStatusSCellAdd to Forbidden.**

When gNB-DU U-Plane for this cell acting as a PCell for the UEs notifies the gNB-DU C-Plane to resume CA relationships as defined in ([11120584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then this cell shall expect gNB-DU C-Plane to resume buffer monitoring activity when requested.[End CB014088-F]

Note 1: QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in ([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call).

Note 2: For simplification, CB010741 CFAM team decided that gNB-DU C-Plane will not send the request to stop monitoring of buffer status to gNB-DU U-Plane.

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-9**  (ID: `12639251`)

SCell Configuration Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Configuration in UL Branch

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `12643624`)

SCell Configuration When gNB-DU hosting the UE’s PCell is triggered to initiate monitoring of all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs (see Note 2) buffer status for purpose of SCell Addition for the given UE ([12639250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CuK5QEC-EfCal_QUJn4xrg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), PCell 5G-L2-PS of the UL branch shall calculate the CA eligible LCGs buffer data volume based on the housekeeping function (see ([11203660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a given UE, and execute ‘UL buffer check’ to determine if UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer overflow criterion is met, i.e. whether data buffer of all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs cannot be drained by the PCell.

‘UL buffer check’ at (t2) is passed, if the condition defined by the formula below is satisfied:

Sum{the data volume for LCG(i,k, t1)} / bsrEstimatePeriod > max{ulSCellConfigLevel [PR864506] * ShortBsr31RedFactor [End PR864506] * eThav(t2), rdUlCaBsrSplitMinDataThreshold}

Where:

the data volume for LCG (i, k) is defined in ([11122441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

i is defined as index of UE index.

k is defined as index of all non-GBR LCGs (i.e. LCG contains only non-GBR DRB bears).

t1 is the time when the latest BSR is received (t1 is the latest time to t2 (t1 is before t2)).

bsrEstimatePeriod = max(rdPeriodScellCheckFr1 / 2^u,min(periodicBSRTimer,sf2560))

rdPeriodScellCheckFr1 is defined in ([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (default: 10)

u is subcarrier spacing (NRBTS/NRCELLGRP.scs) configuration index (3GPP TS 38.211 Table 4.2-1)

periodicBSRTimer is defined in NIDD: NRBTS.periodicBSRTimer (default: sf10)

ulSCellConfigLevel is defined in NIDD: NRBTS/NRCELL.ulSCellConfigLevel (default: 10) [PR864506]

ShortBsr31RedFactor is defined as:

If NRCELL.actShortBsrLimitAdaptation = true, and short BSR of bufferSizeIndex = 31 (the highest possible value) is received then:

ShortBsr31RedFactor = 0.2 // See Note 3

Else // all other cases

ShortBsr31RedFactor = 1 [End PR864506]

eThav is defined in ([11204528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

t2 is the time when buffer evaluation check happens.

rdUlCaBsrSplitMinDataThreshold is threshold for the minimum buffered data of non-GBR LCGs in UE to start UL buffer split ([11124087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If the ‘UL buffer check’ is passed for NRBTS/NRCELL.ulScellConfigLevelNum (default: 3) consecutive checks, then the UL buffer notification condition for FR1 UL CA is met and gNB-DU shall:

  * stop all UL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs buffer monitoring for SCell Addition, and

  * send to gNB-CU F1AP::BUFFER CRITERION NOTIFICATION with UL buffer overflow indication.




Notes:

  1. In the ‘UL buffer check’ condition above, it is assumed that BSR is reported every periodicBSRTimer (regular and padding BSR is not considered) and checked whether the data volume from single BSR cannot be exhausted in max(rdPeriodScellCheckFR1, periodicBSRTimer) period (assuming each slot can transmit ulSCellConfigLevel * eTh data).

  2. QoS Flow eligibility for data split for CA is determined in ([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for SA call). [PR864506]

  3. ShortBsr31RedFactor is a reduction factor introduced to increase the aggressiveness level of SCell Addition procedure when the Short BSR=31 is received because maximum value of Short BSR is mapped to the value which would be too low to trigger SCell Addition (see [11151222](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24gqa_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). [End PR864506]

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-10**  (ID: `12774706`)

SCell Configuration Evaluation of DL Pathloss Reference During Buffer Monitoring for UL CA Consideration

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `12774707`)

SCell Configuration Upon reception of a request to start a buffer monitoring procedure for SCell configuration with an indication to support DL pathloss consideration for UL CA, the gNB-DU shall perform the following:

  * Calculate DL pathloss for PCell per ([11121446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_se2TcPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and save the result as a "reference DL pathloss".
  * If there is already a stored "reference DL pathloss", overwrite it with the latest DL pathloss.
    * L2-PS does not restart the monitoring procedure if it's already running. It keeps the internal counters for the procedure but captures a new "reference DL pathloss"
    * If L2-PS unilaterally stops the DL buffer monitoring procedure, see ([11120432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_lY8AsPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for possible reasons, it continues to save "reference DL pathloss
  * Clear the "reference DL pathloss" for a UE:
  * If a request to stop buffer monitoring is received from the gNB-DU C-Plane



This requirement applies for [CB014587-C] both UL and [End CB014587-C] DL buffer monitoring

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-11**  (ID: `12739482`)

SCell Configuration Evaluation of DL Pathloss Difference During DL Buffer Monitoring for UL CA Consideration

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `12739483`)

SCell Configuration When the DL buffer criteria for SCell configuration is met (overflow), per ([11120516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_l_gRcPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the gNB-DU shall capture the latest DL pathloss (referred to here as "DL pathloss for met criterion")

If there is a valid, stored "reference DL pathloss" for the UE, from ([12774706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_W8ogIIrMEfCrqOdGJPoCRA)): 

  * Calculate a "DL pathloss difference" equal to "DL pathloss for met criterion" - "reference DL pathloss"
  * The "DL pathloss difference" difference is rounded up to 1 dB resolution. It can have a positive or negative value
  * Include the "DL pathloss difference" in the DL buffer criterion indication message sent to the gNB-DU C-Plane (per UL buffer status execution in ([11120516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_l_gRcPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



Else

  * Do not include the "DL pathloss difference" in the DL buffer criterion indication message sent to the gNB-DU C-Plane



The "DL pathloss difference" calculation must support a range of at least plus or minus 127dB and have a 1dB resolution

Notes:

  * The "DL pathloss difference" does not need to be saved.
  * Once L2-PS stores a "reference DL pathloss", it is maintained in UE Context.
  * DL buffer monitoring procedure could be requested again by gNB-DU C-Plane without a "start-dl-pl". In this case, the last "reference DL pathloss" is reused to derive a new "DL pathloss difference" once buffer criterion is met
  * DL pathloss difference derivation runs concurrently for DL and UL Buffer monitoring. Whenever either UL or DL buffer criteria is met, the "DL pathloss difference" is calculated and sent towards L3.

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-12**  (ID: `12765367`)

SCell Configuration Evaluation of DL Pathloss Difference During UL Buffer Monitoring for UL CA Consideration

---

**3.7.1.2.0-8.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `12765368`)

SCell Configuration When an UL buffer criteria is met (overflow), per ([12639251](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Qew7UEC-EfCal_QUJn4xrg)), the gNB-DU shall capture the latest DL pathloss (referred to here as "DL pathloss for met criterion")

  * If there is a valid, stored "reference DL pathloss" for the UE per ([12774706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_W8ogIIrMEfCrqOdGJPoCRA)) :
  * Calculate a "DL pathloss difference" equal to "DL pathloss for met criterion" - "reference DL pathloss"
    * The "DL pathloss difference" difference is rounded up to 1 dB resolution. It can have a positive or negative value
  * Include the "DL pathloss difference" in the UL buffer criterion indication message sent to the gNB-DU C-Plane (per UL buffer status execution in ([12639251](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Qew7UEC-EfCal_QUJn4xrg)).
  * Else
  * Do not include the "DL pathloss difference" in the UL buffer criterion indication message sent to gNB-DU C-Plane

  * The "DL pathloss difference" calculation must support a range of at least plus or minus 127dB and have a 1dB resolution




Notes:

  * The "DL pathloss difference" does not need to be saved.
  * Once L2-PS stores a "reference DL pathloss", it is maintained in UE Context.
  * DL buffer monitoring procedure could be requested again by gNB-DU C-Plane without a "start-dl-pl". In this case, the last "reference DL pathloss" is reused to derive a new "DL pathloss difference" once buffer criterion is met
  * DL pathloss difference derivation runs concurrently for DL and UL Buffer monitoring. Whenever either UL or DL buffer criteria is met, the "DL pathloss difference" is calculated and sent towards L3.
