### 3.7.1.3 CA Relationship Management

#### 3.7.1.3.0-1 CA Relationship Management P(S)Cell Context in SCell 5G-L2-PS for FR1 CA (ID: 11120547)

**3.7.1.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11120556`)

CA Relationship Management P(S)cell context associated to NRREL between remote P(S)cell and current cell (acting as Scell) contains the following:

  1. [Before CNI-88614]If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is not appliable, according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), According to 5G_UP_1383_replaced([11358572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uciT7vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of pipeline solution for CA UE HARQ-ACK solution, SCell 5G-L2-PS shall include full K1 table built by the P(S)Cell according to 5G_UP_ALG_2478_replaced([11116165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp1v8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to signal DCI to the UE and K1 values allowed for scheduling in SCell. To avoid no PUCCH F1 resource for P(S)Cell scheduling, SCell 5G-L2-PS will reserve certain number of PUCCH F1 resource for P(S)Cell scheduling. [End CNI-88614]



If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), SCell 5G-L2-PS shall include K1 table built by the P(S)Cell according to 5G_UP_ALG_2473_replaced([11116092](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to signal DCI to the UE and K1 values allowed for scheduling in SCell.

If distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) algorithm is enabled, on FDD carrier shared with LTE, SCell 5G-L2-PS shall include Scell K1 table built by the P(S)Cell according to 5G_UP_ALG_2473_replaced([11116092](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to signal DCI to the UE and K1 values allowed for scheduling in SCell.

  1. To support co-scheduling of CA UE with P(S)cell 5G-L2-PS, SCell 5G-L2-PS shall include P(S)cell PsPeerCtrl address in its related P(S)cell context.

  2. P(S)Cell MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/scs and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/CellTechnology.

  3. P(S)Cell available PUCCH F1 resources and PUCCH F3 resources for HARQ-ACK. 




Note:

[Before CNI-88614]If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is not appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), - Scell scheduler need to have the list of cell level PUCCH resources for PUCCH token maintenance according to 5G_UP_ALG_4598_replaced([11187352](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CNI-88614]

#### 3.7.1.3.0-2 CA Relationship Management SCell Context in P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS for FR1 CA (ID: 11120559)

**3.7.1.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11120572`)

CA Relationship Management Scell context associated to NrRel between current cell (acting as P(S)cell) and remote Scell contains the following:

  1. P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall initiate the PUCCH receiving of CSI report and beam report after SCell activation successfully, so P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall be stored related SCell parameters in SCell context for number of UCI bit for SCell channel state report and beam report*.



\- Scell dlMimoMode for number of UCI bits for channel state report according to 5G_UP_ALG_3626_replaced([11160044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktN0EfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

\- Scell actBeamforming _, nActivatedSsPbch_ and nrBtsBeamRefinementP2 _for number of UCI bits for SCell beam report_ according to 5G_UP_ALG_28236_replaced([11160420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktN0F_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3631_replaced([11160432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktN0GfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

\- In case Scell dlMimoMode is "ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4", N1 & N2 according to 5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of FR1 TDD Scell so PCell will calculate the uciBits for UCI decoding over PUCCH or PUSCH(Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3626_replaced([11160044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktN0EfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  1. To support co-scheduling of CA UE with Scell 5G-L2-PS, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall include SCell PsPeerCtrl address in its related SCell context.

  2. P(S)Cell MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/scs and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/CellTechnology.

  3. scellLoadStateForActivation flag, initialized to low load when CA relationship is setup and updated according to 5G_UP_ALG_8848_replaced([11123534](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkIs_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




[CB008898-A],

  1. SRS beamforming sync up indicator for indicating how to sync up beamforming information from Pcell to Scell (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_10012_replaced([11302559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqgVc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



[End CB008898-A]

  * beamforming / beam report is not used in FDD and FDD CA.



dlMimoMode: NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode

actBeamforming: NRBTS.NRCELL.actBeamforming

nActivatedSsPbch: Number of activated SS/PBCH (see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

#### 3.7.1.3.0-3 CA Relationship Management CA Relationship for FR1 Inter-GNB Carrier Aggregation (ID: 11120576)

**3.7.1.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11120580`)

CA Relationship Management [PR690694]

For FR1 Inter-gNB CA relationship setup procedure, PCell L2 PS shall re-send CA relationship setup request message to ext-SCell if PCell L2 PS does not receive CA relationship setup response message from ext-SCell in specified time duration. Detailed information left to EFS.

[End PR690694]

---

#### 3.7.1.3.0-4 CA Relationship Management CA Relationship management for FR1 due to scheduler processing overload (ID: 11120584)

**3.7.1.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11120588`)

CA Relationship Management If NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) _is set to 0 gNB-DU shall perform the following steps else shall skip these steps:_

The severity metric mentioned below could be DL PCell specific or the UL PCell specific (if the UL PCell is on different or same core) but only DL PCell must peform the following actions and not the UL PCell.

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of **rdCaSuspendRelFddPerCent**(5G_UP_ALG_32492_replaced([11216909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxbltfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD cell or rdCaSuspendRelTddPerCent **(5G_UP_ALG_32494_replaced([11216949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD cell, then** _*_** *

gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the cell that is acting as PCell for the UEs in this cell, shall request gNB-DU C-Plane hosting this cell to suspend all following CA relationship:

(1) new CA UEs with this cell acting as Pcell

(2) new SCell addition to existing UEs for which this cell is acting as PCell

(3) this cell as a Scell candidate for those UEs for which some other cell is acting as PCell

When the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is below the value set for deactivation threshold of **rdCaSuspendRelFddPerCent**(5G_UP_ALG_32492_replaced([11216909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxbltfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD cell or rdCaSuspendRelTddPerCent **(5G_UP_ALG_32494_replaced([11216949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD cell**, then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the cell that is acting as PCell for the UEs in this cell, shall request gNB-DU C-Plane hosting this cell to resume all CA relationship that were suspended as listed above.****_*_** *

Rationale: The UL PCell and DL PCell respective schedulers can be hosted on different/same core, it is rather simpler to restrict the above in DL PCell only since DL is the master in coordinating the relationships and there cannot be any decision that is DL independent. However, since the DL and UL schedulers run independent of each other, and if the above restriction observed in DL PCell in a different time, e.g later to a time when the UL is overloaded (e.g due to RT processing load), then there are no specific actions from the UL PCell. The DL PCell shall send the message to the Control Plane function handling the cell, and the above actions are perfromed in both the DL and UL direction.

---

### 3.7.1.4 SCell Release

#### 3.7.1.4.0-1 SCell Release Transient Period of Scell Release for FR1 CA (ID: 11120596)

**3.7.1.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11120600`)

SCell Release Overview

---

**3.7.1.4.0-1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12578420`)

SCell Release 5G-L2-PS shall consider transient state of Scell release for CA UE during the SCell release period.

\- 5G-L2-PS will refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2689_replaced([11120617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb7vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as start of transient state;

\- 5G-L2-PS will refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2692_replaced([11120624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as stop of transient state;

\- 5G-L2-PS shall not trigger aperiodic SRS during the transient state if nrofSrsPorts is changed in Scell release;

\- For FR1 CA where PCell is a TDD cell, 5G-L2-PS shall conduct DL scheduling using only CSS (DCI 1_0);

\- For FR1 CA where PCell is a FDD cell, transient period of the SCell Release is handled only when the last configured SCell is being released (i.e. for CA release procedure only). In this case DL assignment shall be sent in CSS only, that is PCell 5G-L2-PS shall schedule UE with DCI 1_0 scrambled with C-RNTI. [Before CNI-137616-B] This handling of transient period of the last SCell Release for FDD PCell is controlled by EFS R&D flag and is enabled by default. [End CNI-137616-B]

In case of DSS, if SCell Release is executed after DSS transient phase (5G_L2_142_replaced([11143994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_233KLvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) was completed and LTE CRS rate matching configuration is known by UE, DL assignment shall be scheduled in PCell with DCI 1_0 scrambled with C-RNTI and PDSCH with configured LTE CRS rate matching pattern (5G_UP_ALG_453_replaced([11098260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km9bEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be applied

**Note:**

  * According to TS38.133 section 8.2.1.2, UE is allowed an interruption on any active serving cells(including P(S)Cell) due to Scell addition or release. **Scheduling shall be interrrupted from the time RRC message for SCell addition is sent and till RRC processing delay timer expiry (see 5G_UP_ALG_29060_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

  * Refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_5360_replaced([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for nrofSrsPorts.

---

**3.7.1.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11120617`)

SCell Release Start Point of Transient State

---

**3.7.1.4.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11120621`)

SCell Release When CA UE with SCell configured with servingCellIndex receives start notification of SCell release procedure from C-Plane and after N DPA scheduling cycle, the CA UE will be configured as start of transient state of SCell release for the SCell with servingCellIndex.

Note: The transient period will be considered in P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS.

The start/end notification of SCell release procedure is received from C-Plane, see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3116_replaced([11315870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr41kPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more information.

Value N can be a R&D parameter, the reason why transient period is postponed by N DPA scheduling cycle is to clean up RLC PDU in SCell buffer knowing that this RRC reconfiguration message won’t be received by UE during the N DPA scheduling cycle, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2695_replaced([11120632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.7.1.4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11120624`)

SCell Release Stop Point of Transient State

---

**3.7.1.4.0-1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11120628`)

SCell Release When CA UE with SCell configured with servingCellIndex in transient state receives end notification of SCell release procedure from C-Plane, the CA UE will be configured as stop of transient period of SCell release for the SCell with servingCellIndex.

Note:

The start/end notification of SCell release procedure is received from C-Plane, see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3116_replaced([11315870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr41kPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more information.

---

**3.7.1.4.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11120632`)

SCell Release Interwork with DPA

---

**3.7.1.4.0-1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11120637`)

SCell Release Please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_22730_replaced([11123985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 3.7.1.4.0-2 SCell Release Transient period of SCell release for SA mode FR2 CA (ID: 11120641)

**3.7.1.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11120644`)

SCell Release During the transient period triggered by SCell release, L2PS shall schedule PDSCH to UE only in the PCell with DCI1-0. the transient period starts when the SCell release notification from C-Plane is received and ends when the SCell release complete notification from C-Plane is received.

Note:

1\. This requirement is initially created for CB008294, but “SCell release without RRC connection release” is not supported in CB008294, and it is de-linked to CB008294. but it should be needed in the future when “SCell release without RRC connection release” is supported.

---

#### 3.7.1.4.0-3 SCell Release SCell Release due to prolonged data inactivity or UE overheating in FR1 CA (ID: 11120649)

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11120652`)

SCell Release Overview

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11120665`)

SCell Release SCell Release due to prolonged data inactivity requires enabling of Buffer based SCell Configuration, see 5G_UP_ALG_15828_replaced([11120371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (i.e. NRBTS.actBufferBasedSCellAddition must not be ‘disabled’).

If UE is configured with SCell and there is neither DL nor UL traffic for a configurable amount of time, gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell shall indicate it to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell. C-Plane shall consider this indication as a trigger for releasing this SCell due to data inactivity.

The point in time when gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell sends the indication to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell depends on setting of NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer and NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB (5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in this particular SCell (see 5G_UP_ALG_16250_replaced([11120669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTC9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If UE is configured with SCell which was deactivated due to UE overheating (5G_UP_ALG_2821_replaced([11121920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell shall indicate it to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s PCell. The indication about SCell deactivation is sent after the amount of time controlled by NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer set in this SCell. C-Plane shall consider this indication as a trigger for releasing this SCell due to UE overheating.

[Before PR767881]

If gNB-DU receives consecutively CQI=0 for the SCell, on top of stopping UE’s DL and UL scheduling in this SCell (5G_UP_1410_replaced([11358968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uckJHPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the SCell Release shall be handled as follows (note, that A2 based SCell Release is not considered here):

If:

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactivationTimerGNB is set to value other than ‘infinity’ and

\- NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = 'enabled_Fr1' and

\- NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount > 0,

the SCell Release procedure shall be handled as SCell Release due to bad RLQ (5G_UP_ALG_16280_replaced([11120732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The SCell shall not be released due to data inactivity, independently on setting of NRBTS-actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell.

If:

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactivationTimerGNB = ‘infinity’ and

\- NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = 'enabled_Fr1' and

\- NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount > 0 and

\- NRBTS-actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell = ‘timer_based_Fr1’

and:

a) if NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellInactivityReleaseTimer is greater than (NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount * NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellChannelEstimationPeriod), the SCell Release procedure shall be handled as SCell Release due to bad RLQ (5G_UP_ALG_16280_replaced([11120732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

b) if NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellInactivityReleaseTimer is lower than (NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount * NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellChannelEstimationPeriod), the SCell Release procedure shall be handled as SCell Release due to data inactivity,

c) if NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellInactivityReleaseTimer equals (NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount * NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellChannelEstimationPeriod), the concurrency of different reasons triggering SCell Release shall be handled according to 5G_UP_ALG_16462_replaced([11120771](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If:

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactivationTimerGNB = ‘infinity’ and

\- (NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = 'disabled' or NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount = 0),

this SCell shall not be released due bad RLQ. But when NRBTS-actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell = ‘timer_based_Fr1’, it is possible to release this SCell due to data inactivity.

[PR767881]

If gNB-DU receives consecutively CQI=0 for the SCell, and:

if:

\- NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = ‘enabled_Fr1’ and

\- NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount > 0,

on top of stopping UE’s DL and UL scheduling in this SCell (5G_UP_1410_replaced([11358968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uckJHPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the SCell shall be released due to bad RLQ (5G_UP_ALG_16280_replaced([11120732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

else if:

\- (NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = ‘disabled’ or NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount = 0),

the SCell, shall not be released due to bad RLQ or data inactivity.

Rationale: SCell Release due to bad RLQ involves NRBTS-sCellExcludelistTimerFr1, which prevents ping-pong of SCell Release/SCell Addition procedures for SCell reported with CQI = 0. In order to avoid above-mentioned ping-pong, SCell with CQI=0 shall never be released due to data inactivity. 

Note 1: Handling of SCell reported with CQI=0 is independent on setting of NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactivationTimerGNB and NRBTS-actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell.

Note 2: Any SCell Release triggered by the C-Plane (e.g. A2 based SCell Release) shall be applicable if it is enabled, but it is not considered here.

[End PR767881]

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11120669`)

SCell Release Handling of SCell Inactivity Release Timer with support of Overheating protection based on UE Overheating Assistance Information

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11120673`)

SCell Release Overview

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11120678`)

SCell Release If NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell is set to any value other than ‘disabled’ in gNB-DU hosting the SCell, the NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer value is used to configure the SCell Inactivity Release Timer in the SCell.

SCell Inactivity Release Timer is handled per UE with configured SCell by SCell DL 5G-L2-PS or SCell UL 5G-L2-PS.

If the SCell Inactivity Release Timer is handled in DL and UL branches, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS and SCell UL 5G-L2-PS maintain this timer separately. The SCell DL 5G-L2-PS works as a master and collects the timer’s status from SCell UL 5G- L2-PS. The SCell Inactivity Release Timer is considered as expired only when it expires in DL and UL branches.

If the SCell Inactivity Release Timer is handled in DL branch only, the SCell DL 5G-L2-PS maintains this timer autonomously.

[CB008311-E]

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

[End CB008311-E]

Concurrency handling of different reasons triggering SCell Release is described in 5G_UP_ALG_16462_replaced([11120771](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note :

Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information (CB008697) is applicable for Stand Alone (SA) Architecture Option 2 only.

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11120682`)

SCell Release Conditions to be satisfied for triggering starting/stopping SCell Inactivity Release Timer

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11120701`)

SCell Release For a given UE’s SCell:

 If NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer != infinity, then:

I. The SCell Inactivity Release Timer is started in SCell 5G-L2-PS in DL or UL branch at any of the following events; except if UE in the TPenabled::SAG ON” state (see 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) :

1\. SCell 5G-L2-PS is informed by SCell gNB-DU C-Plane that the SCell was configured at the UE, and:

For intra-gNB CA:

a. if NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod != blind:

 if the SCell has not been activated yet

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only (see Note 1)

b. if NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod = blind:

 if SCell was blindly activated, however it has not been scheduled yet

 For DL only SCell the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only

 For DL+UL SCell the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in both SCell DL 5G-L2-PS and SCell UL 5G-L2-PS

For inter-gNB CA:

c. (regardless of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod set in ext-gNB):

 if the SCell has not been activated yet (see Note 3)

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only (see Note 1)

2\. 

a. if NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB != infinity:

 if SCell is deactivated either due to expiration of SCell Inactivity Deactivation Timer (5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or because of UE overheating (5G_UP_ALG_2821_replaced([11121920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), see Note 2)

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only (see Note 1)

 if SCell is in the deactivated state due to UE exit from the TPenabled::SAG ON state

the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only (see Note 1)

b. if NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB = infinity:

 [PR767881] when gNB-DU does not receive from UE CSI report containing CQI = 0, and [End PR767881] if DL scheduling of the UE in the DL only or DL+UL SCell is stopped, i.e. SCell’s buffer level for all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs reaches ‘0’ (5G_UP_ALG_4561_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), or the DL scheduling has not started after the SCell became active

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS

 [PR767881] when gNB-DU does not receive from UE CSI report containing CQI = 0, and [End PR767881] if UL scheduling of the UE in the DL+UL SCell is stopped, i.e. BSR split from P(S)Cell UL 5G-L2-PS indicates a ‘0’ split for all CA eligible LCGs (5G_UP_ALG_9496_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or once the uplink housekeeping buffer data rrmBufferedDataUlTotal_bytes become ‘0’ (5G_UP_ALG_5118_replaced([11203660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), or the UL scheduling has not started after the SCell became active

\- the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell UL 5G-L2-PS

 if SCell is deactivated due to UE overheating (5G_UP_ALG_2821_replaced([11121920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), see Note 2)

  * the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only (see Note 1)



[PR767881]

 when CQI in CSI report received by gNB-DU for the SCell is changed from CQI = 0 to CQI > 0:

 The SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS and, in case of DL+UL SCell, in SCell UL 5G-L2-PS

[End PR767881]

c. if NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = disabled and NRBTS.sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount > 0:

 if the SCell configured for the UE was deactivated by P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS due to bad SCell RLQ according to 5G_UP_ALG_2774_replaced([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer starts in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS only (see Note 1)

II. The SCell Inactivity Release Timer is stopped and cleared in SCell 5G-L2-PS in DL or UL branch at any of the following events:

1\. 

a. if NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB != infinity and any of the following :

 if the SCell is activated

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer stops in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS as it was running in the DL branch only (see Note 1)

 if UE enters the “TPenabled::SAG ON” state (see 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

b. if NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB = infinity and any of the following :

 if DL scheduling of UE in the (DL only or DL+UL) SCell is started, i.e. SCell’s buffer level for all DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs becomes greater than ‘0’ (5G_UP_ALG_4561_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer is stopped in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS

 if UL scheduling of the UE in the DL+UL SCell is started, i.e. BSR split from P(S)Cell UL 5G-L2-PS indicates a buffer size greater than ‘0’ for all CA eligible LCGs (5G_UP_ALG_9496_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

\- the SCell Inactivity Release Timer stops in SCell UL 5G-L2-PS

 if the SCell is activated (e.g. SCell was not activated yet or was deactivated due to overheating)

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer stops in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS as it was running in the DL branch only (see Note 1)

 if UE enters the “TPenabled::SAG ON” state (see 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[PR767881]

 when gNB-DU receives from UE CSI report containing CQI = 0 for the SCell:

 the SCell Inactivity Release Timer stops in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS and, in case of DL+UL SCell, in SCell UL 5G-L2-PS

[End PR767881]

III. The SCell Inactivity Release Timer is considered as expired at any of the following events:

1\. If the SCell Inactivity Release Timer running only in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS expires, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS reports it to P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS – for details see description in 5G_UP_ALG_18266_replaced([11120707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTDBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2\. If the SCell Inactivity Release Timer running in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS and SCell UL 5G-L2-PS:

a. when timer is expired in uplink branch, SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will notify the SCell Inactivity Release Timer expiration to SCell DL 5G-L2-PS

b. in case SCell DL 5G-L2-PS received the uplink SCell Inactivity Release Timer expiration notification, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS checks whether downlink SCell Inactivity Release Timer is expired or not:

\- if yes, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS reports it to P(S)Cell – for details see description in 5G_UP_ALG_18266_replaced([11120707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTDBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- if no, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS waits for downlink SCell Inactivity Release Timer expiration. 

 If NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer = infinity, SCell 5G-L2-PS shall never start/stop the SCell Inactivity Release Timer and the SCell will be never released due to data inactivity.

When NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB = infinity:

1\. SCell 5G-L2-PS shall keep the SCell Inactivity Release Timer running in both DL and UL branches during DRX inactive period in the same manner as it executed while handling the SCell Inactivity Deactivation Timer during DRX – see 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the reference

2\. Expiration of SCell Inactivity Release Timer is indicated from SCell DL 5G-L2-PS to P(S)Cell DL 5G-L2-PS, while uplink BSR is split by P(S)Cell UL 5G-L2-PS to SCell UL 5G-L2-PS. It may happen that above two procedures happen at the same time, it's left to CP3 how to handle such corner case.

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

Concurrency handling of different reasons triggering SCell Release is described in 5G_UP_ALG_16462_replaced([11120771](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

CA eligible DRB refers to 5G_UP_10576_replaced([11358417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uchs1_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note 1:

For inactive SCell there is no need to maintain the SCell Inactivity Release Timer in SCell UL 5G-L2-PS (no data scheduling, particularly in UL). Therefore in this case SCell Inactivity Release Timer is handled solely in SCell DL 5G-L2-PS independently if the SCell is DL only or DL+UL.

Note 2:

Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information (CB008697) is applicable for Stand Alone (SA) Architecture Option 2 only.

Note 3:

In inter-gNB CA configuration, ext-SCell Activation mechanism depends only on setting of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB (see 5G_UP_ALG_16091_replaced([11121973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note 4: There is no impact to condition of Scell Inactivity Release timer start for a blind method UE in TPenabled::SAG ON” state.

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11120707`)

SCell Release Indication of expiration of SCell Inactivity Release Timer to C-Plane

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11120711`)

SCell Release If the SCell Inactivity Release Timer is considered as expired (see point III in 5G_UP_ALG_18265_replaced([11120682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTDAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SCell DL 5G-L2-PS shall report it to P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS. Then, [CB008311-E] if NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell is set to any value other than ‘disabled’ in gNB-DU hosting the P(S)Cell [End CB008311-E], P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will indicate expiration of the SCell Inactivity Release Timer to gNB-DU C-Plane [CB008311-E] hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell [End CB008311-E] as a trigger to release the respective SCell at the UE. The P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall include the sCellIndex and the SCell Inactive Reason. P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS selects the SCell Inactivity Reason as follows:

if the SCell is deactivated AND (number of configured SCells is greater than limits arising from AllowedNoOfActSCellsDL and AllowedNoOfActSCellsUL):

then SCell Inactive Reason = 'ue-overheating'

else SCell Inactive Reason = 'inactivity-timer' 

where:

AllowedNoOfActSCellsDL and AllowedNoOfActSCellsUL – maximum number of allowed SCells DL and DL+UL respectively provided by gNB-DU C-Plane (i.e. requested by the UE due to overheating, 5G_UP_ALG_2824_replaced([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB008311-E]

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

[End CB008311-E]

Concurrency handling of different reasons triggering SCell Release is described in 5G_UP_ALG_16462_replaced([11120771](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note 1:

Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information (CB008697) is applicable for Stand Alone (SA) Architecture Option 2 only.

Note 2:   
Only one SCell is included in each indication to the gNB-DU C-Plane.

  * For sCellIndex refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_940_replaced([11245482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tm-gYPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11120716`)

SCell Release Online reconfiguration of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11120720`)

SCell Release In case NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell is online reconfigured during cell reconfiguration procedure, 5G-L2-PS instances of P(S)Cell and SCell are provided with the new setting by gNB-DU C-Plane [CB008311-E] hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell and SCell [End CB008311-E] when the SCell is configured in the U-Plane for the UE (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3111_replaced([11315716](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4Of_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [CB008311-E] P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS and [End CB008311-E] SCell 5G-L2-PS shall update the UE context with new value of this parameter and use:

 the old value of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell for all CA UEs which were configured with this SCell while the NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell was changed

 new setting of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell for all CA UEs with this SCell upon SCell Addition

[CB008311-E]

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

[End CB008311-E]

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11120724`)

SCell Release Online reconfiguration of SCell Inactivity Release Timer (NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer)

---

**3.7.1.4.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11120727`)

SCell Release In case SCell Inactivity Release Timer (NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer) is online reconfigured during cell reconfiguration procedure, SCell 5G-L2-PS is provided with the new setting by gNB-DU C-Plane [CB008311-E] hosting the UE’s SCell [End CB008311-E] when the SCell is configured in the U-Plane for the UE (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3111_replaced([11315716](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4Of_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Then SCell 5G-L2-PS shall update the UE context with new value of this parameter and use:

 the old value of SCell Inactivity Release Timer for all CA UEs which were configured with this SCell while the NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer was changed

 new setting of SCell Inactivity Release Timer for all CA UEs with this SCell upon SCell Addition

[CB008311-E]

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

[End CB008311-E]

---

#### 3.7.1.4.0-4 SCell Release SCell Release due to bad SCell RLQ in FR1 CA (ID: 11120732)

**3.7.1.4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11120735`)

SCell Release Overview

---

**3.7.1.4.0-4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11120748`)

SCell Release If UE is configured with SCell which was permanently deactivated due to bad SCell RLQ (5G_UP_ALG_2774_replaced([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell shall indicate it to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell immediately. C-Plane shall consider this indication as a trigger for releasing this bad SCell RLQ.

[Before PR767881]

If gNB-DU receives consecutively CQI=0 for the SCell, on top of stopping UE’s DL and UL scheduling in this SCell (5G_UP_1410_replaced([11358968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uckJHPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the SCell Release shall be handled as follows (note, that A2 based SCell Release is not considered here):

If:

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactivationTimerGNB is set to value other than ‘infinity’ and

\- NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = 'enabled_Fr1' and

\- NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount > 0,

the SCell Release procedure shall be handled as SCell Release due to bad RLQ. The SCell shall not be released due to data inactivity, independently on setting of NRBTS-actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell.

If:

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactivationTimerGNB = ‘infinity’ and

\- NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = 'enabled_Fr1' and

\- NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount > 0 and

\- NRBTS-actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell = ‘timer_based_Fr1’

and:

a) if NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellInactivityReleaseTimer is greater than (NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount * NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellChannelEstimationPeriod), the SCell Release procedure shall be handled as SCell Release due to bad RLQ,

b) if NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellInactivityReleaseTimer is lower than (NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount * NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellChannelEstimationPeriod), the SCell Release procedure shall be handled as SCell Release due to data inactivity (5G_UP_ALG_16243_replaced([11120649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTC8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

c) if NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellInactivityReleaseTimer equals (NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount * NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellChannelEstimationPeriod), the concurrency of different reasons triggering SCell Release shall be handled according to 5G_UP_ALG_16462_replaced([11120771](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If:

\- NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactivationTimerGNB = ‘infinity’ and

\- (NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = 'disabled' or NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount = 0),

this SCell shall not be released due bad RLQ. But when NRBTS-actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell = ‘timer_based_Fr1’, it is possible to release this SCell due to data inactivity.

[PR767881]

If gNB-DU receives consecutively CQI=0 for the SCell, and:

if:

\- NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = ‘enabled_Fr1’ and

\- NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount > 0,

on top of stopping UE’s DL and UL scheduling in this SCell (5G_UP_1410_replaced([11358968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uckJHPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the SCell shall be released due to bad RLQ.

else if:

\- (NRBTS-actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq = ‘disabled’ or NRBTS-sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount = 0),

the SCell, shall not be released due to bad RLQ or data inactivity.

Rationale: SCell Release due to bad RLQ involves NRBTS-sCellExcludelistTimerFr1, which prevents ping-pong of SCell Release/SCell Addition procedures for SCell reported with CQI = 0. In order to avoid above-mentioned ping-pong, SCell with CQI=0 shall never be released due to data inactivity. 

Note 1: Handling of SCell reported with CQI=0 is independent on setting of NRBTS/NRCELL-sCellDeactivationTimerGNB and NRBTS-actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell.

Note 2: Any SCell Release triggered by the C-Plane (e.g. A2 based SCell Release) shall be applicable if it is enabled, but it is not considered here.

[End PR767881]

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

Note 1: This functionality does not require enabling of Buffer based SCell Configuration, see 5G_UP_ALG_15828_replaced([11120371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (i.e. NRBTS.actBufferBasedSCellAddition can be set to any value).

---

**3.7.1.4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11120751`)

SCell Release Procedure

---

**3.7.1.4.0-4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11120758`)

SCell Release If:

\- NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq is set to ‘enabled_Fr1’ in gNB-DU hosting the P(S)Cell, and

\- the SCell configured for the UE was deactivated by P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS due to bad SCell RLQ according to 5G_UP_ALG_2774_replaced([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will immediately indicate it along with sCellIndex to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell as a trigger to release the respective SCell at the UE with SCell Inactive Reason ‘bad RLQ’.

[03599183]

If:

 NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq is set to ‘enabled_Fr1’ and NRBTS.sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount is set to value other than '0' in gNB-DU hosting the P(S)Cell, and

 gNB-DU receives consecutively CQI = 0 for the SCell for a time period defined by (NRBTS.sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount * NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellChannelEstimationPeriod)

P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will immediately indicate it along with sCellIndex to gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell as a trigger to release the respective SCell at the UE with SCell Inactive Reason ‘bad RLQ’.

gNB-DU shall not send to UE SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC CE for this SCell before releasing the SCell.

Note 1:

According to 5G_UP_1411_replaced([11358974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uckJHfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU suspends UE’s scheduling in the SCell for which CQI = 0 is reported and this SCell is left active.

[End 03599183]

If:

\- NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq is set to ‘disabled’ in gNB-DU hosting the P(S)Cell, and

\- the SCell configured for the UE was deactivated by P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS due to bad SCell RLQ according to 5G_UP_ALG_2774_replaced([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

SCell 5G-L2-PS shall start SCell Inactivity Release Timer and the SCell shall be released according to 5G_UP_ALG_16243_replaced([11120649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTC8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

Concurrency handling of different reasons triggering SCell Release is described in 5G_UP_ALG_16462_replaced([11120771](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqTqD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:   
Only one SCell is included in each indication to the gNB-DU C-Plane.

  * For sCellIndex refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_940_replaced([11245482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tm-gYPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.7.1.4.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11120763`)

SCell Release Online reconfiguration of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq

---

**3.7.1.4.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11120767`)

SCell Release In case NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq is online reconfigured during cell reconfiguration procedure, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS is provided with the new setting by gNB-DU C-Plane [CB008311-E] hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell [End CB008311-E] when the SCell is configured in the U-Plane for the UE (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3111_replaced([11315716](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4Of_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall update the UE context with new value of this parameter and use:

 the old value of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq for all CA UEs which were configured with this SCell while the NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq was changed

 new setting of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseBadSCellRlq for all CA UEs with this SCell upon SCell Addition

[CB008311-E]

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

[End CB008311-E]

---

#### 3.7.1.4.0-5 SCell Release Concurrency handling of different reasons triggering SCell Release (ID: 11120771)

**3.7.1.4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11120774`)

SCell Release Concurrency of SCell Release due to bad SCell RLQ and (data inactivity or UE overheating)

---

**3.7.1.4.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11120779`)

SCell Release If the following concurrent events are detected in SCell 5G-L2-PS:

1\. bad SCell RLQ, and

2\. expiration of SCell Inactivity Release Timer due to prolonged UE data inactivity or UE overheating (see Note) in this SCell

SCell 5G-L2-PS shall report to P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS SCell’s state: ‘bad RLQ’. Consequently, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will indicate it to gNB-DU C-Plane [CB008311-E] hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell [End CB008311-E] as a trigger to release the respective SCell at the UE with SCell Inactive Reason ‘bad RLQ’.

[CB008311-E]

The term ‘SCell’ refers to both cases: SCell in intra-gNB or ext-SCell in inter-gNB configuration.

[End CB008311-E]

Note 1:

Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information (CB008697) is applicable for Stand Alone (SA) Architecture Option 2 only.

---

#### 3.7.1.4.0-6 SCell Release ext-SCell Release controlled by OAM setting in prime-gNB and ext-gNB in FR1 Inter-gNB CA (ID: 11120781)

**3.7.1.4.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11120792`)

11120792: SCell Release 11120792: SCell Release 11120792: SCell Release 11120792: SCell Release 11120792: SCell Release 11120792: SCell Release 11120792: SCell Release 11120792: SCell Release In Inter-gNB DL CA case, prime-gNB and ext-gNB may be configured with different values of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell.

Setting of this parameter is not synchronized between prime-gNB and ext-gNB and consequently:

\- prime-gNB is not aware of configuration of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell in ext-gNB and vice versa

\- there is no consistency check of NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell set in prime-gNB and ext-gNB

Behavior related to ext-SCell Release due to data inactivity or UE overheating based on prime-gNB and ext-gNB parameters is summarized in the table below:

[docx_desc] Parameter setting in prime-gNB Parameter setting in ext-gNB Behavior for ext-SCell only NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell= disabled NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell= disabled ext-SCell Release due to data inactivity is disabled. ext-SCell is not released due to data inactivity. NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell= timer_based_Fr1 NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell= disabled ext-SCell Release due to data inactivity is disabled. ext-SCell is not released due to data inactivity. NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell= timer_based_Fr1 NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell= timer_based_Fr1 NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer > 0 for the ext-SCell ext-SCell release due to data inactivity is enabled. The ext-SCell will report SCell Inactivity Release Timer expiration and cause to the PCell. PCell triggers the SCell release. (see also 5G_UP_ALG_16250) NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell= disabled NRBTS.actSCellReleaseForInactiveSCell= timer_based_Fr1 NRCELL.sCellInactivityReleaseTimer > 0 for the ext-SCell ext-SCell release due to data inactivity is disabled. The ext-SCell will report SCell Inactivity Release Timer expiration and cause to the PCell. PCell ignores this indication. ext-SCell is not released due to data inactivity. (see also 5G_UP_ALG_16250)[/docx_desc][docx_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/attachments/m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file6453_0.docx[/docx_path]

**3.7.1.4.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11120797`)

SCell Release ext-SCell Release due to bad SCell RLQ in FR1 CA

---

**3.7.1.4.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11120803`)

SCell Release 11120803: SCell Release 11120803: SCell Release 11120803: SCell Release 11120803: SCell Release 11120803: SCell Release 11120803: SCell Release 11120803: SCell Release 11120803: SCell ### 3.7.1.5 Scell Change

#### 3.7.1.5.0-1 Scell Change (ID: 11120811)

**3.7.1.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11120813`)

Scell Change When P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS received UserModifyReq with SCell change for a FR1 CA UE, P(S)Cell shall stop Distributed PUCCH algorithm pre-allocation for the SCell and delay the SCell change to UE till the end of corresponding scheduling cycle. After that gNB shall send UserModifyResp to CPRT, restrict to P(S)Cell scheduling only, and enter transient period of SCell change.

---

### 3.7.2 SCell Activation/Deactivation

#### 3.7.2.0-2 SCell Activation/Deactivation Document Owner Deputy Jerzy Grabowski; Kaifeng Yang; Jingbo Huang (ID: 11120824)

#### 3.7.2.1 Blind Scell Activation

##### 3.7.2.1.0-1 Blind Scell Activation Blind SCells Activation (ID: 11120833)

**3.7.2.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12877591`)

Blind Scell Activation The 5G-L2-PS shall support blind activation of all SCells configured in the UE by triggering 5G-L2-LO to send the SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC Control Element to the UE.

The blind activation of the SCells is selected by the NIDD parameter NRBTS/sCellActivationMethod set to ‘blind’.

The blind activation of the SCells is also used in SCell Change procedure, if indication from Control Plane is received for immediate activation and if removed SCell was activated before SCell Change. In such case, 5G-L2-PS shall skip buffer based activation procedure and activate added SCell immediately as in Blind SCell activation procedure. The SCell activation excluding condition shall still be checked as per (5G_UP_ALG [11121235](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWtXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in order to avoid overload on added SCell.

[CB010741-C]  
The blind activation of the SCells is also used in case of SCell Upgrade procedure (5G_CP_OTH [11597749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y28SZ_wOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) if upgraded SCell was activated before SCell Upgrade trigger. In such case, gNB-DU hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell shall skip buffer based activation procedure and activate upgraded SCell immediately after the SCell Upgrade procedure is completed (as in Blind SCell activation procedure).   
[End CB010741-C] 

5G-L2-PS shall apply guard period between activation of the SCell and start of scheduling according to (5G_UP_ALG [11121815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of maximum number of HARQ retransmissions is reached for TB carrying the SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC Control Element, 5G-L2-PS shall include SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC Control Element until the successful HARQ ACK is received.

sCellActivationMethod of ‘blind’ is supported for FR1 DL CA and FR2 SA CA, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall trigger the SCell activation after RRC reconfiguration complete message (5G_CP_IF_RRC [11316765](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wTec1fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has been received to indicate SCell addition successfully for SA and NSA (refer to ueAddCause) and also after RA procedure done for NSA UE.

SCells with high load status (refer to 5G_UP_ALG [11121235](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWtXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be activated. As a restriction, such SCell will never be activated again.

sCellActivationMethod of ‘blind’ is supported for FR1 UL CA. If a SCell is activated, both downlink and uplink are activated.

For FR2 CA, if NRBTS.actHighNumberOfUEs is TRUE and rdActAutoScellDeactivationOnLoad is TRUE, when trying to activate a SCell, the SCell to be activated shall be selected in the following prioritization sequence:

  * tier1: DL&UL mode > DL only mode;
  * tier2: lower activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL > higher activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL;
  * tier3: lower carrier load > high carrier load;
  * tier4: smaller SCell index > larger SCell index.



and no more than maxAllowedActiveSCells SCell(s) can be activated per UE.

Where:

  * “A > B” means "candidates with property A is prioritized over candidates with property B, that is: candidates with property A will always be selected first if there exist both candidates with property A and candidates with property B; candidate(s) with property B can be selected only there does not exist any candidate with property A";
  * activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL: see (5G_UP_ALG [11122140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
  * carrier load: number of UEs with active serving cell on this carrier;
  * maxAllowedActiveSCells is defined in (5G_UP_ALG [11122157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

---

##### 3.7.2.1.0-2 Blind Scell Activation SCell Deactivation due to data inactivity based on SCell Inactivity Deactivation Timer (FR1 CA) (ID: 11120850)

**3.7.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11120854`)

Blind Scell Activation If

\- gNB hosting the P(S)Cell is configured with NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod = blind , and

\- NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB is configured in the SCell with value other than 0 (infinity)

the blindly activated SCells shall be permanently deactivated due to data inactivity after the sCellDeactivationTimerGNB expires (see Note).

SCell Deactivation based on SCell Inactivity Deactivation Timer in case NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod = blind is executed in the same manner as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

Note: Such settings of SCell activation/deactivation parameters are possible in the following cases:

1\. in inter-gNB CA configuration (see 5G_UP_ALG_16091_replaced([11121973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

2\. in intra-gNB CA configuration (for ongoing calls only) after SCell activation/deactivation parameters have been online changed as follows:

\- NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod: ‘blind’ -> ‘bufferBased’

NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is stored per UE context (i.e. it is not overwritten by a recently changed value), thus for ongoing calls NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod still has old setting ‘blind’, whereas for new calls this parameter shall be set to new value, and

\- NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB: ‘infinity’ -> other than ‘infinity’

NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB is stored per cell context (i.e. it is immediately overwritten by a recently changed value), thus for ongoing and new calls NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod shall be set to new value.

Details regarding storing of the parameters per UE/cell context are not in scope of SFS.

---

###### 3.7.2.2 Common Procedure for Buffer and Buffer/Quality based SCell Activation/Deactivation

###### 3.7.2.2.1 Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation

###### 3.7.2.2.1.0-1 Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation SCell activation / deactivation evaluation (ID: 11120866)

**3.7.2.2.1.0-1.0-8**  (ID: `13471723`)

Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation 13471723: Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation 13471723: Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation 13471723: Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation 13471723: Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation 13471723: Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation 13471723: Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation The evaluation of the SCell activation/deactivation procedure for the buffer based and joint buffer and radio link quality-based method shall be coordinated in the DL branch of 5G-L2-PS when selected by the NIDD parameter sCellActivationMethod set to ‘bufferBased’ or ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ and comprises the chronological sequence of the evaluation period and the period during that the evaluation shall be paused. The chronological sequence shall be kept all the time, independent of the decision whether a SCell shall be activated/deactivated or not. For FR1 CA, 5G-L2-PS will evaluate the Scell activation/deactivation procedure based on buffer only for both ‘bufferBased’ or ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ (**Note: Same behaviour for ‘bufferBased’ or ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’) accordingly to 5G_UP_ALG_2709_replaced([11120941](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and start to monitor Scell radio link quality after Scell is active state according to 5G_UP_ALG_2763_replaced([11121567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **for downlink and 5G_UP_ALG_11867_replaced([11121616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for uplink.**_* For FR1 CA, the evaluation of SCell activation, which is buffer based only, shall be executed in P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS upon receipt of the RRC reconfiguration complete message (5G_CP_IF_RRC_800_replaced([11316765](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wTec1fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) indicating the successful addition of the SCell and any time when there is (are) inactive SCell(s) which potentially could be activated. Buffer status monitoring for CA UEs shall be evenly distributed in a time window, if NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh is TRUE, the time interval between 2 checks for a specific UE may vary depending on the number of UEs awaiting check in a specific slot, because not all UEs with check opportunity in a specific slot can be checked in one occurrence of that slot, and the buffer check can be suspended due to scheduler overload; else all UEs with check opportunity in a specific slot shall be checked in one occurrence of that slot and the check shall not be impacted by scheduler overload. If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE, If rdModifiedCaOvlActionEnabled = False ([13399508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_txS0IAsHEfGu_4itz1o3RA)), then, if gNB-DU detects overload in the CPU core to which the PCell(s) DL branch is/are deployed as per the checks defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31958_replaced([11122225](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or gNB-DU detects overload for any of the scheduler(s) deployed on the core as per the checks defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31922_replaced([11120584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then gNB-Du shall suspend buffer status monitoring for SCell activation (only actions defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2716_replaced([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL branch, for all the PCell schedulers(s) deployed on the core. Else if rdModifiedCaOvlActionEnabled = True ([13399508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_txS0IAsHEfGu_4itz1o3RA)) * gNB-DU shall follow the same rules as defined in [11120462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqRNxPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) to suspend the buffer status monitoring for the Pcell scheduler(s) deployed in the core. * If gNB-DU detects overload in the CPU core to which the PCell(s) DL branch is/are deployed as per the checks defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31958_replaced([11122225](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) then gNB-Du shall suspend buffer status monitoring for SCell activation (actions defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2716_replaced([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL branch. Note that evaluation in UL is also suspended as a result) for all the PCell scheduler(s) deployed on the core Else, when gNB-DU detects scheduler overload (see 5G_L2_19965_replaced([11213408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj3vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the CPU core to which PCell is deployed, buffer status monitoring for SCell activation shall be suspended. If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE, If rdModifiedCaOvlActionEnabled = False ([13399508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_txS0IAsHEfGu_4itz1o3RA)), then If gNB-DU detects that the CPU core to which the PCell(s) DL branch is/are deployed recover from overload as per the checks defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31958_replaced(11122225) then, gNB-Du shall resume buffer status monitoring for SCell activation for all the PCell scheduler(s) deployed on the core. Else if rdModifiedCaOvlActionEnabled = True ([13399508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_txS0IAsHEfGu_4itz1o3RA)) * gNB-DU shall follow the same rules as defined in [11120462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqRNxPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) to resume the buffer status monitoring for the Pcell scheduler(s) deployed in the core. * If gNB-DU detects that the CPU core to which the PCell(s) DL branch is/are deployed recover from overload as per the checks defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31958_replaced([11122225](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) then, gNB-Du shall resume buffer status monitoring for SCell activation for all the PCell scheduler(s) deployed on the core. Else, when gNB-DU detects all schedulers recover from overload (see 5G_L2_19965_replaced([11213408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-rj3vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the CPU core to which PCell is deployed, buffer status monitoring for SCell activation shall be resumed. _*[Before CB013712-B] For SA mode FR2 CA, in case NRBTS.scellActivationMethod is set to “bufferBased” or “bufferAndRLQualityBased”: * DL branch of 5G-L2-PS shall start DL buffer evaluation for SCell activation / deactivation when it receives from C-Plane the notification that RRC reconfiguration complete message has been received which confirms the success of SCell addition. If there exists at least one SCell in “DL and UL” operation mode, UL branch of 5G-L2-PS shall also start UL buffer evaluation for SCell activation / deactivation. * DL buffer evaluation shall be stopped when the last SCell is released; UL buffer evaluation shall be stopped when the last SCell in “DL and UL” operation mode is released. **[End CB013712-B]**5G-L2-PS shall not check activation / deactivation condition for a SCell in the transient period of SCell release [5G_UP_ALG ([11120600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] or SCell Addition/SCell Upgrade (see [11120310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqPYnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). For sCellActivationMethod is set to ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ and ‘bufferBased’, 5G-L2-PS shall check further whether the one of UE activated Scell is in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). if one of activated Scell is in overheating status, 5G-L2-PS shall evaluate the Scell for deactivation only. In the case of scheduler processing overload, gNB-DU U-Plane shall perform the checks defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31954_replaced([11122234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_31955_replaced([11122241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SCell deactivation. If UE is overheated (based on UE overheating assistance information as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2821_replaced([11121920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then L2-PS shall not activate more SCells than value of MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL and MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2822_replaced([11121925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If a UE is in the power saving bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1865_replaced([11111133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpKajvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then 5G-L2-PS shall not activate any SCells for that UE. The activation/deactivation of the SCells either for the DL only or for DL and UL shall be coordinated in the DL branch of the 5G-L2-PS: The length of the evaluation period is defined by a R&D parameter **[Before CB013712-B] rdPeriodScellCheck (5G_L2_1148_replaced([11184595](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR2 as P(S)Cell and**[End CB013712-B] rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 (5G_L2_1388_replaced([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1 as P(S)Cell and shall take into account the maximum number of UEs for which the carrier aggregation mode can be configured, ensuring that all the CA UEs are equally distributed amongst the checking occasions within the evaluation period and that only a certain number of UEs can be processed per checking occasion. Both, the conditions for activation and deactivation of SCells shall be checked for the UL branch and for the DL branch. To assure the joint evaluation of the checks in the DL branch of 5G-L2-PS, the UL branch shall be checked before the DL branch. Based on these conditions a fix checking pattern can be determined for all CA UEs.******[Before CB013712-B]The following figure shows an example about the principle of the checking procedure for an evaluation period of 10 slots length for FR2.**[image-0][image_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating the coordination of buffer-based SCell evaluation without SCell activation/deactivation. evaluation period consists of 3 checks in UL and DL, respectively. As shown in the figure, the checks shall be repeated similarly during the next evaluation period until the configured number of checks is processed. On completion of the checking sequence the evaluation of the SCell activation/deactivation conditions shall be paused until the next checking sequence takes place. The number of continuous checks is specified by R &D parameter **[Before CB013712-B]rdNumOfScellChecks (5G_L2_1149_replaced([11184600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR2 as P(S)Cell and**[End CB013712-B] rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1 [5G_L2_1390_replaced([11184651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for FR1 as P(S)Cell in downlink and rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1UL (5G_UP_ALG_10051_replaced([11124102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in uplink. The pause between the checking sequence is specified by the R&D parameter **[Before CB013712-B]rdProhibitScellCheck (5G_L2_1150_replaced([11184607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR2 (Note: default 68 so the prohibit period is same as before) and **[End CB013712-B] rdProhibitScellCheckFR1 (5G_L2_1392_replaced([11184664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1, which starts either at the end of the evaluation period if 5G-L2-PS doesn’t request the activation/deactivation of a SCell or with the reception of the HARQ ACK corresponding to the transport block carrying the MAC-C element for activating/deactivating the SCell. The check of the buffer utilization shall be started again after expiration **[Before CB013712-B]rdProhibitScellCheck for FR2 and **[End CB013712-B]rdProhibitScellCheckFR1 for FR1 when the next evaluation period starts.****_*_** **_Upon SCell activation, if sCellActivationMethod is set to ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’, 5G-L2-PS shall start radio link quality evaluation after expiration of rdProhibitScellCheck timer when the next evaluation period starts._ *[Before CB013712-B]** In FR2, if active UE load based SCell deactivation is supported, gNB-DU shall do the active UE load check together with the check on buffer and RLQ, see 5G_UP_ALG_27443_replaced([11120929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfM_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more information. **[End CB013712-B]** sCellActivationMethod: NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod**

---

###### 3.7.2.2.1.0-2 Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation Avoid SCell deactivation during CQI measurement and link adaptation startup (ID: 11120911)

**3.7.2.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11120916`)

Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation Initially, upon SCell activation, 5G-L2-PS shall skip triggering of DL radio link quality based deactivation until CQI report is received and DL MCS is updated by LA function. This is to avoid deactivation of the SCell due to low setting of initial DL MCS in NIDD (dllaIniMcs <mcsDeactSCellDl).

Initially, upon SCell activation, 5G-L2-PS shall skip triggering of UL radio link quality based deactivation until L2-PS receives SINR measurement from L1-UL and UL MCS is updated by LA function (first UL data transmission on PUSCH is received). This is to avoid deactivation of the SCell due to low setting of initial UL MCS in NIDD (ullaIniMcs<mcsDeactSCellUl) and no UL data transmission that is needed by LA feature for updating UL MCS. In case LA function applies initial UL MCS due to no UL data transmission for the duration of rdSinrExpiryTimer (5G_UP_ALG_3078_replaced([11130719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krANl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced([11131515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_1029_replaced([11186254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_274Hf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall skip triggering of UL radio link quality based deactivation until L2-PS receives SINR measurement from L1-UL and UL MCS is updated by LA function (first UL data transmission on PUSCH is received).

In case LA function applies initial DL MCS due to missing CQI reports for the duration of rdCqiExpiryTime timer (5G_UP_ALG_3005_replaced([11125595](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3045_replaced([11125301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqt5svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_1026_replaced([11184999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27u9ifvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), initial DL MCS shall be considered by radio link quality based SCell deactivation algorithm and in case it is lower than mcsDeactSCellDl, SCell deactivation due to DL radio link quality shall be triggered. In case LA function applies initial DL MCS due to Scell is recovered from overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3005_replaced([11125595](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), initial DL MCS shall not be considered by radio link quality based SCell deactivation algorithm and in case it is lower than mcsDeactSCellDl, SCell deactivation due to DL radio link quality shall not be triggered.

dllaIniMcs: NRBTS.NRCELL.dllaIniMcs

mcsDeactSCellDl: NRBTS.mcsDeactSCellDl

ullaIniMcs: NRBTS.NRCELL.ullaIniMcs

mcsDeactSCellUl: NRBTS.mcsDeactSCellUl

---

###### 3.7.2.2.1.0-3 Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation Timing of sending SCell activation / deactivation MAC-CE (ID: 11120921)

**3.7.2.2.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13341667`)

Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation The MAC-C element for activating a SCell shall be sent out after the evaluation period if the condition for activating a SCell is fulfilled. The MAC-C element for deactivating a SCell shall be sent out after the evaluation period if the triggering condition for deactivating a SCell is fulfilled (see 5G_UP_ALG_2758_replaced([11121561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and execution of all ongoing HARQ processes – means after reception of an HARQ ACK feedback for all ongoing HARQ processes. In case there are some issues for receiving HARQ feedback, 5G-L2-PS shall consider all ongoing HARQ processes are finished after 200 TTIs.

[CB015279-A] If [Before CB015279-F] NRCELL.actMultiTags [CB015279-F] NRCELL.actMultipleTags [End CB015279-F] is not disabled and a UE supports multiple timing alignment groups (TAGs), then for Scells belonging to a different TAG, the activation is performed similar to the single TAG case via MAC CE when the buffer status check for SCell activation in UL (depicted in [11120998](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) is satisfied. Once an Scell is activated, it will initiate UL timing alignment based on PDCCH order (as depicted in [13341712](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_xe7jgNykEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ)). [End CB015279-A]

SCell deactivation can be triggered also due to UE overheated based on UE overheating assistance information as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2822_replaced([11121925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), in this case MAC-CE element for deactivating shall be sent at least MIN {after reception of an HARQ ACK feedback for all ongoing HARQ processes, after 32 TTIs} for FDD SCell case and MIN {after reception of an HARQ ACK feedback for all ongoing HARQ processes, after 64 TTIs} for TDD FR1 SCell case.

The gNB shall consider the SCell as activated or deactivated only if the MAC-C element is received by the UE and corresponding Non-DTX ACK HARQ feedback is received by gNB, the evaluation of the buffer condition shall be repeated with beginning of the next evaluation period if sCellActivationMethod is set to 'bufferBased', and the evaluation of the radio link quality condition shall be repeated with beginning of the next evaluation period if sCellActivationMethod is set to ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ .

For FR2:

 The value of rdProhibitScellCheck for FR2 shall be greater than sCellActivationPeriod (see 5G_UP_ALG_2792_replaced([11121815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which specifies the time needed for activating/deactivating the SCell. If rdProhibitScellCheck for FR2 is set to a smaller value than sCellActivationPeriod, rdProhibitScellCheck **for FR2 shall be set in 5G-L2-PS to the value of sCellActivationPeriod.**

For FR1:

 Directly after MAC CE to activate the Scell has been sent, rdProhibitScellCheckFR1 defines the minimum interval between expiry of sCellActivationPeriod guard timer (see 5G_UP_ALG_2792_replaced([11121815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the next Scell activation/deactivation check according 5G_UP_2758_replaced([11392311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufdFDfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 Directly after MAC CE to deactivate the Scell has been sent, rdProhibitScellCheckFR1 defines the minimum interval between triggering the Scell deactivation MAC CE and the next Scell activation/deactivation check according 5G_UP_2758_replaced([11392311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufdFDfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).This interval must be at least 3ms, due to UEs deactivation delay.

  * Else, rdProhibitScellCheckFR1 defines the minimum interval between two consecutive Scell activation/deactivation checks according 5G_UP_2758_replaced([11392311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufdFDfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



SCell activation method (_sCellActivationMethod) can be changed on-line. A change will take affect only for the new UEs for which the UE context setup was established after the change. Already connected UEs will be handled according to the method that was valid at the time of UE context setup._

The MAC-C element for SCell activation/deactivation shall be sent out while UE is in DRX active status if UE is DRX enabled.

File: 5G_RAN_UP_CoordinationofSCellActDeact.xlsx

Folder: [https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane?csf=1&web=1&e=V8ishU](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane?csf=1&web=1&e=V8ishU)

---

###### 3.7.2.2.1.0-4 Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation Coordination of various SCell activation / deactivation check (ID: 11120929)

**3.7.2.2.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11120933`)

Coordination of SCell activation/deactivation If gNB-DU needs to check whether SCell needs to be deactivated due to active UE load for current UE (auLoadBaseSCellDeactCheck [5G_UP_ALG_26309_replaced([11122151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] = 1 for current UE), gNB-DU shall do the check as follows:

if (auLoadBasedSCellDeactCheck == 1)

{

Determine the number of SCell(s) that shall be deactivated due to active UE load as per 5G_UP_ALG_26313_replaced([11122168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbDPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), denote the number of SCell(s) to be deactivated as nSCellTobeDeactDueToAuLoad;

Determine the SCells that shall be deactivated due to bad RLQ, denote the number of SCell(s) that are deactivated due to bad RLQ as nSCellDeactDueToRLQ;

if (nSCellTobeDeactDueToAuLoad > nSCellDeactDueToRLQ)

{

Continue to select m SCell(s) to deactivate according to 5G_UP_ALG_21703_replaced([11121800](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqaXvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), m = nSCellTobeDeactDueToAuLoad – nSCellDeactDueToRLQ;

start rdProhibitScellCheck timer;

[CB012734-J]

for each SCell that shall be deactivated

{

Counter SCELL_DEACT_CC_LOAD_NRCELLGRP shall be pegged;

if (UE connects to cell group in SA mode)

{

Counter SCELL_DL_DEACT_CC_LOAD_SA shall be pegged;

if (SCell operates in “DL and UL” mode)

{

Counter SCELL_UL_DEACT_CC_LOAD_SA shall be pegged;

}

}

else // UE connects to cell group in NSA mode

{

Counter SCELL_DL_DEACT_CC_LOAD_NSA shall be pegged;

if (SCell operates in “DL and UL” mode)

{

Counter SCELL_UL_DEACT_CC_LOAD_NSA shall be pegged;

}

}

}

[End CB012734-J]

skip the check for SCell activation/deactivation on buffer;

}

else if (nSCellTobeDeactDueToAuLoad == 0)

{

Continue to check the conditions for SCell activation / deactivation on buffer.

}

auLoadBasedSCellDeactCheck = 0

}

else //auLoadBasedSCellDeactCheck = 0

{

check the condition for SCell deactivation due to bad RLQ (5G_UP_ALG_2745_replaced([11121442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYijfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

check the condition for SCell re-activation due to path loss change (5G_UP_ALG_2758_replaced([11121561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

check the condition for SCell activation / deactivation due to buffer (5G_UP_ALG_2713_replaced([11120950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2738_replaced([11120974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

If ((NRCELLGRP.actHighNumberOfUEs == TRUE) && (rdActAutoScellDeactivationOnLoad [5G_UP_ALG_26569_replaced([11124322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]== 1))

{

[Before PR796424]

If ((auLoadReductionTimer [5G_UP_ALG_26309_replaced([11122151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] is running) OR (number of activated SCell(s) >= maxAllowedActiveScells [5G_UP_ALG_26311_replaced([11122157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]) OR (totalActiveUeLoad [5G_UP_ALG_26307_replaced([11122140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] [PR787445] + activePendingCcNum + 1 (5G_UP_ALG_30184_replaced([11122182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End PR787445] >= scellReductionThreshold [5G_UP_ALG_26309_replaced([11122151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]) )

[PR796424]

If ( (auLoadReductionTimer is running) OR ((number of activated SCell(s) of current UE >= maxAllowedActiveSCells) AND (The SCell to be activated is a DL only SCell)) )

[End PR796424]

{

gNB-DU shall avoid activating new SCell(s) for current UE;

}

}

}
