Activation/Deactivation 11120970: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120970: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120970: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120970: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120970: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120970: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation For more information please see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS of the DL branch shall evaluate the load conditions in DL transmission buffer whenever requested as specified by 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The load conditions shall be evaluated for triggering the activation and for triggering the deactivation of the SCell differently.

If the total amount of user data awaiting in DL transmission buffer is for n consecutive checks above the activation threshold, the request for activating an additional SCell related to the DL shall be forwarded to the entity, which coordinates the SCell activation/deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The request for deactivating a SCell shall be forwarded to the entity, which coordinates the SCell activation/deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if the average amount of user data awaiting in DL transmission buffer is for n consecutive checks below the deactivation threshold. Checks are taken with a period of 10 slots. The average load of the DL transmission buffer shall be calculated by load samples, which are captured between the checks. A sample for calculating the average load shall be taken if the buffered load changes between the slots.

The number n of consecutive checks is specified by the R&D parameter rdNumOfScellChecks (see 5G_L2_1149_replaced([11184600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The activation threshold dlScellActivationThreshold shall be determined by the m times greater data volume accumulated over all current DL data rate related to the UE’s activated PSCell and SCells (see 5G_UP_ALG_4242_replaced([11175309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Cells for that a radio link failure is detected are not taken into account. The factor m is defined by the R&D parameter rdScellActivationLevel (see 5G_L2_1151_replaced([11184560](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6OfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The following calculation rule defines the activation threshold

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula is: dlScellActivation Threshold[i, t] = rdScellActivation Level × ∑ rrmCurrentDiUeDataRate_BytePerSlot[i,j,t] Above the summation symbol, the text "active PSCell" and "and Scell" are present. The summation symbol has an index 'j' below it.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6489.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

with

i: Index of the UE

j: Index of the PSCell and activated SCells which is not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

t: NR slot the calculation relates to

The deactivation threshold dlScellDeactivationThreshold is calculated in the same manner as the activation threshold, but is the kth fraction of the accumulated current DL data rate related to the UE’s activated PSCell and SCells. The fraction k is defined by the R&D parameter rdScellDeactivationLevel (see 5G_L2_1154_replaced([11184574](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6PPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [PR806418] or by R&D parameter rdScellDeactLvlCB012734 (5G_UP_ALG_32503_replaced([11124428](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqq2YPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End PR806418].

The following calculation rule defines the deactivation threshold [PR806418] if NRCELLGRP.actHighNumberOfUEs is False: [End PR806418]

[image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: `dlScellDeactivationThreshold[i,t] = rdScellDeactivationLevel * Σ rrmCurrentDlUeDataRate_BytePerSlot[i,j,t]` Above the summation symbol, it is indicated that the sum is over "active PSCell and SCell". The summation index is 'i'.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6489.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]

[PR806418]

If NRCELLGRP.actHighNumberOfUEs is True:

dlScellDeactivationThrehsold[i, t] = rdScelDeactLvlCB012734 * SUM(rrmCurrentDlUeDataRate_BytePerSlot[i,j, t] over all eligible serving cell[j])

[End PR806418]

with

i: Index of the UE

j: Index of the PSCell and activated SCells which is not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

t: NR slot the calculation relates to

If the UE is configured with no more than 3 Scells and indicated by CPRT with flag potentialSdx50 in PsUser_UserSetupReq is true, the calculation rule for the deactivation threshold shall be defined as below:

dlScelldeactivationThreshold[i,t] = rdScelldeactivationLevel*rrmCurrentDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i,j,t];

with:

i: Index of the UE

j: Index of the PScell

t: NR slot the calculation relates to

An empty DL transmission buffer shall be indicated separately to the coordination entity in DL 5G-L2-PS.

  * rrmCurrentDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i,j,t]: The current DL data rate of a 5G UE, which is valid in NR slot t for the carrier j (see 5G_UP_ALG_4242_replaced([11175309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3334_replaced([11252247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tngr1vvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for potentialSdx50.

Activation/Deactivation 11120993: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120993: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120993: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120993: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120993: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 11120993: Buffer-based SCell Activation/Deactivation 5G-L2-PS of the UL branch shall evaluate the load conditions of the UE’s transmission buffer based on the housekeeping (see 5G_UP_ALG_5115_replaced([11203641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfxn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) whenever requested as specified by 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If the total amount of user data awaiting in UE’s transmission buffer is for n consecutive checks above the activation threshold, the request for activating an additional SCell related to the UL shall be forwarded to the entity, which coordinates the SCell activation/deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). A request for deactivating a SCell related to the UL shall be forwarded if the housekeeping indicates for n consecutive checks a utilization of the UE’s transmission buffer below the deactivating threshold.

The number n of consecutive check is specified by the R&D parameter rdNumOfScellChecks (see 5G_L2_1149_replaced([11184600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The activation threshold ulScellActivationThreshold shall be determined by the m times greater data volume accumulated over all current UL data rate related to the UE’s activated PSCell and SCells (see 5G_UP_ALG_4856_replaced([11195916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv_bQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Cells for that a radio link failure is detected are not taken into account. The factor m is defined by the R&D parameter rdScellActivationLevel (see 5G_L2_1151_replaced([11184560](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6OfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The following calculation rule defines the activation threshold

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula is: ulScellActivationThreshold[i,t] = rdScellActivationLevel × ∑ rrmCurrentUlUeDataRate_BytePerSlot[i,j,t] Above the summation symbol, the text "active PSCell" and "and Scell" are present. The summation symbol has an index 'i' below it.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6492.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

with

i: Index of the UE

j: Index of the PSCell and activated SCells which is not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

t: NR slot the calculation relates to

The deactivation threshold ulScellDeactivationThreshold is calculated in the same manner as the activation threshold, but is the kth fraction of the accumulated current UL data rate related to the UE’s activated PSCell and SCells. The fraction k is defined by the R&D parameter rdScellDeactivationLevel (see 5G_L2_1154_replaced([11184574](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6PPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [PR806418] or by R&D parameter dScellDeactLvlCB012734 (5G_UP_ALG_32503_replaced([11124428](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqq2YPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End PR806418].

The following calculation rule defines the deactivation threshold [PR806418] if NRCELLGRP.actHighNumberOfUEs = False: [End PR806418]

[image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: `ulScellDeactivationThreshold[i,t] = rdScellDeactivationLevel * ∑ rrmCurrentUlUeDataRate_BytePerSlot[i,j,t]` Above the summation symbol, it is indicated that the sum is over "active PSCell and SCell". The summation index is `i`.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6492.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]

[PR806418]

If NRCELLGRP.actHighNumberOfUEs = True:

ulScellDeactivationThreshold[i, t] = rdScellDeactLvlCB012734 * SUM(rrmCurrentUlUeDataRate_BytePerSlot[i, j, t] over all eligible serving cell[j])

[End PR806418]

with

i: Index of the UE

j: Index of the PSCell and activated SCells which is not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

t: NR slot the calculation relates to

If the UE is configured with no more than 3 Scells and indicated by CPRT with flag potentialSdx50 in PsUser_UserSetupReq is true, the calculation rule for deactivation threshold shall be defined as below:

ulScelldeactivationThreshold[i,t] = rdScelldeactivationLevel*rrmCurrentUlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i,j,t];

with:

i: Index of the UE

j: Index of the PScell

t: NR slot the calculation relates to

An empty UL transmission buffer shall be indicated separately to the coordination entity in DL 5G-L2-PS.

  * rrmCurrentUlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot: The current UL data rate of a 5G UE, which is valid in NR slot t for the carrier j (see 5G_UP_ALG_4856_replaced([11195916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv_bQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3334_replaced([11252247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tngr1vvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for potentialSdx50.

Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 11121356: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 11121356: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 11121356: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 11121356: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 11121356: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 11121356: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 11121356: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 11121356: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Maintenance of the burstCount with the purpose to avoid unnecessary buffer based SCell deactivation with bursty TCP traffic model It was observed that due to the bursty TCP traffic SCell deactivation was triggered too fast and maximum data rate for the CA configured UEs was not reached. To avoid too fast SCell deactivation in case of bursty TCP traffic, internal counters burstCount and deactSkipCount are introduced. Initial value of  burstCount is set to rdCABurstCountInitialValue (see 5G_L2_1158_replaced( 11184629 )), Initial vaule of deactSkipCount is set to 0 Each time SCell deactivation based on buffer is triggered, L2-PS will check the correlation between burstCount and deactSkipCount. If burstCount value is bigger than deactSkipCount deactivation is skipped (“No action” is forced) and deactSkipCount is increased for 1. Deactivation is skipped until burstCount is same or smaller than deactSkipCount. If the checking result is RLQ deactivation after rdNumOfScellChecks (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced( 11120862 )), deactSkipCount is also increased by 1, but the deactivation is performed immediately without compare with burstCount . For other checking result after rdNumOfScellChecks (No action or Activation), deactSkipCount is reset to 0. Each time SCell deactivation due to 0 buffer is performed, value of burstCount is increased by 1 and value of deactSkipCount is reset to 0. Graphical representation of introduced algorithm using burstCount and deactSkipCount to prolong SCell deactivation when bursty traffic is detected: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a line graph illustrating the "Number of active Cells" over "Time". The y-axis represents the "Number of active Cells", and the x-axis represents "Time". A dashed horizontal line indicates a threshold of "min[(configured SCells+1), 4]". The graph shows a stepped line in cyan, representing the number of active cells, which increases over time. Several callout boxes explain the state of "burstCount" and "deactSkipCount" at different points in time, along with the conditions for SCell deactivation. Here's a breakdown of the information presented in the callout boxes: Initial State: * "Initially burstCount = 0 and deactSkipCount = 0 and therefore SCell deactivation is triggered at first 0 buffer trigger and after deactivation burstCount is increased by 1 and deactSkipCount remains 0" First Increase in Active Cells: * This segment is associated with "burstCount=0 =&gt; 1" and "deactSkipCount=0". * A callout box states: "burstCount = 1 and therefore SCell deactivation is triggered at second 0 buffer trigger when deactSkipCount=1 and after deactivation burstCount is increased by 1 and deactSkipCount is reset to 0". Second Increase in Active Cells: * This segment is associated with "burstCount=1 =&gt; 2" and "deactSkipCount=1 =&gt; 0". * A callout box states: "burstCount = 2 and therefore SCell deactivation is triggered at third 0 buffer trigger when deactSkipCount=2 and after deactivation burstCount is increased by 1 and deactSkipCount is reset to 0". Third Increase in Active Cells: * This segment is associated with "burstCount=2 =&gt; 3" and "deactSkipCount=2 =&gt; 0". Other Callout Boxes: * "burstCount=1", "deactSkipCount=0 =&gt; 1" * "burstCount=2", "deactSkipCount=0 =&gt; 1" * "burstCount=2", "deactSkipCount=1 =&gt; 2" At the bottom of the graph, there are two text boxes: * "Buffer bases SCell Activation" * "Each cycle duration is sum of: rdProhibitScellCheck + (rdNumOfScellChecks x rdPeriodScellCheck)" The graph visually depicts a process where the number of active cells increases in steps, influenced by the "burstCount" and "deactSkipCount" variables, and SCell deactivation events. The duration of each cycle is defined by a specific formula.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6551.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Impact of RLQ based deactivation and reset of the burstCount to rdCABurstCountInitialValue (see 5G_L2_1158_replaced( 11184629 )) if 0 buffer is indicated for more than 300ms: [image-1][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the behavior of "burstCount" and "deactSkipCount" in relation to "Number of active Cells" over "Time". The diagram uses a step-like graph to represent the "Number of active Cells" and includes several text boxes with explanations and annotations. The graph starts with the "Number of active Cells" at a low level, then increases in steps. The x-axis represents "Time", and the y-axis represents "Number of active Cells". There are several callout boxes explaining the state changes: 1. Top Left Callout: "Initially burstCount = 0 and deactSkipCount = 0 and therefore SCell deactivation is triggered at first 0 buffer trigger and after deactivation burstCount is increased by 1 and deactSkipCount remains 0" 2. Middle Left Callout: "If RLQ deactivation is triggered on SCell, SCell is deactivated, and after deactivation burstCount is not increased and deactSkipCount is increased by 1" 3. Top Right Callout: "burstCount = 1 and therefore SCell deactivation is triggered at second 0 buffer trigger when deactSkipCount=1 and after deactivation burstCount is increased by 1 and deactSkipCount is reset to 0" 4. Middle Right Callout: "burstCount = 2 and therefore SCell deactivation is triggered at third 0 buffer trigger when deactSkipCount=2 and after deactivation burstCount is increased by 1 due to 0 buffer and deactSkipCount is reset to 0." Below the graph, there are annotations indicating changes in "burstCount" and "deactSkipCount" at different points in time: * "burstCount=0 =&gt; 1" and "deactSkipCount=0" are shown at the beginning of the graph. * "burstCount=1 =&gt; 2" and "deactSkipCount=1 =&gt; 0" are shown as the graph rises. * A duration of "&lt;300ms" is indicated. * "burstCount=2 =&gt; 3" is shown. * A duration of "300ms" is indicated. * "burstCount=3 =&gt; 0" is shown. * "deactSkipCount = 0 =&gt; 1 =&gt; 2" is shown below the graph. * "burstCount=0 =&gt; 1" and "deactSkipCount=0" are shown towards the end of the graph. There are also two text boxes at the bottom of the image: 1. Bottom Left Text Box: "No burstCount reset since 0 buffer trigger was indicated for les than 300ms" 2. Bottom Right Text Box: "burstCount is reset to 0 since 0 buffer trigger was indicated for 300ms"[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6551.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] Graphical representation of introduced algorithm using burstCount and deactSkipCount to prolong SCell deactivation when traffic is stabilized - burstCount reset: [image-2][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a process related to "Number of active Cells" over "Time". The diagram uses a step-like blue line to represent the number of active cells, which increases at certain points in time. Various text boxes with explanations and conditions are connected to different segments of the timeline and the step graph. Here's a breakdown of the text and elements: Axes: * Y-axis: Labeled "Number of active Cells". * X-axis: Labeled "Time". Key Events and Conditions: * "First 0 buffer trigger (3 validation with 0 buffer)" : This event occurs early in the timeline and is associated with an initial increase in the number of active cells. * "Second 0 buffer trigger (3 validation with 0 buffer)" : This event occurs later and is associated with another increase in active cells. * "If 0 buffer trigger (3 validation with 0 buffer) was not issued, burstCount=2 is kept while deactSkipCount is reset to 0" : This condition is shown to be active during a period where the number of active cells is stable. * "No 0 buffer is triggered (after 3 consecutive validation)" : This indicates a state where 0 buffer triggers are not occurring. * "rdDataStableForBurstCntResetTime" : This is a time duration indicated by a horizontal arrow spanning a significant portion of the timeline. * "If 0 buffer trigger (3 validation with 0 buffer) was not issued for the duration of rdDataStableForBurstCntResetTime, burstCount is reset to 0" : This condition is linked to the end of the rdDataStableForBurstCntResetTime period. * "Since burstCount = 0 and deactSkipCount = 0 SCell deactivation is triggered for all SCells at first 0 buffer trigger and after deactivation burstCount is increased by 1 and deactSkipCount remains 0" : This is a detailed explanation of a specific state and its consequences. State Changes (indicated by arrows and text boxes below the timeline): * "burstCount=2 deactSkipCount=0 =&gt; 1" : This indicates a transition where burstCount remains 2 and deactSkipCount changes from 0 to 1. * "burstCount=2 deactSkipCount=1 =&gt; 2" : This indicates a transition where burstCount remains 2 and deactSkipCount changes from 1 to 2. * "burstCount=2 deactSkipCount=2 =&gt; 0" : This indicates a transition where burstCount remains 2 and deactSkipCount changes from 2 to 0. * "burstCount=2 =&gt; 0 deactSkipCount=0" : This indicates a transition where burstCount changes from 2 to 0 and deactSkipCount remains 0. Summary Equation: * "Each cycle duration is sum of: rdProhibitScellCheck + (rdNumOfScellChecks x rdPeriodScellCheck)" : This equation defines how the duration of each cycle is calculated.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6551.003.png[/image_path][/image-2] If the value of the rdDataStableForBurstCntResetTime is within the range {300...5000ms}, timer is started if not running and restarted if running each time 0 buffer is triggered (all 3 validations indicate 0 buffer). If data traffic is stabilized and there are no new bursts triggering 0 buffer due to the gap of no data between the bursts, rdDataStableForBurstCntResetTime timer will not be restarted (as long as there are no 0 buffer triggers) and At expiry of the timer burstCount is reset to rdCABurstCountInitialValue  (see 5G_L2_1158_replaced( 11184629 )) The rdDataStableForBurstCntResetTime parameter have a special value 299 and if set to this value functionality is not in use, meaning timer is not started and burstCount is never reset to 0. Timer is specified by the R&amp;D parameter rdDataStableForBurstCntResetTime defined in 5G_L2_1157_replaced( 11184680 ). (ID: 11121356)

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-1 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Overview of buffer based SCell activation/deactivation in FR1 CA (ID: 11120999)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13423047`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) **For SCell activation:**

PCell DL L2-PS controls the SCell selection for activation, because PCell DL L2-PS has the full knowledge of where the SCell activation request comes from.

PCell DL L2-PS evaluates **buffer status for SCell activation in DL branch according to (5G_UP_ALG[11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), if the condition is met, it counts as the SCell activation request coming from DL branch.**

PCell UL L2-PS evaluates **buffer status for SCell activation in UL branch according to (5G_UP_ALG[11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), if the condition is met, PCell UL L2-PS informs PCell DL L2-PS, and it counts as the SCell activation request coming from UL branch.**

For the carrier aggregation with a same or different number of SCells in DL and UL, the origin of the SCell activation request determines if a DL only SCell or a joint DL/UL SCell shall be activated.

PCell DL L2-PS determines of number of SCells to be activated according to (5G_UP_ALG [11121245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

PCell DL L2-PS selects SCells to be activated according to (5G_UP_ALG [11121256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and sends SCell activation MAC CE containing all the candidates.

[CB014088-F]

When gNB-DU detects overload in the CPU core to which the PCell(s) is/are deployed as per the checks defined in (5G_UP_ALG [11122225](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or (5G_UP_ALG [11120462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqRNxPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for overload, or gNB-DU deems a SCell unavailable for activation as per the checks defined in (5G_UP_ALG [11122209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the DL branch, and (5G_UP_ALG [11122218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UL branch then buffer status monitoring for SCell activation (i.e actions defined in (5G_UP_ALG [11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL branch and (5G_UP_ALG [11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL branch) shall be suspended.

When gNB-DU detects that the CPU core to which the PCell(s) deployed recover from overload as per the checks defined in (5G_UP_ALG [11122225](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and (5G_UP_ALG [11120462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqRNxPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and gNB-DU deems a SCell available for activation as per the checks defined in (5G_UP_ALG [11122209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the DL branch, and (5G_UP_ALG [11122218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UL branch then, buffer status monitoring for SCell activation shall be resumed.

In case the conditions for SCell activation is met for DL branch alone and not for UL branch, then gNB-DU shall suspend the actions defined in (5G_UP_ALG [11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UL branch alone.

Depending on the above checks and actions, a Joint DL/UL configured SCell can activated either in the DL alone or in both DL and UL.

[End CB014088-F]

**For SCell deactivation:**

Unlike in FR2 CA where PCell DL L2-PS selects SCells for deactivation, in FR1 CA PCell DL L2-PS does not select SCells for deactivation for neither DL nor UL. Instead SCell deactivation is based on inactivity timer (NIDD: NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB):

For DL only SCell: when inactivity timer is expired in DL branch, SCell DL L2-PS shall send deactivation request to PCell DL L2-PS, see (5G_UP_ALG [11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For joint DL/UL SCell: when inactivity timer is expired in both DL and UL branchs, SCell DL L2-PS shall send deactivation request to PCell DL L2-PS, see (5G_UP_ALG [11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB014088-F]

In the case of scheduler processing overload, gNB-DU U-Plane shall perform the checks defined in (5G_UP_ALG [11122234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and (5G_UP_ALG [11122241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SCell deactivation.

[End CB014088-F]

In case of SCell Upgrade procedure (5G_CP_OTH [11597749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y28SZ_wOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), if the SCell was activated before SCell Upgrade trigger, gNB-DU hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell shall deactivate upgraded SCell once receives the SCell Upgrade notification from gNB-DU C-Plane hosting the UE’s P(S)Cell.  
This SCell shall be activated again when the SCell Upgrade procedure is finished successfully (see [11120833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqURHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-2 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Activation in DL Branch - Validity (ID: 11121013)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `13409225`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) If NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is configured to ‘bufferBased’ or ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) that 5G-L2-PS shall consider ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ same as ‘bufferBased’ method), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS of the DL branch shall evaluate the sum of buffer level (the sum of RLC SDU buffer level in L2-Hi and all RLC PDU buffer level in 5G-L2-LO) of all non-GBR bearers of CA eligible(5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SA call and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NSA call) for CA UE (receiving RRC reconfiguration complete message (5G_CP_IF_RRC_800_replaced([11316765](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wTec1fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to indicate SCell addition successfully) to trigger the decision for SCell activation. The evaluation of buffer level will take a period of rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 (see 5G_L2_1388_replaced([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) slots, the average buffer level across rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 slots will be calculated for the evaluation. If the total buffer level is 0, current SCell activation check shall be skipped and consider the DL buffer condition for SCell activation is not satisfied, but this decision shall NOT prevent SCell activation due to UL buffer.

In case UE SCell is deactivated permanently due to bad radio link quality according to 5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the SCell will not be included for SCell activation based on buffer evaluation. **SCells which are not deactivated permanently shall be included for SCell activation/deactivation based on buffer evaluation. Note: If all SCells are deactivated permanently, P(S)Cell will not do buffer evaluation for SCell activation.**

If NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactInPoorRf = 'Deact_Scells_VoNr_SAg' (for the PCell) and the UE is in the “TPenabled::SAG On” state as per 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), no SCell will be included for SCell activation.

For FDD + TDD FR1 UL Tx switching UE, if UE is in the “TPenabled::SAG On” state as per 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), TDD SCell with UL Tx switching will not be included for SCell activation, no matter what NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactInPoorRf is.

In case UE FR1 TDD SCell is not valid for SCell scheduling according to 5G_UP_ALG_2878_replaced([11123344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) due to measurement GAP setup, the SCell will not be included for SCell activation based on buffer evaluation while SCell shall be included for SCell activation based on buffer evaluation due to valid for SCell activation after measurement GAP release.

During transient period of SCell release according to 5G_UP_ALG_2687_replaced([11120600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the SCell with servingCellIndex will not be included for SCell activation based on buffer evaluation.

[CB010741-C]

When transient state due to SCell Upgrade is started (see [11120331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_pPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), PCell's gNB-DU shall stop evaluating DL buffer level for purpose of SCell Activation.  
When transient state due to SCell Upgrade is stopped (see [11120344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_p_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), and DL buffer level monitoring for purpose of SCell Activation was running before this transient state, PCell's gNB-DU shall re-start evaluating DL buffer level for purpose of SCell Activation. [End CB010741-C]

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-3 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Activation in DL Branch - Threshold (ID: 11121031)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11121044`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) When requested as specified by 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall calculate rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) as threshold for one or more SCell activation where K is the number of all active SCells. P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall calculate rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) for UE by taken into account CA UE’s expected throughput from P(S)Cell and all active SCell. The expected throughput shall be calculated by sum of estimatedFullBufferTbs(j) of [Before PR816804] all [End PR816804] non-GBR bearers of CA eligible(5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SA call and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NSA call) across all active carriers according to 5G_UP_ALG_4676_replaced([11192682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). (Note: for 2CC only P(S)Cell expected throughput is used for the threshold calculation).

When 2 or more SCells are configured, PCell L2-PS instance and SCell L2-PS with already activated SCell(s) shall calculate their own expected throughput.

Each of such SCell 5G-L2-PS shall send to the PCell L2-PS its expected throughput along with RLC SDU buffer level in L2-HI and RLC PDU buffer level in 5G-L2-LO.

Since PCell L2-PS may receive the RLC SDU buffer level (in L2-HI) from own PCell 5G-L2-LO and also from each of SCell L2-PS (hosted by prime-gNB or ext-gNB), PCell L2-PS shall select only one, the newest RLC SDU buffer level (in 5G-L2-HI).

Primary L2-PS of PCell shall then evaluate the total nonGbr buffer size for all non-GBR bearers of CA eligible(5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SA call and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NSA call) as the sum of the last received RLC SDU buffer level value and all RLC PDU buffer level in 5G-L2-LO instances (PCell and activated SCell(s)).

Note 1: The detailed communication between system components is described in CP3 phase of CB008140. It is proposed, that DPA (Distributed PUCCH Allocation) messages shall not be used anymore for piggybacking of expected throughput, RLC SDU buffer levels (in 5G-L2-HI) and RLC PDU buffer levels (5G-L2-LO). Nevertheless, the internal communications is left to EFS/implementation decision.

P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall apply the minimum limit for the threshold as follows:

rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) = max(rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K), (K+1)* sCellActivationMinDataThreshold)

Where:

\- rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) is the expected throughput of P(S)Cell and all current active Scells for [Before PR816804] all [End PR816804] non-GBR bearers of CA eligible(5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SA call and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NSA call). For FR1 CA up to 2CC only one TDD SCell can be supported, so the expected throughput shall be P(S)Cell expected throughput;

\- K, the number of active Scells;

\- NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellActivationMinDataThreshold according to definition in 5G_UP_ALG_2719_replaced([11121228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWtW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_2729_replaced([11121304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

Note 2: L2PS SW didn't align the unit(bits for sCellActivationMinDataThreshold to bytes) until 23R4 through PR737368.

[PR816804]

Note 3:

estimatedFullBufferTbs(j) is delivered to P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS only for the DL non-GBR CA eligible DRBs, for which some data is still buffered in P(S)Cell or active SCells 5G-L2-LO after the UE's latest scheduling in the respective serving cell. This is independent on setting of NRBTS/NRCELL-actOptimizedFlowControl. For more details see 5G_UP_ALG_4676_replaced([11192682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In the case of NRBTS/NRCELL-actOptimizedFlowControl = optimizedAllUe, this functionality can be enabled or disabled by the R&D flag rdActNoEstimatedFullBufferTbsForDrbWithNoDlData (5G_UP_ALG_33121_replaced([11124437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqq2YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In case of NRBTS/NRCELL-actOptimizedFlowControl = nonOptimized this functionality is always enabled.

[End PR816804]

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-4 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Activation in DL Branch - Execution (ID: 11121048)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11121062`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will check the activation condition by comparing the total amount of non-GBR data of CA eligible(5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SA call and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NSA call) (Note: For 3CC UEs, it includes data from all Serving Cells)waiting for initial transmission divided by the configured parameter NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellActivationLevel. If the total amount of non-GBR data awaiting for initial transmission in buffer divided by NRBTS.NRCELLs.CellActivationLevel exceeds the threshold rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K) above and the non-GBR data of CA eligible(5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SA call and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NSA call) buffered in L2-Hi exceeds the threshold rdDlCaMinNonGbrDataInL2HiThreshold (see 5G_UP_ALG_8545_replaced([11124063](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) multiplied by rlcBundleBuildupFactor in rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1 [5G_L2_1390_replaced([11184651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] consecutive checks, then there is enough data in buffer for simultaneous transmission over more SCell carriers and P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall determine the number of SCell(s) to be activated (5G_UP_ALG_2722_replaced([11121245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) followed by selection of the most appropriate SCell(s) (5G_UP_ALG_2724_replaced([11121256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). After that, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will trigger the SCell(s) activation for the CA UE.

If P(S)Cell is selected for Dummy load generation toward UE/all UEs as per 5G_UP_ALG_25972_replaced([11184088](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvP0ZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and rdEnableDummyLoadDl (5G_L2_12664_replaced([11189570](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 'true' , 5G-L2-PS of P(S)Cell shall put L2-Hi buffer equal to the value of rdDummyLoadDlBsr (5G_L2_12668_replaced([11189594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) multiplied by the number of Component Carrier in calculations above.then there is enough data in buffer for simultaneous transmission over more SCell carriers and P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall determine the number of SCell(s) to be activated (5G_UP_ALG_2722_replaced([11121245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) followed by selection of the most appropriate SCell(s) (5G_UP_ALG_2724_replaced([11121256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). After that, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will trigger the SCell(s) activation for the CA UE.

If number of Serving cells (active) is 1, rlcBundleBuildupFactor = 1, else rlcBundleBuildupFactor = number of serving cells * 1.25.

Note: It is left to implementation how the Total non-GBR data waiting for initial transmission is made available to P(S)Cell’

Rationale for dividing the amount of non-GBR data of CA eligible(5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3109_replaced([11315610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr3nbvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SA call and 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5990_replaced([11315673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr4OePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NSA call) awaiting initial transmission by the activation level is that this parameter is a configurable conservativeness such that a further SCell shall only be activated if it is estimated that the non-GBR buffer will not be drained within the next sCellActivationLevel TTIs.

In case the SCell activation of current evaluation is just after SCell deactivation according to 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS will skip the SCell activation for this evaluation.

  * rrmDlCaNonGbrBufferThres(K): is the expected throughput of P(S)Cell and all current active SCells for [Before PR816804] all [End PR816804] non-GBR bearers of CA eligible (5G_UP_ALG_14136_replaced([11121031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-5 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Evaluation of Buffer Status for SCell Activation in UL Branch (ID: 11121066)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-5.0-9**  (ID: `13422546`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13422546: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13422546: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13422546: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13422546: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13422546: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13422546: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13422546: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13422546: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) If NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is configured to ‘bufferBased’ or ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’(refer to ([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) that 5G-L2-PS shall consider ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ same as ‘bufferBased’ method), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS of the UL branch shall evaluate the CA eligible LCGs buffer data volume based on the housekeeping function (see ([11203660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) whenever requested as specified by ([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if [Before CB014067-B]a joint DL/UL [CB014067-B] at least one DL+UL [End CB014067-B] SCell is configured but not activated yet:

The buffer evaluation in UL branch is in sync with the buffer evaluation in DL branch, and they are checked once every rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 (5G_L2_1388_replaced([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) slots.

If the check condition in UL branch is met for rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1UL (see ([11124102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) consecutive checks, the request from UL branch for activating an additional SCell shall be forwarded to the DL branch, which coordinates the SCell activation (see ([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The check condition in UL branch is met if:

{

1\. 

[image-0][image_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6516.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

AND

2.

[Before CB014067-B]

[image-1][image_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6516.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]

[CB014067-B]

[image-2][image_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-03271718.png[/image_path][/image-2]

[End CB014067-B]

}

OR

The number of continuous short BSR index 31 is larger than a threshold (refer to ([11121217](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWtWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note:

  1. In the condition above, it assumes BSR is reported every periodicBSRTimer (regular and padding BSR is not considered), and if the data volume from single BSR can not be exhausted in max(rdPeriodScellCheckFR1(5G_L2_1388_replaced([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), periodicBSRTimer) period (assuming each slot can transmit sCellActivationLevelUL*eTh data), then an additional SCell shall be activated.

  2. 11 Bytes is the maximum size of the BSR MAC CE plus its subheader (refer to 5G_L2_372_replaced([11151301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24hRefvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  3. the data volume for LCG (i, k) is defined in ([11122441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). t2 is the time when buffer evaluation check happens. t1 is the latest time to t2 (t1 is before t2) where BSR is received from UE and the CA eligible **LCGs buffer data volume is updated by the BSR.**

  4. eThav is defined in ([11204528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  5. periodicBSRTimer and sCellActivationLevelUL is defined in NIDD.

  6. rdUlCaBsrSplitMinDataThreshold is defined in ([11124087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  7. The purpose to activate an additional SCell is when the data rate provided by PCell can not satisfy the CA UE data rate. But due to the fact that BSR reported from UE is not well controlled:




a) BSR periodicity can be changed by NIDD parameter: periodicBSRTimer and the value varies from sf1 to infinite (L2PS treates infinite as sf2560).

b) BSR report requires UL scheduling, if there is no UL scheduling, BSR periodicity become larger.

c) The 1st BSR report depends on the time between data arrived in UE and the SR opportunity UE can use. The larger value of SR periodicity, the more likely UE sends big BSR at the beginning because UE accumulated big buffer until SR is trigger. Therefore in SCell activation test, it suggests to use the smallest value (slots20) for NIDD:srPeriodicity. But smaller value of srPeriodicity will reduce the cell capacity for RRC connected UE, so it does not suggest to change this parameter in the filed, instead operator can activate feature 5GC002271, so that minSrPeriod will be used when min number of RRC connected users is in the cell.

d) How UE reports BSR is vendor specific.

e) BSR report from UE is an index with upper limit, not a exact value, gNB always uses the upper limit, so that gNB may see higher data rate.

f) For short BSR, the index 31 means buffer size larger than 150000 bytes, gNB treats index 31 as 85000000 bytes (big enough) in order to achieve max UL throughput in some scenarios. The drawback is that if operator set NIDD:periodicBSRTimer to a larger value, e.g. sf1280, and UE will report BSR index 31 even data rate is small, then SCell will be activated. However, if NRBTS.NRCELL.actShortBsrLimitAdaptation = true, gNB treats index 31 according to ([11203806](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwg_wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

[CB014067-B]

8\. numActiveSCellDLUL is a number of active DL+UL SCells.

[End CB014067-B]

Due to above reason, the recommended value for NIDD:periodicBSRTimer is the default value sf10, if operator set this parameter to a larger value, e.g. sf40 or even larger, then SCell may be activated even when user data rate does not reach the maximum data rate provided by PCell. And an activated SCell can not be deactivated even when user data rate become small.

In case UE FR1 TDD SCell is not valid for SCell scheduling according to ([11123344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) due to measurement GAP setup, the SCell will not be included for SCell activation based on buffer evaluation while SCell shall be included for SCell activation based on buffer evaluation due to valid for SCell activation after measurement GAP release.

If UE capability does not support lch-ToSCellRestriction, when first VoNR bearer is setup for this UE, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS of the UL branch shall stop to evaluate the UE’s CA eligible **LCGs buffer data volume. After the last VoNR bearer is released, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS of the UL branch shall start to evaluate the UE’s** CA eligible LCGs buffer data volume.****

In case UE SCell is deactivated permanently due to bad radio link quality according to ([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the SCell will not be included for SCell activation based on buffer evaluation.

If any one of activated SCells (no matter DL only SCell or joint DL/UL SCell) is in overheating status according to ([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), UL 5G-L2-PS shall not evaluate the buffer status for SCell activation. When overheating SCell (according to ([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is released or changed or swapped, its corresponding overheating status shall be removed in PCell.

During transient period of SCell release according to ([11120600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the SCell with servingCellIndex will not be included for SCell activation based on buffer evaluation in uplink.

If the prohibit timer rdProhibitBufEvalULFR1 ([11124165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is running according to ([11121204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWtVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PCell shall not evaluate uplink buffer status. After prohibit timer rdProhibitBufEvalULFR1 ([11124165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is expired, PCell shall start to evaluate uplink buffer status.

If UEOverheated=True and _MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL is smaller than or equal to_ NumofActSCellsUL according to ([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PCell shall not evaluate uplink buffer status.**

If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to FALSE, OR (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND 5QI1 DRB is not configured for the UE)

  * For FDD + TDD FR1 R15 UL CA UE or inter-band FDD + FDD UL CA UE or (inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE with PPowerClass,PCell for TDD PCell equal to or less than PPowerClass,CA), in case transform precoder is enabled according to ([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) on PCell and [image-4][image_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6516.004.png[/image_path][/image-4] is equal to [image-5][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6516.005.png[/image_path][/image-5], UL 5G-L2-PS shall not evaluate the buffer status for SCell activation.



Else if (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND 5QI1 DRB is configured for the UE)

PCell UL 5G-L2-PS does not trigger SCell deactivation directly if the UE’s transmission buffer become smaller, instead PCell UL 5G-L2-PS triggers stopping BSR split if the condition is met, see ([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (formula 2 [CB014067-B] for 2CC UL CA or Formula_3CC_4 or Formula_3CC_5 for 3CC UL CA [End CB014067-B]). Then inactivity timer based SCell deactivation is performed according to ([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-6 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Prohibit timer for uplink buffer status evaluation (ID: 11121204)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11121212`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) If SCell uplink enter bad RLQ status, SCell can be deactivated due to following reasons:

  1. Both downlink and uplink inactivity timers are expired (note 1 and 2), SCell shall be deactivated due to inactivity timer expiration.

  2. SCell is selected to be deactivated due to UE overheating assistance information according to 5G_UP_ALG_2826_replaced([11121946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  3. SCell is deactivated permanently due to downlink bad RLQ according to 5G_UP_ALG_2774_replaced([11121607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




For reason 1 and reason 2, PCell shall record the uplink RLQ status of SCell before deactivation, if the SCell has rrmScellRLQStatusUL = "bad" [CB006137-C] or SCell is in pause state due to NACK flood according to 5G_UP_ALG_3158_replaced([11138143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krdglfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB006137-C], PCell shall start to evaluate uplink buffer status (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9698_replaced([11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only after a prohibit timer expired. The prohibit timer is specified by the R&D parameter rdProhibitBufEvalULFR1 [5G_UP_ALG_12693_replaced([11124165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]. The rationale for this prohibit timer is to avoid frequent ping-pong between SCell activation due to uplink buffer request  SCell enter UL bad RLQ  SCell deactivation due to inactivity timer expiration  SCell activation due to uplink buffer request again.

For reason 3, this SCell shall never be activated again, therefore uplink buffer status evaluation will never start again.

Note:

  1. SCell downlink inactivity timer expiration requires below conditions:

  2. SCell downlink RLQ is good; otherwise if SCell downlink RLQ is bad, the DL inactivity timer is stopped according to 5G_UP_ALG_2767_replaced([11121583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  3. L2-Hi stop data split to SCell due to any reason, e.g. low buffer, large delay in SCell downlink transmission.

  4. SCell is not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), otherwise both downlink and uplink inactivity timers are stopped.




-rrmScellRLQStatusUL: SCell uplink radio link quality for active joint DL/UL SCell (5G_UP_ALG_11868_replaced([11121619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-7 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Handling of continuous short BSR index 31 (ID: 11121217)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11121224`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) When NRCELL.actShortBsrLimitAdaptation = true:

UL 5G-L2-PS shall count the number of continuous short BSR index 31, if it's larger than a threshold, then the condition of SCell activation in UL branch (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9698_replaced([11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the condition of transmission buffer split (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9496_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is treated as satisfied.

Short BSR index 31 may come from any [Before CB009059-BB]non-GBR [CB009059-BB] CA eligible [End CB009059-BB] LCG and may come from either PCell or SCell. Number of continuous short BSR index 31 is reset to 0 if any short BSR index other than 31 or long BSR is received which does not satisify the formula 1 of Condition of Transmission Buffer Split (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9496_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The threshold is defined as ceil(rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1UL * rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 / 2^u / periodicBSRTimer * sCellActivationLevelUL)

rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1UL is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_10051_replaced([11124102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 is defined in 5G_L2_1388_replaced([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

periodicBSRTimer and sCellActivationLevelUL is defined in NIDD.

Rationale: If NRCELL.actShortBsrLimitAdaptation = true, when short BSR of bufferSizeIndex = 31 is received, buffer size is computed by UL 5G-L2-PS according to 5G_UP_ALG_5131_replaced([11203806](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwg_wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), but the calculated value may not be enough for UL SCell activation and buffer split when sCellActivationLevelUL is larger than 1.

actShortBsrLimitAdaptation: NRBTS.NRCELL.actShortBsrLimitAdaptation

sCellActivationLevelUL: NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellActivationLevelUL

periodicBSRTimer: NRBTS.periodicBSRTimer

[CB009059-BB]

CA eligible DRB refers to 5G_UP_10576_replaced([11358417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uchs1_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB009059-BB]

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-8 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) *Minimum Threshold Definition for SCell Activation in DL Branch (ID: 11121228)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11121231`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) To avoid the activation of Scell when low UE expected throughput at data switch mode or division for very small buffer split at split mode which will cause small TBS with low efficiency due to MAC header overheads, 5G-L2-PS define the minimum threshold for activating N Scells based on configuration parameter of NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellActivationMinDataThreshold (see 5G_UP_ALG_15995_replaced([11124273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (default: 6000 bits) *N. The lower value will provide more aggressive behavior for Scell activation which will lead small TBS over one carrier, the higher value will provide more conservative behavior for Scell activation.

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-9 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Excluding SCells with high load status from SCell activation candidate list (ID: 11121235)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11121241`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Each time PCell 5G-L2-PS need to select SCells for activation, PCell 5G-L2-PS shall exclude those SCells whose scellLoadStateForActivation flag in database is high load (5G_UP_ALG_2683_replaced([11120559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR03PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from the SCell activation candidate list. **[CB014088-F] If there are still candidate SCells available then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell shall perform the checks specified in 5G_UP_ALG_31930_replaced([11122209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL branch and 5G_UP_ALG_31931_replaced([11122218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL branch and 5G_UP_ALG_31958_replaced([11122225](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and the final number **of candidate SCells for activation shall depend on the outcome from these checks. **Note: The above overload check is applicable for only Buffer based SCell activation method.**[End CB014088-F]**_*_** *

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-10 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Determination of number of SCells to be activated (ID: 11121245)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-10.0-3**  (ID: `13423966`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) When evaluation of DL or UL buffer status requests for SCell Activation ([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall firstly exclude SCells with high load status according to ([11121235](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWtXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and if there are still candidate SCells available, then P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall determine the number of configured SCells to be activated as follows:

Step 0: Initilize NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate and NumSCellsRemainToActivate to 0.

Step 1: If SCell activation request coming from UL branch or from both UL branch and DL branch, PCell DL L2-PS set number of joint DL/UL SCell (NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate) as per the following:

[Before CB014067-B]

if the check defined for overload for DL branch and for UL branch, passes then,

Joint DL/UL SCell is selected

Set NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate = 1

else

NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate = 0

[CB014067-B]

  * gNB-DU shall exclude those DL+UL SCells that are overloaded based on the checks defined for overload for DL branch and for UL branch and still there are configured SCells not yet activated, then proceeds to the next steps mentioned below.



if at least one DL+UL SCell is available for activation

if none of configured SCells is active

NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate = min (numInitialSCellsToActivate，numAvaliableSCellsDLULForActivation);

else

NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate = 1;

else

NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate = 0;

where:  
\- numAvaliableSCellsDLULForActivation: the number of inactive DL+UL SCells, which pass the overload check for DL and UL branches.

\- numInitialSCellsToActivate: initial number of SCells to be jointly activated when no configured SCell is active; this number is set by NRCELL.iniNumSCellsToActivate

[End CB014067-B]

If UEOverheated=True according to ([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate = min {NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate, max(0, MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL - NumofActSCellsUL), max(0, MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL - NumofActSCellsDL)}

Step 2: After Step 1, if SCell activation request coming from DL branch or from both UL branch and DL branch, PCell DL L2-PS decides the number of remaining candidates NumSCellsRemainToActivate as:

  * gNB-DU shall exclude those SCells that are overloaded based on the checks defined for overload for DL branch and still there are configured SCells not yet activated, then proceeds to the next steps mentioned below.
  * If none of configured SCells is active: [Before CB014067-B]NumSCellsRemainToActivate = max (0, iniNumSCellsToActivate - NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate).[CB014067-B] NumSCellsRemainToActivate = max (0, numInitialSCellsToActivate - NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate). [End CB014067-B]
  * If at least one of configured SCells is active: NumSCellsRemainToActivate = max (0, 1 - NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate).



If UEOverheated=True according to ([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), NumSCellsRemainToActivate = min {NumSCellsRemainToActivate, max(0, MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL - NumofActSCellsDL)}

After step1 and step2, the number of configured SCells to be activated = NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate + NumSCellsRemainToActivate.

Note:   
[Before CB014067-B]

  1. NIDD parameter iniNumSCellsToActivate only works when the SCell activation request comes from PCell DL L2-PS branch (see ([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), but it does not works when the SCell activation request comes from PCell UL L2-PS branch (see ([11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) because currently there is at most one SCell with UL.  
[End CB014067-B]

  2. If iniNumSCellsToActivate is greater than number of SCells Configured or iniNumSCellsToActivate=0, then set iniNumSCellsToActivate as number of SCells Configured (it means all SCells to be activated in single step).

  3. If at least one of configured SCells is active, further SCell Activation shall be executed in step-wise manner with step size of 1 SCell.

  4. If a SCell has high load status in DL, it's also excluded from SCell activation even if the SCell activation request coming from UL branch.

  5. SCells which are permanently deactivated according to ([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall not considered for determining number of SCells to be activated.

  6. NumofActSCellsDL, MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL and NumofActSCellsUL, MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL are defined in ([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




**iniNumSCellsToActivate: NRBTS.NRCELL.iniNumSCellsToActivate**

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-11 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) SCell Selection for SCell Activation (ID: 11121256)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-11.0-5**  (ID: `13424163`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Step 1: If NumSCellsJointDLULToActivate determined in ([11121245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is [Before CB014067-B] 1 [CB014067-B] greater than 0 [End CB014067-B]:

[Before CB014067-B]Joint DL/UL SCell is selected.[CB014067-B] the corresponding number of DL+UL SCells shall be selected according to the following priority:

a) The DL+UL SCell with highest metric of {SCell's Available UL Resources (AUR) * BWPratio} shall be selected.

b) The tie-break: SCell index (the smallest index selected)

where:

AUR calculation follows [13388195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QW2dJAKoEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9),

BWPratio - see the description below

[End CB014067-B]

Step 2: If NumSCellsRemainToActivate determined in ([11121245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is larger than 0:

When evaluation of DL buffer status requests an SCell Activation ([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the number of SCells NumSCellsRemainToActivate to be activated is determined according to ([11121245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the SCells shall be sorted and selected according to the following criteria, if UEOverheated=True according to ([11121931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and activating the selected SCell will cause number of activated DL SCell exceed MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL or number of activated UL SCell exceed MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL, then this SCell is skipped for activation and try next candidate:

If (All SCells in the SCell activation candidate list ([11121235](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWtXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) have available inference response ([11229878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyq70vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) // AI/ML based SCell selection algorithm is applied

{

a) The SCell with highest metric of {Available DL Resource (ADR) * SE * BWPratio},

}

Else //legacy algorithm is applied

{

a) The SCell with highest metric of {SCell's Available DL Resource (ADR) * BWPratio} shall be selected.

}

b) 1st tie-break normPrbSizeDl (the highest value selected)

c) 2nd tie-break SCell index (the smallest index selected)

Where:

SE value is from ([11229867](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyq70PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

ADR calculation follows ([11121273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

BWPratio is calculated as below:

If dedicated BWPs are non-aligned (CB012299) without PRB blanking and when normal or limited bandwidth modes is active( [12657028: Normal and limited bandwidth modes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SuX0YEg7EfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) :

BWPratio = 0.5 (50%)

Rationale:

For this case CA UEs are always scheduled only in the dedicated small BWP which corresponds to limited bandwidth mode.

else

BWPratio = SCell_BW_of_dedicated_BWP_configured_currently_for_UE / SCell_BW_of_largest_dedicated_BWP,

Rationale: selection the best of configured SCells to be activated is driven by the following assumptions:

1) the more available SCell’s PDSCH resources the better SCell,

2) there is enough SCell’s PDCCH resources to serve at least one additional UE i.e. the PDCCH load is below threshold controlled by R&D parameter rdPdcchLoadThr (5G_L2_2971_replaced([11184477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27rTKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))); if the PDCCH load exceeds rdPdcchLoadThr penalty for ADR is applied,

3) using BWPratio scaling factor is simplified workaround to support multiple BWPs in the SCell, which assumes that the load in the SCell is equally distributed over the largest BWP and smaller BWPs, which may not be true in some cases, thus the final ADR for small BWP may be not precise. For precise result of each BWP, ADR needed to be calculated in the SCell per each BWP separately and transmitted together to the PCell which would require modification in the SCell to PCell interface. To avoid interface change simplified solution is chosen for PR810498 fix,

Note:

If Joint DL/UL SCell is not selected in Step 1, then it can be selected in Step 2 together with DL only SCell if the check defined in ([11122218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) passes, according to the sorted criteria.

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-12 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) ADR calculation for an SCell (ID: 11121273)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11121278`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) The **Available DL Resources (ADR) of an SCell is calculated as follows:**

if _pdcchLoad < _rdPdcchLoadThr**

ADR = (1 - _pdschLoad) *_ normPrbSizeDl**

else

ADR = (1 - _pdschLoad) *_ normPrbSizeDl ** (1 - _pdcchLoad) / (1-_ rdPdcchLoadThr)*****

where:

\-  _pdschLoad and pdcchLoad is as per 5G_UP_ALG_2727_replaced([11121281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._

\-  _normPrbSizeDl is normalized PRB number calculated among a slot pattern, considering different numerologies, DL/UL ratio, PRB blanking._

It’s calculated by summation of PRB number of every slot, and then divided by rrmSlotPatternLength, and then multiply by 2^µ.

For DL slot, **[Before CB008917-D] the PRB number is full bandwidth PRB.**[CB008917-D] the PRB number is largest dedicated BWP size. **[End CB008917-D]** ****

For Special slot, **[Before CB008917-D] the PRB number is full bandwidth PRB if it can be used for PDSCH; otherwise 0.**[CB008917-D] the PRB number is largest dedicated BWP size if it can be used for PDSCH; otherwise 0. **[End CB008917-D]** ****

For UL slot, the PRB number is 0.

For SSB slot, the PRB number is numPdschPrbInSsbSlots (if actPdschAtSsbSlots is false; numPdschPrbInSsbSlots=0).

For TRS slot, the PRB number is numPdschPrbInTrsSlots (if actPdschRmCsirsForTracking is false; numPdschPrbInTrsSlots=0).

For SSB and TRS slot, the PRB number is min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots, numPdschPrbInTrsSlots).

If actPRBBlanking is true:

subtract (NIDD: nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL + nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL) from the PRB number calculated above with minimum value 0. Note: this is for easy implementation, it does not reflect the real number of PRB in scheduling.

\-  _rdPdcchLoadThr (default = 0.8) is an R &D parameter defining the threshold for the load on PDCCH (see 5G_L2_2971_replaced([11184477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27rTKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), above which the SCell with high PDCCH load gets a penalty reducing the ADR_

Each of 5G-L2-PS instance of configured SCells shall send to PCell 5G-L2-PS its _ADR._

Note: In future development, when multiple DL BWPs are implemented, the SCell selection algorithm may be enhanced.

Note: Currently, only one Dedicated BWP is supported and its size is always set to total channel bandwidth. In future, if more Dedicated BWPs are supported, this value could be less than size of the channel BW.

Note: All SCells shall calculate this irrespective of if the cell is DSS or not.

Note: in calculation of _normPrbSizeDl, different symbol length in each slot is not considered for simplicity._

**rrmSlotPatternLength: The period of rrmSlotPattern is rrmSlotPatternLength (see 5G_UP_ALG_3808_replaced([11166365](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktkZb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

**actPdschAtSsbSlots: NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschAtSsbSlots**

**actPdschRmCsirsForTracking: NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschRmCsirsForTracking**

**actPRBBlanking: NRBTS.NRCELL.actPRBBlanking**

**nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL: NRBTS.NRCELL.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL**

**nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL: NRBTS.NRCELL.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL**

**numPdschPrbInSsbSlots: defined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2040_replaced([11277571](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpN8BfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**

**numPdschPrbInTrsSlots: defined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2041_replaced([11277590](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpN8B_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-13 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) AUR calculation for an SCell (ID: 13388195)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `13388196`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) The **Available UL Resources (AUR) of an DL+UL SCell is calculated as follows:**

if _pdcchLoad <= _rdPdcchLoadThr / 100**

AUR = (1 - _puschLoad) *_ normPrbSizeUl**

else

AUR = (1 - _puschLoad) *_ normPrbSizeUl ** (1 - _pdcchLoad) / [1- (_ rdPdcchLoadThr / 100)]*****

where:

\-  _pdcchLoad is calculated as per[11121281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)._

\-  _puschLoad is calculated as per[13421342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kRQ0pBfGEfGFMKAOrP5qqw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)._

\-  _normPrbSizeUl is normalized PRB number calculated among a slot pattern, considering different numerologies, DL/UL ratio, PRB blanking._

It’s calculated by summation of PRB number of every slot, and then divided by rrmSlotPatternLength, and then multiply by 2^µ.

In case of TDD DL+UL SCell:

For UL slot, the PRB number is the largest dedicated BWP size.

For Special slot, the PRB number is the largest dedicated BWP size if it can be used for PUSCH; otherwise 0.

For DL slot, the PRB number is 0.

_normPrbSizeUl_ = max { [Sum(PRBs usable for PUSCH per slot within rrmSlotPattern) / rrmSlotPatternLength] * 2^µ - nbrOfBlankedPRBs , 0},**

where:

nbrOfBlankedPRBs = nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL + nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL, if actPRBBlanking is true;

nbrOfBlankedPRBs = 0, if actPRBBlanking is false;

Note: this is for easy implementation, it does not reflect the real number of PRB in scheduling.

\-  _rdPdcchLoadThr is an EFS R &D parameter defining the threshold for the load on PDCCH ([11184477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27rTKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), above which the DL+UL SCell with high PDCCH load gets a penalty reducing the AUR._

Each of 5G-L2-PS instance of configured DL+UL SCells shall send to PCell 5G-L2-PS its _AUR.  
Note 1: It is proposed that the SCell provide PCell with the AUR in the same way as implemented for ADR ([11121273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) delivery. That is, the AUR value may be piggybacked on messages exchanged by Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA) algorithm. The communication between 5G-L2-PS instances (SCell to PCell) shall be specified in EFS._

Note 2: in calculation of _normPrbSizeUl, different symbol length in each slot is not considered for simplicity._

_rdPdcchLoadThr: EFS R &D parameter defining the threshold for the load on PDCCH ([11184477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27rTKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))_

rrmSlotPattern: The slot pattern (see [11166365](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktkZb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**rrmSlotPatternLength: The period of rrmSlotPattern is rrmSlotPatternLength (see[11166365](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktkZb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**

**actPRBBlanking: NRBTS.NRCELL.actPRBBlanking**

**nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL: NRBTS.NRCELL.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL**

**nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL: NRBTS.NRCELL.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL**

µ: numerology index (see 38.211. section 4.2)

---
