Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Each Serving Cell (having atleast one FR1 CA UE) irrespective of if the cell is DSS or not shall calculate \-  _pdschLoad is an average load on PDSCH * based on [image-0][image_desc]The image is entirely black. There is no discernible content, text, or patterns within the image.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6539.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] (for detailed description see below)._**_-_ pdcchLoad = _Nbr_CCE_used_DL /_ Nbr_CCE_avail_DL, which is a load on PDCCH (see below)**_Note: The communication between 5G-L2-PS instances (SCell to P(S)Cell) shall be specified in CP3 phase. It is proposed that above mentioned pdschLoad and pdcchLoad values may be piggybacked together with messages exchanged by Distributed PUCCH Allocation algorithm.__pdschLoad_ _The calculation of the estimated average load is as follows: The instantaneous load at time, i.e. radio frame, t is defined as_ L _NR__ used (t) = number of PRBs assigned by L2-PS for NR PDSCH at time instant t** __ L _NR__ avail (t) = number of PRBs available for L2-PS for NR PDSCH at time instant t** __ L _NR (t) =_ L _NR__ used (t) / _L_ NR__avail (t)_**_*_** The PRBs shall be weighted equally, not taking into account the number of PDSCH symbols in different slots. Slots with SSB and CSI-RS are not available for PDSCH. Radio frames without any PDSCH available shall be skipped. _L_ NR shall be calculated per radio frame allocated to NR and per cell, and used as input to an exponential filter with a time constant _T_ LNR for averaging:**_* [image-1][image_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6539.002.png[/image_path][/image-1](2) The averaging time constant _T _LNR should be given by a R &D parameter _rdLoadBalancingAvgConst (5G_L2_1310_replaced([11182174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27ZmVfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with a range of 1, 2, …, 10000, default 250.**___pdcchLoad_ _then L2-PS shall count *_ Nbr_CCE_avail_DL: number of CCEs available for downlink scheduling _*_ Nbr_CCE_used_DL: the number of CCEs used for downlink scheduling in the common search space _*_ Nbr_CCE_avail_UL: the number of CCEs available for uplink scheduling _*_ Nbr_CCE_used_UL: the number of CCEs used for uplink scheduling in both common and dedicated search space _Only slots available for NR and including PDCCH shall be considered. If dedicated BWPs are non-aligned (CB012299) without PRB blanking and when limited bandwidth modes is active ([12657028: Normal and limited bandwidth modes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SuX0YEg7EfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) : loads calculated for SCell Activation shall be additionally corrected pdschload = min(pdschload + rdPdschLoadCorrection,1) pdcchload = min(pdcchload + rdPdcchLoadCorrection,1) where rdPdschLoadCorrection and rdPdcchLoadCorrection (default values: 50%) are compensations controlled via r&d params defined in: [12722875: rdPdschLoadCorrection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SHv_8W3wEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [12722984: rdPdcchLoadCorrection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D_EjIW3yEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) respectively, as for this case (CB012299) CA UEs are always scheduled only in the dedicated small BWP which size is the half of the size of the largest BWP. __Note1: Usage of PDCCH for SIB, SI messages, paging is considered as downlink scheduling as well_ ___Note2: Values may be counted by DL or UL scheduler, but are send to CRM by L2-PS DL_ ___Note3: Separation of CCEs for DL and UL are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).____Note3: If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/lteNrDssMode > 1, When PRB sharing in slot 0/5/9 (rrmLteDLPrbSharing=TRUE,([11172097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) __[CB007372-M] and NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss=false_ _[End CB007372-M] number of CCEs available shall be adjusted to consider only CCE assigned to NR in slots 5/9 according to values received in EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST Slot 0 if assigned to NR is fully availlabled for NR therefore this restriction doesn't apply for it. __[CB007372-H] Note4: If NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss=true the PDCCH load for the Load Calculation for SCell Activation shall be calculated like for the legacy non DSS FDD cells. PDCCH load for DSS shall be calculated according to the[11172370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuLdgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). __[End CB007372-H]_**_*_** **

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-15 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) UL Load Calculation for DL+UL SCell Activation**** (ID: 13421342)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `13421343`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) 13421343: Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Each DL+UL SCell (serving at least one FR1 UL CA UE) shall calculate: \-  _puschLoad is an average load on PUSCH * based on [image-0][image_desc]$\overline{L_{N H}(t)}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6539.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] (for detailed description see below)._**__ *puschLoad** Note: puschLoad metric re-uses the mechanism implemented for evaluating of pdschLoad ([11121281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). The calculation of the estimated average load is as follows: The instantaneous UL load of DL+UL SCell is calculated as a sum of PUSCH PRBs for all UL slot during the whole DPA Measurement Processing Cycle ([11123510](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). The duration of the Measurement Processing Cycle defines the time period 't', over which the following load values are defined: _L_ NR__used (t) = number of PRBs assigned by 5G-L2-PS for NR PUSCH at time instant t_**_L _NR__ avail (t) = number of PRBs available for 5G-L2-PS for NR PUSCH at time instant t_** _L_ NR (t) =  _L_ NR__used (t) /_ L _NR__ avail (t)**_*_**_The PRBs shall be weighted equally, without taking into account the number of PUSCH symbols in different slots. PRBs used for PRACH and PUCCH are not available for PUSCH. Radio frames with no PUSCH resources available shall be skipped._ L _NR shall be calculated per radio frame, and used as input to an exponential filter with a time constant_ T _LNR for averaging:_**_[image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation and an initial condition._ *Equation:** $\overline{L_{NR}}(t) = \frac{1}{T_{LNR}} L_{NR}(t) + \left(1 - \frac{1}{T_{LNR}}\right) \overline{L_{NR}}(t_{previous})$ **Initial Condition:** $L_{NR}(0) = 0$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6539.002.png[/image_path][/image-1](2) The averaging time constant _T_ LNR is given by an EFS R&D parameter _rdLoadBalancingAvgConst_ _([11182174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27ZmVfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._**** If dedicated BWPs are non-aligned (CB012299) without PRB blanking and when limited bandwidth mode is active ([12657028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SuX0YEg7EfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), puschLoad calculated for DL+UL SCell Activation shall be additionally corrected as follows: puschLoad = min(puschLoad + rdPuschLoadCorrection,1) where: \- rdPuschLoadCorrection is a compensation factor defined in [13421355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CBpXYRfLEfGFMKAOrP5qqw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). Rationale: This correction applies because, when CB012299 is enabled and the conditions in the if statement above are met, CA UEs are always scheduled only within the dedicated small BWP, whose size is half the size of the largest BWP.

**3.7.2.3.1.0-16.0-1**  (ID: `11121308`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) If NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellActivationLevel or NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellActivationMinDataThreshold is changed during cell reconfiguration procedure and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is still set to ‘bufferBased’, 5G-L2-PS (P(S)Cell) will keep current value to evaluate the buffer status for Scell activation according to 5G_UP_ALG_2715_replaced([11120998](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and start to use the new value at next evaluation period according to 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**3.7.2.3.1.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11121317`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) If NRBTS.NRCELL.iniNumSCellsToActivate is changed during cell reconfiguration procedure and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is still set to ‘bufferBased’ or ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’, 5G-L2-PS (P(S)Cell) will apply the new value while determining the number of SCells to be activated according to 5G_UP_ALG_2722_replaced([11121245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-18 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Scell Deactivation based on Scell Inactivity Timer (ID: 11121319)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-18.0-3**  (ID: `11121332`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) In case configuration parameter sCellDeactivationTimerGNB don't equal to 'infinity', SCell 5G-L2-PS shall monitor the CA UE's activity, which is done based on the SCell inactivity timer per UE per each active SCell. If absence of data scheduling over SCell for the CA UE during the period of SCell inactivity timer, then SCell will indicate the result to P(S)Cell and P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will trigger the SCell deactivation.

For DL only SCell:

  * Once SCell state is in active state according to 5G_UP_ALG_2804_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), SCell DL 5G-L2-PS will start the timer of sCellDeactivationTimerGNB for the CA UE over current SCell.
  * SCell DL 5G-L2-PS will stop the timer of sCellDeactivationTimerGNB for the CA UE over current SCell each time buffer status indication to indicates a buffer utilization(bufferedBytes) greater than 0 for non-GBR bearers according to 5G_UP_ALG_4561_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when sCellDeactivationTimerGNB is running.
  * SCell DL 5G-L2-PS will start the timer of sCellDeactivationTimerGNB once the buffer level(bufferedBytes) reaches 0 for non-GBR bearers when sCellDeactivationTimerGNB is not running.
  * When the inactivity timer expired, [CNI-101738]If UE is not selected for dummy load or rdEnableDummyLoadDl (5G_L2_12664_replaced([11189570](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 'false' as per 5G_UP_ALG_25972_replaced([11184088](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvP0ZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CNI-101738] SCell DL 5G-L2-PS will send indication of SCell deactivation to P(S)Cell.



For joint DL/UL SCell:

  * SCell DL 5G-L2-PS and SCell UL 5G-L2-PS maintains the inactivity timer separately, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS works as a master and collects the inactivity timer status from SCell UL 5G-L2-PS. When inactivity timer expired in both sides, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS will send SCell deactivation indication to P(S)Cell.
  * Once SCell state is in active state according to 5G_UP_ALG_2804_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), SCell DL 5G-L2-PS and SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will start the timer of sCellDeactivationTimerGNB separately in downlink branch and uplink branch.
  * The start and stop of inactivity timer in downlink branch are the same as DL only SCell.
  * The start and stop of inactivity timer in uplink branch are as follow:



When timer is running, SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will stop the timer each time BSR split from PCell UL 5G-L2-PS indicates a buffer size greater than 0 for CA eligible LCGs according to 5G_UP_ALG_9496_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When timer is not running, SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will start the timer each time BSR split from PCell UL 5G-L2-PS indicates a 0 split for all CA eligible LCGs or once the uplink housekeeping buffer data rrmBufferedDataUlTotal_bytes become 0 according to 5G_UP_ALG_5118_replaced([11203660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * When timer is expired in uplink branch, SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will notify the uplink inactivity timer expiration to SCell DL 5G-L2-PS; after that if SCell UL 5G-L2-PS received non-zero data split again, SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will cancel the uplink inactivity timer expiration to SCell DL 5G-L2-PS.
  * In case SCell DL 5G-L2-PS received the uplink inactivity timer expiration, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS checks whether downlink inactivity timer is expired or not: if yes, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS sends indication of SCell deactivation to P(S)Cell; if no, SCell DL 5G-L2-PS wait for downlink inactivity timer expiration.



In case P(S)Cell received the indication of SCell deactivation due to inactivity timer expires, P(S)Cell will trigger the SCell deactivation by sending MAC-CE to UE to deactivate the SCell [CNI-101738]If UE is not selected for dummy load over this SCell or rdEnableDummyLoadDl (5G_L2_12664_replaced([11189570](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 'false' as per 5G_UP_ALG_25972_replaced([11184088](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvP0ZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CNI-101738]. During transient period of SCell release for the SCell with servingCellIndex according to 5G_UP_ALG_2687_replaced([11120600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will ignore the indication of SCell deactivation due to inactivity timer expires and will not trigger the MAC-CE to UE.

If SCell is in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall stop the inactivity timer for the SCell in downlink and in uplink (for joint DL/UL SCell), and start the inactivity timer once UE is recovered from the SCell overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) unless UE was in bad radio condition before beginning of overheating.

5G-L2-PS(SCell) shall keep the inactivity timer(sCellDeactivationTimerGNB) running in both DL and UL scheduler during DRX inactive period. Note: refer to 5G_UP_1346_replaced([11358134](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucgesPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the concept of DRX cycle together with inactivity timer.

SCell deactivation is indicated from SCell DL 5G-L2-PS to PCell DL 5G-L2-PS, while uplink BSR is split by PCell UL 5G-L2-PS to SCell UL 5G-L2-PS. It may happen that above two procedures happen at the same time, it's left to CP3 how to handle such corner case.

In downlink, for SCell channel quality is 'bad', 5G-L2-PS(SCell) shall stop the inactivity timer and restart the inactivity timer when channel quality is changed from 'bad' to 'good'.

In uplink, for SCell channel quality is changed from 'good' to 'bad', 5G-L2-PS(SCell) shall start the inactivity timer if no buffer is split; and stop the inactivity timer when channel quality is changed from 'bad' to 'good' if buffer is split again.

Rationale: CQI measurements are only available when the SCell is activated so this approach allows the 5G-L2-PS(SCell) to detect an improvement in SCell channel conditions (e.g. from bad to good). The cost of this solution is increased UE battery consumption.

sCellDeactivationTimerGNB: NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB

CA eligible DRB refers to 5G_UP_10576_replaced([11358417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uchs1_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.7.2.3.1.0-19 Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) Reconfiguration of Scell Inactivity Timer for Scell Deactivation (ID: 11121337)

**3.7.2.3.1.0-19.0-1**  (ID: `11121340`)

Buffer Based Scell Activation/Deactivation (FR1 CA) In case Scell inactivity timer - sCellDeactivationTimerGNB is reconfigured during SCell reconfiguration procedure, SCell 5G-L2-PS shall consider the following scenarios. Note: based on the discussion, 5G-L2-PS will use Scell configured inactivity timer for CA UE Scell deactivation.

Case 1: sCellDeactivationTimerGNB from 'infinity' to actual value

5G-L2-PS will update the CA UE context with new inactivity timer and start the inactivity timer for all CA UEs per each activated Scell.

Case 2: sCellDeactivationTimerGNB from actual value to 'infinity'

5G-L2-PS will update the UE context with new inactivity timer to 'infinity' and stop all the inactivity timer for all CA UEs.

Case 3: sCellDeactivationTimerGNB from one value to another value

5G-L2-PS will update the UE context with new inactivity timer and keep all current running inactivity timer, and use the new timer value at next timer startup.

sCellDeactivationTimerGNB: NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB

---

##### 3.7.2.4 Radio Link Quality based SCell Activation/Deactivation

###### 3.7.2.4.0-1 Radio Link Quality based SCell Activation/Deactivation Radio Link Quality based SCell Activation/Deactivation - Overview (ID: 11121363)

**3.7.2.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11121368`)

Radio Link Quality based SCell Activation/Deactivation Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2745_replaced([11121442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYijfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Buffer and Radio Link Quality Based SCell Activation/Deactivation for FR2 CA.

Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2763_replaced([11121567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Radio Link Quality Based SCell Deactivation for FR1 CA [CB006137-BB] in downlink.

Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_11867_replaced([11121616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Radio Link Quality Based SCell Suspending for FR1 CA in uplink [End CB006137-BB].

If UE is configured with the 64QAM MCS table, the value specified by the parameters above are used directly in the decision (see 5G_UP_ALG_2745_replaced([11121442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYijfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for FR2 CA; see 5G_UP_ALG_2763_replaced([11121567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for FR1 CA).

if UE is configured with 256QAM MCS table [PR865446] or 1024QAM MCS table [End PR865446], the values set by the parameters shall be mapped according to the table below to get the values that are actually used in the decision.

Mapping between MCS threshold for 64QAM and the MCS threshold for 256QAM is obtained from MCS Index tables in 38.214 chapter 5.1.3.1 in such a way that mapped DL MCS from table 2 have the same Spectral efficiency as the MCS in table 1. Remaining MCSs from the table 1 (with Spectral efficiency not used in table 2) are mapped to the same MCS in table 2 as the higher MCS in table 1 that is mapped to the MCS in table 2. Remaining MCSs from the table 1 (with Spectral efficiency not used in table 4) are mapped to the same MCS in table 4 as the higher MCS in table 4 that is mapped to the MCS in table 4. [End PR865446]

The tables list various Modulation Coding Scheme (MCS) indices, their corresponding modulation orders, target code rates, and spectral efficiencies. The MCS indices range from 0 to 31 in both tables. ###### 3.7.2.4.1.0-3 MCS mapping between 64QAM and 256QAM and 64QAM LowSE MCS threshold for RLQ based SCell deactivation in UL (ID: 11121423)

**3.7.2.4.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11121436`)

MCS mapping between 64QAM and 256QAM and 64QAM LowSE [Before CNI-103796-L]

For FR1 UL CA UE, L2-PS shall determine for each UE if it is configured with 64QAM or 256QAM or 64QAMLowSE in uplink.

  * If UE is configured with 64QAM, 5G-L2-PS shall take the same UL MCS value as defined by NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellBadChannelQualityThUL as threshold for bad RLQ sample (sCellBadChannelQualityThUL for 64QAM).
  * If UE is configured with 256QAM, 5G-L2-PS shall take the mapped UL MCS value according to the table below as threshold for bad RLQ sample (sCellBadChannelQualityThUL for 256QAM).
  * If UE is configured with 64QAMLowSE, 5G-L2-PS shall take the mapped UL MCS value according to the table below as threshold for bad RLQ sample (sCellBadChannelQualityThUL for 64QAMLowSE)



The MCS threshold value is used in periodic monitoring of SCell channel quality according to 5G_UP_ALG_11868_replaced([11121619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

|  |   
---|---|---  
sCellBadChannelQualityThUL for 64QAM = NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellBadChannelQualityThUL | sCellBadChannelQualityThUL for 256QAM | sCellBadChannelQualityThUL for 64QAMLowSE  
0 | 0 | 6  
1 | 1 | 7  
2 | 1 | 8  
3 | 2 | 9  
4 | 2 | 10  
5 | 3 | 11  
6 | 3 | 12  
7 | 4 | 13  
8 | 4 | 14  
9 | 5 | 15  
10 | 5 | 15  
11 | 5 | 16  
12 | 6 | 17  
13 | 7 | 18  
14 | 8 | 19  
15 | 9 | 20  
  
Note:

  1. The logic of this mapping table is the same as 5G_UP_ALG_2756_replaced([11121378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYigPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  2. The MCS index table for PUSCH with transform precoding (38.214 Table 6.1.4.1-1) has same spectral efficiency as the MCS index table for PUSCH with CP-OFDM (38.214 table 5.1.3.1-1) when index is smaller than or equal to 16, therefore no additional mapping is needed for PUSCH with transform precoding.




[CNI-103796-L]

For FR1 CA UE, the MCS threshold for RLQ decision in uplink is configured by NRBTS. NRCELL. sCellBadChannelQualityThUL.

If UE is configured with 64QAM MCS table, the value specified by NIDD parameter shall be used for RLQ decision directly (see 5G_UP_ALG_11867_replaced([11121616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If UE is configured with 256QAM MCS table or 64QAM lowSE MCS table, the value specified by NIDD parameter shall be mapped according to the following table to get the value that is actually used for decision:

|  |   
---|---|---  
MCS threshold set by NIDD parameter (assuming 64QAM MCS table is used) | MCS threshold used for decision if 256QAM MCS table is configured | MCS threshold used for decision if 64QAM_lowSE MCS table is configured  
0 | 0 | 6  
1 | 1 | 7  
2 | 1 | 8  
3 | 2 | 9  
4 | 2 | 10  
5 | 3 | 11  
6 | 3 | 12  
7 | 4 | 13  
8 | 4 | 14  
9 | 5 | 15  
10 | 5 | 15  
11 | 5 | 16  
12 | 6 | 17  
13 | 7 | 18  
14 | 8 | 19  
15 | 9 | 20  
  
Note:

1\. The logic of this mapping table is the same as 5G_UP_ALG_2756_replaced([11121378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYigPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2\. The MCS index table for PUSCH with transform precoding (38.214 Table 6.1.4.1-1) has same spectral efficiency as the MCS index table for PUSCH with CP-OFDM (38.214 table 5.1.3.1-1) when index is smaller than or equal to 16, therefore no additional mapping is needed for PUSCH with transform precoding.

3\. See 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2348_replaced([11284548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpsdIvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the PUSCH MCS table configured for UE.

[End CNI-103796-L]

SCell Buffer and Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR2 CA The radio link quality for requesting an additional SCell shall be evaluated on PCell only. The radio link quality check on PCell is sufficient due to the assumption of not too divergent radio conditions between the PCell and the SCells within the same sector and the always availability of the PCell. Any check on a deactivated SCell, which could be a candidate to be activated, is not possible due to absence of measurements related to the SCell.

The measurement for evaluating the SCell activation condition in DL is the pathloss of the PCell reported by means of the PHR. According to 3GPP 38.213 chapter 7.7.1 and 7.1.1 the type 1 PHR is defined as

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $PH_{type1,f_c}(i, j, q_d, l) = P_{CMAX,f_c}(i) - {P_{o,PUSCH,f_c}(j) + 10\log_{10}(2^\mu - M_{RB,f_c}^{PUSCH}(i)) + \alpha_{f_c}(i) \cdot PL_{f_c}(q_d) + \Delta_{TF,f_c}(i) + f_{f_c}(i, l)}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6570.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Finally, there is an opening parenthesis, a lowercase "t", and a closing parenthesis.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6570.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] and [image-2][image_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "f_r(t, b)". The UL link adaptation restricts the number of PRBs for MCS=0 if needed (see 5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced([11131515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Hence the number of PRBs carrying the PHR has to be considered for the evaluation of the PHR.

The pathloss in DL shall be calculated with reception of each PHR and is valid until the next valid and in sequence PHR is received. PHR reports, which are received out of sequence due to HARQ retransmissions, are obsolete for the pathloss calculation.

[Before 03044716, PR697600]

Editor's note: The rule for calculating the pathloss for DL shall be updated if the Closed Loop Power Control (5GC000884) will come in a future release.

[End 03044716, PR697600]

[03044716]

Note: The DL pathloss estimation is not compensated with accumulated TPC by Closed Loop Power Control due to risk of mismatch and error between UE and gNB.

If NRULCLPC_PROFILE.clpcPusch.sinrtargetOffset linked to the NRCELL is set to 0 dB, the long term of averaged TPC should be close to zero.

[End 03044716]

###### 3.7.2.4.2.0-2 SCell Buffer and Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR2 CA Evaluation of the radio link quality in UL branch (ID: 11121531)

**3.7.2.4.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13237053`)

SCell Buffer and Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR2 CA The pathloss related to the UL branch shall be calculated for the PCell as the difference of the UE’s PUSCH transmission power and the UL receive power detected at the gNB. For this purpose, the UE’s PUSCH transmission power shall be evaluated based on the type 1 PHR received continuously with the data stream in UL. The type 1 PHR provides with the UE’s maximum transmission power PCMAX and the power headroom the basis for calculating the transmission power in UL. Furthermore, the so evaluated transmission power shall be normalized to one PRB. Basis for the normalization to one PRB is the number of PRBs of the transport block the PHR is piggy-packed. The UL receive power is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_1684_replaced([11108694](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kouVp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The following equation defines the calculation rule for determining the pathloss in UL.

[CB008465-AA] If UL CoMP is NOT active ([12740784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PBhWcXv0EfCiUemk-K-C4g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), then [End CB008465-AA] 

  * UL Pathloss(i) = PCMAX,f,c(i) - max{0, PHtype1,f,c(i, qd, l)} - 10log10(MPUSCHRB,f,c(i)) - rxPower(i)



[CB008465-AA] else,

  * UL Pathloss(i) = PCMAX,f,c(i) - max{0, PHtype1,f,c(i, qd, l)} - 10log10(MPUSCHRB,f,c(i)) - PreEqRxPowerHarmAve(i)



[End CB008465-AA] 

with:

  * PHtype1,f,c(i, qd, l):Power Headroom received with the PHR
  * PCMAX,f,c(i): Maximum UL transmission power received with the PHR
  * MPUSCHRB,f,c(i): The bandwidth of the PUSCH resource assignment carrying the PHR expressed in number of resource blocks for PUSCH transmission period _i on carrier_ f of serving cell _c_ **
  * rxPower(i): PUSCH receive power is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_1684_replaced([11108694](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kouVp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * [CB008465-AA] PreEqRxPowerHarmAve(i): the harmonic average of the serving cell antenna-wise power ([11108734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kou8tfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). (An example of how harmonic average is done is already described in [11131461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB008465-AA]



The UL link adaptation restricts the number of PRBs for MCS=0 if needed (see 5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced([11131515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Hence the number of PRBs carrying the PHR has to be considered for the evaluation of the PHR.

The pathloss in UL shall be calculated with reception of each PHR and is valid until the next valid and in sequence PHR is received. PHR reports, which are received out of sequence due to HARQ retransmissions, are obsolete for the pathloss calculation.

---

###### 3.7.2.4.2.0-3 SCell Buffer and Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR2 CA Timer based control of the SCell activation for SCells deactivated due to RL quality (ID: 11121553)

**3.7.2.4.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11121556`)

SCell Buffer and Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR2 CA In some rare cases it is possible that SCell is deactivated due to bad RL quality in DL or UL and at the same time DL or UL pathloss of the PCell is low. In this case SCell will be deactivated and due to the low pathloss of the PSCell at the time of deactivation, condition for SCell activation will never be fulfilled. This happens because low pathloss (stored) will newer drop for NRBTS.pathlossDeltaActSCellDl or NRBTS.pathlossDeltaActSCellUl and due to this SCell will remain permanently deactivated.

In order to avoid such a situation timer based control of the SCell activation for SCells deactivated due to RL quality is introduced. 5G-L2-PS shall start rdRlqScellDeactExpiryTime timer (5G_L2_1163_replaced([11184531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6NPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at the time of SCell deactivation due to bad radio link quality in DL or UL. At expiry of the timer SCell can be activated even if conditions for the pathloss on PCell are not fulfilled but the condition for the SCell activation due to buffer status requires additional SCell.

If SCell is activated due to drop of the pathloss on the PSCell while timer is still running, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the timer.

This approach will not be valid for FR1 CA.

---

###### 3.7.2.4.2.0-4 SCell Buffer and Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR2 CA Trigger conditions for activation/deactivation a SCell when sCellActivationMethod is set to ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ (ID: 11121561)

**3.7.2.4.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11121564`)

SCell Buffer and Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR2 CA Note: For FR1 CA, 5G-L2-PS will consider ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ method same as ‘bufferBased’ method according to 5G_UP_ALG_2715_replaced([11120998](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_2763_replaced([11121567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Scell activation, deactivation and release.

For deactivating a SCell the following conditions shall be fulfilled:

For DL

·If either the DL transmission buffer is for n consecutive checks below the deactivating threshold (see 5G_UP_ALG_2709_replaced([11120941](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

·or the MCS provided by the DL Link Adaptation for the SCell is for n consecutive checks below the threshold determined according to 5G_UP_ALG_2756_replaced([11121378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYigPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note: 5G-L2-PS shall not start with the evaluation of the SCell deactivation before the first CQI report is received. 5G-L2-PS shall not consider DL MCS for Scell deactivation in case Scell is in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

the request for deactivating a SCell in DL shall be forwarded to the entity, which coordinates the SCell activation/deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For UL

·If either the UL transmission buffer is for n consecutive checks below the deactivating threshold (see 5G_UP_ALG_2738_replaced([11120974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

·or the MCS provided by the UL Link Adaptation for the SCell is for n consecutive checks below the threshold defined by the O&M parameter NRBTS.mcsDeactSCellUl. Note: 5G-L2-PS shall not consider initial, default UL MCS for SCell deactivation, but only use the MCS that is updated by UL Link Adaptation. (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 5G-L2-PS shall not consider UL MCS for Scell deactivation in case Scell is in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

the request for deactivating a SCell in UL shall be forwarded to the entity, which coordinates the SCell activation/deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Whenever a SCell is deactivated L2-PS shall capture the pathloss related to the PCell and shall buffer the pathloss for DL and UL separately. The buffered pathloss shall be the basis for the activation of the SCell again. For each buffered pathloss the index of the corresponding SCell shall be buffered as well for assignment purposes.

The trigger condition for activation a SCell when the NIDD parameter NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is set to ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ is a two-fold check of buffer utilization and radio link quality.

For activating an additional SCell the following conditions shall be fulfilled:

For DL

·If the pathloss defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2746_replaced([11121446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYikPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is for n consecutive checks smaller than the corresponding DL pathloss buffered when the SCell is deactivated reduced by the delta pathloss defined by the O&M parameter NRBTS.pathlossDeltaActSCellDl, or the timer rdRlqScellDeactExpiryTime is expired (see 5G_UP_ALG_2750_replaced([11121553](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

·and the buffer utilization condition defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2709_replaced([11120941](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is fulfilled as well

the request for activating an additional SCell in DL shall be forwarded to the entity, which coordinates the SCell activation/deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For UL

·If the pathloss defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2748_replaced([11121531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYik_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is for n consecutive checks smaller than the corresponding UL pathloss buffered when the SCell is deactivated reduced by the delta pathloss defined by the O&M parameter NRBTS.pathlossDeltaActSCellUl, or the timer rdRlqScellDeactExpiryTime is expired (see 5G_UP_ALG_2750_replaced([11121553](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

·and the buffer utilization condition defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2738_replaced([11120974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is fulfilled as well

the request for activating an additional SCell in UL shall be forwarded to the entity, which coordinates the SCell activation/deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The number n of consecutive checks is specified by the R&D parameter rdNumOfScellChecks (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

###### 3.7.2.4.3 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink

###### 3.7.2.4.3.0-1 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink Periodic Monitoring of Scell Channel Quality (Scell) (ID: 11121572)

**3.7.2.4.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13354229`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink When Scell is activated, Scell 5G-L2-PS will start to monitor the Scell radio link quality periodically for 'blind', ‘bufferBased’ or ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ Scell activation method(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) that 5G-L2-PS shall consider ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ same as ‘bufferBased’ method). The period will be defined per slot pattern defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) determined by rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 (5G_L2_1388_replaced([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1 [5G_L2_1390_replaced([11184651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] and rdProhibitScellCheck (5G_L2_1150_replaced([11184607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Scell 5G-L2-PS will maintain following parameters for each CA UE:

  * rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ;

  * rrmSamplesScellGoodRLQ;

  * rrmSamplesScellBadRLQ;

  * rrmScellBadRLQTimes;

  * rrmScellRLQStatus;




After each time Scell activation done, above parameters are initialized to 0 and rrmScellRLQStatus as "good".

For each time Scell check the channel radio link quality for CA UE over Scell, Scell 5G-L2-PS will take care of following steps.

**Step 1: 5G-L2-PS will check the validity of rrmDlProposedMcs for current Scell according to 5G_UP_ALG_3045_replaced([11125301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqt5svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

  * If it is valid(not in earlyDllaMode mode), 5G-L2-PS will increase rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ by 1, and go to next step;

  * If it is not valid(in earlyDllaMode mode), 5G-L2-PS will skip this time of checking Scell radio link quality for this CA UE, and continue to check for next CA UE with current Scell in activation state until all the matched CA UE are checked;




**Step 2: 5G-L2-PS will check the channel quality as follows.**

  * If rrmDlProposedMcs > sCellGoodChannelQualityThreshold



Increase rrmSamplesScellGoodRLQ by 1;

  * If rrmDlProposedMcs < sCellBadChannelQualityThreshold



Increase rrmSamplesScellBadRLQ by 1;

**Note: [Before PR865446] In case DL 256QAM is enabled, then the thresholds of MCS for sCellBadChannelQualityThreshold shall be mapped according to 5G_UP_ALG_2756_replaced([11121378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYigPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and map of sCellGoodChannelQualityThreshold of 28 to 27 due to MCS = 28 is not supported for 256QAM. [PR865446]**

In case DL 256QAM or DL 1024 QAM is enabled, then the threshold of MCS for sCellBadChannelQualityThreshold and sCellGoodChannelQualityThreshold shall be mapped according to [11121378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYigPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [End PR865446]

In case Ue is configured with LowSE Mcs table in the SCell, then the thresholds of MCS for sCellBadChannelQualityThreshold and sCellGoodChannelQualityThreshold shall be mapped according to 5G_UP_ALG_24376_replaced([11121409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYihPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Step 3: Evaluate whether period of channel quality is reached as follows.**

  * If (rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 * rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1 [5G_L2_1390_replaced([11184651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] + rdProhibitScellCheck) * rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ / (2^µ) >= sCellChannelEstimationPeriod then



Evaluate the Scell channel quality for current CA UE per 5G_UP_ALG_2767_replaced([11121583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); After each evaluation, 5G-L2-PS shall reset rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ, rrmSamplesScellGoodRLQ and rrmSamplesScellBadRLQ to 0 for next evaluation.

While µ is current Scell numerology; **Note: Here the slots which 5G-L2-PS send the MAC-CE and wait for HARQ-ACK are not considered for simplicity.**

  * Else



Continue to check for next CA UE with current Scell in activation state until all the matched CA UE are checked;

**Step 4: If rrmScellBadRLQTimes reachs to sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount while it is not 0(infinity), Scell will indicate P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS to trigger Scell permanently deactivation due to "bad" radio link quality.**

**sCellGoodChannelQualityThreshold: NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellGoodChannelQualityThreshold**

**sCellBadChannelQualityThreshold: NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellBadChannelQualityThreshold**

**sCellChannelEstimationPeriod: NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellChannelEstimationPeriod**

**sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount: NRBTS.sCellDeactivationBadRlqCount**

---

###### 3.7.2.4.3.0-2 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink Evaluation of Scell Channel Quality (Scell) (ID: 11121583)

**3.7.2.4.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12828710`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink When Scell of CA UE is in active state, Scell 5G-L2-PS shall evaluate the Scell radio link quality rrmScellRLQStatus for each active Scell as follows. Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for definition of rrmScellBadRLQTimes and rrmScellRLQStatus for each CA UE.

If 100 * rrmSamplesScellGoodRLQ/rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ > sCellGoodChannelEstimationPercent and current rrmScellRLQStatus is not "good" channel quality

  * SCell 5G-L2-PS start the flow control for Scell and start the Scell scheduling accordingly. [CB015535-A]If NRCELL.actFddDlSchedPrevent is equal to true, then for an FDD SCell configured with the DlAndUl mode for FR1 TDD + FDD UL CA scenario, the SCell 5G-L2-PS shall not initiate flow control procedure, consequently the corresponding stop flow control shall not be executed. Start and Stop Flow Control shall not be sent to L2LO for any procedure, including SCell Activation, Suspend, Resume, or Deactivation, occurring between SCell Activation and SCell Deactivation.[End CB015535-A]



\- rrmScellRLQStatus = "good";

  * SCell 5G-L2-PS shall inform P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS about “good” radio link quality;

  * restart Scell inactivity timer running to monitor the Scell inactivity according to 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

  * rrmScellBadRLQTimes = 0;




Else if 100 * rrmSamplesScellBadRLQ/rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ > sCellBadChannelEstimationPercent and current rrmScellRLQStatus is not "bad" channel quality

  * Scell 5G-L2-PS stop the flow control for Scell and stop the Scell scheduling accordingly;

  * rrmScellRLQStatus = "bad";

  * SCell 5G-L2-PS shall inform P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS about “bad” radio link quality without trigger the SCell permanent deactivation.

  * Stop Scell inactivity timer;

  * Increase number of bad radio link quality report rrmScellBadRLQTimes ;

  * Reset rrmDeltaCqi[i,j,t] of current carrier to initial value according to 5G_UP_ALG_3060_replaced([11129299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq78IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));




Else if ((100 * rrmSamplesScellGoodRLQ/rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ<= sCellGoodChannelEstimationPercent) (**Note: need to count the rrmScellBadRLQTimes in case the channel quality is not "good") and (current rrmScellRLQStatus is "bad" channel quality))**

  * Increase number of bad radio link quality report rrmScellBadRLQTimes;



**Note: In case there is no RL quality samples(rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ = 0) during due to Scell deactivation after inactivity timer expires, 5G-L2-PS will keep the Scell RL quality as "good" due to channel quality is "good" before deactivation triggered by inactivity timer expiration.**

**sCellGoodChannelEstimationPercent: NRBTS.sCellGoodChannelEstimationPercent**

**sCellBadChannelEstimationPercent: NRBTS.sCellBadChannelEstimationPercent**

**rrmScellRLQStatus: radio Quality Status good or bad (5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

**rrmScellBadRLQTimes: number of evaluations where the mcs is considered bad**(5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))****

**rrmSamplesScellGoodRLQ: number of checks where mcs is considered good**(5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))****

**rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQ: number of checks performed during the evaluation (5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

**rrmSamplesScellBadRLQ:** number of checks where mcs is considered bad **(5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))******

**rrmDeltaCqi: WB-CQI correction provided by OLLA (5G_UP_ALG_17364_replaced([11129497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq8jMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

---

###### 3.7.2.4.3.0-3 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink Reconfiguration of MCS Threshold for Scell Channel Quality (ID: 11121592)

**3.7.2.4.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11121596`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink Scell 5G-L2-PS shall update the configuration parameters of MCS thresholds (NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellGoodChannelQualityThreshold and NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellBadChannelQualityThreshold) for Scell radio link quality monitoring at each time of Scell cell reconfiguration procedure.

Note: based on the CFAM discussion, Scell configuration parameters will be used for CA UE radio link quality monitoring.

After the parameters are updated in Scell, the parameters will be valid immediately to be used in the next Scell radio quality evaluation according to 5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.7.2.4.3.0-4 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink Reconfiguration of Period and Threshold for Scell Channel Quality Evaluation (ID: 11121599)

**3.7.2.4.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11121602`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink Scell 5G-L2-PS shall update the configuration parameter of evaluation period (NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellChannelEstimationPeriod) for Scell radio link quality evaluation at each time of Scell cell reconfiguration procedure.

Note: based on the CFAM discussion, Scell configuration parameters will be used for CA UE radio link quality monitoring.

After the parameters are updated in Scell, the parameters will be valid immediately to be used in the next Scell radio quality evaluation according to 5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.7.2.4.3.0-5 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink Permanant Scell Deactivation Due to bad RL Quality (ID: 11121607)

**3.7.2.4.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11121612`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Downlink In case Scell permanant deactivation triggered due to bad RL quality according to 5G_UP_ALG_2764_replaced([11121572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will trigger the MAC-CE to deactivated the Scell.

During transient period of Scell release for the Scell with servingCellIndex according to 5G_UP_ALG_2687_replaced([11120600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will ingore the indication of Scell deactivation due to bad RL quality and will not trigger the MAC-CE to UE.

In case of maximum number of HARQ retransmissions is reached for TB carrying the SCell Deactivation MAC-CE, 5G-L2-PS shall only trigger the Scell deactivation based on next bad RL quality report.

---

###### 3.7.2.4.4 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink

###### 3.7.2.4.4.0-1 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink Periodic Monitoring of SCell Channel Quality (ID: 11121619)

**3.7.2.4.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11121628`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink When joint DL/UL SCell is activated, SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will start to monitor the SCell radio link quality in uplink periodically for 'blind', ‘bufferBased’ or ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ SCell activation method(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) that 5G-L2-PS shall consider ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ same as ‘bufferBased’ method). The period will be defined per slot pattern defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) determined by rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 [5G_L2_1388_replaced([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))], rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1 [5G_L2_1390_replaced([11184651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] and rdProhibitScellCheck [5G_L2_1392_replaced([11184664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will maintain following parameters for each CA UE which has uplink activated:

  * rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL;

  * rrmSamplesScellBadRLQinUL;

  * rrmScellRLQStatusUL;




After each time SCell activation done, above parameters are initialized to 0 and rrmScellRLQStatusUL as "good".

For each time SCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall check the channel radio link quality in uplink with following steps.

Step 1: SCell UL 5G-L2-PS will check whether scaled MCS comes from initial or default MCS ullaIniMcs (first scheduling or rdSinrExpiryTime (5G_L2_1029_replaced([11186254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_274Hf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) timer expired), or SCell is in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * If NO, 5G-L2-PS will increase rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL by 1, and go to next step;

  * If YES, 5G-L2-PS will skip this time of checking SCell radio link quality in uplink for this CA UE, and continue to check for next CA UE with current SCell in activation state until all the matched CA UE are checked;




Step 2: 5G-L2-PS will check the channel quality as follows.

  * If scaled MCS < sCellBadChannelQualityThUL



Increase rrmSamplesScellBadRLQinUL by 1 ;

Calculate the SCell downlink pathloss and average the pathloss according to 5G_UP_ALG_13950_replaced([11121669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ;

Note:

  * In case UL 256QAM is enabled [PR727318, CB008246-K] or in case 64QAMLowSE is configured in UL [End PR727318, CB008246-K], then the thresholds of MCS for sCellBadChannelQualityThUL shall be mapped according to 5G_UP_ALG_12639_replaced([11121423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYih_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * In case scaled MCS > sCellBadChannelQualityThUL, SCell downlink pathloss is not recorded and is not calculated for averaging.
  * Scaled MCS is calculated based on the number of PRB assigned from FDM, before MCS downgrade.



Step 3: Evaluate whether period of channel quality is reached as follows.

  * If (rdPeriodScellCheckFR1 [5G_L2_1388_replaced([11184635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] * rdNumberOfScellChecksFR1 [5G_L2_1390_replaced([11184651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] + rdProhibitScellCheckFR1 [5G_L2_1392_replaced([11184664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shTvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]) * rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL / (2^µ) >= NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellChannelEstimationPeriod then



Evaluate the SCell channel quality for current CA UE per 5G_UP_ALG_11871_replaced([11121633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); After each evaluation, 5G-L2-PS shall reset rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL and rrmSamplesScellBadRLQinUL to 0 for next evaluation.

While µ is current SCell numerology; Note: Here the slots which 5G-L2-PS send the MAC-CE and wait for HARQ-ACK are not considered for simplicity.

  * Else



Continue to check for next CA UE with current SCell in activation state until all the matched CA UE are checked;

sCellBadChannelQualityThUL: NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellBadChannelQualityThUL

---

###### 3.7.2.4.4.0-2 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink Evaluation of SCell Channel Quality (ID: 11121633)

**3.7.2.4.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11121637`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink When joint DL/UL SCell of CA UE is in active state, SCell 5G-L2-PS shall evaluate the SCell uplink radio link quality rrmScellRLQStatusUL for active joint DL/UL SCell as follows. Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_11868_replaced([11121619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for definition of rrmSamplesScellBadRLQinUL, rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL and rrmScellRLQStatusUL.

If 100 * rrmSamplesScellBadRLQinUL/rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL > NRBTS.sCellBadChannelEstimationPercent and current rrmScellRLQStatusUL is not "bad" channel quality

\- rrmScellRLQStatusUL = "bad".

\- SCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall inform PCell DL & UL 5G-L2-PS about “bad” radio link quality; PCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall stop uplink buffer split to SCell according to 5G_UP_ALG_11884_replaced([11121639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * SCell UL 5G-L2-PS increase the counter "Number of S-Cell UL schedule suspending due to bad uplink radio link quality in S-Cell" by 1.



Note: In case there is no RL quality samples (rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL = 0) during due to SCell deactivation after inactivity timer expires, 5G-L2-PS will keep the SCell RL quality as "good" due to channel quality is "good" before deactivation triggered by inactivity timer expiration.

---

###### 3.7.2.4.4.0-3 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink Suspend SCell uplink scheduling (ID: 11121639)

**3.7.2.4.4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11121648`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink If PCell UL 5G-L2-PS receives "bad" uplink radio link quality indication from SCell, PCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall stop buffer split to SCell according to 5G_UP_ALG_10516_replaced([11122476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[Before PR698968], and adjust UE TX power on PCell according to 5G_UP_ALG_10919_replaced([11119940](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End PR698968].

SCell UL L2-PS shall continue pending retransmission and start inactivity timer if zero buffer split received from PCell.

---

###### 3.7.2.4.4.0-4 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink Recover SCell uplink scheduling (ID: 11121652)

**3.7.2.4.4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11121665`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink 11121665: SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink Due to the fact that SCell scheduling is suspended after SCell enter "bad" uplink radio link quality status, then the uplink MCS will reset to default value after timer expired and never get a chance to be updated anymore, therefore SCell uplink RLQ can not be evaluated again even if SCell uplink RLQ may become better.

To solve this issue, SCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall record the SCell DL pathloss when rrmScellRLQStatusUL changes from "good" to "bad", and after that check the pathloss every time PHR is received, whether the pathloss is for n consecutive checks δ dB smaller than the pathloss recorded. If yes then SCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall set rrmScellRLQStatusUL to "good", and inform PCell DL & UL 5G-L2-PS about “good” radio link quality. SCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall increase the counter "Number of S-Cell UL schedule recovery from suspending due to uplink radio link quality recovery in S-Cell uplink" by 1. This check shall be run as long as SCell is active, even when uplink inactivity timer is expired but SCell is still active due to downlink inactivity timer is not expired.

SCell DL pathloss is calculated according to 5G_UP_ALG_2746_replaced([11121446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYikPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), in case PHR report is based on a reference format (V = 1), [image-0][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6600.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] is calculated according to 5G_UP_ALG_10873_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If PCell UL 5G-L2-PS receives "good" uplink radio link quality indication from SCell, PCell shall start buffer split to SCell as first split with rdRatioForFirstUeTransBufSplitToScell (5G_UP_ALG_10305_replaced([11124127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ratio according to 5G_UP_ALG_9591_replaced([11122888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhFYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[Before PR698968], and initialize split TX power on PCell and SCell according to 5G_UP_ALG_10879_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End PR698968].

SCell UL L2-PS shall stop inactivity timer when non-zero buffer split received from PCell.

The number n of consecutive checks is specified by the R&D parameter rdNumOfChecksforRecovScellULFR1 (see 5G_UP_ALG_12689_replaced([11124148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaJPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The δ dB is specified by the R&D parameter rdPathlossDeltaforRecovScellULFR1 (see 5G_UP_ALG_12691_replaced([11124155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

-rrmScellRLQStatusUL: SCell uplink radio link quality for active joint DL/UL SCell (5G_UP_ALG_11868_replaced([11121619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End PR668422]

DL pathloss is averaged by an exponential filter defined below:

averageDlPathloss(n) = (1-rdDlPathlossFilterConst) * averageDlPathloss(n-1) + rdDlPathlossFilterConst * instanceDlPathloss(n)

\- rdDlPathlossFilterConst is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_14095_replaced([11124173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- the 1st calculated DL pathloss is used as the initial input for this exponential filter.

The pathloss in DL shall be calculated with reception of each PHR and is valid until the next valid and in sequence PHR is received. PHR reports, which are received out of sequence due to HARQ retransmissions, are obsolete for the pathloss calculation.

Note:

  1. [image-13][image_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "f_r(t, b)". The text is in a light color against a white background, with some blurriness and a slight purple hue.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6603.014.png[/image_path][/image-13] is not considered in the calculation, but it does not matter because only delta value of PL change is considered in SCell recovery.

###### 3.7.2.4.4.0-6 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink Reconfiguration of MCS Threshold for SCell Channel Quality (ID: 11121747)

**3.7.2.4.4.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11121751`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink SCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall update the configuration parameters of MCS thresholds (sCellGoodChannelQualityThUL and NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellBadChannelQualityThUL) for SCell radio link quality monitoring in uplink at each time of SCell cell reconfiguration procedure.

Note: based on the CFAM discussion, SCell configuration parameters will be used for CA UE radio link quality monitoring.

After the parameters are updated in SCell, the parameters will be valid immediately to be used in the next time of check according to 5G_UP_ALG_11868_replaced([11121619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

###### 3.7.2.4.4.0-7 SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink Reconfiguration of Period for SCell Channel Quality Evaluation (ID: 11121754)

**3.7.2.4.4.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11121759`)

SCell Radio Link Quality Monitoring for FR1 CA in Uplink SCell 5G-L2-PS shall update the configuration parameter of evaluation period (NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellChannelEstimationPeriod) for SCell radio link quality evaluation at each time of SCell cell reconfiguration procedure.

Note: based on the CFAM discussion, SCell configuration parameters will be used for CA UE radio link quality monitoring.

After the parameters are updated in SCell, the parameters will be valid immediately to be used in the next time of check according to 5G_UP_ALG_11868_replaced([11121619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 3.7.2.5 SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2)

###### 3.7.2.5.0-1 SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) One step SCell Activation/Deactivation to avoid some UEs RL failure (ID: 11121767)

**3.7.2.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11121770`)

SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) In case SCell deactivation results in PSCell and active SCell being noncontiguous in frequency with two inactive SCells between PSCell and SCell, some type of UE could have an issue in decoding DCI on PSCell and this leads to RLF. In 5G19A we have CAS-297005-L2F8 to avoid such issue. But this issue is existing too in 5G19B.

To overcome this issue, for the UE is configured with no more than 3 SCells and indicated by CPRT with flag potentialSdx50 in PsUser_UserSetupReq is true, the processing is below:

If the scell activation and deactivation is set to “bufferAndRLQualityBased”, when any scell need to be deactivated due to RL Quality, all scells shall be deactivated. And when any scell need to be activated due to RL quality, all scells shall be activated only if the RL quality for all scells are good enough to be activated. The buffer based scell deactivation and activation shall take effective only in case no scell is deactivated triggered by RL quality. For buffered based scell activation, all the scells shall be activated once buffer-based evaluation triggers first scell activation. For buffer based scell deactivation, if UE is configured with more than 0 scell in UL, all the scells shall be deactivated only in case both UL and DL require scell deactivation. Otherwise, all the scells shall be deactivated in case DL require scell deactivation.

For the case cell deleted without UE notification, all the scells shall be kept deactivation and shall not be activated any more.

For the UE which is configured with more than 3 SCells, above specific processing is not applicable.

Notes:

  * This issue is not existed for all UEs but only UEs with QC SDX50 so far. So this requirement is a WA for such kind of UE.

  * Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3334_replaced([11252247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tngr1vvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for potentialSdx50.

---
