Activation/Deactivation (FR2) 11121789: SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) 11121789: SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) 11121789: SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) 11121789: SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) 11121789: SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) 11121789: SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) 11121789: SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) 11121789: SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) For the carrier aggregation with a same or different number of SCells in DL and UL the origin of the SCell activation request determines if a DL only SCell or a joint DL/UL SCell shall be activated.

If UL L2-PS branch is requesting additional SCell activation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2738_replaced([11120974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it provides DL L2-PS request with the list of inactive SCells with lowest load. DL L2-PS branch selects for SCell activation the SCell from the UL proposed list with lowest DL load. Activation for the selected DL/UL SCell is triggered. Same procedure is applied in case both UL and DL branch are requesting SCell activation. 

If only DL L2-PS branch is requesting additional SCell activation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2709_replaced([11120941](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall first check if there is any inactive DL only SCell and if so, select the one with the lowest load. If no DL only SCells are available, L2-PS shall select inactive DL/UL SCell with lowest DL load. In this case UL load is not considered since there is no request coming from UL branch with the list of UL cells with lowest load. If more than one SCell have the same lowest load L2-PS shall randomly select one SCell.

When NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is set to ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ the triggers for SCell activation coming from the UL branch and from the DL branch are based on the radio link quality as well as on the buffer utilization (see 5G_UP_ALG_2758_replaced([11121561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The set of SCells that can be activated is limited to the SCells, which fulfil the pathloss conditions or were not previously deactivated due to radio link quality and hence the pathloss for activating the SCell is not specified (see 5G_UP_ALG_2758_replaced([11121561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The load conditions of the SCells shall be considered when triggering the request for an additional SCell activation. With each request from UL branch, [Before CB012734-C-UPD001] [Before CB012734-C] the UL counters instantNumOfActiveCellUEUL [CB012734-C] activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierUL [End CB012734-C] [CB012734-C-UPD001] carrier load (Note1) [End CB012734-C-UPD001] of all configured and inactive UL SCells shall be compared and those with lowest load shall be proposed to the DL branch for activation. DL branch considers [Before CB012734-C-UPD001][Before CB012734-C] DL counters instantNumOfActiveCellUEDL [CB012734-C] activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL [End CB012734-C][CB012734-C-UPD001] carrier load (Note 1) [End CB012734-C-UPD001] of all proposed SCells and select the one with lowest DL load for activation. If there are still several SCells which fulfill the condition for activation, [CB012734-C] the one on the carrier with least number of active UEs ([image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression starts with a summation symbol followed by the index 'i'. The term being summed is "activeLoadPerBeamPerCarrier DL[][]".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6613.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] [CB012734-C-UPD001] or instantNumOfActiveCellUEDL [End CB012734-C-UPD001] for DL trigger, and [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression starts with a summation symbol followed by the index 'i'. After the summation symbol, the text "activeLoadPerBeamPerCarrier UL[][]" is present. The text is slightly blurry.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6613.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] [CB012734-C-UPD001] or instantNumOfActiveCellUEUL [End CB012734-C-UPD001] for UL trigger) shall be selected; if there are still more than one candidates, [End CB012734-C]one SCell out of the candidates shall be selected randomly, and the activation shall be requested by triggering 5G-L2-LO to send the SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC Control Element to the UE.

[CB012734-C-UPD001]

Notes:

1\. if ((NRCELLGRP. actHighNumberOfUEs == TRUE) && (rdActAutoScellDeactivationOnLoad == 1))

{

activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierUL[i][j] (see below) is used to indicate carrier load on UL;

activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL[i][j] (see below) is used to indicate carrier load on DL;

}

else

{

Counter instantNumOfActiveCellUEUL is used to indicate carrier load on UL;

Counter instantNumOfActiveCellUEDL is used to indicate carrier load on DL;

}

[End CB012734-C-UPD001]

[CB012734-C]

activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierUL[i][j]: number of active UEs on beam i carrier j, and operation mode of the serving cell on carrier j is “DL and UL”, defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26307_replaced([11122140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL[i][j]: number of active UEs on beam i carrier j, defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26307_replaced([11122140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

i: index of UE’s best beam.

j: index of carrier.

[End CB012734-C]

The PM counter 'SCell activations' is incremented for each SCell activated.

This requirement covers only the case where SCell activation request is triggered by single or both branches. More detailed scenarios with different combinations of UL and DL request types (Activation, Deactivation, No Action) is covered by EFS and implementation.

In the implementation, since SCell load for UL and DL are maintained separately in UL and DL L2-PS branch, and activation/deactivation decision is done in DL L2-PS branch, so the UL load is not always considered in the final decision.

---

###### 3.7.2.5.0-3 SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) Joint DL and UL SCell Activation impacted by DL or UL only activation (ID: 11121792)

**3.7.2.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11121796`)

SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) In case of L2 PS DL try to activate new Scell and if there is no more DL only SCells then a joint DL/UL SCell shall be activated, When DL MAC CE has been ACKed and CA activition timer expired, then the UL Scell will be active also (intra TTI message notify the L2 PS UL), and UL load for this Scell also need to be increased. Similar if DL_UL_BOTH Scell has been selected by 5G-L2-PS UL for activation and in 5G-L2-PS DL there is no need to activate additional Scell, then after the MAC CE has been ACKed and CA activition timer expired, the DL Load for the Scell will be also increased;

For the above two cases, it can cause the such result: there is UL Scell has been actived but the target Scell will not be used, and there is same case for DL.

---

###### 3.7.2.5.0-4 SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) Selection of SCell for deactivation - asymmetrical carrier aggregation (ID: 11121800)

**3.7.2.5.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11121808`)

SCell selection for Activation/Deactivation (FR2) Scell in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall not be selected for deactivation in case there is still exsiting Scells which are not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For the carrier aggregation with a same or different number of SCells in DL and UL the origin of the SCell deactivation request determines if a DL only SCell or a joint DL/UL SCell shall be deactivated.

If UL L2-PS branch is requesting buffer based SCell deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2738_replaced([11120974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it provides DL L2-PS branch with request containing the list of active SCells with highest load. If DL L2-PS branch is also requesting buffer based SCell deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2709_replaced([11120941](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), DL L2-PS branch selects the SCell from the UL proposed list with the highest DL load [CB012734-C] (note1) [End CB012734-C] for SCell deactivation, else if DL L2-PS branch is not requesting buffer based SCell deactivation, SCell deactivation is not triggered.

If only DL L2-PS branch is requesting buffer based SCell deactivation (see 5G_UP_ALG_2709_replaced([11120941](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and no UL proposal is triggered, a DL only SCell with the highest load shall be deactivated and if there is no active DL only SCell, the request shall be ignored.

[CB012734-B-UPD001]

If gNB-DU needs to check whether SCell deactivation due to active UE load shall be applied to current UE (auLoadBasedScellDeactCheck is set to 1 in UE context), then n SCell(s) [Before PR796424] with highest activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL shall be selected for deactivation irrespective of the operation mode of the SCell, that is, no matter the operation mode is “DL only” or “DL and UL”. [PR796424] shall be selected for deactivation according to the following prioritization sequence:

if (number of active DL only SCells > roundup(scellReductionThreshold * rdMinDlOnlySCellPercent / 100) )

{

  * Tier1: “DL only” mode > “DL and UL” mode;
  * Tier2: higher activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL > lower activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL;
  * Tier3: higher carrier load > lower carrier load;
  * Tier4: larger SCell index > smaller SCell index.



}

else //number of active DL only SCells <= roundup(scellReductionThreshold * rdMinDlOnlySCellPercent / 100)

{

  * Tier1: “DL and UL” mode > “DL only” mode;
  * Tier2: higher activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL > lower activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL;
  * Tier3: higher carrier load > lower carrier load;
  * Tier4: larger SCell index > smaller SCell index.



}

[End PR796424]

Where:

[PR796424]

  * scellReductionThreshold: see 5G_UP_ALG_26309_replaced([11122151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
  * “A > B” means “A is prioritized over B” ;
  * activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL: see 5G_UP_ALG_26307_replaced([11122140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
  * carrier load: number of UEs with active serving cell on this carrier;
  * rdMinDlOnlySCellPercent: minimum percentage of DL only SCell to be retained during SCell deactivation due to active UE overload, defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31680_replaced([11124312](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));



[End PR796424]

  * activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26307_replaced([11122140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * n is number of SCell(s) that needs to be deactivated of current UE, see 5G_UP_ALG_26311_replaced([11122157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the computation method of n.



[End CB012734-B-UPD001]

When NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is set to ‘bufferAndRLQualityBased’ the triggers for SCell deactivation coming from the DL branch and/or from the UL branch are based either on the radio link quality or on the buffer utilization (see 5G_UP_ALG_2758_replaced([11121561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). SCell is deactivated based on radio link quality if request for SCell deactivation is triggered by only DL branch, or by only UL branch, or by both branches of this SCell. If simultaneous deactivation of multiple SCells is triggered due to bad radio link quality, all the SCells that triggered SCell deactivation due to bad radio link quality shall be deactivated. If requests for deactivating SCell based on buffer utilization and radio link quality are received simultaneously, only requests for deactivating SCell based on radio link quality are processed and corresponding SCell(s) are deactivated, request for deactivating SCell based on buffer utilization is ignored.

All SCell shall be deactivated with a single SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC Control Element if rdNumOfScellChecks (5G_L2_1149_replaced([11184600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) consecutive checks for both UL branch and DL branch indicate an empty transmission buffer. If only the DL branch indicates an empty transmission buffer for rdNumOfScellChecks consecutive checks and there is no trigger from UL branch, all DL SCells shall be deactivated with a single SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC Control Element.

The PM counter 'SCell deactivations due to Buffer Status' is incremented for each SCell deactivated if the trigger for deactivating is caused by low buffer utilization.

This requirement covers only the case where SCell deactivation request is triggered by single or both branches. More detailed scenarios with different combinations of UL and DL request types (Activation, Deactivation, No Action) is covered in EFS and implementation.

The PM counter 'SCell deactivations due to Channel State' is incremented for each deactivated SCell if the trigger for deactivation is based on radio link quality. If simultaneous deactivation of multiple SCells is triggered due to radio link quality, the PM counter 'SCell deactivations due to Channel State' of each deactivated SCell is incremented. In case of simultaneous buffer and radio link quality-based deactivation triggers, only radio link quality-based deactivation will be processed and only the PM counter 'SCell deactivations due to Channel State' of the deactivated SCell will be increased.

In the implementation, since SCell load for UL and DL are maintained separately, and activation/deactivation decision is done in DL branch, so the UL load is not always considered in the final decision.

[CB012734-C]

Notes:

[CB012734-C-UPD001]

1\. If ((NRCELLGRP.actHighNumberOfUEs == TRUE) && (rdActAutoScellDeactivationOnLoad == 1))

{

[End CB012734-C-UPD001]

The UL branch of L2-PS shall use activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierUL[i][j] as SCell load, the DL branch of L2-PS shall use activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL[i][j] as SCell load.

[CB012734-C-UPD001]

}

else

{

UL branch of L2-PS use counter instantNumOfActiveCellUEUL as SCell load; DL branch of L2-PS shall use counter instantNumOfActiveCellUEDL as SCell load.

}

[End CB012734-C-UPD001]

where:

  * activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierUL[i][j]: number of active UEs on beam i and carrrier j, and the serving cell on carrier j operates in "DL and UL" mode, defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26307_replaced([11122140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL[i][j]: number of active UEs on beam i and carrier j, defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26307_replaced([11122140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * i: index of UE’s best beam.
  * j: index of carrier.



[End CB012734-C]

##### 3.7.2.6 Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation

###### 3.7.2.6.0-1 Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation Guard period between activation of the SCell and start of scheduling (ID: 11121815)

**3.7.2.6.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13467496`)

Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation 13467496: Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation 13467496: Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation 13467496: Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation 13467496: Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation 13467496: Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation 13467496: Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation 13467496: Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation 13467496: Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation A guard period has to be kept before 5G-L2-PS can start with the scheduling of user data after activation of the SCell by means of the MAC-C element. 3GPP defines the guard period as the time until the UE is in the position to transmit valid CSI reports and apply actions related to the activation command for the SCell being activated [3GPP TS 38.133 chapter 8.3.2]. Based on 3GPP’s definition, the guard period is defined by the following equation

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a sans-serif font. The equation is: `sCell.ActivationPeriod = T_HARQ + T_activation_time + T_CSI_reporting`[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6621.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

with

THARQ: Timing between DL data transmission and acknowledgment [3GPP TS 38.321]

Tactivation_time: SCell activation delay

TCSI_reporting: Delay uncertainty in acquiring the first available CSI report [3GPP TS 38.331]

The parameter THARQ is deduced from the K1 parameter used in DCI for granting the transport block carrying the MAC-C element.

If FR1, the SCell activation delay Tactivation_time is defined by R&D parameters. Two R&D parameters shall be implemented in 5G-L2-PS. rdScellActDelayFr1 (5G_L2_1160_replaced([11184613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall determine the SCell activation delay for FR1 bands.[Before CB013712-B] and rdScellActDelayFr2 (5G_L2_1161_replaced([11184618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shRPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR2 bands.[End CB013712-B]

TCSI_reporting is the delay uncertainty in acquiring the first available CSI reporting resources. This shall be specified in 38.331 but is currently missing and therefore we will introduce R&D parameter rdScellActCsiDelay (5G_L2_1162_replaced([11184623](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shRfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) that will enable alignment to the 38.331.

The guard period sCellActivationPeriod starts with sending and resending due to HARQ retransmission the MAC-C element for activating the SCell.

In the implementation, 5G-L2-PS shall start the activation timer for the guard period when receive the ACK for SCell activation MAC CE from L1. So the guard period will start from the PUCCH receiving time, and the length of this guard period is equal to Tactivation_time + TCSI_reporting.

NOTE: For each UE in FR1 FDD, the UE shall not be scheduled in CSI slots until the above-described guard period has been expired.

[Before CB013712-B] If FR2, Tactivation_time + TCSI_reporting are defined by _scellActivationDelay_ms in 5G_UP_ALG_2794_replaced([11121826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB013712-B]_

---

###### 3.7.2.6.0-2 Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation SCell Activation Delay Calculation (ID: 11121826)

**3.7.2.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11121842`)

The expression is a fraction. The numerator is "T HARQ" and the denominator is "NR slot length". The expression is: n + (THARQ + scellActivationDelay) / (NR slot length)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6623.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]and shall consider the related CSI report after slot [image-2][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: n + (THARQ + scellActivationDelay) / (NR slot length)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6623.002.png[/image_path][/image-2],according to 3GPP TS 38.133 §8.3.2. NOTE: Exact dynamic calculation of the SCell activation delay is complex in implementation and testing and the gain is limited. Instead a the SCell activation delay is calculated at UE setup. In worst case, this can cause lost multiplexed reports in one additional slot. The impact to Link Adaptaion and Beam Management is limited which can handle this e.g. by OLLA or Beam Failure Recovery, respectively. Where: * THARQ (in ms) is the timing between DL data transmission and acknowledgement as specified in TS 38.213 [3] * scellActivationDelay_ms is defined as delay_ms = maximum(average(Tactivation_time+TCSI_reporting), maximum(Tactivation_time+TCSI_reporting)-csiReportPeriod). * average(Tactivation_time+TCSI_reporting) shall be calculated = average(Tactivation_time) + average(TCSI_reporting) * maximum(Tactivation_time+TCSI_reporting) shall be calculated = maximum(Tactivation_time) + maximum(TCSI_reporting) * Tactivation_time is the SCell activation delay in millisecond. Tactivation_time is TFirstSSB+ 5ms, since FR2 and at least one active serving cell is assumed, according to 3GPP TS 38.133 §8.3.2. * TFirstSSB: is the time to first SSB indicated by the SMTC after slot n + THARQ+3ms. TFirstSSB can have a value range between 0ms and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/ssBurstSetPeriod. * Accordingly, maximum(Tactivation_time) shall be set = 5ms + MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/ssBurstSetPeriod and average(Tactivation_time) shall be set = (5ms + MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/ssBurstSetPeriod) / 2. * csiReportPeriod is defined in CSI-RS-Periodicity * NR slot length in ms (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2571_replaced([11299301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqS6EfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) * TCSI_reporting is the delay (in ms) including uncertainty in acquiring the a) first available downlink CSI reference resource, b) UE processing time for CSI reporting and c) uncertainty in acquiring the first available CSI reporting resources as specified in TS 38.331 [2]. * TCSI_reporting a) can have a value range between 0ms and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/periodicCsiAcquisition/csiReportPeriodicity * NR slot length * TCSI_reporting b) shall be assumed ueCsiProcessingTime_ms = 3ms * TCSI_reporting c) shall not be considered by 5G-L2-PS. The reason is that gNB is allocating the CSI report resouce as configured according to the figure below. If after TCSI_reporting b), then with related SCell report in the multi-CSI-PUCCH-resource. * Accordingly, maximum(TCSI_reporting) shall be set = ueCsiProcessingTime_ms + MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/periodicCsiAcquisition/csiReportPeriodicity * NR slot length and average(TCSI_reporting) shall be set = (ueCsiProcessingTime_ms + MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/periodicCsiAcquisition/csiReportPeriodicity * NR slot length) / 2. ###### 3.7.2.6.0-4 Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation SCell Deactivation interaction with DPA (ID: 11121868)

**3.7.2.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11121872`)

Delay for SCell Activation/Deactivation If any SCell need to be deactivated after the SCell shared the cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx to P(S)Cell in the measurement cycle x of distributed PUCCH algorithm, P(S)Cell shall delay the deactivation of SCell to UE (i.e sending MAC-CE) till the end of corresponding scheduling cycle.

During the delay of the first Scell deactivation, if the second Scell need to be deactivated, L2PS need to restart delay timer and combine 2 scells deactivation into one MAC-CE. P(S)Cell shall delay the deactivation of two SCells to UE (i.e sending MAC-CE) till the delay timer expires.

Note:

for cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2893_replaced([11123516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.7.2.7 Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling

##### 3.7.2.7.0-1 Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling Carrier activation status (ID: 11121880)

**3.7.2.7.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12828667`)

Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the activation status for each serving cell. Each serving cell will be in 1 of the 3 statuses, active, activeStopped or inactive. The status activeStopped indicates an intermediate state during that the serving cell is basically activated for the UE, but the UE is taken out of scheduling for initial transmissions. HARQ retransmissions can be scheduled if the serving cell stays in activeStopped.

When UE is setup in 5G-L2-PS, PSCell is in active status, and all SCells are in inactive status.

When RA procedure is finished and the blind activation is selected, 5G-L2-PS shall trigger SCell activation for all SCell according to 5G_UP_ALG_2703_replaced([11120833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqURHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when there is any SCell in inactive status. If the buffer based activation is selected, the buffer utilization of the gNB’s or UE’s transmission buffers may trigger the change of the SCell status from inactive to active (see 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Furthermore, the radio link quality is another indicator for changing the SCell status as define by 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When HARQ failure happened for SCell activation MAC CE and blind SCell activation is selected, status for all SCell are still inactive, and trigger another SCell activation MAC CE scheduling immediately, until the ACK for MAC CE is received.

For FR1 CA **when HARQ failure happened for Scell activation MAC-CE and blind SCell activation is selected, Scell status shall be still inactive status and trigger another Scell activation MAC-CE scheduling immediately until HARQ ACK for the MAC-CE is received.**

Different to the blind activation, the buffer-based method or the buffer and radio link quality based method shall handle the HARQ ACK for Scell activation MAC CE as follows:

 When HARQ failure happened for SCell activation MAC CE and there is no Scell in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), status for related SCells are still inactive. the buffer based method allows the activation of only one SCell per MAC CE and the status change of the SCell is triggered at dedicated events.

 When HARQ failure happened for SCell activation MAC CE and there is at least one Scell in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), status for related SCell are still inactive, 5G-L2-PS shall not trigger further activation MAC CE scheduling.

The HARQ ACK feedback corresponding to the transport block carrying the MAC-C element for activating the SCell shall change in a first step the status from inactive to activeStopped for the SCell the request of activation is raised. In a second step the status shall change after the guard period (see 5G_UP_ALG_2792_replaced([11121815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or after reception of an CSI report from activeStopped to active. The status inactive shall be kept if an HARQ NACK is received from the transport block the MAC-C element is carried.

**NOTE:If the Scell CSI report is configured on a multi-CSI-PUCCH-resource (5G_UP_ALG_3639_replaced([11160485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktObIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),"after reception of an CSI report" can only be after the guard period.**

For **FR1 CA with TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD**[End CB008577-D] Scell NRBTS/NRCELL/actBeamforming = true, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will update the Scell status in both downlink and uplink to active both timeout of activation timer and valid target beam avaible for the CA UE.****

For **FR1 CA with SCell NRBTS/NRCELL/actBeamforming = false [CB008577-D]/FDD BF enabled****[End CB008577-D], if SCell status is changed to active, if CoreSet-Id is configured equal 0 in UE-specific Search Space of active BWP (5G_UP_ALG_17926_replaced([11110850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-SfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), a MAC CE for PDCCH TCI state indication (5G_UP_ALG_2103_replaced([11112673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for SCell shall be sent.**

NOTE: Same function as in beamforming case with multiple carriers as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2108_replaced([11112694](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: For UL CA, the MAC CE shall be sent after each SCell RACH procedure. This case is assumed to be covered in the condition "if SCell status is changed to active"**.**

When Scell status is active for FR1 CA, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will take following actions:

 Provide Scell 5G-L2-PS with Scell active status through PsPeerCtrl interface according to 5G_UP_ALG_2683_replaced([11120559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR03PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for related CA UEs.

 When NRBTS/NRCELL/actEnhDtxOptimizedScheduler is set to false or NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler/caSupportEnabled is set to false any UE with the dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class assigned (see 5G_UP_ALG_8549_replaced([11174294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuat9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be switched to the drbTraffic request class instead (see 5G_UP_ALG_4178_replaced([11174242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuaG5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In that case, all associated DTX optimized scheduling timers shall be stopped.

After Scell 5G-L2-PS receives the indication for Scell status update for CA UE for FR1 CA **Scell 5G-L2-PS will:**

  * Update status of Scell in both downlink and uplink to active state for related CA UEs;
  * Start the flow control in the Scell (5G_UP_ALG_5735_replaced([11221101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxzZMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **while including _eTh _av per bearer and_ maxThput according to 5G_UP_ALG_11651_replaced([11192714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CB015535-A]If NRCELL.actFddDlSchedPrevent is equal to true, then for an FDD SCell configured with the DlAndUl mode for FR1 TDD + FDD UL CA scenario, the SCell 5G-L2-PS shall not initiate flow control procedure, consequently the corresponding stop flow control shall not be executed. Start and Stop Flow Control shall not be sent to L2LO for any procedure, including SCell Activation, Suspend, Resume, or Deactivation, occurring between SCell Activation and SCell Deactivation.[End CB015535-A]_****



The status of the SCell for that the deactivation shall be requested, changes at the end of the evaluation period in a first step from active to activeStopped and from activeStopped to inactive after reception of the HARQ ACK feedback corresponding to the transport block carrying the MAC-C element for deactivating the SCell and is kept in state activeStopped if an HARQ NACK is received as feedback from the DL transmission carrying the MAC-C element.

For activated SCells for that the radio link failure is detected shall change the status from active to activeStopped. After clearing the radio link failure, the status shall enter the status active again or inactive after releasing the UE.

In the implementation, both UL PS and DL PS will maintain the carrier activation status separately. DL PS will handle the activation behaviour. And after the status changed, DL PS will inform UL PS by internal interface, and UL PS will update the status and use it from next slot after the internal message is received.

---

##### 3.7.2.7.0-2 Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling Timing of CSI-RS and CSI reporting at SCell Activation/Deactivation (ID: 11121898)

**3.7.2.7.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13327727`)

Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling 13327727: Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling When SCell is deactivated UE does not measure any CSI-RS and does not report any CSI measurements, neither for Beam Management nor for Channel state feedback.

5G-L2-PS does not transmit any UE specific CSI-RS (for channel state feedback) nor request reception of CSI Reports from 5G-L1-UL for the SCells that are deactivated.

This requirement describes the timing in 5G-L2-PS related to the start of the CSI-RS transmission and start of reception of CSI measurement reports at SCell activation and the timing in 5G-L2-PS related to the stop of CSI-RS transmission and the stop of reception of CSI measurement reports at SCell deactivation.

**Beam Management**

For digital beamforming in FR1 (_rrmBeamformingType =_ digitalBf, see 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

  * [CB008577-D] For FDD: PMI beam is from CSI report for channel acquisition. CSI-RS for channel acquisition is cell specific.
  * For TDD:[End CB008577-D] CSI reporting for beam management is done based on SSB (without beam refinement) or based on CSI-RS (with beam refinement)
  * SSB /CSI-RS for beam refinement [CB008577-D]/CSI-RS for channel acquisition [End CB008577-D]are Cell specific and same resources are configured for all the UEs for beam management on PSCell as well as on SCell. These signals are transmitted continuously independently on the SCell activation status.
  * CSI reporting is done on PSCell and UE report only CSI for active SCell.
  * Since in digital beamforming, beam management is done separately for PSCell and Scell, at the time of SCell activation 5G-L2-PS does not have information about the best beam on the SCell until it receives CSI report for beam management [CB008577-D] for TDD or CSI-RS for channel acquisition for FDD [End CB008577-D]. Therefore, 5G-L2-PS shall postpone start of the PDSCH scheduling until the user context is contains valid information about best beam(s). For FR1 CA, Scell [CB008577-D] TDD BF [End CB008577-D] 5G-L2-PS shall get the initial target beam based on 5G_UP_ALG_2017_replaced([11112151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_1992_replaced([11112073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in case Scell actBeamforming = true according to 5G_UP_ALG_2683_replaced([11120559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR03PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CB008577-D] For FR1 CA, Scell FDD BF 5G-L2-PS shall get the initial target beam based on [11112962: PMI beam change procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).[End CB008577-D]
  * At SCell activation (transmission of MAC-CE), 5G-L2-PS shall start requesting SCell related CSI reporting from 5G-L1-UL
  * 5G-L2-PS shall start scheduling PDSCH/PUSCH on that SCell in the UE selected Beam
  * At the time of SCell deactivation (transmission of MAC-CE), 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling PDSCH/PUSCH on that SCell and at the same time 5G-L2-PS shall stop requesting CSI reports related to that SCell form 5G-L1-UL.



For analog beamforming in FR2 (_rrmBeamformingType =_ analogBf, see 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

  * CSI reporting for beam management is done based on SSB only and on PSCell only
  * There is no beam management done on SCells
  * When SCells are activated they are scheduled by the same beam as the one used on PSCell



**Channel State Feedback**

Applicable for both digital and analog beamforming:

  * **CSI-RS for channel state feedback are Cell specific or if Scell is FDD , and these signals are transmitted on SCell as long as any UE is configured with such signals, and it's independent on the SCell activation status.**
  * CSI-RS for channel state feedback are UE specific and transmission of those signals is stopped with the SCell deactivation and started when SCell is activated.
  * At the time of SCell activation (transmission of MAC-CE), 5G-L2-PS shall start transmission of UE specific CSI-RS for channel state feedback on that SCell and 5G-L2-PS shall start requesting CSI reports related to that SCell form 5G-L1-UL once target beam is available based on 5G_UP_ALG_2017_replaced([11112151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_1992_replaced([11112073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in case Scell actBeamforming = true according to 5G_UP_ALG_2683_replaced([11120559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR03PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * 5G-L2-PS can start scheduling on PDSCH/PUSCH at the _sCellActivationPeriod expiry (see 5G_UP_ALG_2792_replaced([11121815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) even if CSI-RS for channel state management is not yet received [CB008577-D] on scell with TDD BF enabled [End CB008577-D]. In that case initial MCS is applied until CSI-RS is received and LA update used MCS based on the received CQI. When dlMimoMode 'OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO' or 'CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO', default precoder settings are given by 5G_UP_ALG_3183_replaced([11139297](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._
  * At the time of SCell deactiavtion (transmission of MAC-CE), 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling PDSCH/PUSCH on that SCell and at the same time 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling UE specific CSI-RS for channel state management and requesting corresponding CSI reports related to deactivated SCell form 5G-L1-UL.



**Notes:**

  * For FR1 CA, if SCell is configured with cell specific CSI-RS, CSI-RS for channel state feedback is transmitted even SCell is not activated, so UE may measure CSI-RS and feedback CSI report for channel acquisition before beam report. In such case, SCell [CB008577-D] with TDD BF enabled [End CB008577-D] 5G-L2-PS shall not start scheduling on PDSCH until target beam is available and TCI state indication MAC CE is sent to UE.
  * Retrieving SSB information from PMI beam is left for further feature.

  * There is a **rare case that the first pCSI report after SCell activation will be detected as DTX: HARQ-ACK of SCell activation / deactivation MAC CE is received after the CSI-RS transmission and before the slot in which the first pCSI of SCell after activation shall be reported, an example is shown in the figure below:  
[image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the timing of SCell activation and related events in a cellular network. The diagram is divided into two main horizontal sections, labeled "PCell" and "SCell," representing two different cells. A horizontal axis labeled "time" runs across the bottom of the diagram. In the "PCell" section:

  * At time 147.2, "SCell activation MAC CE is Transmitted". This is indicated by a downward arrow from the time axis.
  * Following this transmission, a blue shaded area labeled "SCell activation timer" starts and gradually decreases in length towards the right, indicating the timer is running down.
  * At time 147.14, "HARQ-ACK of SCell activation MAC CE received". This is shown by a downward arrow originating from the end of the blue timer bar.
  * At time 153.4, "SCell activation timer expires". This is marked by an upward arrow.
  * Just before the timer expires, at time 153.14, a yellow speech bubble indicates "PCSI for SCell is expected".
  * Immediately after the timer expires, a yellow starburst shape with a jagged edge declares "PCSI is detected as DTX!". This implies that the expected PCSI was not received or was corrupted, leading to a DTX (Discontinuous Transmission) detection. In the "SCell" section:
  * At time 146.0, "CSI-RS in SCell is transmitted". This is indicated by a downward arrow from the time axis.
  * At time 154.0, "CSI-RS in SCell is transmitted". This is indicated by another downward arrow from the time axis. The diagram visually represents a scenario where an SCell is activated, a timer is running, and then the expected PCSI (Physical Cell Shared Information) is detected as DTX, potentially due to issues with the SCell's CSI-RS transmission or reception.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6635.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]  
As the probability of this case is very low and the ratio of DTX due to this reason is also very low, while the effort to avoid this DTX is relatively high, so this case is left as a known issue and unresolved.**



**actBeamforming: NRBTS.NRCELL.actBeamforming**

**dlMimoMode: NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode**

---

##### 3.7.2.7.0-3 Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling SSSG Switching on PCell depending on number of active SCells (ID: 11121912)

**3.7.2.7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11121916`)

Activation Status and Channel Status Information Handling When at least one Scell status is active for FR1 CA, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall stop SSSG Switching for any UE for which the SSSG Switching is configured and switch the UE to the Dense SSSG state (see 5G_UP_ALG_31041_replaced([11168736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktx0y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall resume SSSG Switching for the UE for which all the SCells are deactivated or deconfigured (no active SCell remains).

For the UE in Sparse SSSG state, UE should be excluded from SCell active evaluation algorithm.

#### 3.7.2.8 Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information

##### 3.7.2.8.0-1 Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information Controlling of CA UE in overheated state based on UE overheating assistace information (ID: 11121925)

**3.7.2.8.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11121928`)

Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information When the user is setup or modified and numOfCellConfiguration is greater than one the P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall be aware about the total number of active SCell(s) [CB006137-BB] in downlink and uplink separately [End CB006137-BB].

When the SCell is successfully activated or deactivated according to 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2 PS shall update the total number of active SCells ([Before CB006137-BB] NumofActSCells [CB006137-BB] NumofActSCellsDL and NumofActSCellsUL [End CB006137-BB]) and which SCell(s) is/are activated (i.e. shall know the SCell index of active SCell) with RLQ information (“bad”, “good”, see 5G_UP_1342_replaced([11358118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucf3rvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_2767_replaced([11121583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Initial value for the Maximum number of active SCells ([Before CB006137-BB] MaxNumofActiveSCells [CB006137-BB] MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL and MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL [End CB006137-BB]) of the UE shall be set value “not limited”.

Initially the UE overheated state is “False” (UEOverheated [True, False]).

---

on UE overheating assistance information 11121942: Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information When the UE Overheating Assistance measurement is configured for the UE then UE may report its overheating status to gNB. When UE overheating status is received by CP-RT, CP-RT decodes the information as described in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3378_replaced([11323211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TsggnPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and provides Number of SCells (**[Before CB006137-BB]_AllowedNoOfActSCells**[CB006137-BB]_AllowedNoOfActSCellsDL and_ AllowedNoOfActSCellsUL **[End CB006137-BB]) info to L2-PS._****_*_ * **[Before CB006137-BB]**-_AllowedNoOfActSCells **defines how many SCells can be active when the UE is overheated or UE is not overheated (value "not limited")._** **[CB006137-BB]** \-  _AllowedNoOfActSCellsDL_ _defines how many SCells in DL can be active when the UE is overheated or UE is not overheated (value "not limited")._**-_AllowedNoOfActSCellsUL **defines how many SCells in UL can be active when the UE is overheated or UE is not overheated (value "not limited")._** **[End CB006137-BB]** L2-PS shall limit the maximum number of active SCells to value **[Before CB006137-BB]_MaxNumofActiveSCells**[CB006137-BB] *MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL for DL and MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL for UL**[End CB006137-BB] _(if other than "not limited")_ by using MAC CE element as described in the figure below. _If there is need to deactivate less number of active SCells than_ _[Before CB006137-BB]_ NumofActSCells **[CB006137-BB] *NumofActSCellsDL or NumofActSCellsUL**[End CB006137-BB], then candidates for SCell deactivation shall be selected in the order defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2826_replaced([11121946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._****_*_** **_*_** ****[Before CB006137-BB]**[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to UE (User Equipment) configuration and active cells. ##### 3.7.2.8.0-3 Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information SCell candidate selection for deactivation due to UE Overheated (ID: 11121946)

**3.7.2.8.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13424172`)

Overheating protection based on UE overheating assistance information UE may request to reduce the SCell CCs in DL as much as it estimates is enough to avoid overheating. In such case it could be that there is no need to deactivate all the active SCells and for that reason L2-PS shall select which SCell(s) must be deactivated in priority order.

L2-PS shall select the SCell(s) for deactivation as many as required to meet the value of _MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL and MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL in the following order:_

  1. SCell(s) in overheating state as defined in ([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

  2. If there is more SCells in overheating state than required for deactivation (for fulfil the _MaxNumofActiveSCellsDL and MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL_ _requirement), they all shall be deactivated._ **

  3. **If _MaxNumofActiveSCellsUL < NumofActSCellsUL, the SCell with uplink activated shall be deactivated [CB014067-B] in the order from the lowest to the highest value of {SCell's Available UL Resources (AUR) * BWPratio}  
where:  
\- AUR calculation follows ([13388195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QW2dJAKoEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)),  
\- BWPratio = SCell_BW_of_dedicated_BWP_configured_currently_for_UE / SCell_BW_of_largest_dedicated_BWP.  
[End CB014067-B]_**

  4. RLQ of SCell(s) status of bad in downlink **(good/bad, as defined in ([11121583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

  5. DL only **SCells in the order from lowest to highest value of {SCell's Available DL Resources (ADR) * BWPratio},  
where:  
\- ADR calculation follows ([11121583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZJmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),  
\- BWPratio = SCell_BW_of_dedicated_BWP_configured_currently_for_UE / SCell_BW_of_largest_dedicated_BWP.**




The SCell with uplink activated is listed in the last.

  1. SCells in the order from highest sCellIndex to lowest sCellIndex.



**Note: This selection algorithm is used only for SCell deactivation when there is room for active SCell(s).**

---

#### 3.7.2.9 Limit Number of CA UEs with activated SCells

##### 3.7.2.9.0-1 Limit Number of CA UEs with activated SCells Controlling of number of CA UEs could have Scell activation (ID: 11121957)

**3.7.2.9.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11121966`)

Limit Number of CA UEs with activated SCells L2 PS shall limit the number of UEs with one or more activated SCells to [Before CB012528-D]MaxActiveCaUe(default value is 40)[CB012528-D] subPoolMaxActiveCaUe [End CB012528-D] . Since configuration of more than [Before CB012528-D]MaxActiveCaUe[CB012528-D] subPoolMaxActiveCaUe [End CB012528-D] CA UEs is possible, a mechanism to fulfill this limit is introduced. The number of UEs with active SCell(s) shall be maintained in rrmNumUeActScells. rrmNumUeActScells shall be initialized to 0.

[CB012528-D]

L2 PS shall limit the number of active CA UE number in the UE's PCell to cellMaxActiveCaUe and limit the number of active CA UE number in the UE's L2 subPool to subPoolMaxActiveCaUe.

For non-pooilng cell:

cellMaxActiveCaUe = min(40,MaxActiveCaUe )

subPoolMaxActiveCaUe = min(40,MaxActiveCaUe )

For FR1 FDD pooling Cell:

if actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 is true and actScheUePooling is true

subPoolMaxActiveCaUe = NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumOfCAUserL2SubPool

cellMaxActiveCaUe = min(MaxActiveCaUe, subPoolMaxActiveCaUe);

end

For FR1 TDD pooling Cell:

if actScheUePooling is true

subPoolMaxActiveCaUe = NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumOfCAUserL2SubPool

cellMaxActiveCaUe = min(MaxActiveCaUe, subPoolMaxActiveCaUe,[PR755572], 40 [End PR755572] );

end

Note:MaxActiveCaUe[Before CB012528-D-UPD001] ( default value is 40 [CB012528-D-UPD001] default value is 64, max value is 72)[End CB012528-D-UPD001]as 5G_L2_6836_replaced([11184745](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27tIXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB012528-D]

If NRBTS/NRDU/flexibleCAmode is set to NumberCellAmount (value 3) and there are more than one cells setup in one L2-PS core, [Before CB012528-D]MaxActiveCaUe(default value is 40)[CB012528-D] subPoolMaxActiveCaUe [End CB012528-D]are shared among the cells in the same L2-PS core.

The number of UEs with one or more activated SCells are counted from any of the cells if the cell is Pcell.

The algorithm for limiting the number of UEs with active SCell(s) shall be conservative such that having more than [Before CB012528-D]MaxActiveCaUe(default value is 40)[CB012528-D] subPoolMaxActiveCaUe [End CB012528-D] UEs with active SCell(s) is strictly avoided even for very short periods. Thus, rrmNumUeActScells shall be incremented already before an SCell is activated for a UE having no active SCells yet. This can be done for a corresponding UE either when the activation SCell is triggered by sending the MAC CE or already when the first check for activating the SCell is passed. rrmNumUeActScells shall be decremented again if the SCell for the corresponding UE is not activated due to failing in a following activation check.

When the last active SCell (all active SCells) is deactivated, rrmNumUeActScells shall be decremented as soon as the MAC CE for deactivation is acknowledged.

rrmNumSCellActiveUe shall also be decremented if all active SCells of a UE are released by higher layers , if a UE with active SCell(s) is deleted by higher layers or a UE with active Scell(s) releases.

---

##### 3.7.2.10 SCell Activation/Deactivation in FR1 Inter-gNB DL Carrier Aggregation

###### 3.7.2.10.0-1 SCell Activation/Deactivation in FR1 Inter-gNB DL Carrier Aggregation ext-SCell Activation/Deactivation controlled by OAM setting in prime-gNB and ext-gNB (ID: 11121973)

**3.7.2.10.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11121976`)

SCell Activation/Deactivation in FR1 Inter-gNB DL Carrier Aggregation In Inter-gNB DL CA case, prime-gNB and ext-gNB may be configured with different values of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod

Setting of this parameter is not synchronized between prime-gNB and ext-gNB and consequently:

\- prime-gNB is not aware of configuration of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod in ext-gNB and vice versa

\- there is no consistency check of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod set in prime-gNB and ext-gNB

If UE is not in overheating status and ext-SCell is not in bad Radio Link Quality for the UE:

\- ext-SCell Activation mechanism depends only on setting of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB

\- ext-SCell shall be deactivated due to data inactivity after expiration of SCell Inactivity Deactivation Timer; the timer is configured in the ext-SCell via NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB

 if prime-gNB is configured with NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod = blind and ext-SCell is configured with NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellDeactivationTimerGNB != infinity, ext-SCells deactivated due to data inactivity shall not be re-activated again.

---

|  |  |   
---|---|---|---

CPRI + eCPRI | 0 |  |

|  |  |   
The delay threshold for Xp-U link monitoring in SCell is decided by corresponding delay threshold **configured in PCell and the offset derived from {PCell tech, SCell tech, PCell FHT + SCell FHT} configuration combination.** |  |  |   
|  |  |   
For example: in case PCell is a TDD cell and PCell front haul type is eCPRI, SCell is a FDD cell and the front haul type is CPRI, the actual delay threshold used for Xp-U link monitoring in the SCell is given by rdMsgDelayThreshSCellTdd (5G_UP_ALG_13334_replaced([11124236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpBN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (**configured in TDD PCell) + delay threshold offset in SCell for the {PCell tech, SCell tech, PCell FHT + SCell FHT} = {TDD, FDD, eCPRI + CPRI} combination.** |  |  |   
|  |  |   
Note: |  |  |   
1\. The “delay threshold offset for PCell” and “delay threshold offset for SCell” are hardcoded and identical in all gNBs. |  |  |   
2\. PCell L2PS sends the delay threshold for delay monitoring in SCell and PCell front haul type to SCell, and SCell compute the actual delay threshold according to the received PCell configuration together with its local configuration (SCell tech, SCell front haul type). |  |  |   
3\. SCell front haul type shall also be informed to PCell so that PCell L2PS can determine the delay threshold to be applied at PCell side; |  |  |   
|  |  |   
**[CB009103-E]** |  |  |   
Starting from 26R1, time margin is used to decide whether the end to end delay is acceptable for inter-gNB CA instead of message delay calculated from receiving slot number and sending slot number. |  |  |   
Time margin of the monitored message is the gap between the time when the information in the received message is used and the time when the message is received, unit of time margin is micro-second. If the monitored message for current DPA cycle is still not received when the included information shall be used, then the time margin shall be set to -1. |  |  |   
If margin of monitored message >= marginThreshold + marginOffset, then end to end delay is acceptable for inter-gNB CA; otherwise, end to end delay is too high for inter-gNB CA, large delay is detected. |  |  |   
|  |  |   
marginThreshold is defined by R&D parameter for each CA configuration: |  |  |   
|  |   
---|---|---  
PCell technology | Used in which serving cell | R&D parameter  
FDD | PCell | rdS2PmarginThreshFddPCell (5G_UP_ALG_32149_replaced([11124389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqqPX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  
SCell | rdP2SmarginThreshFddPCell (5G_UP_ALG_32153_replaced([11124409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqqPbfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |   
TDD | PCell | rdS2PmarginThreshTddPCell (5G_UP_ALG_32151_replaced([11124398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqqPa_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  
SCell | rdP2SmarginThreshTddPCell (5G_UP_ALG_32155_replaced([11124417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqqPb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |   
The marginThreshold for delay monitoring in SCell is decided by rdP2SmarginThreshXddPCell configured in PCell. |  |   
|  |   
marginOffset is the difference between the delayTolerance of the monitored message and the most time critical message: marginOffset = delayTolerance of monitored message – delayTolerance of the most time critical message. marginOffset is different for each {PCell technology, PCell front haul type, SCell technology, SCell front haul type} combination. margin offsets are hardcoded as the following table. |  |   
marginOffset used in PCell (SCell to PCell direction) |  |   
|  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---  
PCell technology | PCell front haul | SCell technology | SCell front haul | marginOffset (w/o UL CA) | marginOffset (w/ UL CA)  
FDD | CPRI | FDD | CPRI | 0 | 0  
FDD | eCPRI | 0 | 0 |  |   
TDD | CPRI | 500 | 500 |  |   
TDD | eCPRI | 500 | 500 |  |   
eCPRI | FDD | CPRI | 0 | 0 |   
FDD | eCPRI | 0 | 0 |  |   
TDD | CPRI | 0 | 500 |  |   
TDD | eCPRI | 0 | 500 |  |   
TDD | CPRI | FDD | CPRI | 500 | 1500  
FDD | eCPRI | 500 | 1500 |  |   
TDD | CPRI | 1000 | 2000 |  |   
TDD | eCPRI | 1000 | 2000 |  |   
eCPRI | FDD | CPRI | 500 | 1000 |   
FDD | eCPRI | 500 | 1000 |  |   
TDD | CPRI | 1000 | 1500 |  |   
TDD | eCPRI | 1000 | 1500 |  |   
Derivation of the margin offset can be found in note4. |  |  |  |  |   
|  |  |  |  |   
marginOffset used in SCell (PCell to SCell direction) is 0 for any configuration. Rationale: |  |  |  |  |   
* The most time critical message (PUCCH pre-allocation indication) is monitored in the PCell to SCell direction. |  |  |  |  |   
* The timing of the monitored message does not change no matter UL CA is active for current UE or not. |  |  |  |  |   
[Before CB009103-E-UPD003]  |  |  |  |  |   
Actual threshold for Xp-U link monitoring in PCell in each case is shown in the following table: |  |  |  |  |   
|  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---  
UE has active DL&UL SCell? | NRDUL. fr1UlCaPreferred | Xp-U link status | UL scheduling in DL&UL SCell suspended? | threshold that shall be used  
N | any | any | NA | marginThreshold + marginOffset w/o UL CA  
Y | dataRatePreferred | available | N | marginThreshold + marginOffset with UL CA  
Y | marginThreshold + marginOffset w/o UL CA |  |  |   
unavailable | NA | marginThreshold + marginOffset w/o UL CA |  |   
ulCaPreferred | any | NA | marginThreshold + marginOffset with UL CA |   
[End CB009103-E-UPD003] |  |  |  |   
In 5G_UP_ALG_12815_replaced([11122016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_12816_replaced([11122039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_12817_replaced([11122057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), “marginThreshold with UL CA” means “marginThreshold + marginOffset with UL CA”; “marginThreshold without UL CA” means "marginThreshold + marginOffset without UL CA”. |  |  |  |   
|  |  |  |

2\. **Middle Left Callout:** "PcellPucchPreallocationlnd is used by ext-SCell L2PS, time stamp: 2950 us; As no valid receiving time stamp, margin = -1 < actualMargin Threshold delay is too high". It describes a situation where the received timestamp is invalid, leading to a negative margin and indicating a high delay. |  |  |  |

The timeline is labeled with "Time" and an arrow indicating the direction of time.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6655.005.png[/image_path][/image-4] |  |  |  |   
Notes: |  |  |  |   
1\. PCell shall send the rdP2SmarginThresholdXddPCell to SCell, and SCell shall use the received threshold for Xp-U link delay monitoring. |  |  |  |   
2\. SCell front haul type shall also be provided to PCell so that PCell can determine the margin offset to be applied at PCell side; |  |  |  |   
3\. Theoretically speaking, in case the monitored message is the most critical message (the message with smallest delay tolerance), the margin threshold is 0 micro-second, that is, if the time margin of received message > 0, then the latency on Xp-U link is sufficiently low to support inter-gNB CA. In case the monitored message isn’t the most critical message, then the margin threshold = delay tolerance of the monitored message - delay tolerance of the most critical message. If the time margin of received message is higher than margin threshold + margin offset, then the latency on Xp-U link is sufficiently low to support inter-gNB CA. But for the convenience of performance tuning, margin thresholds are still provisioned with R&D parameters. |  |  |  |   
4\. Delay tolerance estimation of the messages for inter-gNB CA can be found in the following file: inter_gNB_CA_delay_tolerance.pptx, URL: |  |  |  |   
|  |  |  |   
**[End CB009103-E]** |  |  |  |

###### 3.7.2.10.1.0-2 ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ Xp-U link delay monitoring in PCell when Xp-U link state is ‘available’ (ID: 11122016)

**3.7.2.10.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13241488`)

ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241488: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ In case an Xp-U link between PCell and ext-SCell is setup, after first configuration of inter-gNB DL CA for a UE which is served by {PCell, ext-SCell} pair, PCell L2-PS shall monitor the delay over the Xp-U link between prime gNB and external gNB. Xp-U link delay shall be monitored for each {PCell, SCell} pair. [CB014119-E] For a cell acting as PCell of inter-gNB CA UE, one state machine (SM) shall be maintained for each {PCell, ext-SCell} pair for the delay monitoring in the direction from ext-SCell to PCell. [End CB014119-E] If Xp-U link is available from PCell point of view (5G_UP_5999_replaced([11356802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucaYG_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PCell shall monitor Xp-U link by counting number of large delay detections in each Xp-U link monitoring period (rdLnkDelayMonitorPeriod, 5G_UP_ALG_12827_replaced([11124183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If time margin of a DPA measurement report message is less than corresponding margin threshold plus margin offset (5G_UP_ALG_13314_replaced([11121985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then a large delay is detected. At the end of each Xp-U link monitoring period, if number of large delay detections in current link monitoring period is larger than rdMsgDelayedCntThresh (5G_L2_8644_replaced([11184805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27tvZ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then PCell should act according to the following state machine. To ease the description, 2 types of CA UEs are defined below: Type1: all SCells of a CA UE are DL only SCell, at least 1 activated SCell is an ext-SCell, denote this case as case1 in state machine. Type2: one activated SCell is DL&UL SCell, at least 1 activated SCell is an ext-SCell; denote this case as case2 in state machine. If marginThreshold with UL CA = marginThreshold without UL CA, the following state machine (SM1) is used to monitor Xp-U link delay in PCell: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a delay monitoring system. The title of the flowchart is "SM1: delay monitoring in PCell if marginThresholdWithUICa = marginThresholdWithoutUICa". There are three main states depicted: "largeDelay" (in a red rounded rectangle), "normal" (in a green rounded rectangle), and two trigger/action boxes (in light blue rectangles with yellow headers). The "largeDelay" state has an upward arrow pointing to it, originating from the bottom. There are two trigger/action boxes. The "normal" state has an arrow pointing to it from the top trigger/action box and an arrow pointing away from it to the bottom trigger/action box. The flowchart depicts a system that monitors time margins relative to a threshold. If the time margin exceeds the threshold, it triggers an action to re-activate "ext-SCell" and transitions to a "normal" state. If the time margin falls below the threshold, it triggers an action to deactivate "ext-SCell" and transitions back to the "largeDelay" state. Special handling when FSM state is “Intermediate”: |  |  |   
* When a DL&UL SCell or an ext-SCell is activated for a UE: |  |  |   
If (UE has both activated DL&UL SCell and activated ext-SCell after the activation) |  |  |   
{ |  |  |   
If (fr1UlCaPreferred == dataRatePreferred) |  |  |   
{ |  |  |   
Suspend UL scheduling in the DL&UL SCell. |  |  |   
} |  |  |   
Else //ulCaPreferred |  |  |   
{ |  |  |   
Deactivated the ext-SCell of UE. |  |  |   
} |  |  |   
} |  |  |   
FSM remains in “Intermediate” state. |  |  |   
* When the last ext-SCell on the Xp-U link is deactivated for a UE: |  |  |   
If (fr1UlCaPreferred == dataRatePreferred && UE has an activated DL&UL SCell) |  |  |   
{ |  |  |   
Try to resume UL scheduling in DL&UL SCell for this UE. |  |  |   
} |  |  |   
FSM remains in “Intermediate” state. |  |  |   
* When all DL&UL SCell are deactivated for a UE: |  |  |   
If (fr1UlCaPreferred == ulCaPreferred && UE has deactivated ext-SCell) |  |  |   
{ |  |  |   
Re-activate ext-SCell for this UE. |  |  |   
} |  |  |   
FSM remains in “Intermediate” state. |  |  |   
* When NRDU.fr1UlCaPreferred is updated online from “dataRatePreferred” to “ulCaPreferred”: |  |  |   
For type 1 CA UE(s): no action. |  |  |   
For type 2 CA UE(s): |  |  |   
Deactivate ext-SCell; |  |  |   
Try to resume UL scheduling in DL&UL SCell. |  |  |   
FSM remains in “Intermediate” state. |  |  |   
* When NRDU.fr1UlCaPreferred is updated online from “ulCaPreferred” to “dataRatePreferred”: |  |  |   
For type1 CA UE(s): no action. |  |  |   
For type2 CA UE(s): |  |  |   
Re-activate ext-SCell; |  |  |   
Suspend UL scheduling in DL&UL SCell. |  |  |   
FSM remains in “Intermediate” state. |  |  |   
[CB014119-E] |  |  |

{ |  |  |

{ |  |  |   
Re-activate ([11122068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) all ext-SCell on the Xp link. |  |  |   
Xp link remains in “Intermediate” state. |  |  |   
} |  |  |   
} |  |  |   
} |  |  |

For type2 CA UEs using current cell as PCell: |  |  |   
For (each Xp link in ‘intermediate’ state) |  |  |   
{ |  |  |   
Deactivate all ext-SCell on the ‘intermediate’ Xp link. |  |  |   
Xp link remains in ‘intermediate’ state. |  |  |

Notes: |  |  |   
1\. In SM2, time margin of DPA measurement report message shall be compared against both margin threshold without UL CA and margin threshold with UL CA in all the 3 states, that is both thresholds are used in each state of the state machine. |  |  |   
2\. When UL scheduling in the DL&UL SCell shall be suspended due to persistent large delay on Xp-U link, it shall be suspended irrespective of other conditions. When UL scheduling in the DL&UL SCell shall be resumed due to decrease of Xp-U link delay, it can be resumed only if all other existing conditions also allow the resumption. |  |  |   
3\. File of state machine for Xp-U link delay monitoring can be found at the following link: [RAN A&S- 5G-CB & 2/3/4G Spec. Repository of Architecture and Specification - TechnicalReference - All Documents](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/Forms/AllItems.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2FASCOP%2FAS%20Documents%2FFS1TAs%2DCFAMs%2FCB%2FCB009000%20%2D%20CB009499%2FCFAM%2FCB009103%20Inter%2DgNB%20FR1%20DL%20CA%20with%20SCells%20across%20multiple%20gNBs%2FTechnicalReference&viewid=73435348%2D8379%2D4262%2Da3aa%2Dffe0b7322e0c&newTargetListUrl=%2Fsites%2FASCOP%2FAS%20Documents&viewpath=%2Fsites%2FASCOP%2FAS%20Documents%2FForms%2FAllItems%2Easpx&PHY&noAuthRedirect=1) |  |  |
