###### 3.7.2.10.1.0-3 ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ Xp-U link delay monitoring in SCell when Xp-U link state is ‘available’ (ID: 11122039)

**3.7.2.10.1.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `13241494`)

ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ 13241494: ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ In case an Xp-U link between PCell and ext-SCell is setup, after first configuration of inter-gNB DL CA for a UE which is served by {PCell, ext-SCell} pair, ext-SCell L2-PS shall monitor the delay over the Xp-U link between prime gNB and external gNB. Xp-U link delay shall be monitored for each {PCell, ext-SCell} pair. [CB014119-E] For a cell acting as external SCell of inter-gNB CA UE, one state machine shall be maintained for each {PCell, ext-SCell} pair for the delay monitoring in the direction from PCell to ext-SCell. [End CB014119-E] If Xp-U link is available from ext-SCell point of view (5G_UP_5999_replaced([11356802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucaYG_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), ext-SCell shall monitor Xp-U link by counting number of large delay detections in each monitoring period (rdLnkDelayMonitorPeriod, 5G_UP_ALG_12827_replaced([11124183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If time margin of a PUCCH pre-allocation indication message is less than corresponding margin threshold (5G_UP_ALG_13314_replaced([11121985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then a large delay is detected. At the end of each Xp-U link monitoring period, if number of large delay detections in current monitoring period is larger than rdMsgDelayedCntThresh (5G_L2_8644_replaced([11184805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27tvZ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then: {  ext-SCell L2-PS changes the Xp-U link state to ‘unavailable’,  DL scheduling in SCell shall be suspended immediately  the ext-SCell L2-PS shall send its Xp-U link status indication as ‘unavailable’ (with request to deactivate) to PCell L2-PS  PCell L2-PS shall determine the Xp-U link state as ‘unavailable’ for this particular {PCell, ext-SCell} pair (5G_UP_5999_replaced([11356802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucaYG_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PM counter IGNB_XPU_LINK_UUSBL shall be pegged in the PCell, Note, the counter IGNB_XPU_LINK_UUSBL will be pegged only in case it hasn’t been incremented yet due to detection of Xp-U link unavailability for this {PCell, ext-SCell} pair on PCell side (5G_UP_ALG_12815_replaced([11122016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  PCell L2-PS shall indicate the Xp-U link status ('unavailable') to prime CP-RT .  PCell L2-PS shall command ext-SCell L2PS to deactivate the ext-SCell (regardless of setting of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB). } In order to facilitate continuous Xp-U link delay monitoring, the PCell L2-PS shall send a dummy PUCCH pre-allocation message to each SCell for the first slot of the bundle window of each scheduling period at the end of DPA split process when DPA split functionality (refer to rdDynamicPucchAlloSplitEnable 5G_UP_ALG_24678_replaced([11124282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled, if there is no real pre-allocation message for that SCell for the first slot of the bundle window; i.e., PCell shall ensure that there is a message, dummy or real for the first slot of the bundle window of each scheduling period for each SCell. Rationale: If there is always a message for the first slot of the bundle window, between two adjacent scheduling cycles for the same SCell it helps in continuous Xp-U link monitoring by ensuring that in the whole receiving period at SCell at least one message is received always which is corresponding to the first slot of the bundle window; there is no need to send dummy message for subsequent slots in the same bundle window if there is no real allocation. Xp-U link delay monitoring in ext-SCell can be done according to the following state machine (SM3): [image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a delay monitoring system in ext-SCell. The flowchart has three main states: "largeDelay" (red rounded rectangle), "normal" (green rounded rectangle), and two trigger/action boxes (yellow and light blue rectangles). The title of the flowchart is "SM3: delay monitoring in ext-SCell". There are two main processes depicted: 1\. **From "largeDelay" to a trigger/action box:** * An arrow points from "largeDelay" to a box with two sections: "Trigger" and "Action". * The "Trigger" section contains the text: "timeMargin > marginThresholdWithoutUICa". * The "Action" section contains the text: "Both cases: change link status to \"available\" and notify PCell". * An arrow then points from this trigger/action box to the "normal" state. 2\. **From "normal" to a trigger/action box:** * An arrow points from the "normal" state to another box with two sections: "Trigger" and "Action". * The "Trigger" section contains the text: "timeMargin < marginThresholdWithoutUICa". * The "Action" section contains the text: "Both cases: suspend DL scheduling, change link status to \"unavailable\" and notify PCell". * An arrow then points from this trigger/action box back to the "largeDelay" state. The flowchart visually represents a feedback loop where the system transitions between a "largeDelay" state and a "normal" state based on the `timeMargin` relative to `marginThresholdWithoutUICa`. When the `timeMargin` is greater than the threshold, the system aims to return to a "normal" state by making the link available. When the `timeMargin` is less than the threshold, the system enters a "largeDelay" state, suspending DL scheduling and marking the link as unavailable.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-01141721.png[/image_path][/image-0] When Xp-U link is available:

|  |  |   
---|---|---|---  
Current state | Trigger conditions | Actions | Target state  
Normal | timeMargin < marginThresholdWithoutUlCa | Link unavailable actions in ext-SCell: * Change link status to “unavailable” * Suspend DL scheduling * Send Xp-U link status indication (“unavailable”) to PCell | largeDelay  
Notes: |  |  |   
1\. Timing and delay tolerance estimation of DPA PUCCH pre-allocation indication messages can be found at: |  |  |   
2\. As the same margin threshold is used for Xp-U link monitoring in the PCell to SCell direction no matter UE has active DL&UL SCell or not, the action to be taken is always deactivating the ext-SCell when persistent large delay is detected. This behaviour is different from that for PCell when persistent large delay is detected. |  |  |

---

###### 3.7.2.10.1.0-4 ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ (ID: 11122057)

**3.7.2.10.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11122065`)

ext-SCell deactivation due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ For each UE configured with ext-SCell(s), when Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’ is determined by PCell, [Before CB008451-C-UPD001][CB008451-C] or when synchronous state change to ‘OutOfSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22304_replaced([11174858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),[End CB008451-C][End CB008451-C-UPD001] PCell L2-PS shall start the SCell deactivation procedure for corresponding ext-SCell (regardless of setting of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB) and mark this ext-SCell as no longer available for activation when buffer based SCell activation is triggered, that is, corresponding ext-SCell remains deactivated. PM counter: IGNB_SCELL_DEACT_XPU_LNK_UUSBL shall be pegged for each ext-SCell deactivated due to Xp-U link state change to ‘unavailable’.

Note that the Xp-U link state ‘unavailable’ can be detected by both PCell and/or ext-SCell at the same time or in different time.

In case ext-SCell L2-PS detects the Xp-U link state ‘unavailable’ before PCell, ext-SCell L2-PS shall send a status indication to PCell L2-PS, requesting deactivation due to Xp-U link state ‘unavailable’, to which the PCell L2-PS triggers deactivation.

In case the PCell L2-PS detects the Xp-U link state ‘unavailable’ before ext-SCell L2-PS, PCell L2-PS triggers deactivation procedure.

No matter which side detects the delay first, the procedure of deactivation of the ext-SCell shall be started by PCell only.

Note that due to Xp-U link delay (causing state change to ‘unavailable’), the peer-to-peer messages between the PCell and ext-SCell L2-PS may get delayed which in turn delays the SCell Deactivation procedure. It is left to the implementation to fasten the delay detection in order to minimize data loss.

---

###### 3.7.2.10.2 ext-SCell re-activation due to recovery of Xp-U link state to 'available'

###### 3.7.2.10.2.0-1 ext-SCell re-activation due to recovery of Xp-U link state to 'available' Xp-U link recovery monitoring in PCell and ext-SCell when Xp-U link state is 'unavailable' (ID: 11122072)

**3.7.2.10.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13241504`)

ext-SCell re-activation due to recovery of Xp-U link state to 'available' In case Xp-U link between PCell and ext-SCell is(are) setup and has(have) ‘unavailable’ state (5G_UP_ALG_12815_replaced([11122016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_12816_replaced([11122039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for purpose of Xp-U link recovery to ‘available’ state L2-PS instances of PCell and ext-SCell shall monitor the latency over this(these) Xp-U link(s).

Xp-U link latency is monitored independently for each of these ext-SCell [CB014119-E] no matter if these ext-SCell are hosted by the same ext-gNB or different ext-gNB. A dedicated state machine shall be maintained for each {PCell, ext-SCell} pair both in PCell for the direction from ext-SCell to PCell and in ext-SCell for the direction from PCell to ext-SCell. [End CB014119-E].

Xp-U link monitoring for Xp-U link recovery reuses DPA messages:

a) DPA measurement reports sent to PCell L2-PS by each ext-SCell and

b) DPA dummy PUCCH pre-allocation messages (defined in 5G_UP_ALG_12816_replaced([11122039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) sent by PCell L2-PS to each ext-SCell (see Note)

If all DPA measurement reports received by PCell L2-PS from the given ext-SCell and all DPA dummy PUCCH pre-allocation messages received by this ext-SCell arrive not later than DPA expected time (margin > margin threshold + margin offset, 5G_UP_ALG_13314_replaced([11121985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the Xp-U link monitoring period (rdConsecPeriodForLnkRecovery * rdLnkDelayMonitorPeriod, 5G_UP_ALG_14310_replaced([11124249](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpBOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_12827_replaced([11124183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PCell L2-PS and ext-SCell L2-PS consider this particular Xp-U link as recovered and change their Xp-U link state to ‘available’. Ext-SCell sends its Xp-U link status indication to PCell L2-PS and Xp-U link is considered as ‘available’. PCell L2-PS shall determine the Xp-U link as ‘available’ for this particular {PCell, ext-SCell} pair (5G_UP_5999_replaced([11356802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucaYG_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PM counter IGNB_XPU_LINK_USBL shall be pegged in the PCell.

PCell L2-PS shall indicate the Xp-U link status (recovered) to prime CP-RT and initiate further procedure for this particular ext-SCell on the recovered Xp-U link. The procedure initiated by PCell L2-PS depends on NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod set in prime-gNB:

a) if sCellActivationMethod = bufferBased, the ext-SCell shall be considered for evaluation of buffer based SCell Activation (5G_UP_ALG_14021_replaced([11122085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcz8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

b) if sCellActivationMethod = blind, the ext-SCell shall be re-activated immediately (5G_UP_ALG_14021_replaced([11122085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcz8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Xp-U link delay monitoring in PCell shall be done according to the state machine defined in [11122016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_wdn2IvvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

When Xp-U link is unavailable:

If marginThrehsoldWithUlCa = marginThresholdWithoutUlCa, SM1 shall be used:

|  |  |   
---|---|---|---  
Current state | Trigger conditions | Actions | Target state  
largeDelay | timeMargin > marginThresholdWithoutUlCa | Link recovery actions in PCell: * Change Xp-U link state to “available” * PM counter IGNB_XPU_LINK_USBL is pegged * Indicate Xp-U link status (recovered) to prime CP-RT * Ext-SCell on the link is eligible for activation | normal  
  
If marginThrehsoldWithUlCa > marginThresholdWithoutUlCa, SM2 shall be used:

|  |  |   
---|---|---|---  
Current state | Trigger conditions | Actions | Target state  
largeDelay | timeMargin > marginThresholdWithUlCa | For both case1 and case2: Link recovery actions in PCell: * Change Xp-U link state to “available” * Peg PM counter IGNB_XPU_LINK_USBL * Indicate Xp-U link status (recovered) to prime CP-RT * Ext-SCell on the link is eligible for activation ~~​​​​​​[CB014119-E]~~ ~~For case2 only:~~ ~~If (fr1UlCaPreferred == dataRatePreferred)~~ ~~{~~ ~~If (no active SCell on any intermediate Xp link)~~ ~~{~~ ~~Try to resume UL scheduling in DL&UL SCell.~~ ~~}~~ ~~}~~ ~~[End CB014119-E]​~~ | Normal  
largeDelay | timeMargin > marginThresholdWithoutUlCa | Case1: Link recovery actions in PCell. Case2: If (fr1UlCaPreferred == dataRatePreferred) Link recovery actions in PCell else //ulCaPreferred Link recovery actions in PCell except re-activation of ext-SCell. | Intermediate  
  
Xp-U link delay monitoring in SCell shall be done according to the state machine defined [11122039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_wofpYPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) (SM3).

When Xp-U link is “unavailable”:

|  |  |   
---|---|---|---  
Current state | Trigger conditions | Actions | Target state  
largeDelay | timeMargin > marginThresholdWithoutUlCa | Link recovery actions in ext-SCell: * Change Xp-U link state to “available” * Send Xp-U link status indication (available) to PCell | normal  
  
Note:

PCell L2-PS monitors the message transmission delay based on the time stamp included in the CS1 attempt ratio measurement report message sent by ext-SCell L2-PS every 10 msec. The messages containing the DPA dummy PUCCH pre-allocation and DPA measurement reports are exchanged by L2-PS instances of PCell and ext-SCell even though the ext-SCell is deactivated or no UE is configured with this ext-SCell.

---

###### 3.7.2.10.2.0-2 ext-SCell re-activation due to recovery of Xp-U link state to 'available' ext-SCell re-activation due to recovery of Xp link state to 'available' (ID: 11122085)

**3.7.2.10.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11122092`)

ext-SCell re-activation due to recovery of Xp-U link state to 'available' For each UE configured with ext-SCell(s) for which Xp-U link recovery to 'available' state is detected by both PCell L2-PS and ext-SCell L2PS (5G_UP_ALG_14019_replaced([11122072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM7vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [Before CB008451-C-UPD001][CB008451-C] or for each UE configured with ext-SCell(s) when synchronous state change to ‘InSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22306_replaced([11174867](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008451-C] [End CB008451-C-UPD001] and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB is set to ‘bufferBased’ or 'bufferAndRLQualityBased', PCell L2-PS shall start considering this(these) ext-SCell(s) for evaluation of buffer-based SCell Activation.

When evaluation of DL buffer status requests for SCell Activation (5G_UP_ALG_2716_replaced([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and SCell Selection for SCell Activation (5G_UP_ALG_2724_replaced([11121256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) selects the ext-SCell(s) on the recovered Xp-U link [Before CB008451-C-UPD001][CB008451-C] or synchronous state of {PCell, ext-SCell(s)} pair change to ‘InSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22306_replaced([11174867](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008451-C][End CB008451-C-UPD001], PCell L2-PS shall:

a) start SCell re-activation over recovered Xp-U link [Before CB008451-C-UPD001][CB008451-C] or synchronous state of {PCell, ext-SCell(s)} pair change to ‘InSync’ [End CB008451-C][End CB008451-C-UPD001] towards this particular ext-SCell L2-PS

b) trigger re-activations of the ext-SCell via SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC CE sent towards UE

For each UE configured with ext-SCell(s) for which Xp-U link recovery to 'available' state is detected by both PCell L2-PS and ext-SCell L2PS (5G_UP_ALG_14019_replaced([11122072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM7vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ) [Before CB008451-C-UPD001][CB008451-C] or for each UE configured with ext-SCell(s) when synchronous state change to ‘InSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22306_replaced([11174867](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008451-C][End CB008451-C-UPD001] and sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB is set to 'blind', PCell L2-PS shall:

a) start SCell re-activation over recovered Xp-U link [Before CB008451-C-UPD001][CB008451-C] or synchronous state of {PCell, ext-SCell(s)} pair change to ‘InSync’ [End CB008451-C][End CB008451-C-UPD001] towards this particular ext-SCell L2-PS

b) trigger re-activations of the ext-SCell via SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC CE sent towards UE

###### 3.7.2.10.3 ext-SCell deactivation due to synchronous state change to ‘OutOfSync’

###### 3.7.2.10.3.0-1 ext-SCell deactivation due to synchronous state change to ‘OutOfSync’ (ID: 11122100)

**3.7.2.10.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11122104`)

ext-SCell deactivation due to synchronous state change to ‘OutOfSync’ For each UE configured with ext-SCell(s), when synchronous state change to ‘OutOfSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22304_replaced([11174858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PCell's 5G-L2-PS shall start the SCell deactivation procedure for corresponding ext-SCell (regardless of setting of NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB) and mark this ext-SCell as no longer available for activation when buffer based SCell activation is triggered, that is, corresponding ext-SCell remains deactivated.

**3.7.2.10.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11122115`)

ext-SCell re-activation due to synchronous state change to ‘InSync’ For each UE configured with ext-SCell(s) for each UE configured with ext-SCell(s) when synchronous state change to ‘InSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22306_replaced([11174867](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB is set to ‘bufferBased’ or 'bufferAndRLQualityBased', PCell's 5G-L2-PS shall start considering this(these) ext-SCell(s) for evaluation of buffer-based SCell Activation.

b) trigger re-activations of the ext-SCell via SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC CE sent towards UE

For each UE configured with ext-SCell(s) for each UE configured with ext-SCell(s) when synchronous state change to ‘InSync’ (5G_UP_ALG_22306_replaced([11174867](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_YvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and sCellActivationMethod in prime-gNB is set to 'blind', PCell's 5G-L2-PS shall:

b) trigger re-activations of the ext-SCell via SCell Activation/Deactivation MAC CE sent towards UE

##### 3.7.2.11 SCell Activation/Deactivation in Presence of UL Slot Aggregation

###### 3.7.2.11.0-1 SCell Activation/Deactivation in Presence of UL Slot Aggregation Activation/Deactivation of SCells Based on Slot Aggregation State (ID: 11122124)

**3.7.2.11.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11122131`)

SCell Activation/Deactivation in Presence of UL Slot Aggregation L2 PS shall decide upon activation and deactivation of SCells per PUSCH Slot Aggregation state as defined below.

  * When the UE enters the TP enabled::SAG On state (see 5G_UP_ALG_18906_replaced([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):
  * If NRBTS/NRCELL.sCellDeactInPoorRf = ‘Deact_Scells_VoNr_SAg’ at PCell and there is at least one configured SCell :
  * Deactivate all of the UE's SCells



[CB012149-DA]

  * Else if the UE is configured with FDD + TDD FR1 UL Tx switching, and TDD SCell with UL Tx switching is activated
  * Deactivate the TDD SCell with UL Tx switching.



[End CB012149-DA]

  * When the UE exits the TP enabled::SAG On state:
  * Follow the SCell activation requirements in per 5G_UP_ALG_2708_replaced([11120938](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

within cell group for FR2 CA 11122146: SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA 11122146: SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA 11122146: SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA 11122146: SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA 11122146: SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA 11122146: SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA If actHighNumberOfUEs is TRUE

AND

(

(rdActAutoScellDeactivationOnLoad (5G_UP_ALG_26569_replaced([11124322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to TRUE [Before CB012734-B-UPD002]and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is set to 'bufferBased'(1) or 'bufferAndRLQualityBased'(2) [End CB012734-B-UPD002])

[CB012734-D]

OR 

(rdActSinglePfMetricPerUeOnLoad (5G_UP_ALG_26826_replaced([11193936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvxY0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is TRUE))

[End CB012734-D]

),

then gNB-DU shall maintain a matrix to store the active UEs per {beam, carrier}: activeUesPerBeamPerCarrier[MAX_BEAM_NUM] [MAX_CC_NUM]. Each row of the matrix corresponds to a beam; each column of the matrix corresponds to a carrier in the cell group; each entry in the matrix is a list of active UEs; number of active UEs in the list is called the load of corresponding {beam, carrier} . where:

  * MAX_BEAM_NUM: maximum number of beams supported in cell group;
  * MAX_CC_NUM: maximum number of carriers configured in cell group;



Each list element shall contain the following information:

  * ueId: UE identity (CRNTI);
  * isPSCell: Is the serving cell UE’s P(S)Cell;
  * operation mode: set to "DL and UL" if the serving cell is configured in both downlink and uplink for UE; set to "DL only" if the serving cell is configured in downlink only.



The matrix shall be updated as follows:

  * When UE context is setup, a list element {ueId = UE ID, isPSCell = TRUE, operation mode = "DL and UL"} shall be appended to the list indexed by {beam = UE’s best beam, CC = UE’s PCell carrier};
  * When a SCell is activated, a list element {ueId = UE ID, isPSCell = FALSE, operation mode = SCell operation mode} shall be appended to the list indexed by {beam = UE’s best beam, CC = this SCell carrier};
  * When a SCell is deactivated or released, the list element corresponding to this SCell shall be removed from the list indexed by {beam = UE’s best beam, CC = this SCell carrier};
  * When a UE is released, the list element(s) corresponding to UE’s P(S)Cell and SCell(s) (if any) shall be removed from the list indexed by {beam = UE’s best beam, CC = UE’s PCell carrier};
  * When beam switch or beam recovery occurs for a UE, gNB-DU shall remove relevant elements in all lists indexed by {beam = UE’s original best beam, CC = UE’s serving cell}, and add new element in all the lists indexed by {beam = UE’s new best beam, CC = UE’s serving cell} for the UE;



[CB012734-B-UPD003]

  * When a cell is deleted, all the list elements corresponding to the deleted cell {beam = any, CC = deleted cell} shall be removed from the matrix.



[End CB012734-B-UPD003]

Number of UEs in the list within each matrix entry is called the active UE load of each matrix entry:

activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL[i][j]: lengthof (activeUesPerBeamPerCarrier[i][j]).

activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierUL[i][j]: number of active UEs on beam i and carrier j, and the serving cell on carrier j operates in "DL and UL" mode.

where:

lengthof(list): returns the number of elements in the list;

i: beam index

j: carrier index

Total number of UEs in all the lists associated with a matrix entry is called the total active UE load of the cell group:

totalActiveUeLoad = [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. It shows a double summation symbol, with indices 'i' and 'j' below the summation signs. To the right of the summation symbols, there is a variable named "activeUeLoadPerBeamPerCarrierDL" followed by indices "[i][j]". The expression is written in a dark color on a white background.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6685.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

---

##### 3.7.2.12.0-2 SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA Periodically calculate maximum allowed active SCells per UE (ID: 11122151)

**3.7.2.12.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11122152`)

SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA If actHighNumberOfUEs is TRUE AND rdActAutoScellDeactivationOnLoad (5G_UP_ALG_26569_replaced([11124322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to TRUE [Before CB012734-B-UPD002] and NRBTS.sCellActivationMethod is set to 'bufferBased'(1) or 'bufferAndRLQualityBased'(2) [End CB012734-B-UPD002], gNB-DU shall periodically [Before PR796424] check the total number of active UEs within one cell group [PR796424] calculate the maximum number of allowed active SCell(s) per UE [End PR796424]. if [Before PR796424] totalActiveUeLoad > scellReductionThreshold [PR796424] the newly calculated maximum number of allowed active SCell(s) per UE is smaller than the existing one [End PR796424], then SCell deactivation due to active UE load shall be triggered.

The periodicity of the check is [Before CB012734-B-UPD001] defined by a R&D parameter rdActiveUeLoadCheckPeriod which is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26319_replaced([11124292](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[CB012734-B-UPD001] set to 8*(rdPeriodScellCheck * rdNumOfScellChecks + rdProhibitScellCheck), where: where: rdPeriodScellCheck is defined in 5G_L2_1148_replaced([11184595](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); rdNumOfScellChecks is defined in 5G_L2_1149_replaced([11184600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); rdProhibitScellCheck is defined in 5G_L2_1150_replaced([11184607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27shQvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB012734-B-UPD001]

scellReductionThreshold is set to R&D parameter rdScellReductionThreshold (5G_UP_ALG_26470_replaced([11124302](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if rdScellReductionThreshold > 0; otherwise, it shall be set to NIDD parameter NRCELLGRP.nbActiveCarriersThreshold.

rdScellReductionThreshold: threshold of total number of active UEs on each {beam, Carrier} within cell group [Before PR796424] beyond which SCell deactivation due to active UE load shall be triggered [PR796424] used for calculating maximum allowed active SCells per UE [End PR796424], defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26470_replaced([11124302](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012734-B-UPD001]

Once SCell deactivation due to active UE load is triggered, gNB-DU shall take the following actions:

  * start timer auLoadReductionTimer, which is a cell group specific timer with length equal to rdPeriodScellCheck*rdNumOfScellChecks + rdProhibitScellCheck; when auLoadReductionTimer is running, SCell activation is not allowed;
  * Set auLoadBasedScellDeactCheck to 1 in UE context of each CA UE to indicate that gNB-DU shall check whether SCell deactivation due to active UE load could be applied to current UE.



Note:

1\. In some extreme cases (e.g. CSI multiplexing is enabled and a SCell is activated just before the trigger of active UE load based SCell deactivation), UE may have no chance to check the conditions for SCell activation / deactivation throughout the period while auLoadReductionTimer is running because the SCell activation delay timer (length: scellActivationDelay_ms, see 5G_UP_ALG_2794_replaced([11121826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is running for the UE. but the active UE load check for the UE won't be missed in this situation, as the auLoadBasedScellDeactCheck flag is still 1 for the UE after the expiry of auLoadReductionTimer, the UE will be checked after the expiry of its SCell activation delay timer.

[End CB012734-B-UPD001]

---

[End CB012734-B-UPD001] [PR796424] * nonCaUeNum: number of RRC connected UEs without any SCell configured; * caUeNum: number of RRC connected UEs with at least 1 SCell configured; [End PR796424]

##### 3.7.2.12.0-4 SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA Deactivate SCell(s) of UE with more SCells than the maximum allowed value when active UE load is triggered (ID: 11122168)

**3.7.2.12.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11122171`)

SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA When SCell deactivation due to active UE load is triggered (see 5G_UP_ALG_26309_replaced([11122151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall check the number of activated SCells for each UE, if UE has n activated SCells and n > maxAllowedActiveSCells, then (n – maxAllowedActiveSCells) SCell(s) of this UE shall be deactivated. The (n – maxAllowedActiveSCells) SCell(s) to be deactivated shall be selected according to 5G_UP_ALG_21703_replaced([11121800](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqaXvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before CB012734-B-UPD001]

When a SCell is deactivated due to active UE load, corresponding PM counter (SCELL_DEACT_CC_LOAD) shall be pegged.

[CB012734-B-UPD001]

The check for SCell deactivation due to active UE load shall be performed together with the check for SCell activation / deactivation due to buffer, see 5G_UP_ALG_9771_replaced([11120866](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB012734-B-UPD001]

---

##### 3.7.2.12.0-5 SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA Reject SCell activation request when active UE load threshold is exceeded (ID: 11122176)

**3.7.2.12.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11122179`)

SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA [Before CB012734-B-UPD001]

When the conditions for SCell activation is verified, if actAutoScellDeactivationOnLoad is set to TRUE, gNB-DU shall check the total number of active UEs within cell group (totalActiveUeLoad) against scellReductionThreshold, if totalActiveUeLoad <scellReductionThreshold, the SCell activation request shall be accepted, and gNB-DU shall proceed on according to 5G_UP_ALG_2785_replaced([11121763](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqaXtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); otherwise, the SCell activation request shall be rejected (ignored).

scellReductionThreshold: a threshold defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26309_replaced([11122151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012734-B-UPD001]

See 5G_UP_ALG_27443_replaced([11120929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfM_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB012734-B-UPD001]

---

##### 3.7.2.12.0-6 SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA Maintaining number of SCells in the transient phase between inactive state and active state (ID: 11122182)

**3.7.2.12.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11122187`)

SCell deactivation based on active UE load within cell group for FR2 CA [Before PR796424]

To get a more accurate active UE load in cell group (5G_UP_2720_replaced([11391897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufbP1fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall maintain an internal counter: activePendingCcNum.

  * activePendingCcNum shall be initialized to 0 at cell group setup (5G_L1L2_FLOW_80_replaced([11177738](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeU56vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * When gNB-DU decides to activate n SCell(s) (see 5G_UP_ALG_2703_replaced([11120833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqURHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for blind SCell activation and 5G_UP_ALG_9771_replaced([11120866](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for buffer based SCell activation), activePendingCcNum shall be increased by n;
  * activePendingCcNum shall be reduced at any of the following events:
  * SCell activation delay timer (Tactivation_time + TCSI_reporting, see 5G_UP_ALG_2792_replaced([11121815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires, in this case, activePendingCcNum shall be reduced by 1 for each SCell with state changed to active.
  * HARQ feedback for the SCell activation MAC-CE is detected to be not HARQ-ACK, in this case activePendingCcNum shall be reduced by the number of SCell(s) to be activated by corresponding SCell activation MAC-CE.
  * SCell is released after gNB-DU decides to activate the SCell for UE and before the expiry of associated SCell activation delay timer; in this case, activePendingCcNum shall be reduced by 1 for each SCell being released.
  * CA UE is released after gNB-DU decides to activate SCell(s) for the UE and before the expiry of associated SCell activation delay timer, in this case, activePendingCcNum shall be reduced by number of SCell(s) to be activated.



[PR796424]

After fixing PR796424, active UE load is controlled by the number of active SCell(s) per UE (maxAllowedActiveSCells: 5G_UP_ALG_26311_replaced([11122157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), total active CCs in the cell group is no longer considered during SCell activation, as a result, number of SCells in the transient phase between inactive state and active state is no longer used.

[End PR796424]

---

##### 3.7.2.13 Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA

###### 3.7.2.13.0-1 Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA Overview of scheduler processing load based Scell Activation/Deactivation (ID: 11122195)

**3.7.2.13.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11122198`)

Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell and SCell shall perform the following functions related to SCell activation/deactivation with respect to scheduler processing overload in PCell and/or SCell

\- share RT and soft-RT/NRT processing overload severity metrics as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31935_replaced([11122202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

\- evaluate SCell processing load status for SCell activation as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31930_replaced([11122209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_31931_replaced([11122218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_31958_replaced([11122225](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

\- evaluate SCell deactivation criteria in DL and DL/UL as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31954_replaced([11122234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_31955_replaced([11122241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 3.7.2.13.0-2 Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA Scheduler processing load measurements shared by Scell to Pcell (ID: 11122202)

**3.7.2.13.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11122207`)

Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) is set to 0, then:-

\- gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell UL scheduler shall send Real-time (RT) processing load severity metric values to the gnb-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell DL scheduler.

\- gnb-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell DL scheduler shall share the following CPU processing load severity metrics to the gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell DL scheduler:

\- Real-time (RT) processing load severity metric in SCell DL and SCell UL (5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

\- soft-RT/NRT processing load severity metric for the CPU core in which the SCell is hosted. (5G_UP_ALG_31303_replaced([11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXURfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

It is left to design decision the internal message communication and frequency in which this information is shared betwwen the SCell(s) and PCell.

Rationale: In FR1 CA, the PCells and the SCells can be hosted in different cores or even in different L2-RT instances, hence the severity metrics needs to be shared between the schedulers.

---

###### 3.7.2.13.0-3 Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA SCell scheduler level processing load status determination for CA activation decision for DL branch (ID: 11122209)

**3.7.2.13.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11122214`)

Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and**NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0)_is set to 0, then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell shall perform the following actions, else it shall skip the following steps._**

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell (5G_UP_ALG_31935_replaced([11122202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of **rdCaForbidScellActOlcFddDlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_31835_replaced([11216884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD SCell or rdCaForbidScellActOlcTddDlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_31837_replaced([11216922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD SCell, then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell shall exclude the SCell(s) from SCell candidate list for activation.****

Otherwise if the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell (5G_UP_ALG_31935_replaced([11122202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is below the value set for deactivation threshold of **rdCaForbidScellActOlcFddDlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_31835_replaced([11216884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD SCell or rdCaForbidScellActOlcTddDlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_31837_replaced([11216922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD SCell, then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell shall not exclude the SCell(s) from SCell candidate list for activation.****

---

###### 3.7.2.13.0-4 Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA SCell scheduler level processing load status determination for CA activation decision for UL branch (ID: 11122218)

**3.7.2.13.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11122220`)

Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) _is set to 0, then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell shall perform the following actions, else it shall skip the following steps._

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell (5G_UP_ALG_31935_replaced([11122202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of **rdCaForbidScellActOlcFddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_31862_replaced([11217069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMzfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD SCell or rdCaForbidScellActOlcTddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_31864_replaced([11217111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD SCell, then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell shall exclude the SCell(s) from SCell candidate list for activation.****

Otherwise if the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell (5G_UP_ALG_31935_replaced([11122202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is below the value set for deactivation threshold of **rdCaForbidScellActOlcFddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_31862_replaced([11217069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMzfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD SCell or rdCaForbidScellActOlcTddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_31864_replaced([11217111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD SCell, then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell shall not exclude the SCell(s) from SCell candidate list for activation.****

---

###### 3.7.2.13.0-5 Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA Core level scheduler processing load status determination for CA activation decision (ID: 11122225)

**3.7.2.13.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11122230`)

Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) _is set to 0, then each gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell(s) on a CPU core, shall perform the following actions, else it shall skip the following steps. Note that the DL direction of the PCell(s) shall perform the following actions._

If the core level soft real-time/non real-time scheduling (soft-RT/NRT) processing load severity metric given by l2PsNrtCoreLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31303_replaced([11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXURfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler for the PCell(s) or the SCell(s) in case the SCell(s) are hosted on a different core, is greater than on equal to value for the activation threshold defined by rdCoreSoftRtNrtStopScellActOlcPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32023_replaced([11217188](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxda4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the each PCell on a CPU core shall suspend SCell activation checks.

If the core level soft real-time/non real-time scheduling (soft-RT/NRT) processing load severity metric given by l2PsNrtCoreLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31303_replaced([11216106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXURfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler for the PCell(s) or the SCell(s) in case the SCell(s) are hosted on a different core, is below the value for the deactivation threshold defined by rdCoreSoftRtNrtStopScellActOlcPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32023_replaced([11217188](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxda4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the each PCell on a CPU core shall resume SCell activation checks.

---

###### 3.7.2.13.0-6 Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA Evaluation of Scell scheduler processing load for Scell deactivation for DL branch (ID: 11122234)

**3.7.2.13.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11122238`)

Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) _is set to 0, then each gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell, shall perform the following actions, else it shall skip the following steps._

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value of the gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell (5G_UP_ALG_31935_replaced([11122202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of **rdCaScellStopDataOlcFddDlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32009_replaced([11216896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxbls_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD SCell or rdCaScellStopDataOlcTddDlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32011_replaced([11216938](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxblufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD SCell then:****

  * gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell shall for DL only SCell or Joint DL/UL SCell, indicate gNB-DU MAC layer to request gNB-DU RLC layer to stop sending data to the SCell
  * gNB-DU shall start the buffer based inactivity timer. See 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the conditions to start the inactivity timer.



After the gNB-DU RLC layer stops sending data, the scheduling is suspended which can bring down the scheduler processing load significantly. While the buffer based inactivity timer is running, if the l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric value goes below the deactivation threshold of rdCaScellStopDataOlcFddDlPerCent/ rdCaScellStopDataOlcTddDlPerCent then

  * gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell shall indicate gNB-DU MAC layer to request gNB-DU RLC layer to resume sending data to the SCell.
  * gNB-DU shall restart the buffer based inactivity timer. See 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the conditions to stop/restart the inactivity timer.



if the buffer based inactivity timer expires then gNB-DU hosting the SCell shall send SCell deactivation request to gNB-DU hosting the PCell. See 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the conditions for SCell deactivation.

Rationale:

To avoid PCell receiving deactivation requests in bulk, SCell allows remaining buffer to be scheduled after indicating to stop data for the UEs. This would let the SCell trigger the deactivation request depending on each UE's remaining buffer waiting to be scheduled and the expiry of respective inactivity timers. From the starting of the inactivity timer till the deactivation it is close to 1280ms, within which time the load situation can change and it is possible that for some UEs, the deactivation can be halted which is good from the KPI perspective.

---

###### 3.7.2.13.0-7 Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA Evaluation of Scell scheduler processing load for Scell deactivation for UL branch (ID: 11122241)

**3.7.2.13.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11122245`)

Scell Activation/Deactivation due to scheduler processing overload for FR1 CA If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) _is set to 0, then each gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell, shall perform the following actions, else it shall skip the following steps._

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the SCell (5G_UP_ALG_31935_replaced([11122202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqdbFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of **rdCaScellStopDataOlcFddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32013_replaced([11217083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMz_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD SCell or rdCaScellStopDataOlcTddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32017_replaced([11217122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD SCell then:****

  * gNB-DU hosting the PCell, for joint DL/UL SCell, shall stop transmission buffer split to the SCell based on the checks defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31939_replaced([11122821](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * gNB-DU shall start the buffer based inactivity timer. See 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the conditions to start the inactivity timer.



After the transmission buffer resplit occured, the scheduling is suspended which can bring down the scheduler processing load significantly. While the buffer based inactivity timer is running if the l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric value goes below the deactivation threshold of rdCaScellStopDataOlcFddUlPerCent / rdCaScellStopDataOlcTddUlPerCent (See 5G_UP_ALG_31939_replaced([11122821](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then.

  * gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell shall resume the trasmission buffer towards the SCell.
  * gNB-DU shall stop the buffer based inactivity timer. See 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the conditions to stop the inactivity timer.



If the buffer based inactivity timer expires then gNB-DU hosting the SCell shall send SCell deactivation request to gNB-DU hosting the PCell.

See 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the conditions for SCell deactivation.

Note: For the gNB-DU hosting the SCell, the deactivation of the SCell shall depend on the DL SCell scheduler processing overload status as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_31954_replaced([11122234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) since gNB-DU shall proceed with the deactivation of a joint DL/UL SCell based on the overload statuses both from DL and UL side.

Note that it is possible that the DL SCell scheduler processing load severity metric does not allow for deactivation of the SCell in which case, the buffer shall remain splitted in the PCell UL direction only.

---

#### 3.7.2.14 UL Timing Alignment for Scells in a Differtent TAG

##### 3.7.2.14.0-1 UL Timing Alignment for Scells in a Differtent TAG Timing Alignment via CFRA (ID: 13345951)

**3.7.2.14.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13342934`)

UL Timing Alignment for Scells in a Differtent TAG If [Before CB015279-F] NRCELL.actMultiTags [CB015279-F] NRCELL.actMultipleTags [End CB015279-F] is not disabled, then for an Scell that has a different TAG than the Pcell, UL data transfer is only possible once UL timing alignment is achieved. For Scells belonging to the same TAG as the Pcell, the UL timing alignment is based on UL timing advance in the Pcells. For Scells belonging to a different TAG than the Pcells, the UL timing alignment is performed as follows:

  * The scheduler in the Scell requests a free CFRA premable from the CPlane. While requesting the preamble, L2-PS mentions the best SSB beam for the UE. The best SSB beam for the UE can be obtained as per [11121898](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-z_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). Thus, the CFRA preamble can only be requested once the UE context has a valid information regarding the best SSB beam.
  * Once a preamble is assigned, gNB-DU(Scell L2-PS) transmits a PDCCH using DCI 1_0. This PDCCH transmission is called PDCCH order for sending CFRA preamble. The information provided in the PDCCH order is provided in [13353948](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oQ52Ue9_EfC3ocOh_n7w7A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
  * Upon receiving the PDCCH order, the UE transmits its corresponding PRACH preamble to Scell.
  * The subsequent algorithm follows the CFRA process depicted in [11152251: Random Access Procedures (CBRA/CFRA](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kse0SfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
  * Once UL timing alignment is completed, Scell will indicate the same to Pcell



Note: When a PDCCH order is sent by the the gNB, and UE has not received it, the handling of this case is as follows. Since preamble ID and its corresponding RACH occasions are known at gNB, it will wait for preambleTransMax number of RACH occasions before releasing the preamble. Once a preamble is released, gNB-DU shall wait for a back-off time before requesting for a preamble again from the Cplane.

[CB015279-F] When the UE undergoes a beam failure recovery, the preamble assigned to CFRA for Scell time alignment shall be released. This is because as per 3GPP, two simultaneous random access is not supported by the UE and the expectation is it will prioritize beam recovery over Scell time alignment. [End CB015279-F]

preambleTransMax: MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/preambleTransMax

---

## 3.7.3 CA UE scheduling

### 3.7.3.0-2 CA UE scheduling Document Owner Deputy Lukasz Rygiel; Haibo 1. Jin; Georg Raffael Janczyk (ID: 11122258)

### 3.7.3.1 Buffer status split for DL CA

#### 3.7.3.1.0-1 Buffer status split for DL CA Overview of Buffer Status Split (ID: 11122266)

**3.7.3.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11122274`)

Buffer status split for DL CA If rrmBufferStatusSplitNeeded == 1, L2 PS shall determine a buffer status split for UEs with active SCell in the TD scheduler. This split gives the amount of data that can be scheduled by the set of selected UE's carriers which FD-Scheduling is handled sequentially on the same CPU core. Rationale of the buffer status split is to reduce the amount of padding bits for CA UEs with limited data in buffer, in a situation where the scheduling of different carriers takes place from different CPU cores in parallel.

The split shall be new determined at each DL Data slot following the steps below:

  * determine the number of CCs that will get a portion of the DRB data in buffer, as described in 5G_UP_ALG_2837_replaced([11122276](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
  * select which CCs will get a portion of the DRB data in buffer, as described in 5G_UP_ALG_2839_replaced([11122284](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
  * split the available amount of data to these CCs, as described in 5G_UP_ALG_2846_replaced([11122312](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));



[Before PR757568]

SRB buffer is not split. SRB data can be transmitted by the UE Pcell or by any of the selected Scells handled by the same FD-Scheduler core (see 5G_UP_ALG_4557_replaced([11186962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXJRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details).

[End PR757568]

Note: [Before PR757568] For FDD-TDD CA (FR1) [PR757568]

For both FR1 CA UE and FR2 CA UE: [End PR757568]

  * SRB buffer is not split. SRB data can be transmitted by the UE Pcell only.
  * GBR DRB buffer shall not be split and shall be transmitted on the UE PCell only. [PR757568] GBR DRB is not supported in FR2 at present.[End PR757568]



The setting of rrmBufferStatusSplitNeeded is described in 5G_UP_ALG_2851_replaced([11122336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.7.3.1.0-2 Buffer status split for DL CA Determination of number of CCs for the Buffer Status Split (ID: 11122276)

**3.7.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11122281`)

Buffer status split for DL CA L2-PS shall calculate how many CCs are needed to transmit the total amount of data available for DL transmission in drbTraffic class (rrmAmountDlDataToBeSplit), assuming that each CC can transmit at least a data amount given by rdMinDataPerCCForSplit:

If rrmAmountDlDataToBeSplit <= (rrmNumActiveCellsOnPCellCore - rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsOnPCellCore)*rdMinDataPerCCForSplit

rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans = rrmNumActiveCellsOnPCellCore – rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsOnPCellCore;

else

rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans = rrmNumActiveCells – rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsOnPCellCore - rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsOnNonPCellCore;

where:

  * rrmNumActiveCellsOnPCellCore = 1 + 'number of active Scells which FD-Scheduling is located on the same Core as Pcell'

  * rrmNumActiveCells = 'number of active serving cells of the UE'

  * rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsOnPCellCore = 'number of active serving Scells on PCell core for the UE in overheating status' according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note: The range shall be from 0 to (rrmNumActiveCellsOnPCellCore-1).

  * rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsOnNonPCellCore = 'number of active serving Scells on non-PCell core for the UE in overheating status' according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note: The range shall be from 0 to (rrmNumActiveCells - rrmNumActiveCellsOnPCellCore).

  * rdMinDataPerCCForSplit value is decribed in 5G_L2_1225_replaced([11184537](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6NfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.7.3.1.0-3 Buffer status split for DL CA Selection of the CCs for the Buffer Status Split (ID: 11122284)

**3.7.3.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11122289`)

Buffer status split for DL CA L2-PS shall select the UE CCs for which the buffer status split should be larger than 0, according to the following rule:

IF(rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans == (rrmNumActiveCellsOnPCellCore - rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsOnPCellCore))

Pcell and the active Scells which are located on the same FD-core as Pcell and not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are selected for the buffer split;

ELSE

All active serving cells which are not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are selected for the buffer split;

where rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans, rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsOnPCellCore and rrmNumActiveCellsOnPCellCore are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2837_replaced([11122276](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.7.3.1.0-4 Buffer status split for DL CA Determination of the Buffer Status Split Factor per Carrier (ID: 11122293)

**3.7.3.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11122298`)

Buffer status split for DL CA Buffer Status Split Factor per Carrier for FR2 CA

---

**3.7.3.1.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13468093`)

Buffer status split for DL CA For the Pcell and for each of the Scells selected in 5G_UP_ALG_2839_replaced([11122284](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2-PS shall calculate the corresponding buffer status split factor rrmBufferSplitFactorServCell. It represents the fraction of the UE's DRB buffer which is assigned to the corresponding serving cell:

rrmBufferSplitFactorServCell(n) = 1 / rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans, for each selected CC n

meaning that each DRB buffer is split equally among the selected serving cells.

Note: This requirement is applicable only for FR2 CA.

  * **rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans: see 5G_UP_ALG_2837_replaced([11122276](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**



[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.7.3.1.0-5 Buffer status split for DL CA Determination of cumulative Buffer Status Split Factors (ID: 11122305)

**3.7.3.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11122309`)

Buffer status split for DL CA If the FD-Scheduling for N of the rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans cells is handled on the same CPU core k, a cumulative buffer split factor shall be determined by summing up the split factors (as calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_2841_replaced([11122293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepJfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of these cells:

rrmBufferSplitFactorCumulated(k) = SUM{n, | FD-Scheduling(n) on Core k}( rrmBufferSplitFactorServCell(n) )

rrmBufferSplitFactorCumulated(k) is calculated for each core of the L2-PS instance hosting the FD-Scheduling processing of one or more of the rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans cells.

The cumulative buffer split factor represents the fraction of the UE's DRB buffer which can be totally scheduled over the N UE's serving cells.

Reason for considering the cumulative split instead of the CC specific split: on a given core the FD-Scheduling of multiple carriers runs sequentially (i.e. one carrier after the other is allocated), meaning that for a CA UE which is scheduled on these cells it is possible to refer to the same buffer split, allowing less data fragmentation (that is: less padding bits) over the different serving cells.

The decision whether do this calculation in the TD or FD Scheduler is left to implementation.

  * rrmNumServCellsForDataTrans: see 5G_UP_ALG_2837_replaced([11122276](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * rrmBufferSplitFactorServCell(n): see 5G_UP_ALG_2842_replaced([11122298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 3.7.3.1.0-6 Buffer status split for DL CA Determination of the UE Buffer Status Split (ID: 11122312)

**3.7.3.1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11122316`)

Buffer status split for DL CA For each cumulative buffer status split factor calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_2844_replaced([11122305](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2-PS shall determine the corresponding buffer status split for each UE DRB j:

IF( core k doesn't include the Pcell)

rrmDrbBufferSplit_bytes(j,k) = FLOOR( rrmBufferSplitFactorCumulated(k) * bufferedBytes(j) )

ELSE

rrmDrbBufferSplit_bytes(j,k) = bufferedBytes(j) - SUM{r, | rrmBufferSplitFactorCumulated(r) calculated for core r, r ≠ k} ( FLOOR( rrmBufferSplitFactorCumulated(r) * bufferedBytes(j) ) )

where bufferedBytes(j) is the amount of DL data in UE's DRB buffer j (5G_UP_ALG_4561_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmDrbBufferSplit_bytes(j,k) represents the amount of DL data from DRB j which can be scheduled over the UE's serving cells which FD-Scheduling is handled by the same core k.

If the core k includes the Pcell, the FD-Scheduler shall also consider the SRB data as available for transmission on any of the selected CCs mapped to core k.

---

#### 3.7.3.1.0-7 Buffer status split for DL CA Update of the Buffer Split Level (ID: 11122320)

**3.7.3.1.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11122324`)

Buffer status split for DL CA After that a CA UE is scheduled in DL by the FD-Scheduler running on core k, the FD-Scheduler shall update its buffer split level as below, for each DRB j allocated in the TB:

rrmDrbBufferSplit_bytes(j,k) = max(rrmDrbBufferSplit_bytes(j,k) - amountBytes(j), 0)

Where amountBytes(j) is the amount of bytes of DRB j which have been transmitted in the TB (see 5G_UP_ALG_4550_replaced([11185672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUs7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * rrmDrbBufferSplit_bytes(j,k): see 5G_UP_ALG_2846_replaced([11122312](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 3.7.3.1.0-8 Buffer status split for DL CA Removal of the CA UE from the CS2 List of the CCs to be scheduled based on its Buffer Split Level (ID: 11122329)

**3.7.3.1.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11122333`)

Buffer status split for DL CA If after the update of the UE buffer split (5G_UP_ALG_2848_replaced([11122320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) all the UE DRB data have been transmitted (i.e. rrmDrbBufferSplit_bytes(j,k) = 0, for each DRB j):

the UE shall be removed from the CS2 lists of the serving cells still to be handled by FD-Scheduling of core k (if present in any of these lists) unless the UE has also other kind of resource requests which are pending on those cells;

  * rrmDrbBufferSplit_bytes(j,k): represents the amount of DL data from DRB j which can be scheduled over the UE's serving cells which FD-Scheduling is handled by the same core k (see 5G_UP_ALG_2846_replaced([11122312](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

#### 3.7.3.1.0-9 Buffer status split for DL CA Enabling/Disabling of the Buffer Status Split (ID: 11122336)

**3.7.3.1.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11122341`)

Buffer status split for DL CA The buffer status split is enabled (or disabled) at L2-PS instance level by setting the internal parameter rrmBufferStatusSplitNeeded.

The buffer status split of CA UEs is needed when the FD-Scheduling of different carriers is deployed on different CPU cores as this implies that the FD-Scheduling of different UE's serving cells can happen in parallel. This configuration can be detected as below:

IF(frequencyRange == FR2)

rrmBufferStatusSplitNeeded = 1;

ELSE

rrmBufferStatusSplitNeeded = 0;

where frequencyRange is received in PsCnfg_AddressDistributionReq.

Note: a separate flag can be defined to discriminate between use (or not) of parallel FD-Scheduling deployment. In this case rrmBufferStatusSplitNeeded shall be set to the value of this flag.

Note: With aggregation of the buffer status split within one core, there is no functional difference if buffer status split is enabled or disabled for setup with single DL scheduling core. Thus, it needs to be decided during CP3 phase if disabled buffer status split algorithm shall be supported.

---

### 3.7.3.2 Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA

#### 3.7.3.2.0-1 Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA Overview of Transmission Buffer Split (ID: 11122349)

**3.7.3.2.0-1.0-8**  (ID: `13358991`)

Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13358991: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA For FR1 UL CA UE with [CB014067-A] at least one [End CB014067-A] activated SCell [CB015279-A] which has obtained its UL timing alignment [End CB015279-A], PCell UL 5G-L2-PS controls the buffer split to [CB014067-A] each active [End CB014067-A] SCell UL 5G-L2-PS with below procedures:

  * SCell UL 5G-L2-PS reports necessary information to PCell UL 5G-L2-PS according to 5G_UP_ALG_10516_replaced([11122476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * PCell UL 5G-L2-PS monitors the triggers of transmission buffer split according to 5G_UP_ALG_10281_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * When any one of above triggers happens, PCell UL 5G-L2-PS further checks whether the condition of transmission buffer split is satisfied according to 5G_UP_ALG_9496_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * If the condition above is met, then PCell UL 5G-L2-PS calculates the transmission buffer split according to 5G_UP_ALG_9591_replaced([11122888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhFYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * After transmission buffer split calculation, if that resulted in non-zero quantity allocated to SCell, in case that the UE is in a Configured Grant firing state (see 5G_UP_ALG_15099_replaced([11172972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuPu0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the resulted split is validated in accordance to the procedure specified in 5G_UP_ALG_22286_replaced([11173280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuSLGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * After transmission buffer split calculation, PCell UL 5G-L2-PS indicates the result to SCell UL 5G-L2-PS according to 5G_UP_ALG_10516_replaced([11122476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * For SCell with bad radio link quality in uplink according to 5G_UP_ALG_11871_replaced([11121633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall stop split transmission buffer to SCell.
  * For SCell enter overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2871_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall stop split transmission buffer to SCell.
  * If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to FALSE, OR (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND 5QI1 DRB is not configured for the UE)

  * For FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE, if UE power state is false (see 5G_UP_ALG_28261_replaced([11123109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhFavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or the UE is not a single Tx UE and aperiodic SRS is configured on PCell and rank1 is used on PCell, gNB-DU shall stop split transmission buffer to SCell.



[CB014067-A]

  * For FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE or inter-band FR1 UL CA UE with one FDD and two contiguous intra-band TDD FR1 CCs with TDD PCell,



if  
(UE power state is false (see [11123109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhFavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or (the UE is not a single Tx UE and aperiodic SRS is configured on PCell and rank1 is used on PCell),

gNB-DU shall stop transmission buffer split to TDD SCell. 

[End CB014067-A]

  * For inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE with PPowerClass,PCell greater than PPowerClass,CA, if UE power state is false (see [12688685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_xnJOsFY5EfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), gNB-DU shall stop split transmission buffer to SCell.

  * For FR1 UL CA, if UE is already configured with DL+UL SCell while step-wise SCell Addition procedure for another DL only SCell is ongoing, PCell’s gNB-DU shall stop split transmission buffer to DL+UL SCell N DPA scheduling cycles after PCell’s gNB-DU receives notification that RRC Reconfiguration for purpose of step-wise SCell Addition has started.




Note: design of internal communication between DPA and PCell’s UL scheduler is left to EFS.

  * inter-band FR1 UL CA with one FDD and two contiguous intra-band TDD FR1 CCs with TDD PCell for UE indicating pa-PhaseDiscontinuityImpacts (see [11371714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wao0y_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [End CB014067-B]



if TDD PCell is configured with the dedicated TDRA list specified in 5G_UP_ALG_29277_replaced([11116009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6zfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), when TDD PCell decides to conduct UL scheduling using Type3-PDCCH, DCI format 0_0 for the transient phase according to 5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). }

13\. UE has both active DL&UL SCell and ext-SCell(s), PCell detects Xp-U link delay is too high to support UL scheduling in the DL&UL SCell and DL scheduling in ext-SCell concurrently, but inter-gNB DL CA can still be supported, and NRDU.fr1UlCaPreferred = “dataRatePreferred”, see 5G_UP_ALG_12815_replaced([11122016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

14\. For:

  * inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE with PPowerClass,PCell greater than PPowerClass,CA [CB014067-A] or
  * inter-band FR1 UL CA with one FDD and two contiguous intra-band TDD FR1 CCs with TDD PCell for UE with PPowerClass,PCell greater than PPowerClass,CA [End CB014067-A]



UE power state is false (see [12688685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_xnJOsFY5EfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). 

Then PCell shall set rrmBufferedDataUlTotal_bytes as 0 and indicate to [CB014067-A] the given active DL+UL [End CB014067-A] SCell explicitly, so that [CB014067-A] this specific active DL+UL [End CB014067-A] SCell shall stop new transmission immediately.**And the pending UL HARQ retransmission in the DL &UL SCell shall be cleared in the following cases:**

  * UL Tx switching UE with FDD PCell (including FDD DSS PCell) and TDD UL SCell; (reason 9)
  * Inter-band 2CC UL CA with 3Tx;
  * Xp-U link delay is too high to support UL scheduling in DL&UL SCell and DL scheduling in ext-SCell concurrently. (reason 13)



Note: In SW implementation clear HARQ retransmission does not prevent HARQ retransmission immediately but allows one more time retransmission, and this may cause one time DTX or HARQ NACK, this is accepted as restriction.

For UL Tx switching option 1 (switchedUL) UE with FDD PCell (including FDD DSS PCell) and TDD UL SCell:

  * When TDD UL SCell received a first non-zero UL buffer split after zero UL buffer split, TDD UL SCell shall proceed scheduling at least 5 slot later.
  * When FDD PCell send a first zero UL buffer split after non-zero UL buffer split, if FDD PCell proceed scheduling in the same slot, FDD PCell shall shorten the PUSCH if the corresponding FDD slot is just after a TDD SCell UL slot. After that FDD PCell does not need to shorten PUSCH due to TDD SCell UL slot any more, but still need to shorten PUSCH due to P-SRS in TDD special slot.



Rationale: TDD scheduler and FDD scheduler have different start time and may cause mismatch when UL buffer split changes from non-zero to zero or vice versa.

HARQ re-transmission can be continued before [CB014067-A] the given active DL+UL [End CB014067-A] SCell is deactivated for reason **1 and 2 and 3 and 4 and 7.**

[CB014067-A] The given active DL+UL [End CB014067-A] SCell shall start UL inactivity timer (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2733_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for reason 1 and 2 and 3 and 4 and 7 and 10 and 14.

PCell UL 5G-L2-PS shall record this result as "stop split" and use it for next evaluation condition of buffer split (5G_UP_ALG_9496_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

5G-L2-PS shall inform L2-Hi the buffer split status when it changes from "stop split" to "start split" or from "start split" to "stop split". Based on this information, L2-Hi shall exclude this [CB014067-A] DL+UL [End CB014067-A] SCell from buffer based DL SCell deprioritize algorithm (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_5755_replaced([11221424](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx1OYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

CA eligible DRB refers to 5G_UP_10576_replaced([11358417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uchs1_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When MRBTS/NRBTS/actUlAmbr set to "SA" and avgAmbrPerUlSlot (5G_UP_ALG_19975_replaced([11205514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwqJpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) exceeds ulAmbrPerSlot (5G_UP_ALG_19982_replaced([11205488](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwqJoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), transmission buffer split shall not be triggered. IF the fake data in transmission buffer is filled by DRB priority PUG, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_30970_replaced([11195605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv9mFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), transmission buffer split shall not be triggered. With: rdBufferExhaustedInMs (see 5G_UP_ALG_10296_replaced([11124111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_10296_replaced([11124111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). rrmScheduledUlData_bytes: counting the amount of data which has been granted to the UE but not yet received (see 5G_UP_ALG_10514_replaced([11203665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) rrmBufferedDataUlLcg_bytes: estimation of the amount of data in UE buffers for that LCG, based on the BSRs and the received data amounts (see 5G_UP_ALG_10514_replaced([11203665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) _eThav: cumulated estimated average throughput of all CA eligible_ _DRBs_ _of FR1 UL CA UE per carrier for BSR split purpose (see 5G_UP_ALG_9491_replaced([11204528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))._**** CA eligible DRB and non CA eligible DRB refer to 5G_UP_10576_replaced([11358417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uchs1_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
