#### 3.7.3.2.0-7 Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA Evaluation criteria for scheduler processing overload in any of the UL carrier (ID: 11122821)

**3.7.3.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11122827`)

Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA If NRBTS.actCaOverloadCtrlEnh = TRUE and NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) _is set to 0, then each gNB-DU U-Plane hosting the PCell, shall perform the following actions, else it shall skip the following steps._

The PCell or SCell shall be deemed unavailable for buffer split due to scheduler processing overload if the following conditions meet:

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value, is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of

rdCaScellStopDataOlcFddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32013_replaced([11217083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMz_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD SCell or rdCaScellStopDataOlcTddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32017_replaced([11217122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD SCell**

If real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value, is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of

rdCaPcellStopDataOlcFddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32015_replaced([11217096](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD PCell or rdCaPcellStopDataOlcTddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32019_replaced([11217137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD PCell**

The PCell or SCell shall be deemed available for buffer split after recovering from scheduler processing overload if the following conditions meet:

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value, is below the value set for deactivation threshold of **rdCaScellStopDataOlcFddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32013_replaced([11217083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMz_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD SCell or rdCaScellStopDataOlcTddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32017_replaced([11217122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD SCell,****

If real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value, is below the value set for deactivation threshold of **rdCaPcellStopDataOlcFddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32015_replaced([11217096](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a FR1 FDD PCell or rdCaPcellStopDataOlcTddUlPerCent (5G_UP_ALG_32019_replaced([11217137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcz3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for a FR1 TDD PCell,****

then the PCell shall resume transmission buffer split towards the UL PCell.

Note:

  1. If both PCell and SCell is deemed unavailable, the transmission buffer split shall be allowed towards PCell.

  2. It is possible that PCell is unavailable for scheduling and UE needs to send SR (e.g to report BSR for UL resources) which should then be still be honoured and PCell shall schedule the SR.

UE's CA eligible DRB transmission buffer shall be split according to a fixed ratio defined by a rd parameter for first time split; otherwise the buffer shall be split according to the ratio of PCell and [CB014067-A] each active DL+UL [End CB014067-A] SCell estimated throughput.

[image-9][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. **Equation:** UL data volume split to SCellj for UEᵢ = ∑ floor[UL data volume for LCG(i,k) * splitRatio(i, SCellj)] k **Description:** This equation defines the "UL data volume split to SCellj for UEᵢ". It is calculated by summing, over all values of 'k', the floor of the product of "UL data volume for LCG(i,k)" and "splitRatio(i, SCellj)". * **UEᵢ** : Represents a specific User Equipment (UE) identified by index 'i'. * **SCellj** : Represents a specific Secondary Cell (SCell) identified by index 'j'. * **∑** : Denotes summation. * **k** : The index over which the summation is performed. * **floor[...]** : The floor function, which rounds down to the nearest whole number. * **UL data volume for LCG(i,k)** : Represents the uplink (UL) data volume for a specific Logical Channel Group (LCG) identified by indices 'i' and 'k'. * **splitRatio(i, SCellj)** : Represents the split ratio for UE 'i' and SCell 'j'.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-02082120.png[/image_path][/image-9]

[image-10][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation: UL data volume split to PCell for UEᵢ = [∑_k UL data volume for LCG(i,k)] - ∑_j UL data volume split for SCellj for UEᵢ[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-02082122.png[/image_path][/image-10]

#### 3.7.3.2.0-11 Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA Evaluate UE power for UL CA for transmission buffer split**** (ID: 13446463)

**3.7.3.2.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `13446466`)

Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA Overview

---

**3.7.3.2.0-11.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13446475`)

Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA For a UE configured with UL CA, the gNB-DU shall determine whether the UE has sufficient power to support the Transmission Buffer Split, which implies enabling parallel UL transmission on the PCell and the DL&UL SCell(s).

The gNB-DU shall evaluate the UE power for each (PCell, DL&UL SCell) pair individually.

The term “UE power state” is introduced per (PCell, DL&UL SCell) pair and is defined as follows:

  * UE power state = true:  
The UE has sufficient power to be allocated to both the PCell and the given DL&UL SCell of the pair; in other words, the UE is not power limited for this (PCell, DL&UL SCell) pair.
  * UE power state = false:  
The UE does not have sufficient power for the given DL&UL SCell of the pair; thus, the UE is power limited for this (PCell, DL&UL SCell) pair.



The evaluation of UE power for UL CA related to Transmission Buffer Split is specified in the dedicated requirements:

  * For 2CC TDD–TDD:

  * intra-band UL CA: see [11123109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhFavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

  * inter-band UL CA: see [12688685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_xnJOsFY5EfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
  * For 3CC TDD–TDD–FDD (with TDD PCell):

  * Mixed intra-band TDD–TDD and inter-band TDD–FDD UL CA: see [13446467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3RgiACeWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

---

**3.7.3.2.0-11.0-2**  (ID: `13446467`)

Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA **Evaluate UE power for mix of inter-band and** intra-band UL CA **for transmission buffer split** ****

---

**3.7.3.2.0-11.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13453025`)

Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13453025: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA When UE is configured with FR1 3CC UL CA TDD-TDD-FDD (TDD PCell) – that is, inter-band FR1 UL CA with 1 FDD + 2 intra-band contiguous TDD CCs – the gNB-DU shall evaluate if UE power is sufficient for parallel UL transmission on the PCell and DL&UL SCells. Note: priority for transmission power reduction is specified in 3GPP TS38.213 section 7.5. After UE is configured with FR1 3CC UL CA TDD-TDD-FDD (TDD PCell) via SCell Addition, [CB014067-D] or SCell Upgrade, [End CB014067-D] gNB-DU shall: * initialize the UE power state for (PCell, TDD DL&UL SCell) and (PCell, FDD DL&UL SCell) pairs ([13446466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vwRlMCeWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) as false, which means that UE Power is not sufficient for UL transmission on either SCell, * evaluate the UE power for (PCell, TDD DL&UL SCell) and (PCell, FDD DL&UL SCell) pairs in order to determine the UE power state for each pair, when PHR report is received. gNB-DU shall evaluate the UE Power and determine UE power state individually for: * (PCell, TDD DL&UL SCell) pair, * (PCell, FDD DL&UL SCell) pair. Step-1: gNB-DU shall determine UE power state for (PCell, TDD DL&UL SCell) pair * For intra-band TDD PCell and TDD DL&UL SCell, gNB-DU shall evaluate UE power and UE power state according to [11123109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhFavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) Step-2 gNB-DU shall determine UE power state for (PCell, FDD DL&UL SCell) pair * If UE power state for (PCell, TDD DL&UL SCell) pair determined in Step-1 is true, if UE power state for (PCell, FDD DL&UL SCell) pair is false, then gNB-DU shall calculate the UE power vs the formula below: 10 _log(rrmNumPuschPrb[i, PCell, tPHR] / rrmLatMaxNumPuschPrb[i, PCell]) + rrmPhr[i, PCell, tPHR] + [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. #### 3.7.3.2.0-12 Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA Evaluate UE power for intra-band UL CA for transmission buffer split (ID: 11123109)

**3.7.3.2.0-12.0-4**  (ID: `13432628`)

Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA 13432628: Buffer status split for FR1 UL CA For UE configured with FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA, in case UE is power limited on PCell, no power can be allocated to the parallel transmission on SCell (note: priority for transmission power reduction is specified in 3GPP TS38.213 section 7.5), so UE power shall be evaluated on PCell for transmission buffer split. Whether UE is power limited on PCell depends on the downlink pathloss and the number of scheduled PRBs on PCell. For FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE, after SCell with FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA is added due to SCell addition or SCell change or SCell Upgrade, UE power state is initialized as false which means there is no UE power for SCell, and UE power shall be evaluated on PCell when PHR report is received. If UE power state is false UE power shall be evaluated as the below formula: [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation and a line of text. **Equation:** $10 \times \log_{10} \frac{\text{rrmNumPuschPrb}[i, c, t_{\text{PHR}}]}{\text{rrmLatMaxNumPuschPrb}[i, c]} + \text{rrmPhr}[i, c, t_{\text{PHR}}] + \tilde{P}_{\text{CMAX}_c}[i] - P_{\text{CMAX}_c}[i, t_{\text{PHR}}] >$ **Text:** uePwrLimitedPCellThresh+rdUePwrLimitedPCellHyst[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6786.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] If the above formula meets for the rdNumOfConsecUePwrEva (defined in 5G_UP_ALG_28276_replaced([11124379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqqPXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) consecutive UE power evaluation UE power state is set to true. else UE power state is kept as false. endif else UE power shall be evaluated as the below formula: [image-1][image_desc]10 * log10(rmNum / rrmLatMaxNumPuschPrb[i,c]) + rrmPhr[i,c, t_PHR] + P_CMAX_c[i] - P_CMAX_c[i, t_PHR] < uePwrLimitedPCellThresh[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6786.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] If the above formula meets UE power state is set to false. else UE power state is kept as true. endif endif Where: * i: UE index; * c: PCell index; * [image-2][image_desc]t_PHR[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6786.003.png[/image_path][/image-2]: time the latest PHR of PCell is received; * [image-3][image_desc]rmNumPuschPrb[i, c, tPHR ][/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6786.004.png[/image_path][/image-3]: the number of PRBs contributing on PCell at the UL transmission carrying the PHR at time [image-4][image_desc]t_PHR[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6786.005.png[/image_path][/image-4]for UE i; * [image-5][image_desc]rrmLatMaxNumPuschPrb[i, c][/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6786.006.png[/image_path][/image-5] is defined as max(ceil(rdDefRatioOfMaxPuschPrb * rrmMaxNumPuschPrb), the maximum number of scheduled PUSCH PRBs on PCell latest for UE i); with \- rdDefRatioOfMaxPuschPrb refers to 5G_UP_ALG_28266_replaced([11124330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). \- rrmMaxNumPuschPrb: number of PRBs available for PUSCH in the particular bandwidth system; \- the maximum number of scheduled PUSCH PRBs on PCell latest for UE i is defined as following: Record the maximum number of scheduled PUSCH PRBs on PCell for UE i in each period specified by rdPeriodForMaxSchePuschPrb, and the maximum number of scheduled PUSCH PRBs on PCell latest for UE i is the maximum number of PRBs during the latest two periods. The expression consists of a tilde symbol above the letter P, followed by the subscript CMAX,PCell, and then the index [i] in square brackets.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-10291725.png[/image_path][/image-9]: configured maximum UE power in PCell for UE i without power reduction, see [11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_fMuWEPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). * PCMAX,PCell[i, tPHR]: configured maximum UE power in PCell for UE i in the slot when PHR is received, power reduction is considered. * rdUePcmaxPCellThresh: see [12688978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PsGK4lZMEfC45IKMrv0u7Q) * rdUePcmaxPCellHyst: see [12689000](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jKjcxlZOEfC45IKMrv0u7Q) * rrmNumPuschPrb[i, PCell, tPHR]: number of PRBs for the PUSCH transmitted by UE i in PCell at time tPHR, a PHR is included in the PUSCH; * rrmLatMaxNumPuschPrb[i, PCell]: defined as MAX {ceil (rdDefRatioOfMaxPuschPrb * rrmMaxNumPuschPrb), the latest maximum number of scheduled PUSCH PRBs in PCell for UE i} * rdDefRatioOfMaxPuschPrb: see [11124330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_-XODMPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) * rrmMaxNumPuschPrb: number PRBs available for PUSCH in particular bandwidth system; * The latest maximum number of scheduled PUSCH PRBs in PCell for UE i is defined as: record the maximum number of scheduled PUSCH PRBs in PCell for UE i in each period specified by rdPeriodForMaxSchedPuschPrb, and the latest maximum number of scheduled PUSCH PRBs in PCell for UE i is the maximum number of PRBs during the latest 2 periods. If the latest period is not ended when UE power is evaluated, then the maximum number until current evaluation is regarded as the latest maximum number. * rdPeriodForMaxSchePuschPrb: see [11124340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_-a5CQPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). * rrmPhr(i, PCell, tPHR): power headroom in PCell at time tPHR reported by UE i. * rdUePwrLimitedPCellIntBandThresh: see [12689032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_oZejQFZPEfC45IKMrv0u7Q). * rdUePwrLimitedPCellHyst: see [11124369](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_-mB7QPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). * rdMinUePwrForSCell: see [12883429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_xCMWW7SmEfCQT7hYUxERAg). For UE configured with simultaneousPUCCH-PUSCH-SamePriority-r17, PCell shall decide parallel transmission in overlapping UL slots flag parallelTxForUlCa as follows: * paralleTxForUlCa is set to false when simultaneousPUCCH-PUSCH-SamePriority-r17 is configured to UE. * When parallelTxForUlCa is false, if {[(1) OR (2)] AND (5)} = TRUE in rdNumOfConsecUePwrEva evaluations, then parallelTxForUlCa is changed to true; * When parallelTxForUlCa is true, if {[(3) AND (4)] OR (6)} = TRUE, then parallelTxForUlCa is changed to false; * When transform precoding is enabled in PCell and PPowerClass,PCell >= PPowerClass, CA (see [11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_fMuWEPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), parallelTxForUlCa shall be set to false; * Whenever value of parallelTxForUlCa changes, PCell shall notify the DL&UL SCell. * UE shall be eligible for UL scheduling in overlapping UL slots if “parallelTxForUlCa” is true in the latest notification and non-zero UL buffer is split to FDD SCell. FDD SCell shall consider UE ineligible for UL scheduling in overlapping UL slots if parallelTxForUlCa is false in the latest notification. Note: UE shall be eligible for UL scheduling in FDD SCell in non-overlapping UL slots no matter if parallelTxForUlCa is true or false as long as UL data split to FDD SCell is greater than 0.

---

### 3.7.3.3 Max data rate split

#### 3.7.3.3.0-1 Max data rate split Max Data Rate Split Between FD Schedulers inside one L2-PS (ID: 11123215)

**3.7.3.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11123227`)

Max data rate split If rrmBufferStatusSplitNeeded == 1, L2 PS shall determine a max data rate split for UEs with active SCell in the TD scheduler. The max data rate split shall be based on the buffer status split and shall be determined per core k.

For FR2 CA UE,

Thus, the max data rate split per core as used in 5G_UP_ALG_4632_replaced([11192333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvj9dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is detemined as follows:

[PR758159] IF (4CC parallelization is not activated) [End PR758159]

IF( core k doesn't include the Pcell)

rrmMaxDataRateSplit(k) = FLOOR( rrmBufferSplitFactorCumulated(k) * (Sum(maxDataRateDl_bpms) across all serving cells in all the cores / 2^µ) )

ELSE

rrmMaxDataRateSplit(k) = (Sum(maxDataRateDl_bpms) across all serving cells in all the cores / 2^µ) - SUM{r, | rrmMaxDataRateSplit(r) calculated for core r, r ≠ k} (rrmMaxDataRateSplit(r)

[PR758159] ELSE

IF( core k doesn't include the Pcell)

rrmMaxDataRateSplit(k) = FLOOR( rrmBufferSplitFactorCumulated(k) * (Sum(maxDataRateDl_bpms)/ 2^µ) * min( 1 – ( (Sum(maxThroughput) - Sum(maxDataRateDl_bpms)) / Sum(maxDataRateDl_bpms),1 )

ELSE

rrmMaxDataRateSplit(k) = (Sum(maxDataRateDl_bpms)/ 2^µ) - SUM{r, rrmMaxDataRateSplit(r) calculated for core r, r ≠ k} (rrmMaxDataRateSplit(r) )

[End PR758159]

Usage of rrmMaxDataRateSplit(k) is specified in 5G_UP_ALG_4632_replaced([11192333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvj9dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

where:

  * maxDataRateDl_bpms is the maxDataRateDl as provided via PsUser_SetupReq or PsUser_ModifyReq message but expressed in bits per millisecond (maxDataRateDl_bpms = maxDataRateDl in kbps).

  * rrmBufferSplitFactorCumulated(k) is as determined in 5G_UP_ALG_2844_replaced([11122305](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqepKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and µ corresponds to the PDSCH numerology (see 38.211 - Table 4.2-1: Supported transmission numerologies).




[PR758159]

  * Sum(maxDataRateDl_bpms) = Sum of maxDataRateDl_bpms over all serving cells in all the cores.

  * Sum(maxThroughput) = Sum of throughput over all serving cells in all the cores taking following condition:




 MCS 27 and numCDMGroupsWithoutData = 1 for cell with enableDlPtrs = TRUE.

 MCS 28 and numCDMGroupsWithoutData = 1 for cell with enableDlPtrs = FALSE.

  * enableDlPtrs corresponds to NIDD parameter MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlPtrs/actDlPtrs.

  * numCDMGroupsWithoutData corresponds to number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data. See 5G_UP_ALG_3054_replaced([11129150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq6uCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details.




[End PR758159]

The setting of rrmBufferStatusSplitNeeded is described in 5G_UP_ALG_2851_replaced([11122336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note that SRB data and MAC CE are not taken into account for the max data rate split to simplify implementation. It is assumed that this is only negligible impact since SRB and MAC CE is usually only small data amount.

Note as well that the TBS granularity is not considered in the maxDataRate split.

[PR758159]

Note that 4CC parallelization formula is created to improve one UE throughput with limited capability. Best result is obtained when UE is scheduled in same condition calculated in Sum(maxThroughput). When UE conditions are degrading it is assumed throughput degradation is negligeable with respect to BLER. In multiuser test condition, no throughput difference is expected with respect to "no 4CC parallelization " formula. Rational: allocate to first parallel thread exacts rrmMaxDataRateSplit corresponding to 2 CC maxThroughput and so perform TBS/MCS approximation only on second parallel thread and so only once in case of limited capacity UE.

[End PR758159]

---

#### 3.7.3.3.0-2 Max data rate split DL Max Data Rate Split for Inter-L2RT CA Scheduling (ID: 11123231)

**3.7.3.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11123236`)

Max data rate split For FR1 CA UE, the non-GBR DRB bearers will be scheduled over either P(S)Cell or Scell or both, so maxDataRateDl based on UE capability shall be used for both P(S)Cell and Scell DL scheduler for correction the MCS according to 5G_UP_ALG_4632_replaced([11192333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvj9dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For Scell, the maxDataRateDl is defined according to 5G_UP_ALG_2670_replaced([11120289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqPYmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For FR1 CA, L2PS shall not split the max data rate as it is computed by CP-RT per carrier as per 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2404_replaced([11285954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp1ABvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.7.3.3.0-3 Max data rate split UL Max Data Rate Split for FR1 CA Scheduling (ID: 11123241)

**3.7.3.3.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13391561`)

Max data rate split For [Before CB014067-A] FDD + FR1 TDD UL CA **UE [CB014067-A] FR1 UL CA with any number of CCs [End CB014067-A], the CA eligible DRB bearers will be scheduled over [Before CB014067-A] either P(S)Cell or Scell or both [CB014067-A]** any combination of P(S)Cell and DL+UL active SCell(s) [End CB014067-A], so maxDataRateUl based on UE capability shall be used for [Before CB014067-A] both P(S)Cell and [CB014067-A] P(S)Cell and each DL+UL [End CB014067-A] SCell UL scheduler for restricting the TBS according 5G_UP_ALG_5108_replaced([11203573](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfxlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

For [CB014067-A] each DL+UL [End CB014067-A] SCell, the maxDataRateUl (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2404_replaced([11285954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp1ABvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of ueCapability structure content within Scell UE context update according to 5G_UP_ALG_2670_replaced([11120289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqPYmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For FR1 CA, L2PS shall not split the max data rate as it is computed by CP-RT per carrier as per 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2404_replaced([11285954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp1ABvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

CA eligible DRB refers to 5G_UP_10576_replaced([11358417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uchs1_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 3.7.3.3.0-4 Max data rate split Max Data Rate Split for Intra-L2RT Inter-Core CA Scheduling (ID: 11123255)

**3.7.3.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11123260`)

Max data rate split For FR1 CA with Intra-L2RT Inter-Core architecture, L2PS shall not split the max data rate as it is computed by CP-RT per carrier as per 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2404_replaced([11285954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp1ABvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

### 3.7.3.4 Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE

#### 3.7.3.4.0-1 Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE Enabling of CA UE overheating status monitoring (ID: 11123269)

**3.7.3.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12578423`)

Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE [Before CNI-137616-B] If rdEnableCAOverheatingMonitor according to 5G_L2_1293_replaced([11184543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6NvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is ‘true’, [End CNI-137616-B] The gNB-DU shall start to monitor CA UE overheating status through checking WB-CQI report carrying a report of 0 over each activated Scell for CA UE according to 5G_UP_ALG_3478_replaced([11159059](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktHGZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.7.3.4.0-2 Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE Initialization of CA UE overheating status for Scell (ID: 11123279)

**3.7.3.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13476793`)

Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE For CA UE attached to FR1 cells, **during user setup or modification procedure and _numOfCellConfiguration is greater than one over both P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS and Scell 5G-L2-PS, L2 PS shall initialize the overheating status of all Scells to deactivated state._**

**[Before CB013712-B] For CA UE attached to FR2 SA cells, the single 5G-L2-PS instance shall initialize the overheating status of all SCell(s) to deactivated state during SCell addition procedure.**[End CB013712-B]****

After successful Scell activation and deactivation according to 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2 PS shall initialize the overheating status of related Scell to deactivated state.

Note: SCell deactivation can be triggered also due to overheating assistance information received from UE. **[Before CB013712-B]Overheating assistance information reporting is not supported for CA UE attached to FR2 SA cells in current release.**[End CB013712-B]****

For CA UE attached to FR1 cells, L2-PS of PCell shall maintain the overheating status of SCell(s). **[Before CB013712-B] For CA UE attached to FR2 SA cells, the single L2-PS instance shall maintain the overheating status of SCell(s).**[End CB013712-B]****

---

#### 3.7.3.4.0-3 Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE Detection of entering overheating status for CA UE activated Scell (ID: 11123293)

**3.7.3.4.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `13476796`)

Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE If monitoring of CA UE overheating status is enabled per 5G_UP_ALG_2865_replaced([11123269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhsevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and current SCell is not in overheating statue, L2 PS will activate the SCell overheating status in case L2 PS receive rdActCAOverheatingFilterConst of CQI-0 for related SCell according to 5G_L2_1294_replaced([11184549](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6N_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For CA UE attached to FR1 cells, **When the L2-PS of SCell activates the overheating status then it shall provide the overheating activation status information for L2-PS of PCell. L2-PS PCell shall maintain the overheating status information as indicated by L2-PS of SCell(s).**

[Before CB013712-B]For CA UE attached to FR2 SA cells, the single 5G-L2-PS instance maintains the overheating status of all SCell(s), SCell overheating status indication from SCell to PCell is not needed. [End CB013712-B]

For CA UE attached to FR1 cells, **if L2-PS of PCell received from a joint DL/UL SCell the indication of entering overheating status, PCell UL L2-PS shall stop buffer split to SCell according to 5G_UP_ALG_10516_replaced([11122476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). SCell UL L2-PS shall stop retransmission and release HARQ process and also stop inactivity timer.**

[Before CB013712-B] For CA UE attached to FR2 SA cells, when 5G-L2-PS detects UE overheating status in a SCell, 5G-L2-PS shall suspend scheduling of current CA UE in that SCell, stop HARQ retransmission in the SCell and release any HARQ process pending for retransmission. [End CB013712-B]

For FR1 TDD/FDD SCell with beamforming activated, 5G-L2-PS shall not activate the SCell overheating status after receiving rdActCAOverheatingFilterConst CQI-0 in case UE run into SCell suspension of scheduling according to 5G_UP_ALG_2878_replaced([11123344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.7.3.4.0-4 Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE Detection of recovery from overheating status for CA UE activated Scell (ID: 11123313)

**3.7.3.4.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `13476798`)

Overheating monitor for Carrier Aggregation UE If monitoring of CA UE overheating status is enabled per 5G_UP_ALG_2865_replaced([11123269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhsevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and current Scell is in overheating status, L2 PS will deactivate the Scell overheating status in case L2 PS receive rdDeactCAOverheatingFilterConst of non-zero CQI report for related Scell according to 5G_L2_1295_replaced([11184553](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27r6OPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For CA UE attached to FR1 cells:

When the L2-PS of SCell deactivates the overheating status then it shall provide the overheating deactivation status information for L2-PS of PCell.

L2-PS PCell shall maintain the overheating status information as indicated by L2-PS of SCell(s).

If L2-PS of PCell received from a joint DL/UL SCell the indication of recovery from overheating status, PCell shall start buffer split to SCell as first split with rdRatioForFirstUeTransBufSplitToScell (5G_UP_ALG_10305_replaced([11124127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ratio according to 5G_UP_ALG_9591_replaced([11122888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhFYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). SCell UL L2-PS shall recover to run inactivity timer when buffer is empty.

[Before CB013712-B]For CA UE attached to FR2 SA cells:

When 5G-L2-PS detects UE has recovered from overheating for a particular SCell, it shall resume scheduling of current CA UE in that SCell. If the SCell is configured in joint DL/UL mode, scheduling of current CA UE shall be resumed on both downlink and uplink.

[End CB013712-B]

### 3.7.3.5 Interworking with Measurement GAP

##### 3.7.3.5.1 Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup &amp; Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell

###### 3.7.3.5.1.0-1 Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup &amp; Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell Overview (ID: 11123344)

**3.7.3.5.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13257314`)

Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup & Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell 5G-L2-PS shall distinguish whether the UE has all beam related report or reference resource dropped in measurement gap in Scell:

If

  * UE is configured with FR1 TDD [CB008577-D] /FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell

  * And Scell beam report which means:

  * CSI-ReportConfig with **reportQuantity as ssb-Index-RSRP or cri-RSRP according to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_7314_replaced([11336104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wVSavPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), while**




\- If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode is not ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4

\- or, for actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true and nActivatedSsPbch (see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is greater than 4 and UE is configured with 4-port UE specific CSI-RS.

  * CSI-ReportConfig with reportQuantity as cri-RI-LI-PMI-CQI [CB008577-D] /cri-RI-PMI-CQI [End CB008577-D] or as ssb-Index-RSRP or cri-RSRP according to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_7314_replaced([11336104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wVSavPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), while

  * CSI-RS for channel measurement of Scell is 8 [CB008577-D] /32 [End CB008577-D] port CSI-RS, refer to 5G_UP_5129_replaced([11351695](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubwQxvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * And configured with setup of measurement GAP (measGapConfig is set to ‘Setup’ according to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2911_replaced([11341740](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWNnwPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),




Then,

\- P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will calculate whether all possible beam reports according to 5G_UP_ALG_2880_replaced([11123359](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or

\- CSI-RS reference signals for channel measurement are within measurement GAP period according to 5G_UP_ALG_2882_replaced([11123379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqi6kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) while

  * CSI-RS for channel measurement of Scell is 8 [CB008577-D] /32 [End CB008577-D] port CSI-RS**.**



If yes, then the UE DL scheduling and UL scheduling **over this Scell shall be suspended and target beam Id for Scell shall be marked as invalid.**

**Note If UE is configured with FR1 TDD Scell but the Scell is configured as actBeamforming = false, then the Dl scheduling in scell shall not be impacted by beam report.**

If UE is configured with release of measurement GAP (measGapConfig is set to ‘Release’ according to5G_CP_IF_RRC_2911_replaced([11341740](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWNnwPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will resume the UE DL scheduling and UL scheduling **over this Scell and target beam Id for Scell shall be marked as invalid. (Note: Scell target beam shall be updated after beam report is received. [CB008577-D] For FDD BF, target beam shall be updated after CSI report. [End CB008577-D])**

If UE is configured with FR1 Scell and **{dlMimoMode of Scell is configured other than ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4 or {actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true and nActivatedSsPbch (see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is greater than 4 and UE is configured with UE specific CSI-RS}} and CSI-RS reference signals for channel measurement are within measurement GAP period according to 5G_UP_ALG_2882_replaced([11123379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqi6kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will skip the scheduling of Scell CSI report according to 5G_UP_ALG_3484_replaced([11159099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktHGa_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If UE is configured with release of measurement GAP (measGapConfig is set to ‘Release’ according to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2911_replaced([11341740](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWNnwPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will resume the scheduling of Scell CSI report according to 5G_UP_ALG_3484_replaced([11159099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktHGa_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

For FR1 TDD [CB008577-D] /FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell which is deployed at different NRCELLGRP with P(S)Cell (different L2PS instances for P(S)Cell and Scell), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall sent the decision for Scell scheduling to Scell 5G-L2-PS through PsPeerCtrl interface. Scell 5G-L2-PS shall update the Scell scheduling decision and invalidate the Scell target beam Id in UE context after receiving the decision from P(S)Cell through PsPeerCtrl interface, in downlink **Scell 5G-L2-PS shall stop the flow control over Scell according to 5G_UP_ALG_5735_replaced([11221101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxzZMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) while need to suspend Scell scheduling, and shall start the flow control over Scell according to 5G_UP_ALG_5735_replaced([11221101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxzZMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** In uplink, Pcell 5G-L2-PS shall stop split buffer to Scell 5G-L2-PS while need to suspend Scell scheduling, and shall start split buffer to Scell 5G-L2-PS while need to resume Scell scheduling.

**Note 1:**

  * For inter-L2PS CA architect P(S)CELL 5G-L2-PS and Scell 5G-L2-PS will be different L2PS instance(different NRCELLGRP); For intra-L2PS CA architect P(S)CELL 5G-L2-PS and Scell 5G-L2-PS will be same L2PS instance(same NRCELLGRP).



**Note 2:**

Based on discussion, simple solution as follows will be proposed in 5G21A for all FR1 CA combination for measurement GAP setup.

  * In case FR1 TDD SCell confliction of CSI-RS/CSI report, setup of measurement GAP will be continous. 5G-L2-PS will validate whether all possible beam report is overlapped with the GAP. If yes, 5G-L2-PS will suspend Scell scheduling due to no target beam available for Scell PDSCH scheduling. The solution is covered by 5GC001390-E update 1.



**actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf: NRBTS.NRCELL.actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf**

**nActivatedSsPbch: Number of Activated SS/PBCH (See 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

**actBeamforming: NRBTS.NRCELL.actBeamforming**

---

###### 3.7.3.5.1.0-2 Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup &amp; Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell Decision of Scell Beam Report in Measurement GAP (ID: 11123359)

**3.7.3.5.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11123364`)

Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup & Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell The algorithm to calculate whether all possible beam reports are configured within measurement GAP period:

\- If Scell beam report period perCsiReportConfig.periodicity (note: unit in ms) is not small than measGapConfig.mgrp (unit in ms), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will consider all possible beam reports are within measurement GAP while one of the value n match the following condition.

measGapConfig.gapOffset - measGapConfig.Mgta + n _measGapConfig.mgrp <= DIV(perCsiReportConfig.slotOffset, 2^(P(S)Cell numerology)) <= measGapConfig.gapOffset - measGapConfig.Mgta + measGapConfig.mgl - 1 + n_ measGapConfig.mgrp

n = 0 .. DIV(DIV(perCsiReportConfig.periodicity, 2^(P(S)Cell numerology)), measGapConfig.mgrp) – 1

Cell numerology is calculated based on cell scs while 0 for scs=15, 1 for scs = 30, 3 for scs = 120;

Note: all above parameters are converted to the value with unit in ms; Measurement GAP parameters refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2919_replaced([11341781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWNn0_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); parameters of periodic resource for beam report refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_7314_replaced([11336104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wVSavPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

  * Otherwise P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will count there is beam report outside of configured measurement GAP.

---

###### 3.7.3.5.1.0-3 Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup &amp; Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell Decision of Scell Channel acquisition in Measurement GAP (ID: 11123369)

**3.7.3.5.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13257307`)

Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup & Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell L2 shall skip sending Csi decode request if the Ul slot for Scell channel feedback is in measurement Gap.

If UE is configured with FR1 Scell and {NIDD: **actCellCsiRsImTddNonBf is true or actCellCsiRsImTddNonBf is true [CB008577-D] or NIDD:dlMimoMode is CL32x4 [End CB008577-D]} :**

For UEs with cell specific CSI-RS **or for UEs with UE specific CSI-RS: L2 shall skip sending Csi decode request for channel acquisition if 1) all slot for CSI-RS for channel acquisition for this report are in measurement gap slot or 2) the Ul slot for Scell channel feedback are in measurement Gap.**

If UE is configured with release of measurement GAP (measGapConfig is set to ‘Release’ according to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2911_replaced([11341740](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWNnwPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will resume the scheduling of Scell CSI report according to 5G_UP_ALG_3484_replaced([11159099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktHGa_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

L2 shall check whether all possible Scell channel feedback are invalid due to measurement Gap, either because of CSI-RS or Ul slot for report is in Gap.

###### 3.7.3.5.1.0-4 Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup &amp; Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell Decision of Reference Signal for Scell Channel Measurement in Measurement GAP (ID: 11123379)

**3.7.3.5.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11123383`)

Scheduling Decision due to Measurement GAP Setup & Release for FR1 TDD [CB008577-D]/FDD [End CB008577-D] Scell The algorithm to calculate whether CSI-RS reference signals for channel measurement are configured within measurement GAP period:

\- If Scell reference signal period perCsiRsResConfig.periodicity (note: unit in ms) is not small than measGapConfig.mgrp (unit in ms), P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will consider reference signal is within measurement GAP while one of the value n match the following condition.

measGapConfig.gapOffset - measGapConfig.Mgta + n _measGapConfig.mgrp <= DIV(perCsiRsResConfig.slotOffset, 2^(SCell numerology)) <= measGapConfig.gapOffset - measGapConfig.Mgta + measGapConfig.mgl - 1 + n_ measGapConfig.mgrp

n = 0 .. DIV(DIV(perCsiRsResConfig.periodicity, 2^(SCell numerology)), measGapConfig.mgrp) – 1

Cell numerology is calculated based on cell scs while 0 for scs=15, 1 for scs = 30, 3 for scs = 120;

Note: all above parameters are converted to the value with unit in ms;

\- Otherwise P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will count there is reference signal outside of configured measurement GAP.

Note: While NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode of Scell is other than ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4, SSB and CSI-RS for beam refinement will not totally fall into the configured MG due to period of SSB and CSI-RS shall be smaller than period of MG(if period of SSB and CSI-RS for refine beam is equal or larger than period of MG, then UE will not be able to receive SSB of current serving cells).

  * Refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2925_replaced([11341805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWOO1vvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for measGapConfig.gapOffset.
  * Refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2919_replaced([11341781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWNn0_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for measGapConfig.mgrp.
  * Refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2919_replaced([11341781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWNn0_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for measGapConfig.Mgta.

---

### 3.7.3.6 Interworking with VoNR and other GBR flows

#### 3.7.3.6.0-1 Interworking with VoNR and other GBR flows VoNR and CA interworking without Capability lch-ToSCellRestriction (ID: 11123394)

**3.7.3.6.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11123414`)

Interworking with VoNR and other GBR flows For Interworking with non CA eligible DRB flows, a simplified approach shall be applied:

  * If logicalChannelConfig.allowedServingCells (see 5G_UP_4814_replaced([11358775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucjiCPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_CP_OTH_334_replaced([11598124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y2_VvfwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not configured, then at setup of any non CA eligible DRB PCell UL 5G-L2-PS suspends the PUSCH scheduling in SCell by stop splitting BSR to SCell, and retransmission in SCell uplink can be continued except FDD + FDD UL CA UE [CB006449-DA] or TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE [End CB006449-DA] which are in Configured Grant firing state (see 5G_UP_ALG_15099_replaced([11172972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuPu0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), at the last non CA eligible DRB release PCell UL 5G-L2-PS resumes the PUSCH scheduling in SCell by restart splitting BSR to SCell.



Notes:

  * PDSCH is not suspended.
  * 5G-L2-HI does not need to be informed about the suspend/resume.



 even when Scell is not scheduled in UL, PHR, BSR and RLC status PDUs can still be received via PCell. As there is no PUSCH scheduling on SCell, they would be needed only locally on PCell.

  * this approach is inline with the legacy approach of interworking of GBR with DL CA, where GBR is scheduled only on PCell's PDSCH, cf. 5G_UP_1397_replaced([11358720](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucjiAPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



CA eligible DRB and non CA eligible DRB refer to 5G_UP_10576_replaced([11358417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uchs1_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

### 3.7.3.7 Scheduling of CA UE with NBR bearer(s)

### 3.7.3.7-1 Scheduling of CA UE with NBR bearer(s)

#### 3.7.3.7-1.0-1 Scheduling of CA UE with NBR bearer(s) For UEs not having parallelTxPRACH-SRS-PUCCH-PUSCH capability If a CA UE is configured with a secondary TAG and if the UE is supposed to transmit a random access preamble in the Scell in an UL slot, PUSCH and aSRS shall be muted in the overlapping UL slot(s) in PCell. For PUCCH and pSRS, the behavior of the UE in the overlapping slots is left up to UE implementation. For UEs having parallelTxPRACH-SRS-PUCCH-PUSCH capability In this case, PUSCH and aperiodic SRS transmissions in overlapping UL slots in the Pcell shall be muted when the UE is supposed to transmit a preamble in the overlapping slot in the Scell. However, note that PUCCH and periodic SRS transmissions in the overlapping UL slot in the Pcell shall be allowed and the transmission power allocation shall be prioritized based on section 7.5 in 38.213. Similarly, For PUSCH (MSG3) Scell, the transmission power allocation shall be prioritized based on section 7.5 in 38.213. For UEs with UL Tx Switching Capability For a multi-TAG UE  configured with UL Tx Switching and having a CA configuration of TDD Pcell+FDD Scell, PUSCH and aperiodic SRS, shall be blocked on the TDD UL slot overlapping with or adjacent to an FDD UL slot where the UE is supposed to send its CFRA preamble to the Scell. If the preamble transmission in the Scell overlaps with or is adjacent to PUCCH/pSRS in the Pcell, the handling is left up to the UE. For a multi-TAG UE  configured with UL Tx Switching and having a CA configuration of FDD Pcell+TDD Scell, no special handling is needed since UL Tx Switching shall favour TDD slots and PRACH transmissions should be feasible without any drawbacks. For more details about transmissions in overlapping slots, refer to Refer to 13454164 and 11208767 . (ID: 13440043)

#### 3.7.3.7.0-1 Scheduling of CA UE with NBR bearer(s) The ratio of PBRi,j to be used for the token bucket on PCell/SCell(s) (ID: 11123423)

**3.7.3.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11123427`)

Scheduling of CA UE with NBR bearer(s) For DL CA UEs, NBR functionality is considered enabled on

  * PCell if actNbrForNonGbrBearers is set to true on PCell.

  * SCell if actNbrForNonGbrBearers is set to true on PCell and on SCell.




For UL CA UEs, NBR functionality is considered enabled on

  * PCell if actNbrForNonGbrBearers is set to true on PCell.



Note:If UE doesn't support the capability: lch-ToSCellRestriction and send UL NBR data in SCell(s), the NBR data will be scheduled as Non-GBR.

As NBR DRBs are scheduled on Pcell only in UL, NBR rrmNbrPbr_kbps(i,j) split for UEs configured NBR bearers with active SCell(s) should only be used for DL CA.

L2 PS shall determine a rrmNbrPbr_kbps(i,j) split for UEs configured NBR bearers with active SCell(s) in the TD scheduler. The ratio between rrmNbrPbr_kbps(i,j) to be used for the token bucket on PCell/SCell(s) as following:

All active serving cells configured with NBR bearers which are not in overheating status according to 5G_UP_ALG_2874_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are selected for the rrmNbrPbr_kbps(i,j) split;

L2-PS shall calculate how many CCs are needed to transmit the total amount of NBR data available for DL transmission in drbTraffic class (NBR Category):

rrmNumServCellsForNBRDataTrans = rrmNumActiveCellsWithNBR – rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsWithNBR

Where:

  * rrmNumActiveCellsWithNBR = 'number of active serving cells of the UE with NBR bearers configured'

  * rrmNumActiveOverheatingSCellsWithNBR = 'number of active serving Scell(s) for the UE with NBR bearers configured in overheating status'




After SCell(s) is/are activated, rrmNbrPbr_kbps_SplitServCell_kbps(i,j,k) shall be initialized to:

1/ rrmNumServCellsForNBRDataTrans * rrmNbrPbr_kbps(i,j)

Note: If all Scell(s) are deactivated, rrmNumServCellsForNBRDataTrans=1.

L2-PS shall determine the corresponding rrmNbrPbr_kbps(i,j) split for each UE when Scell(s) activation/deactivation status change or serving cell(s) overheating status change:

The rrmNumServCellsForNBRDataTrans will be updated.

rrmNbrPbr_kbps_SplitServCell_kbps(i,j,k) =1/ rrmNumServCellsForNBRDataTrans * rrmNbrPbr_kbps(i,j)

where:

rrmNbrPbr_kbps(i,j) defined in 5G_UP_ALG_22083_replaced([11175539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuj34fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For FR1 CA, PCell should signal the rrmNbrPbr_kbps_SplitServCell_kbps(i,j,k) to relative Scell

---

## 3.7.4 Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm

### 3.7.4.0-2 Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm Document Owner Deputy Piotr Legutko; Tomasz Wojcik (ID: 11123441)

### 3.7.4.1 Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm

#### 3.7.4.1.0-1 Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm Applicablility of Distributed PUCCH Allocation algorithm (ID: 11123453)

**3.7.4.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11123462`)

Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm If( NRBTS/NRDU.flexibleCAMode is set to a value greater than 0 and cell type is not FR2)

{

L2PS shall perform Distributed PUCCH Allocation(DPA) Algorithm;

If pucchModeSelect is set as shortPucch, the Cell can only be Scell

Note: UE with SCell activated shall be considered as CA UE

}

[Before CNI-88614]else

{

the L2PS shall perform Pipeline(5G_UP­_1383) PUCCH Allocation Algorithm for FDD+TDD CA UE;

}

Note:Pipeline solution is not supported anymore.

[End CNI-88614]

Note: Although the UE is eligible for Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm, it may happen that for a UE in a particular slot, based on K1 value as mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_2473_replaced([11116092](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), UE is not allocated PUCCH resource as per 5G_UP_ALG_2924_replaced([11123706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), UE on P(S)Cell shall use normal PUCCH Allocation Algorithm.

Note: For UE configured with FR1 TDD + FDD CA, Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA) shall be also be deployed to allocate PUCCH; there is no extra update to existing SFS requirements for DPA, this requirement is created and linked to 5GC002329 to avoid missing impact/effort analysis in subsequent CFAM stages; For the details of DPA algorithm, see 5G_UP_ALG_2890_replaced([11123479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2892_replaced([11123510](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2938_replaced([11123876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqmk9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

pucchModeSelect: NRBTS.NRCELL.pucchModeSelect

Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm 11123475: Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm 11123475: Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm 11123475: Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm 11123475: Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm 11123475: Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm 11123475: Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm 11123475: Applicability of Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm The definition of DPA cycle is as follows, while including 3 parts: UE Measurement Cycle, Measurement Processing Cycle and Scheduling Cycle.  UE Measurement Cycle (unit: ms) – Cycle while 5G-L2-PS will measure CA UE CS1 attempt ratio in all activated serving cells;  Measurement Processing Cycle (unit: ms) – Cycle while P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS will coordinate all measurement result from all CA UEs’ serving cells, and pre-allocate available PUCCH resources in next Scheduling Cycle for HARQ A/N for CA UEs’s scheduling over all activated serving cell;  Scheduling Cycle (unit: ms) – Cycle while all serving cells schedule DL PDSCH for CA UEs based on PUCCH resource allocation for HARQ A/N in Measurement Processing Cycle. All above cycles shall be same for all serving cells with CA relationship, while Scheduling cycle shall be aligned to SFN boundary so the available PUCCH resource can be calculated based on frame structure and related configurations, say start point of scheduling cycle shall match the condition of (Frame number mod Scheduling cycle = 0). Note: The lengths of Measurement Processing Cycle and UE measurement cycle shall be based on the processing capability(defined based on implementation) and will not need to be aligned to SFN boundary. The detail is as following diagram. [image-0][image_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating two "DPA Cycles," labeled DPA Cycle-1 and DPA Cycle-2. Each cycle is represented by a timeline divided into segments. DPA Cycle-1 starts with a series of blue blocks, labeled "UE Measurement Cycle(Unit:ms)". This is followed by a section of red blocks, labeled "Measurement Processing Cycle(Unit:ms)". After the red blocks, there are yellow blocks representing "Scheduling Cycle(Unit:ms based on PUCCH Slots)". Within the yellow blocks, individual slots are marked as "D/U". An arrow labeled "K1" points from the end of the red blocks to the beginning of the yellow blocks. Below this, a longer arrow indicates the "Actual Scheduling Cycle(Unit:ms based on PDSCH Slots)". The cycle is bounded by "SFN Boundary" markers. DPA Cycle-2 is shown below DPA Cycle-1 and is offset in time. A label on the left indicates "Timing difference between two continuous DPA cycle = Scheduling Cycle". Similar to DPA Cycle-1, it begins with blue blocks for "UE Measurement Cycle(Unit:ms)", followed by red blocks for "Measurement Processing Cycle(Unit:ms)", and then yellow blocks for "Scheduling Cycle(Unit:ms based on PUCCH Slots)". The yellow slots are also marked as "D/U". An arrow labeled "K1" is present, and an arrow indicates the "Actual Scheduling Cycle(Unit:ms based on PDSCH Slots)". This cycle is also bounded by "SFN Boundary" markers. The diagram visually represents the timing and relationships between different processing and scheduling cycles within a communication system, highlighting the measurement, processing, and scheduling phases, as well as the concept of actual scheduling based on PDSCH slots. The offset between the two DPA cycles is explicitly defined as the "Scheduling Cycle".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6840.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Note: There is one corner case where PUCCH resource is allocated during Measurement Processing Cycle however Scell deactivation happened during Scheduling Cycle. gNB will still schedule DCI based on original c-DAI/t-DAI calculation which UE behaviour is unknown, the proposal can be to delay the Scell deactivation till the boundary of Scheduling Cycle to avoid the ambiguity. The corner case can be considered later based on IoDT with UE considering the big effort. File: DPA Cycle.xlsx Folder:

### 3.7.4.2 UE Measurement Cycle

#### 3.7.4.2.0-1 UE Measurement Cycle Cell Measurements in UE measurement cycle (ID: 11123485)

**3.7.4.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11123491`)

UE Measurement Cycle Prior to sharing the measurement information to P(S)Cell Scheduler, each DL Scheduler (including the P(S)Cell Scheduler) shall calculate cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx for each CA UE with distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which is just the ratio of number of times UE is in the pre-scheduler candidate list to the number of DL slots in the UE measurement cycle(rdAvgTimeSCSAttRatio_msec (default 40 msec)). The calculation of DL slots for CA UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate list should not take account into DRX from on duration to off duration.

If CA UE with distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not measured in the previous measurement cycle (eg: The SCell is from deactivated to activated and in pre-scheduler candidate list after the measurements are sent), the UE shall have cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx = rdDefaultCs1AttempRatio(default value is 0.75) in the next measurement cycle (5G_UP_ALG_2936_replaced([11123865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqmk8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), so that it gets preference in the next scheduling cycle. If Scell from activated to deactivated, the UE shall no cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx.

Note: This ratio is calculated for the time period of last rdAvgTimeSCSAttRatio_msec (default 40 msec).

  * rdAvgTimeSCSAttRatio_msec (5G_L2_1468_replaced([11184390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27qsGfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * rdDefaultCs1AttempRatio (5G_L2_1470_replaced([11184401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27qsG_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

#### 3.7.4.2.0-2 UE Measurement Cycle Serving Cell Measurements for Distributed PUCCH Algorithm (Dynamic PUCCH Split) (ID: 11123496)

**3.7.4.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11123507`)

UE Measurement Cycle P(S)Cell DL Pre-Scheduler shall calculate initial value of numNonCAUe as following:

numNonCAUe=Sum(the number of all UE in the pre-Scheduler candidate list) -Sum(the number of CA UEs in the pre-Scheduler candidate list)

P(S)Cell DL Pre-Scheduler, for each UE(j), shall also keep a cumulative count of

For every slot(i), numUe(i) across all j

P(S)Cell DL Pre-Scheduler, for each UE(j) with Scell activation, shall also keep a cumulative count of

For every slot(i), numCAUe(i) across all j

numNonCAUe(i) = numUe(i) - numCAUe(i)

where:

numUe(i) is the number of all UEs in the pre-Scheduler candidate list on slot i

numCAUe(i) is the number of CA UEs in the pre-Scheduler candidate list on slot i

numNonCAUe(i) is the number of Non-CA UEs in the pre-Scheduler candidate list on slot i

This info is stored for the last [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec (default 10ms) (see 5G_L2_1464_replaced([11184335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27qFFfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ](default 10ms) (see 5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: For more details on Distributed PUCCH algorithm, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2884_replaced([11123433](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqi6nfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: For more details on checking the PUCCH resource availability, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4217_replaced([11174808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: To determine which bearers of a CA UE does not need data split, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2834_replaced([11122266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqeCH_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: This requirement is applicable only if distributed PUCCH algorithm is enabled(5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Note: Each DL SCell Scheduler need to share the above information to P(S)Cell Scheduler every [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ](5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced\(\[11123971\]\(https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ\)\)).

Note: If the Scell UE is [RLQ bad] or [Overheating], Scell does not send this UE's info to PCell by msg PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep.

Upon reception of notification to stop DPA measurement for the designated SCell UE located in ext-gNB, SCell located in ext-gNB shall exclude this UE in measurement process procedure.

### 3.7.4.3 Measurement Processing Cycle

#### 3.7.4.3.0-1 Measurement Processing Cycle Share Measurements by SCell to P(S)Cell (ID: 11123516)

**3.7.4.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11123530`)

Measurement Processing Cycle For CA UEs with distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), each SCell Scheduler shall share the cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx (5G_UP_ALG_2891_replaced([11123485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value to the P(S)Cell Scheduler.

Note: P(S)Cell will use the previous value if it does not receive the necessary information for the UE.

Note: Each DL SCell Scheduler need to share the above information to P(S)Cell Scheduler every [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ](5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced\(\[11123971\]\(https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ\)\)).

Note: If the Scell UE is [RLQ bad] or [Overheating], Scell does not send this UE's info to PCell by msg PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep.

Upon reception of notification to stop DPA measurement for the designated SCell UE located in ext-gNB, SCell located in ext-gNB shall exclude this UE in measurement process procedure.

#### 3.7.4.3.0-2 Measurement Processing Cycle Share cell load status flag by SCell to P(S)Cell (ID: 11123534)

**3.7.4.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11123545`)

Measurement Processing Cycle Each SCell Scheduler shall share the scellLoadStateForActivation flag (5G_UP_ALG_8844_replaced([11174560](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudKNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to the P(S)Cell Scheduler.

P(S)Cell shall update the scellLoadStateForActivation flag in its database (5G_UP_ALG_2683_replaced([11120559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR03PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the information from SCells.

Note: P(S)Cell will use the previous value if it does not receive the necessary information for the SCell.

SCell shall share measurement process cycle (MeasProcTime(11ms) (5G_UP_ALG_2936_replaced([11123865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqmk8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) prior to PDSCH scheduling cycle.

Note: Each DL SCell Scheduler need to share the above information to P(S)Cell Scheduler every [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ] (5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

#### 3.7.4.3.0-3 Measurement Processing Cycle Slot Pattern information needed by P(S)Cell - used for determining HARQ C-DAI/T-DAI (ID: 11123549)

**3.7.4.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13333317`)

Measurement Processing Cycle For PUCCH allocation(5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), following is configured in the slot pattern

A slot format indicates the number of DL and/or UL symbols in the slot:

\- DLx indicates a 14 OFDM symbol slot with x DL OFDM symbols only, followed by (14-x) GP OFDM symbols. 

\- ULy indicates a 14 OFDM symbol slot with y UL OFDM symbols only, preceeded by (14-y) GP OFDM symbols.

\- BIx y indicates a 14 OFDM symbol slot with x DL OFDM symbols starting from 0, followed by (14-x-y) GP OFDM symbols, and y UL symbols until the end of the slot.

Note: The information is given by CP-RT as part of its User setup / modify procedures.

In addition, CP-RT shall also give information to P(S)Cell if the serving cell is DSS or non-DSS. This is needed for P(S)Cell to calculate c-dai/t-dai. The slot pattern change of the serving cells which are in DSS [CB007372-H] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-H] mode are considered while allocating PUCCH resources for the UE as mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_2924_replaced([11123706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). SCells, if DSS [CB007372-H] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-H], shall share the slot pattern change to P(S)Cell.

---

#### 3.7.4.3.0-4 Measurement Processing Cycle DSS cell Information of P(S)Cell needed by SCells (ID: 11123558)

**3.7.4.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11123563`)

Measurement Processing Cycle CP-RT shall also give information to SCells if the P(S)Cell is DSS or non-DSS.
