#### 3.7.4.3.1 P(S)Cell Processing the measurements

##### 3.7.4.3.1-1 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE

###### 3.7.4.3.1-1.0-2 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE Once the mapping is done (UE to a PUCCH resource for the scheduling cycle (5G_UP_ALG_2938_replaced( 11123876 ))) as per 5G_UP_ALG_2924_replaced( 11123706 ), following info shall be shared to each of the SCells. a) mapping of CA UE (applicable for the SCell) to the PUCCH F1 resource unit. b) mapping of CA UE (applicable for the SCell) to the PUCCH F3 resource unit. [CB008140-AC] If inter-gNB CA is enabled (NRNBTS/NRDU.actInterGnbCa = TRUE): - the message size for delivering DPA allocation result from PCell to SCell shall not exceed the MTU (1280 bytes) of ethernet, that is, the DPA allocation result shall be delivered to SCell individually for each UL slot in the scheduling period, one message per UL slot. [End CB008140-AC] [CB008140-BE] - if no UE among the UEs configured with the given ext-SCell is scheduled in this particular ext-SCell within the Scheduling Cycle, the dummy PUCCH pre-allocation indication message shall be sent to this ext-SCell for purpose of Xp link delay monitoring (5G_UP_ALG_12816_replaced( 11122039 )) [End CB008140-BE] Notes: 1. This requirement is applicable only If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced( 11123447 ). 2. PUCCH resource unit refers to PUCCH resources in both time and frequency domain. For ex: if 12 F1 PUCCH resources are configured, in span of 10 slots, we have 10*12 PUCCH F1 resource units. (ID: 11123860)

##### 3.7.4.3.1-2 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE

###### 3.7.4.3.1-2.0-1 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE Length of the Measurement Processing Cycle shall be controlled via MeasProcTime_msec (11ms) Note: This requirement is applicable only if Distributed PUCCH algorithm is enabled(5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced( 11123447 )) (ID: 11123870)

##### 3.7.4.3.1.0-1 P(S)Cell Processing the measurements Order of PUCCH F1 and F3 resources (ID: 11123572)

**3.7.4.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11123577`)

P(S)Cell Processing the measurements For the cell with distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the scheduler shall assign random values for PUCCH F1 resource unit rank (pucchF1ResUnitRank) for FDD as P(S)Cell and F3 resource unit rank (pucchF3ResUnitRank) separately.

Note: Randomization is done for avoiding resource assignment in the same order all the time which could produce sub optimal resource utilization. The random value is selected from range (0..1) with adequate granularity, so that there is unique rank value for each resource.

Note: PUCCH resource unit refers to PUCCH resources in both time and frequency domain. For ex for FDD as P(S)Cell: if 12 F1 PUCCH resources are configured, in a span of 10 UL slots during Scheduling Cycle, we have 10*12 PUCCH F1 resource units.

---

##### 3.7.4.3.1.1 Measurement Processing

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-1 Measurement Processing The Ratio of CA UE in pre-scheduler candidate list (cs1AttemptRatio) (ID: 11123588)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11123594`)

Measurement Processing For CA UEs with distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), measurements from the PCell and all active SCells are added up and averaged:

cs1AttemptRatio = max (cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx)

Note: Ncc refers to number of Active Serving Cells.

If Scellx are changed from activation to deactivation during Measurement period, cs1AttempRatioServingCellx shall not be considered.

If Scellx are changed from deactivation to activation during Measurement period, cs1AttempRatioServingCellx shall be considered.

Note: For cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2893_replaced([11123516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-2 Measurement Processing The sum of ratio of UEs in pre-scheduler candidate list (totalCS1AttemptRatio) (ID: 11123599)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11123602`)

Measurement Processing Distributed PUCCH algorithm needs to determine the totalCS1AttemptRatio of CA UEs with distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

totalCS1AttemptRatio = sum of cs1AttemptRatio of all UEs which uses Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm in the cell.

Note: For cs1AttemptRatio, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2903_replaced([11123588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkIvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-3 Measurement Processing Number of available PUCCH F1 and F3 resources (ID: 11123608)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11123618`)

Measurement Processing Distributed PUCCH algorithm needs to determine how many of PUCCH resources used for ACK/NACK are available for UEs.

  * f1Addressable is the union of Cell level PUCCH Format 1 resources during pucch scheduling cycle([Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec (default 10 msec)[CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ] ),number of PUCCH F1 resources used for HARQ A/N, that is,f1Addressable = MIN{configuredPf1ForHarqAn *numUlSlotWithinSchedulingCycle, SUM(rrmNumOfF1ForHarq[i])};
  * f3Addressable is the union of Cell level PUCCH Format 3 resources based on number of UL slots during Scheduling Cycle considering P(S)Cell frame structure, number of PUCCH F3 resources used for HARQ A/N, that is, f3Addressable = MIN{configuredPf3ForHarqAn*numUlSlotWithinSchedulingCycle, SUM(rrmNumOfF3ForHarq[i])};



Where:

configuredPf1ForHarqAn: number of PUCCH format1 resources for HARQ-AN feedback of all the RRC connected UEs, the detailed method for determine configuredPf1ForHarqAn is left for CP3 stage.

configuredPf3ForHarqAn:number of PUCCH format3 resources for HARQ-AN feedback of all the RRC connected UEs, for example: there are 2 RRC connected UEs in the cell, for UE#1, the configured PUCCH format3 resources for HARQ-AN are: {#0, #1, #2, #3, #4, #5, #6, #7}; for the UE#2 the configured PUCCH format3 resource for HARQ-AN are : {#1, #2, #3, #4, #5, #6, #7, #8}, in this case configuredPf3ForHarqAn is 9, the detailed method for determineing numPf3ForHarqAn is left for CP3 stage.

numUlSlotWithinSchedulingCycle: number of UL slots within one scheudling cycle of DPA;

i: UL slot index within scheudling cycle;

rrmNumOfF1ForHarq[i]: number of PUCCH format1 resources that can be used for HARQ-AN in UL slot[i] as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2465_replaced([11116066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

Note: rrmNumOfF1ForHarq[i] may be not accurate because DPA is pre-allocation and the number of connected UEs may be different on next scheduling cycle of DPA.

rrmNumOfF3ForHarq[i]: number of PUCCH format3 resources that can be used for HARQ-AN in UL slot[i] as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2465_replaced([11116066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

For number of PUCCH resources used for HARQ ACK/NACK for FDD as P(S)Cell, refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2859_replaced([11309978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrMSC_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For number of PUCCH F3 resources used for HARQ A/N per UL slot for TDD as P(S)Cell, refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2862_replaced([11310025](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrM5BPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for #PRB(HARQ AN).

PUCCH format1 refer to 5G_L2_947_replaced([11180342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MK8_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and PUCCH format 3 refer to 5G_L2_954_replaced([11180444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MyA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec refer to 5G_L2_1464_replaced([11184335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27qFFfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ] (5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: Each DL SCell Scheduler need to share the above information to P(S)Cell Scheduler every [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ] (5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-4 Measurement Processing Calculation of UE weight (ID: 11123623)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11123633`)

Measurement Processing Distributed PUCCH algorithm needs to determine the priority of CA UEs with distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the PUCCH resources assignment. The priority (ueWeight) is based on the normalized cs1AttemptRatio. Note: Normalization is needed when the total demand for PUCCH resources (totalCS1AttemptRatio) is higher than all available PUCCH resources.

For FDD Cell as P(S)Cell:

If totalCS1AttemptRatio > (totalF1PUCCHDistributedResourceUnits + f3Addressable)/PUCCH slots in [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec[CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec [End CB012528-D ]

ueWeight(i) for user i = (totalF1PUCCHDistributedResourceUnits +f3Addressable)/PUCCH slots in [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec[CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec [End CB012528-D ]

* (cs1AttemptRatio for user i / totalCS1AttemptRatio )

else

ueWeight(i) for user i = cs1AttemptRatio for user i.

For FR1 TDD Cell as P(S)Cell:

ueWeight(i) for user i = cs1AttemptRatio for user i

Where f1Addressable and f3Addressable are the number of available PUCCH F1 and F3 resources, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2907_replaced([11123608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Where totalCS1AttemptRatio is the sum of ratio of UE in the pre-scheduler candidate list, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2905_replaced([11123599](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

where cs1AttemptRatio is the ratio of UE in the pre-scheduler candidate list, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2903_replaced([11123588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkIvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before CB012528-D ]

where rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec is defined in 5G_L2_1464_replaced([11184335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27qFFfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012528-D ]

where rrmSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB012528-D ]

where totalF1PUCCHDistributedResourceUnits and pucchF1SplitDistributed are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2918_replaced([11123676](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-5 Measurement Processing Calculation of Number of CA UE(P(S)Cell Scheduler) (ID: 11123639)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11123647`)

Measurement Processing Each DL P(S)cell Scheduler shall calculate numCAUe for all downlink slots in the last frame of UE measurement cycle.

With FDD or FR1 TDD as P(S)Cell:

rrmNumCAUe = Roundup((sum of max(cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx of each CA UE across all activated serving cells) of all CA UEs) * rrmNumOfDlSlotInPCell * weight); 

Where

weight define the weight for number of CA UE calculation to avoid the calculation is too optimistic or pessimistic. The value shall be defined based on implementation(proposed default value: 0.8)

rrmNumOfDlSlotInPCell defines the number of DL slots in PCell in following scheduling cycle(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

f3Addressable is the union of PUCCH Format 3 resources configured for all UEs during [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec (default 10 msec)[CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ].

Rational: To calculate the CA UE ratio for PUCCH pre-allocation, 5G-L2-PS needs to calculate the number of CA UEs running into CS1 list and the number of non-CA UEs running into CS1 list per scheduling cycle. However it is not possible to calculate the CA UEs running into CS1 across multiple scheduler, so the simple algorithm is as follows:

 cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx refer to ratio of CA UEs in pre-scheduler list in last measurement cycle while number of non-CA UE in pre-scheduler list is calculated based on the last period (the length equals scheduling cycle time) during last measurement cycle. Note: the length of measurement cycle is different to scheduling cycle, however still use the cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx in last measurement cycle for simplicity.

 Maximum of cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx across all activated serving cells define the maximum scheduling opportunity for one CA UE;

 Sum of maximum cs1AttemptRatioServingCellx for all CA UEs will be counted as approximation of number of CA UEs in last scheduling cycle. Note: the calculation will be a bit optimistic which can be adjusted by the weight.

Each DL P(S)Cell Scheduler shall also calculate Sum(numNonCAUe(i)) for all the slots in the last [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec (default 10ms)[CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ]

Note: For numNonCAUe(i), please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4215_replaced([11123496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: Each DL Scheduler need to calculate the above every [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ] (5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-6 Measurement Processing Processing of Measurements needed for PUCCH F1 format resources split (ID: 11123653)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11123661`)

Measurement Processing rrmNumNonCAUe = Sum(numNonCAUe(i))

CARatio = rrmNumCAUe / max((rrmNumCAUe+rrmNumNonCAUe), 1) across all downlink slots in the last frame of UE measurement cycle

NonCARatio = rrmNumNonCAUe / max((rrmNumCAUe+rrmNumNonCAUe), 1) across all downlink slots in the last frame of UE measurement cycle.

The P(S)Cell scheduler shall calculate the above every [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ] (5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: This requirement is applicable only If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is applicable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

numNonCA(i) is the number of Non-CA UEs in slot number i. Please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4215_replaced([11123496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in detail. 

rrmNumNonCAUe is the number of non-CA UE during last scheduling cycle.

rrmNumCAUe is the number of CA UE estimated during last Measurement Cycle(Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2912_replaced([11123639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-7 Measurement Processing PUCCH F3 Split Ratio for Distributed PUCCH Allocation (ID: 11123667)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11123672`)

Measurement Processing following ratios shall be calculated for PUCCH F3 resources split between CA UEs and non-CA UEs per scheduling cycle(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If rrmNumCAUe > 0 then

rrmCARatioF3 = rrmNumCAUe / (rrmNumCAUe + rrmNumNonCAUe) ;

Otherwise

rrmCARatioF3 = 0;

Where:

rrmNumNonCAUe is the number of non-CA UE during last scheduling cycle which is sum(numNonCA(i)). numNonCA(i) is the number of Non-CA UEs in slot number i (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4215_replaced([11123496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmNumCAUe is the number of CA UE estimated during last Measurement Cycle(Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2912_replaced([11123639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-8 Measurement Processing PUCCH F1 Resources Split (ID: 11123676)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11123688`)

Measurement Processing Only some PUCCH F1 resource units which are applicable for Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm and the number of PUCCH F1 resource units are applicable for Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm is calculated as mentioned below.

Step 1:

Dynamic adjustment PUCCH F1 format resource units Split based on the number of non-CA UEs and CA UEs on P(S)cell

This is applicable if rrmNumNonCAUe and rrmNumCAUe as per 5G_UP_ALG_2914_replaced([11123653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvy_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are available and if pucchF1SplitDistributed is calculated in the previous [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ] (5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

pucchF1SplitDistributed = min (CARatio, 0.8)

Step 2: For CA UEs, allocate PUCCH format 1 resources based on distributed PUCCH algorithm. The remains PUCCH format 1 resource Units will be used by non-CA UEs.

a.Calculate the number of F1 resources for CA UEs during the whole scheduling cycle based on the available PUCCH F1 resources of UL slots in the scheduling cycle and split factor(pucchF1SplitDistributed) based on ration of CA UEs over CA UEs and non-CA UEs:

rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq = roundup(SUM(rrmNumOfF1ForHarq[i]) * pucchF1SplitDistributed);

b. Calculate the number of F1 resources for CA UEs per UL slot based on split factor(pucchF1SplitDistributed) and dynamic calculated maximum number of F1 resource per UL slot (rrmNumOfF1ForHarq):

rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq[i] = rounddown(rrmNumOfF1ForHarq[i] * pucchF1SplitDistributed);

c. The delta F1 resource of step a and step b:

delta =rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq – SUM(rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq[i]);

For the first number of delta slots during scheduling cycle, the number of F1 resources that can be used for CA UEs HARQ-AN in slot[i] is as followed:

rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq[i] = rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq[i] + 1;

For the remaining slots during scheduling cycle, the number of F1 resources that can be used for CA UEs HARQ-AN in slot[i] is as followed:

rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq[i] = rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq[i];

The number of PUCCH F1 resources that can be allocated by DPA to CA UEs in slot[i] is as followed:

numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i] = MIN{ rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq[i], roundup(configuredPf1ForHarqAn* pucchF1SplitDistributed)};

where:

i:index of UL slot within DPA scheduling cycle;

rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq:the number of F1 resources that can be used for CA UEs HARQ-AN during the whole scheduling cycle

rrmNumOfCAF1ForHarq[i]:the number of F1 resources that can be used for CA UEs HARQ-AN in slot[i]

rrmNumOfF1ForHarq[i]: number of PUCCH format1 resources that can be used for HARQ-AN in UL slot[i] as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2465_replaced([11116066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

configuredPf1ForHarqAn: see 5G_UP_ALG_2907_replaced([11123608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i]: number of PUCCH F1 resources that can be allocated by DPA to CA UEs in slot[i];

The remaining PUCCH F1 resources in each UL slot can be used for non-CA UE scheduling in Scheduling Cycle.

Step 3: The number of PUCCH F1 resource units needed for Distributed PUCCH Allocation algorithm.

totalF1PUCCHDistributedResourceUnits = max (sum(numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i]), rrmNumUeActScells)

Note:If the CA UEs but no pre-allocation PUCCH resource Unit, the CA UE can use non-CA UE Resource Unit(Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4217_replaced([11174808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note:f1Addressable is the union of PUCCH Format 1 resources configured for all UEs during [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec(default 10 msec) [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec[End CB012528-D ] (Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2907_replaced([11123608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: The selection of resource unit for the above can be random or any other method and can be decided in CP3 requirement.

Note: This requirement is applicable only If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is applicable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: rrmNumUeActScells is the number of UEs with active SCell(s) (see 5G_UP_ALG_10438_replaced([11121957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqbl2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.1.0-9 Measurement Processing PUCCH F3 Resources Split for FR1 TDD P(S)Cell (ID: 11123693)

**3.7.4.3.1.1.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11123699`)

Measurement Processing PUCCH resources for HARQ A/N during Scheduling Cycle shall be split for CA UEs and non-CA UEs scheduling per UL slots. The algorithm to split PUCCH resources will be as follows:

Step 1: Define the split ratio for PUCCH resource

pucchF3SplitRatioforDPA = min (rrmCARatioF3, 0.8)

where

  * rrmCARatioF3, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2912_replaced([11123639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))



Step 2: Determine the number of PUCCH F3 resource units needed for Distributed PUCCH Allocation algorithm.

totalF3PUCCHDistributedResourceUnits = roundup(pucchF3SplitRatioforDPA * numberOfF3ResourceUnits).

Where:

numberOfF3ResourceUnits is the number of PUCCH F3 resources in union of f3Addressable (Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2907_replaced([11123608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Step 3: Distribute PUCCH F3 resources to CA UEs within DPA loop per UL slot in Scheduling Cycle

delta = roundup(SUM(rrmNumOfF3ForHarq[i]) * pucchSplitRatioForDPA) – SUM(rounddown(rrmNumOfF3ForHarq[i] * pucchSplitRatioForDPA));

if(MOD(delta, numUlSlotWithinSchedCycle) > 0)

{

extra = rounddown(delta / numUlSlotWithinSchedCycle);

For the first N = MOD(delta, numUlSlotWithinSchedCycle) UL slot(s) in scheduling cycle:

{

numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i] = rounddown(rrmNumOfF3ForHarq[i] * pucchSplitRatioForDPA) + extra + 1;

}

For the rest UL slot(s) in scheduling cycle:

{

numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i] = rounddown(rrmNumOfF3ForHarq[i] * pucchSplitRatioForDPA) + extra;

}

}

else

{

extra = delta / numUlSlotWithinSchedCycle;

numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i] = rounddown(rrmNumOfF3ForHarq[i] * pucchSplitRatioForDPA) + extra;

}

numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i] = MIN{numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i], roundup(configuredPf3ForHarqAn * pucchSplitRatioForDPA)};

where:

i: index of UL slot within DPA scheduling cycle;

rrmNumOfF3ForHarq[i]: number of PUCCH format3 resources that can be used for HARQ-AN in UL slot[i] as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2465_replaced([11116066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

configuredPf3ForHarqAn: see 5G_UP_ALG_2907_replaced([11123608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

numPucchResForCaUePerSlot[i]: number of PUCCH F3 resources that can be allocated by DPA to CA UEs in slot[i];

The remaining PUCCH F3 resources in each UL slot can be used for non-CA UE scheduling in Scheduling Cycle.

Note:

  * Precondition is to activate PUCCH and PRACH multiplexing with DPA algorithm.
  * There is PUCCH resources for HARQ A/N over all UL slots.
  * If the CA UEs but no pre-allocation PUCCH resource Unit, the CA UE can use non-CA UE Resource Unit. (Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4217_replaced([11174808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

##### 3.7.4.3.1.2 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE

##### 3.7.4.3.1.2-1 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE

###### 3.7.4.3.1.2-1.0-2 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE In order to determine PUCCH resource allocation and C/T-DAI, P(S)Cell shall know the slot pattern of  SCells as mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_2895_replaced( 11123549 ) For non DSS cells [CB007372-H] and for DSS cells with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true [End CB007372-H], search space start symbol is 0. Note: The information is given by CP-RT during User Setup / Modify Procedures. (ID: 12678490)

###### 3.7.4.3.1.2.0-1 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE PUCCH Resource Allocation for CA UE (ID: 11123707)

**3.7.4.3.1.2.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `11123747`)

Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE [CB011081-A] No functional changes, split from the previous version [End CB011081-A]

Overview

PUCCH resource allocation for CA UEs is performed by Distributed PUCCH Allocation (DPA) algorithm. 

The Distributed PUCCH Allocation algorithm works per UL slot (HARQ bundling window) separately for Format 1 (Round-2 see 5G_UP_ALG_28065_replaced([11123772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql94fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and Format 3 (Round-1 see 5G_UP_ALG_28063_replaced([11123756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FDD or FR1 TDD as P(S)Cell. 

To assign PUCCH resources to CA UEs, DPA: 

 Orders UEs according to calculated UE weight from the highest to the lowest (ueWeight as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2910_replaced([11123623](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkvxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and 

 Orders PUCCH resource unit ranks according to assigned random values from the highest to the lowest (pucchF1ResUnitRank and pucchF3ResUnitRank as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2900_replaced([11123572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkIu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 

Outcome of above allocation is a kind of matrix with time over PUCCH resources assigned to CA UEs. FDD eg: 

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
|  | slot n | slot n+1 | slot n+2 | slot n+3 | slot n+4 | slot n+5 | slot n+6 | slot n+7 | slot n+8 | slot n+9  
PUCCH F3 | #0 | UE1 | UE4 | UE4 | UE1 | UE4 | UE8 | UE13 | UE1 | UE15 | UE4  
PUCCH F3 | #1 | UE4 | UE6 | UE8 | UE4 | UE11 | UE1 | UE15 | UE4 | UE8 | UE15  
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |   
PUCCH F1 | #0 | UE2 | UE12 |  | UE8 | UE16 | UE4 |  | UE16 | UE1 | UE1  
PUCCH F1 | #1 | UE5 | UE3 | UE12 | UE16 | UE2 | UE18 | UE4 | UE3 | UE4 | UE11  
PUCCH F1 | #2 | UE9 | UE1 | UE2 | UE20 | UE3 | UE5 | UE8 | UE8 | UE3 | UE5  
PUCCH F1 | #3 | UE10 | UE5 | UE15 | UE2 | UE6 | UE16 | UE5 | UE2 | UE6 | UE3  
PUCCH F1 | #4 | UE3 | UE8 | UE6 | UE18 | UE5 | UE9 | UE3 | UE9 | UE9 | UE2  
PUCCH F1 | #5 | UE11 | UE7 | UE9 | UE3 | UE7 | UE11 | UE6 | UE5 | UE12 | UE8  
PUCCH F1 | #6 | UE7 | UE9 | UE18 | UE5 | UE9 | UE7 | UE10 | UE11 | UE7 | UE6  
PUCCH F1 | #7 | UE12 | UE10 | UE7 | UE10 | UE12 | UE10 | UE11 | UE12 | UE16 | UE7  
PUCCH F1 | #8 | UE15 | UE18 | UE11 | UE9 | UE17 | UE20 | UE7 | UE17 | UE10 | UE9  
PUCCH F1 | #9 | UE17 | UE13 | UE14 | UE15 | UE10 | UE19 | UE12 | UE18 | UE17 | UE10  
PUCCH F1 | #10 |  | UE11 | UE20 | UE13 | UE19 | UE14 | UE17 | UE10 | UE18 | UE14  
PUCCH F1 | #11 | UE13 | UE17 | UE19 | UE17 |  | UE15 | UE18 | UE19 | UE13 | UE17  
  
In FDD cell, when rdDynamicPucchAlloSplitEnable (5G_UP_ALG_24678_replaced([11124282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 1 (enabled), L2PS shall split the PUCCH resource allocation (Round1 and Round2) to predefined DPA processing slots for PUCCH format1 and PUCCH format3. Details refer to implementation. 

Note: PUCCH resource unit refers to PUCCH resources in both time and frequency domain. For eg: if 12 F1 PUCCH resources are configured, in a span of 10 slots, we have 10*12 PUCCH F1 resource units. 

Note: This requirement is applicable only for UEs which use Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 

Note: UE serving cell in overheating/vRLF status is not considered in the PUCCH resource allocation. (For later improvement)

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.2.0-2 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE Round-1: PUCCH F3 Resource Allocation for FDD or TDD as P(S)Cell (ID: 11123756)

**3.7.4.3.1.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13333430`)

Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE DPA algorithm assigns PUCCH F3 resources to the UEs which have any one of below conditions: 

 Configured with FDD P(S)Cell and at least two active FDD SCells, or 

 Configured with FDD P(S)Cell and at least one active TDD SCell with two Downlink slots corresponding to FDD P(S)Cell downlink slot **where all PUCCH F3 resources are involved, or**

 Configured with FR1 TDD Cell as P(S)Cell 

With following manner:

**Common for FDD or TDD P(S)Cell:**

 In each slot UEs are pre-allocated with the PUCCH F3 resources in the order of ueWeight and pucchF3ResUnitRank (i.e highest ueWeight is mapped to highest pucchF3ResUnitRank if applicable). 

 When UE is assigned to the PUCCH F3 resource in a given slot, its ueWeight is reduced by rdPUCCHWeightStep = 1/ PUCCH slots during Schedule PUCCH Cycle (For FDD PUCCH slots=rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec default value is 10 and step is 0.1) and this UE is not considered to the allocation in that slot anymore. 

 If UE cannot be allocated to the certain PUCCH resource, the next CA UE with the same or lower ueWeight is considered. 

 If more than one UE has the same ueWeight, only one of CA UEs shall be selected. The decision is up to CP3. 

 If pCSI report is expected to be transmitted in the same slot as HARQ-AN, PUCCH Resource Allocation for CA UE over pCSI UL Slot is applicable (see 5G_UP_ALG_2930_replaced([11123814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql96PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 If scheUePoolingAllowed (5G_RAN_OP_1938_replaced([11692648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Y_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to true, the maximum number of PUCCH F3 HARQ resources for FDD cells per slot shall not be greater than rrmNumOfF3ForHarq (is the number of PUCCH F3 for A/N reporting defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2465_replaced([11116066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 

 When all PUCCH F3 resources are assigned to UEs or there are no UEs that can be assigned with free PUCCH F3 resources, algorithm goes to the next round (see 5G_UP_ALG_28065_replaced([11123772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql94fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 

**In Case of FDD as P(S)Cell:**

 For UEs configured with FDD P(S)Cell if all the following conditions are fulfilled (i.e.)

o At least in one MO, MOD(V_T_DAI(m) – 1, 4) <= 1; (No more than 2 DL assignments can be transmitted in current MO (PDCCH monitoring occasion))

o In the last MO, V_T_DAI(m) >= 3; (3 or more DL assignments can be transmitted in current bundle window)

then one PUCCH format3 resource and one PUCCH format1 resource (double allocation) with identical index must be allocated to UE for such slots. where: V_T_DAI(m) is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2941_replaced([11123890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqmk9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

**Rationale: In case double allocation would not happen. i.e. if only a PUCCH format3 resource is allocated to UE, but UE only detects DL assignments in the “PF1 MO” and all the DL assignments in other MOs are missed(rare and mostly theoretical case) , then UE will transmit HARQ-AN on a PUCCH format1 resource with the index indicated by gNB in the DL assignments, while gNB will try to decode the HARQ-AN on a PUCCH format3 resource with the same index and cause mismatch between UE and gNB. On the other hand, if the PUCCH format1 resource with the same index is allocated to other UE, strong interference between UEs will arise in this case.**

o **Note1: F1 resource which is pre-allocated together with F3 resource is marked as allocated and not used in the second-round of algorithm (put reference to round 2 req)**

o **Note2: If UEs are pre-allocated with both PUCCH F3 resource and a F1 resource in the same slot during the first round PUCCH resource pre-allocation, the pre-allocated F1 resources in the slot may exceed F1 split limitation i,e. allocated F1 numbers exceeded general F1 split ratio pucchF1SplitDistributed (5G_UP_ALG_2918_replaced([11123676](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

 In case UE is configured with 3CC and above **FR1 DL CA with FDD as PCell** activated, if the downlink slots can be scheduled only on max 2 CCs and the rest of serving cells cannot be scheduled **(eg. due to SSB slot or TRS slot or DSS [CB007372-H] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-H]), F3 resource shall not be allocated for the UE. This is because only F1 resource is enough for the UE in this slot.** ****

**In case of TDD as P(S)Cell:**

 In FR1 TDD cell, for UEs with this cell as P(S)Cell : 

o In the UL slot with SR resource configured for CA UE, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2927_replaced([11123805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql95vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PUCCH resource allocation. 

o In the UL slot with pCSI resource configured for CA UE, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2930_replaced([11123814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql96PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PUCCH resource allocation. 

o In all other cases than above 2: 

 if actLongPucchResourceOpt is set to ‘1’, pucchF3ResUnitRank is not used. Instead, DPA will select a PUCCH F3 resource in ascending order of PUCCH resource index in PUCCH resource set1. 

 If actLongPucchResourceOpt is set to ‘0’, pucchF3ResUnitRank is used for PUCCH F3 resource selection. 

If a PUCCH F3 is selected by any of above 3 scenarios, DPA algorithm shall check whether the following conditions are true: 

  1. The selected PUCCH F3 is free. 

  2. PRB of selected PUCCH F3 resource is not occupied by other allocated F1 resources. 

  3. The PUCCH F1 resource with same PUCCH resource index in PUCCH resource set 0 as the selected PUCCH F3 resource is free. 

  4. PRB of the PUCCH F1 resource with same PUCCH resource index in PUCCH resource set 0 as the selected PUCCH F3 is not occupied by other allocated F3 resources. (Note, PRB occupied by other F1 shall not block this check). 




Else if any of the above conditions is false, DPA shall not allocate the selected PUCCH F3 resource to the UE and shall check for another F3 resource. If actLongPucchResourceOpt is set to ‘1’, DPA shall select the next F3 resource candidates one after the other one or finally fail to allocate any PUCCH resource to the UE. 

**Remarks:**

 This requirement is applicable only if distributed PUCCH algorithm is applicable (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 For CA UE with FR1 TDD as P(S)Cell, 5G-L2-PS will allocate PUCCH F3 resource while implicitly allocate the PUCCH F1 with same PUCCH resource index. (Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2920_replaced([11310861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrTmu_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) regarding PUCCH resource configuration to UE for HARQ A/N which implicitly define the same index for PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 0 and pucch-ResourceSetId = 1 to same PRB for PUCCH for HARQ A/N) 

 For rdPUCCHWeightStep see 5G_L2_1478_replaced([11184466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27rTKPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.2.0-3 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE Round-2: PUCCH F1 Resource Allocation for FDD Cell as P(S)Cell (Not applicable to TDD P(S)Cell, since F3+F1 assignment done in Round-1) (ID: 11123772)

**3.7.4.3.1.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13333096`)

13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE 13333096: Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE DPA algorithm shall assign PUCCH F1 resources to the UEs which use Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm regardless of the number of active SCells with following steps: 

 ueWeight of UEs which have more than 1 active SCell reflects the value after the Round-1 completed. 

 In each slot UEs are assigned to the PUCCH Format 1 resources in the order of ueWeight and pucchF1ResUnitRank (i.e. highest ueWeight is mapped to highest pucchF3ResUnitRank if applicable).

 If the UE cannot be allocated to a certain PUCCH F1 resource, the next CA UE with the same or lower ueWeight is considered. 

 If more than one UE has the same ueWeight, only one of CA UEs shall be selected. The decision is up to CP3. 

 When UE is assigned to the PUCCH F1 resource in a given slot, its ueWeight is reduced by rdPUCCHWeightStep = 1/PUCCH Slots during Scheduling Cycle (For FDD PUCCH slots=rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec default value is 10 and step is 0.1) and this UE is not considered to the allocation in that slot anymore. 

 When all PUCCH F1 resources are assigned to UEs or there are no UEs that can be assigned with free PUCCH F1 resources, algorithm is finished. 

When only PUCCH Format 1 is assigned for UE in each slot instead of PUCCH Format 3, then not all activated SCells can be scheduled. In such case, generalized algorithm below describes how to select a smaller number of serving cells for scheduling than the actual schedulable cells. 

 If the UE with FDD P(S)Cell has pre-allocated F1 PUCCH resource, but the number of its active SCells is higher than one FDD SCell or at least one TDD SCell, then PCell and only one of the FDD SCells or TDD SCell slot 1 or 2 should be scheduled.

 The FDD SCell / TDD SCell slot selection shall be in round robin manner with assumptions: 

a) Round robin queue is ordered from the SCell with lowest SCell index (FDD SCell or TDD SCell slot 1) 

b) If available, next active SCell with ascending SCell index is added to the queue (FDD SCell or TDD SCell slot 1) 

c) When all FDD SCells and TDD SCells slot 1 are added to the queue, then TDD SCells slot 2 are added to the queue ordered ascendingly by SCell index as well. 

d) If FDD PCell is not schedulable in the slot (e.g., due to DSS [CB007372-H] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-H]) up to 2 SCells can be selected from the round robin queue, but if only one TDD SCell is selected, both DL slots 1 and 2 can be used. 

e) If the SCell is not schedulable in the slot (e.g., due to DSS [CB007372-H] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-H]), this SCell is skipped and next schedulable SCell is chosen from the round robin queue. 

f) Round robin queue shall be handled in a loop within PUCCH scheduling cycle (rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec (default 10 ms)). Starting SCell index shall be randomly selected. 

e.g. For 4CC DL CA configuration 2F+2T the selection is: PCell FDD + SCell1 FDD, PCell FDD + SCell2 TDDs1, PCell FDD + SCell3 TDDs1, PCell FDD + SCell2 TDDs2, PCell FDD + SCell3 TDDs2, ... 

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a table showing the slot allocation for different cells. The table has four rows representing "FDD Pcell", "FDD Scell1", "TDD SCell2", and "TDD SCell3". The columns represent time slots: "Slot n", "slot n+1", "slot n+2", "slot n+3", and "slot n+4". Green colored cells indicate that the corresponding cell is active during that slot, while white cells indicate inactivity. Here's the table in markdown format:

| Slot n | slot n+1 | slot n+2 | slot n+3 | slot n+4  
---|---|---|---|---|---  
FDD Pcell | Green | Green | Green | Green | Green  
FDD Scell1 | Green | White | White | White | White  
TDD SCell2 | White | Green | White | Green | White  
TDD SCell3 | White | White | Green | White | Green  
  
**_*Note: Assumptions d, e and f are not depicted in the example above._** *

 In case of FR1 CA, if all the serving cells are DSS [CB007372-H] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-H]and because of slot pattern change as per 5G_UP_ALG_2895_replaced([11123549](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkItvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), all the serving cells cannot be scheduled in the slot, F1 resource shall not be allocated for the UE. This is because, F1 resource is not needed for the UE in this slot.

**Remarks:**

 This requirement is applicable only if distributed PUCCH algorithm is applicable(5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 Number of slots in the PUCCH scheduling cycle is defined in rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec (5G_UP_ALG_2948_replaced([11123971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 For rdPUCCHWeightStep see 5G_L2_1478_replaced([11184466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27rTKPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Only PUCCH F1 resource units as mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_2918_replaced([11123676](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are to be used.

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.2.0-4 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE PUCCH resource allocation exceptions in DPA algorithm (ID: 11123795)

**3.7.4.3.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11123800`)

Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE CA UE cannot be allocated to the certain PUCCH F1 and/or F3 resource in case of: 

 UE has been pre-allocated with other PUCCH resource in a given slot (e.g., FDD 3CC UE is allocated F3 resource in round-1 and is not allocated F1 resource in round-2). Note: except cases where double allocation (F1 and F3 resources used together) is applied.

 Given PUCCH resource is not addressable by the CA UE. 

 /NRBTS/NRCELL/actSharedSr is set to true and /NRBTS/NRCELL/pucchModeSelect is set to longPucch and the cell-related parameter sharedSrPrb (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_7088_replaced([11278984](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbkfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal to the parameter startingPrb of the UE’s SR resource (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2973_replaced([11311385](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrYfOPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and only the UE’s shared SR resource is configured in the next UL slot. 

 CA UEs are during the SCell de-activation [CB011081-A] of the last SCell [End CB011081-A] or SCell release period [CB011081-A] of the last SCell [End CB011081-A].

 maxPayloadSize (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_8300_replaced([11312344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrhpIPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PUCCH resource set1 of a FDD PCell is configured with a value smaller than 8 and the slot where PUCCH resource is to be allocated to the UE coincides with CSI report slot for that UE, then UE shall not be considered by DPA for that slot and ueWeight is not changed (The UE with multiplexing capability of CSI report and HARQ ACK/NACK can still be scheduled but does not need F1 resource allocated). 

 CA UEs with DRX configured, if they are in off-duration during the next Scheduling Cycle based on PCell DRX status, UE shall not be considered for that slot and keep its ueWeight. If they are in on-duration during the next Scheduling Cycle (including the extension due to DRX inactivity timer) based on PCell DRX status, the CA UE shall be pre-allocated with PUCCH resource. 

Remark:

Only the UEs eligible for scheduling in the slots are considered for DPA and their ueWeight are updated if UEs have been pre-allocated with PUCCH resources (e.g., if the UE is not active because of DRX/Measurement gaps/RLF, it will not be considered for DPA. For uplink slots of SCell or downlink slots can't schedule on SCell, the CA UE still can be scheduled on PCell and can be pre-allocated with F1 PUCCH resource).

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.2.0-5 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE PUCCH Resource Allocation for CA UE over SR Only UL Slot (FR1 TDD as P(S)Cell) (ID: 11123805)

**3.7.4.3.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11123811`)

Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE For UE(s) configured with FR1 TDD cell as P(S)Cell, in the UL slot in which UE might report SR, there shall be no extra prioritization to the PUCCH resources in PUCCH resource set1, that is, all the PUCCH resources in PUCCH resource set1 shall be prioritized according to 5G_UP_ALG_2900_replaced([11123572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqkIu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Rationale: when CB006138 is implemented, maxPayloadSize of PUCCH resource set1 will be increased from 8 to 12 for CA UEs (including both 2CC CA UEs and 3CC CA UEs; for non-CA UEs, maxPayloadSize of PUCCH resource set1 is kept 8), and the maximum number of HARQ-AN bits per bundle window is 11, plus 1bit for SR, all HARQ-AN+SR bits can be transmitted on a PUCCH in PUCCH resource set1; On the other hand, the Qualcomm UE bug (count CRC bits as UCI bits in case number of UCI bits > 11) is said to exist for few UEs and those UEs are restricted to a specific operator, so the workaround for the bug (set maxPayloadSize of set1 to 8 and copy 4 PUCCH resource in set1 to set2) is no longer applied, that is, no PUCCH resource in set1 will be copied to set2 for both CA UEs and non-CA UEs.

---

###### 3.7.4.3.1.2.0-6 Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE PUCCH Resource Allocation for CA UE over pCSI UL Slot (FR1 TDD as PCell) or (FDD as PCell) (ID: 11123814)

**3.7.4.3.1.2.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `11123834`)

Assign PUCCH Resources to the UE During PUCCH resource allocation for CA UE with FR1 TDD cell as P(S)Cell, or for CA UE with FDD cell as PCell and being configured with maxPayloadSize of PUCCH resource set1 [CB009854-AA] greater than or [End CB009854-AA] equals to 8, DPA need to consider the PUCCH allocation as follows when there is configured pCSI resource in the UL slot.

  * If simultaneousHarqAckCsi = False, PUCCH resource will not be allocated. (To avoid the drop of CSI report)
  * If simultaneousHarqAckCsi = True for the CA UE:



if (PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 2 is configured)

{

if (number of UCI bit in pCSI report plus 1 bit for SR if SR is configured in the same slot with pCSI is larger than or equal to maxPayloadSize of PUCCH-ResourceSet with pucch-ResourceSetId = 1)

{

DPA will mark the PUCCH resource is available while HARQ A/N will be multiplexed with pCSI report.

}

else (need extra PUCCH F3 resource in PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 1 together with pCSI PUCCH resource in PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 2)

{

DPA will check whether PUCCH resource in PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 1 with same index as pCSI resource in PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 2 is available, if yes DPA will allocated the resource to the CA UE, otherwise DPA will not allocate the PUCCH resource to the CA UE.

}

}

else // PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 2 is NOT configured:

{

DPA will check whether the PUCCH resource in PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 1 is available, if yes DPA will allocated the resource to the CA UE, otherwise DPA will not allocate the PUCCH resource to the CA UE.

}

Rational: DPA algorithm will allocate the PUCCH resource to CA UE in advance of Scell scheduling, in case the index of allocated PUCCH resource in PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 1 is different to index of pCSI resource in PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 2, then there is mismatch for all serving cell to fill "PUCCH resource indicator" in DCI format 1_1 due to the switch from PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 1 to PUCCH-ResourceSets with pucch-ResourceSetId = 2.

Note:

  * Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2920_replaced([11310861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrTmu_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for TDD PCell or 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3004_replaced([11311737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrbijfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for FDD PCell regarding the PUCCH resources in each PUCCH-ResourceSet.
  * Refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_3819_replaced([11348132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wXgBPPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PUCCH-ResourceSets and to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_3822_replaced([11348145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wXgoQPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for pucch-ResourceSetId.
  * Refer to 5G_CP_IF_RRC_3816_replaced([11348112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wXgBN_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for simultaneousHarqAckCsi.
  * Refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_8300_replaced([11312344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrhpIPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for maxPayloadSize.

---

### 3.7.4.4 Scheduling Cycle

### 3.7.4.4-1 Scheduling Cycle

#### 3.7.4.4-1.0-7 Scheduling Cycle When SCell is activated, gNB-DU shall suspend and resume DPA for RRC reconfiguration which contains at least one of below contents: 1. Scell release 2. DL MCS table of the P(S)cell update. 3. PUCCH format 3 DMRS sequence modification (from R15 DMRS to R16 DMRS and vice versa). 4. DL DMRS configuration type of the P(S)cell update. 5. dmrsAdditionalPosition of the P(S)cell update 6. Step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] for UE, which is already configured with SCell(s), when the SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] procedure requires also change of L1 configuration in the PCell or retained SCell(s). When gNB-DU P(S)Cell receives start notification of the specific RRC reconfiguration mentioned above: - If modification of a certain DL or UL L1 parameter in the PCell or retained SCell(s) requires DL or UL branch of PCell’s 5G-L2-PS to enter the transient state (see Note 2), PCell’s gNB-DU shall stop DPA processing cycle to assign PUCCH resource, and wait N DPA scheduling cycles before entering the reconfiguration transient phase, until the PUCCH resources which have been pre-allocated to the SCell(s) are exhausted. After that the DL scheduling and UL is restricted to the P(S)Cell and the gNB-DU can enter the reconfiguration transient phase. If DL branch of PCell’s 5G-L2-PS enters the transient state, DL assignments in PCell shall be sent in CSS only, that is, DCI format 1_0 shall be used for DL scheduling. If UL branch of PCell’s 5G-L2-PS enters the transient state, UL assignments in PCell shall be sent in CSS only, that is, DCI format 0_0 shall be used for UL scheduling. After transient period of the specific RRC reconfiguration mentioned above, if there is still active SCell, gNB-DU P(S)Cell shall restart DPA for this UE. - Else, if modification of a certain DL/UL L1 parameter does not require entering to transient phase of DL or UL branch of PCell 5G-L2-PS (see Note 2), UE’s scheduling in the P(S)Cell shall remain unchanged. Note 1: Value N can be a R&amp;D parameter, which represents the minimum time expected for RRC reconfiguration reach to UE. gNB-DU shall delay the RRC reconfiguration message so that it won’t be received by UE before N DPA scheduling cycle is finished. Note 2: Not all L1 configuration changes in the PCell accompanying the step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] require PCell’s gNB-DU to enter the transient state. For details refer to ( 11120310 ). (ID: 12647019)

### 3.7.4.4-2 Scheduling Cycle

#### 3.7.4.4-2.0-3 Scheduling Cycle Upon the start of a User Reconfiguration Transient Phase in UL, the gNB-DU shall stop the DPA processing cycle to assign a PUCCH resource for a P(S)Cell if all the following are true: semiStatic betaOffset configuration for UE [Before PR771227] Reconfiguration updates any of the following: MCS table update in UL involving 64QAMLowSE MCS table, i.e, 64QAMLowSE MCS table&lt;-&gt;any other MCS table UE's SAg Mode change [End PR771227] Reconfiguration also updates any of the following: Any of betaOffsetAck indexes (betaOffsetAckIndex1, betaOffsetAckIndex2, betaOffsetAckIndex3) After the DPA processing cycle is stopped and PUCCH resources assigned are exhausted in scheduling cycle, the gNB-DU shall restrict to P(S)Cell scheduling only. if there is still active SCell after the end of the User Reconfiguration Transient Phase, the gNB-DU shall restart DPA for this UE. Notes: User Reconfiguration Transient Phase defined as period between the reception of a user modify request message and reception of a user reconfiguration complete request message. dynamicBetaOffsetInd reflects UE Capability. The enableDynamicBetaOffsets value reflects cell level configuration. Both are specified by 5G_UP_ALG_3500_replaced( 11159329 ) Two ways for semiStatic configuration: [1] UE does not support dynamic (dynamicBetaOffsetInd = false); [2] UE supports dynamic  (dynamicBetaOffsetInd = true), but cell does not (enableDynamicBetaOffsets = 'disable') Definitions for betaOffsetAck indexes specified in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2595_replaced( 11301063 ) DL scheduler could skip the scheduling during transient phase per 5G_UP_ALG_23479_replaced( 11174440 ) UL scheduler could skip the scheduling in the slot for HARQ feedback per 5G_UP_ALG_23614_replaced( 11195156 ) (ID: 11124029)

#### 3.7.4.4.0-1 Scheduling Cycle K1 value for Distributed PUCCH Allocation Algorithm (ID: 11123879)

**3.7.4.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11123884`)

Scheduling Cycle DL Scheduler shall consider K1 value as per 5G_UP_ALG_2473_replaced([11116092](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the CA UEs with distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the PUCCH F1 / PUCCH F3 resource allocated as per 5G_UP_ALG_2934_replaced([11123848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql97_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

13320139: Scheduling Cycle 13320139: Scheduling Cycle 13320139: Scheduling Cycle _Note: 5GC002640-AA extends the algorithm to the generic case, i.e. applicable for any number of Component Carriers with FDD PCell._ 5G-L2-PS shall calculate c-DAI/t-DAI for each CA UE over the HARQ A/N bundling window with PUCCH resource allocated (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2924_replaced([11123706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The details are as follows: Set m = 0 (PDCCH monitoring occasion in the HARQ A/N bundling window) V_C_DAI(m, c) = 1; V_T_DAI(m) = 1; While m < M (PDCCH monitoring occasions in current HARQ bundling window, refer to 9.1.3.1 of TS 38.213) Set c = 0 (iterator over the serving cell(s), which in a given PDCCH monitoring occasion ‘m’ could transmit DCI format 1_1 including c-DAI/t-DAI for a given CA UE; lower iterators correspond to lower RRC indexes of corresponding cell) While c < N (number of configured DL cells for CA UE which could transmit a DCI format 1_1 in monitoring occasion ‘m’) if CA UE is not limited by DRX configuration: if c = 0 and m <> 0 V_C_DAI(m, c) = V_T_DAI(m-1) + 1; if c <> 0 V_C_DAI(m, c) = V_C_DAI(m, c-1) + 1; c = c+1; End while; V_T_DAI(m) = V_C_DAI(m, c-1); m = m+1; End while; The actual c-DAI (value of the counter DAI in DCI format 1_1) for scheduling on serving cell c in PDCCH monitoring occasion m and t-DAI (value of the total DAI in DCI format 1_1) in PDCCH monitoring occasion m will follow Table 9.1.3-1 of TS 38.213. c-DAI(m,c) = Mod(V_C_DAI(m, c)-1, 4); t-DAI(m) = Mod(V_T_DAI(m)-1, 4); Where: \- The calculation shall be executed during PUCCH resource allocation to UE (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2924_replaced([11123706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \- The serving cell which is not activated during PUCCH resource allocation to UE will not be considered for c-DAI and t-DAI calculation and will not be considered for PDSCH scheduling in next Scheduling Cycle. An example of the DAI computation is shown in the following figure: For FDD PCell: [CB007372-H] Note: In the example there is symmetric DSS cell (NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false) with the first PDCCH occasion in symbol#2. DSS cells with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true have the first PDCCH occasion in symbol#0, like non DSS cells. [End CB007372-H] [vsd_desc]=== Diagram Content === Text Drag the side handles to change the width of the text block. The details are as follows: Set m = 0 (monitoring occasion in the HARQ A/N bundling window) c = 0; V_T_DAI(m) = 1; V_C_DAI(m, c) = 1; While( m < M(monitoring occasions in current HARQ bundling window, refer to 9.1.3.1 of TS38.213) ) { Set c = 0 (serving cell index of the CA UE) While( c < N (number of configured DL cells for CA UE)) { if( current serving cell is activated and CA UE is not limited by scheduling over current serving cell due to PUCCH resource limitation(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2927_replaced([11123805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql95vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or DRX configuration) { If( c == 0 ) { if(m > 0) { V_C_DAI(m, c) = V_T_DAI(m-1) + 1; } else //m = 0 { V_C_DAI(m, c) = 1; } } else { V_C_DAI(m, c) = V_C_DAI(m, c-1) + 1; } } c = c + 1; } //end while (c < N) V_T_DAI(m) = V_C_DAI(m, c-1); m = m + 1; }//end while(m < M) The actual c-DAI (value of the counter DAI in DCI format 1_1) for scheduling on serving cell c in PDCCH monitoring occasion m and t-DAI (value of the total DAI in DCI format 1_1) in PDCCH monitoring occasion m will follow Table 9.1.3-1 of TS 38.213. If(PUCCH resource set[1] is the last PUCCH resource set) { maxHarqAn = ceiling[(#UCI(HarqAn) + 1)/4]*4 - 1; [Before PR728073]

# UCI(HarqAn) is determined by querying the 2nd table in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_9064_replaced([11312258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrhCE_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with current CA configuration of UE;

[PR728073]

# UCI(HarqAn) is retrieved from the message sent by C-Plane to setup / modify UE context in L2-PS for SCell addition / release.

[End PR728073] } Else //PUCCH resource set[2] is configured { maxHarqAn = maxPayloadSize of PUCCH resource set[1] - 1; } if(V_C_DAI(m, c) > maxHarqAn) { c-DAI(m, c) = INVALID_VALUE; } else { c-DAI(m,c) = MOD(V_C_DAI(m, c) – 1, 4); } if(V_T_DAI(m) > maxHarqAn) { t-DAI(m) = MOD(maxHarqAn -1, 4); } else { t-DAI(m) = MOD(V_T_DAI(m) – 1, 4); } Where: * The calculation shall be executed during PUCCH resource allocation to UE(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2924_replaced([11123706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqlW1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) * The serving cell is not activated during PUCCH resource allocation to UE will not be considered for c-DAI and t-DAI calculation and will not be considered for PDSCH scheduling in next Scheduling Cycle. The bundle window is divided into slots, labeled "Slot #0" and "Slot #1". Each cell has multiple sub-slots within these slots, indicated by gray and light blue rectangles. |  |  |  |   
Within the slots, numbers are displayed in a "numerator/denominator" format. For example, in Slot #0 for PCell, it shows "0/2". In Slot #1 for PCell, it shows "3/1". SCell1 shows "1/2" in Slot #0 and "0/1" in Slot #1. SCell2 shows "2/2" in Slot #0 and "1/1" in Slot #1. |  |  |  |   
A blue text box at the bottom left of the image contains the text: "Slots overlapping with measurement gap are not numbered for DAI setting". Arrows point from this text box to the gray rectangles in Slot #0 and Slot #1, indicating that these specific slots are not numbered for DAI (Discontinuous Reception) setting due to their overlap with the measurement gap.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6924.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] |  |  |  |

Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle 11123965: Scheduling Cycle After P(S)Cell scheduler receive the SCell scheduling result, P(S)Cell scheduler shall generate the HARQ A/N codebook mapping to scheduling monitoring occasion of each serving cell as follows which is for decoding the HARQ A/N over PUCCH or PUSCH. (refer to Section 9.1.3 of TS38.213)

5G-L2-PS determines the [image-0][image_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6926.001.png[/image_path][/image-0], for a total number of [image-1][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6926.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] HARQ-ACK information bits, according to:

\- Firstly in ascending order of serving cell index;

\- Secondly in ascending order of PDCCH monitoring occasion index [image-2][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6926.003.png[/image_path][/image-2], where [image-3][image_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6926.004.png[/image_path][/image-3].

Considering DPA algorithm introducing the fake scheduling(no actual scheduling over one PDSCH slot, but considered in c-DAI/t-DAI calculation), 5G-L2-PS shall also mark the fake scheduling in the codebook bitmap so ignore the NACK from UE due to the fake scheduling.

Note:

  * Due to DCI missing which may cause the ambiguity between gNB and UE, gNB will now aware the ambiguity and will not trigger the multiple decoding of UCI over PUCCH/PUSCH. This will cause wrong decoding(lower SINR for UCI decoding) of HARQ A/N codebook, which can only be resolved with retransmission of all related PDSCH scheduling.

  * Considering the delay of scheduling result from SCell to P(S)Cell, 5G-L2-PS will consider the enough timing for scheduling result sending back from SCell to P(S)Cell, so relationship of K1 and K2 shall be considered which is part of implementation.




For example of ambiguity case, with following example UE missed all DCIs of first two monitoring occasions while gNB will expect 8 bits of HARQ A/N, however UE will report only 4 bits of HARQ A/N.

[image-4][image_desc]The image contains a table with a green header row and white rows and columns. The header row contains the text "UE (c-DAI, t-DAI)". The first column has the labels "Pcell" and "Scell". The subsequent columns are labeled "D", "D", "D", and "U". The cells within the table contain pairs of numbers in parentheses, such as "(0,1)", "(2,3)", "(1,1)", and "(3,3)". The cell under the "U" column for "Pcell" contains the text "A/N: 4 bit". Some cells are shaded gray.

| D | D | D | D | U  
---|---|---|---|---|---  
Pcell | (0,1) | (2,3) | (0,1) | (2,3) | A/N: 4 bit  
Scell | (1,1) | (3,3) | (1,1) | (3,3) |

#### 3.7.4.4.0-5 Scheduling Cycle Length of Scheduling Cycle. (ID: 11123971)

**3.7.4.4.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11123979`)

Scheduling Cycle Length of the Scheduling Cycle can be controlled via [Before CB012528-D ] rdSchedulePUCCHCycle_msec (default: 10 ms) (5G_L2_1464_replaced([11184335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27qFFfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB012528-D ] rrmSchedulePucchCycle_msec (10ms) [End CB012528-D ]

The scheduling Cycle shall be aligned to SFN boundary.

Note: This requirement is applicable only if Distributed PUCCH algorithm is enabled(5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

## 3.7.5 Carrier Aggregation Counters

### 3.7.5.0-3 Carrier Aggregation Counters Distributed PUCCH algorithm Counters (ID: 11124049)

**3.7.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11124053`)

Carrier Aggregation Counters For each configured subcell, 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the following internal counters for the PM counter report. The internal counter shall be saved in cell database.

For L2-PS UL:

M55316CRD50001--Number of CA UE allocations with F1 resource based on UL slot by distributed PUCCH

M55316CRD50002--Number of CA UE allocations with F3 resource based on UL slot by distributed PUCCH

For L2-PS DL:

M55316CRD50003--Number of CA UE scheduling with both P(S)cell and S-Cell, or P(S)cell only, or S-Cell only

M55316CRD50004--Number of non-CA UE blocked scheduling due to lack of PUCCH resource units

M55316CRD50005--Number of CA UE blocked scheduling due to lack of PUCCH resource units

Initial value of all distributed PUCCH counters are set to 0.

When DPA algorithm assign PUCCH F1 resource to each CA UE in each UL slot with PUCCH resource units, for Pcell 5G-L2-PS, M55316CRD50001 is increased by 1;

When DPA algorithm assign PUCCH F3 resource to each CA UE in each UL slot with PUCCH resource units, for Pcell 5G-L2-PS, M55316CRD50002 is increased by 1; When both PUCCH F3 and F1 resources to one CA UE at the same time, only update M55316CRD50002.

When each CA UE is scheduled, PCell L2-PS DL scheduler shall record the number of CA UE scheduling which are scheduled in P(S)-Cell and S-Cell, P(S)-Cell only, or S-Cell only, and increase M55316CRD50003 by 1 when distributed PUCCH algorithm pre-allocated PUCCH is used.

When each non-CA UE can’t be scheduled due to lack of PUCCH resource, L2-PS DL scheduler shall record the number of non-CA UEs blocked scheduling due to lack of PUCCH resource, and increase M55316CRD50004 by 1.

Note:If CA UE is not pre-allocated PUCCH resource and is scheduled as non-CA UE, if the UE can’t be scheduled due to lack of PUCCH resource, L2-PS DL scheduler shall record the number of non-CA UEs blocked scheduling due to lack of PUCCH resource, and increase M55316CRD50004 by 1.

When each CA UE is in CS1 list but not pre-scheduled PUCCH resource, SCell L2-PS DL scheduler shall record the number of CA UEs blocked scheduling due to lack of PUCCH resource but report cell ID is SCell ID, and increase M55316CRD50005 by 1.

Note:As Scell can't get PCell ID based on current implementation, M55316CRD50005 report Scell ID.

---

### 3.7.6.0-17 R&amp;D parameters rdMsgDelayThreshSCellTdd (ID: 11124236)

Default value: 7

Unit: slot

Online modifable: No

Step size: 1

This R&D parameter is obsolete after CB009103-E, delay threshold used in SCell in case PCell is a TDD cell is replaced by time margin threshold used in SCell (rdP2SmarginThreshTddPcell), see 5G_UP_ALG_32155_replaced([11124417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqqPb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

### 3.7.6.0-35 R&amp;D parameters rdS2PmarginThreshFddPCell (ID: 11124389)

**3.7.6.0-35.0-1**  (ID: `11124393`)

R&D parameters This parameter specifies the time margin threshold used to decide whether delay on Xp-U link is too high for inter-gNB CA in case UE’s PCell is a FDD cell, that is, if time margin of the DPA measurement report message from ext-SCell to PCell is less than rdS2PmarginThreshFddPCell, then large delay is detected by PCell.

time margin = time when information included in a message is used – time when the message is received.

Value range: 0, …, 1000

Default value: 0

Unit: micro-second

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Used in: 5G_UP_ALG_13314_replaced([11121985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqcM4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

### 3.7.6.0-39 R&amp;D parameters rdScellDeactLvlCB012734 (ID: 11124428)

**3.7.6.0-39.0-1**  (ID: `11124432`)

R&D parameters This parameter specifies the fraction of current data rate in all active serving cells of a FR2 CA UE, below which SCell deactivation will be triggered. this parameter will be used only when CB012734 is activated (NRCELLGRP.actHighNumberOfUEs = True).

Value range: 0 ~ 3

Default value: 0.1

Unit: none

Online modifiable: No

Step size: 0.1

Used in: 5G_UP_ALG_2713_replaced([11120950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2738_replaced([11120974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqVfO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

During the PET test of CB012734, throughput unstable and lower than expectation was observed if sCellActivationMethod is set to bufferBased, and this problem disappears if rdScellDeactivationLevel is set to 0.1 (default value 0.9). To avoid impact on KPI of legacy features, FOT decided to introduce a new R&D parameter with default value 0.1 and replace rdScelDeactivationLevel in SCell deactivation threshold calculation when CB012734 is activated.

R&D parameters If the rrmULProposedMcs is higher than or equal to this parameter then buffer split to SCell is done, or when SCell is deactive, buffer status check shall be considered for SCell activation as defined in [12652679](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YQ-LkUYdEfCO0aKCUF-F5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YQ-LkUYdEfCO0aKCUF-F5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")

value range: [17,22]

default value: 17

Unit: none

Online modifable: No

Step size: 1

Used in: [12652679](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YQ-LkUYdEfCO0aKCUF-F5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YQ-LkUYdEfCO0aKCUF-F5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")

### 3.7.6.0-45 R&amp;D parameters rdPdschLoadCorrection (ID: 12722875)

**3.7.6.0-45.0-1**  (ID: `12722876`)

R&D parameters This parameter specifies additional compensation for PDSCH Load Calculation used for SCell Activation when limited bandwidth modes is active ( [12657028: Normal and limited bandwidth modes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SuX0YEg7EfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

For this case (CB012299) CA UEs are always scheduled only in the dedicated small BWP which size is the half of the size of the largest BWP.

value range: [0,100]

default value: 50

Unit: none

Online modifable: No

Step size: 1

Used in: [11121281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqXUcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

### 3.7.6.0-48 R&amp;D parameters rdMinUePwrForSCell (ID: 12883429)

**3.7.6.0-48.0-1**  (ID: `12883431`)

R&D parameters This parameter specifies the minimum UE power left for SCell to support parallel UL transmission in overlapping UL slots for UEs configured with TDD(PCell) + FDD UL CA and ~~simultaneousPUCCH-PUSCH-SamePriority-r17~~ parallelTxPUCCH-PUSCH-SamePriority-r17, that is, if configured maximum UE power in PCell without consideration of power reduction (PCMAX,PCell , dBm) – PUCCH transmission power (dBm) > rdMinUePowerForSCell (dB), then parallel UL transmission in overlapping UL slots are allowed. Otherwise, parallel UL transmission in overlapping UL slots is not allowed.

Value range: [0, 26]

Default value: 1

Unit: dB

Online modifiable: no

Step size: 1

Used in: [12882346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_cGa14bR4EfCQT7hYUxERAg)

---

### 3.7.6.0-49 R&amp;D parameters rdPathLossGap (ID: 12884350)

**3.7.6.0-49.0-1**  (ID: `12884352`)

R&D parameters This parameter specifies the gap between path loss of PUSCH and path loss of PUCCH, PUCCH path loss (dB) = PUSCH path loss (dB) + rdPathlossGap (dB). The gap originates from the difference between beamforming gain of PUSCH receiving beam and beamforming gain of PUCCH receiving beam.

Value range: [-6, 12]

Default value: 2

Unit: dB

Online modifiable: no

Step size: 0.5

Used in: [12882346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_cGa14bR4EfCQT7hYUxERAg)

---
